### [1] [Collision Energy Dependence of Hypertriton Production in Au+Au Collisions at RHIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18214)
*The STAR Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: STAR合作组测量了11个不同对撞能量下超氚核（${}^{3}_Λ$H）的横向动量谱和积分产额，发现其产额随对撞能量降低而显著增加，但比热模型预测低约2倍，且平均横向动量低于轻强子冻出参数的Blast-Wave预期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究超氚核（hypertriton）在不同对撞能量下的产生特性，以理解超子-核子（hyperon-nucleon）相互作用与核子-核子相互作用的差异，特别是在相对论重离子碰撞中的奇特核形成机制。

Method: 在STAR实验中测量了金+金（Au+Au）对撞在11个能量点（3.2-27 GeV）下，中心快度区（|y|<0.5）的超氚核横向动量谱和pT积分产额，并与热模型（thermal model）预测及Blast-Wave模型进行比较。

Result: 超氚核产额及其与Λ的产额比在中心碰撞中随对撞能量降低而显著增加，但比热模型预测低约2倍；平均横向动量低于基于轻强子冻出参数的Blast-Wave预期；双重比值（${}^{3}_Λ$H/Λ)/(t/p)在测量能量范围内保持恒定值~0.4。

Conclusion: 在聚结（coalescence）框架下，恒定的双重比值直接反映了弱束缚超氚核相对于氚核的形成概率显著抑制，这源于超子-核子相互作用比核子-核子相互作用更弱。

Abstract: The STAR Collaboration reports measurements of the collision energy dependence of hypertriton (${}^{3}_Λ$H) transverse momentum spectra and $p_{\rm T}$-integrated yields at mid-rapidity ($|y|<$0.5) in Au+Au collisions at 11 collision energies between 3.2 and 27\,GeV. The measured ${}^{3}_Λ$H yields and ${}^{3}_Λ$H/$Λ$ yields ratio in central collisions increase strongly with decreasing collision energy, and are a factor of $\sim$2 lower than thermal model predictions at this energy range. The mean $p_{\rm T}$ of ${}^{3}_Λ$H is lower than the Blast-Wave expectation using the freeze-out parameters from light hadrons. Furthermore, the observed double ratio $({}^{3}_Λ{\rm{H}}/Λ)/(t/p)$ maintains a constant value of $\sim$0.4 across the measured energy range. Within the coalescence framework, this ratio directly reflects the significantly suppressed formation probability of the weakly-bound hypertriton relative to the triton, which results from the weaker hyperon-nucleon interaction compared with the nucleon-nucleon interaction.

</details>

### [2] [Classical Percolation from Quantum Metric in Flat-Band Delocalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17438)
*Bo Yin Zhijun Wang,Quansheng Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了无序（disorder）如何使线性响应电导率对量子度量（quantum metric）敏感，在二维多平带晶格中识别出由量子度量决定的临界离域化区域，并建立了与经典渗流（percolation）模型的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究认为在清洁极限下线性响应电导率对量子度量不敏感，而贝里曲率（Berry curvature）贡献本征反常霍尔效应。本研究旨在探索无序如何改变这一情况，并揭示量子度量在输运中的新作用。

Method: 结合解析推导与数值计算，聚焦于二维多平带stub-pyrochlore晶格，分析无序对线性响应电导率的影响。通过连接实空间量子度量标记（quantum metric marker）与万尼尔函数（Wannier function）展宽，构建了方格上的键渗流（bond-percolation）模型。

Result: 发现了一个介于平带局域化（flat band localization）与安德森局域化（Anderson localization）之间的临界离域化区域，其特征为有限的几何电导率（geometric conductivity）。加入自旋轨道耦合（spin orbit coupling）后，该区域演变为扩散金属相，构成二维逆安德森转变（inverse Anderson transition）。渗流模型结果与临界离域化区域定量吻合，其指数支持经典渗流普适类（classical percolation universality class）。

Conclusion: 平带离域化可理解为量子度量"水坑"（quantum metric puddles）的经典渗流过程。这一发现推进了对量子几何贡献输运的理解，并确立了线性响应测量作为获取量子度量的新途径。

Abstract: The quantum metric is a fundamental ingredient of band quantum geometry and has recently at tracted intense interest, with most of its transport signatures appearing in the intrinsic second order nonlinear conductivity. In the clean limit, previous works argued that linear response conductivity is insensitive to the quantum metric, while the Berry curvature yields an intrinsic anomalous Hall con tribution. Here we combine analytic derivations with new numerics to show that disorder modifies the linear response conductivity dominated by geometric conductivity which is determined by the real space quantum metric. Focusing on a two dimensional multi-flatband stub-pyrochlore lattice, we identify a critical delocalized regime sandwiched between flat band localization and Anderson localization, characterized by finite geometric conductivity. Upon including spin orbit coupling, this regime evolves into a diffusive metallic phase, constituting a two dimensional inverse Anderson transition. Moreover, exploiting the connection between the real space quantum metric marker and the Wannier function spread, we construct a bond-percolation model on a square lattice. The resulting percolation region quantitatively coincides the critical delocalized regime, the exponent of which supports a classical percolation universality class. These findings suggest that flat band de localization can be understood as a classical percolation of quantum metric puddles. This advances our understanding of quantum geometric contributions to transport and establishes linear response measurements as a new avenue for accessing the quantum metric.

</details>


### [3] [The vibrational spectrum of vitreous silica: rigorous decomposition via recursive orthogonal splitting analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17933)
*Nikita S Shcheblanov,Anaël Lemaître*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了递归正交分割分析（ROSA）框架，用于系统分解非晶固体（如二氧化硅玻璃）的振动谱，揭示振动自由度的层次结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对固体振动的理解主要基于晶体周期性概念，无法应用于非晶材料。缺乏系统框架将非晶固体的振动谱分解为与明确原子运动类型相关的贡献，这阻碍了对基于声学、热学或光学性质测量的线性响应实验探针的解释。

Method: 构建了递归正交分割分析（ROSA）框架，通过递归应用投影形式主义（projection formalism）分解振动空间。该过程利用主导刚度对比（dominant stiffness contrast）将振动位移子空间分割为两个弱耦合的正交补集（orthogonal complements）。

Result: 将ROSA应用于典型共价玻璃（vitreous silica）时，成功分离出键拉伸、对称和反对称氧运动、各向同性和偏斜四面体应变以及不同类别的四面体弯曲，揭示了涉及六个相互正交子空间的振动自由度层次结构。这些子空间选择性捕获了所有显著光谱特征，包括低频范围的双峰结构、800 cm⁻¹附近的峰值和高频双重峰。

Conclusion: ROSA仅依赖于与局部结构单元点对称性相关的对比刚度尺度（contrasted stiffness scales）的存在，以及通过投影形式主义强制执行几何约束进行分离，因此可直接应用于广泛的共价网络玻璃（covalent network glasses）类别。

Abstract: Our understanding of vibrations in solids currently rests on concepts and techniques designed for crystals and explicitly relying on periodicity, hence inapplicable to amorphous materials. As a consequence, no established framework enables a systematic decomposition of the vibrational spectrum of amorphous solids into contributions associated with well-defined types of atomic motions. This methodological gap obscures the interpretation of various experimental probes of linear response, based on the measurements of acoustic, thermal, or optical properties. Here, we construct such a framework-Recursive Orthogonal Splitting Analysis (ROSA)-which decomposes the vibrational space by recursive applications of the projection formalism. Each step of the procedure exploits a dominant stiffness contrast to split a vibrational displacement subspace into two weakly coupled orthogonal complements. We illustrate ROSA by applying it to the archetypal covalent glass-vitreous silica. Successively separating bond-stretching, symmetric and antisymmetric oxygen motions, isotropic and deviatoric tetrahedral strains, and distinct classes of tetrahedral bending, reveals a hierarchical structure of the space of vibrational degrees of freedom, involving six mutually orthogonal subspaces. These subspaces selectively capture all salient spectral features, including the two-humped structure in the low-frequency range, the peak near 800 cm -1 , and the high-frequency doublet. In the low-frequency range, rigid-unit tetrahedral rotations do not constitute independent degrees of freedom but are kinematically enslaved to bending coordinates by no-stretch constraints. Because ROSA relies solely on the existence of contrasted stiffness scales associated with the point symmetry of local structural units, and on their separation by enforcing geometric constraints via the projection formalism, it is directly applicable to a broad class of covalent network glasses.

</details>


### [4] [Replica Theory of Spherical Boltzmann Machine Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17936)
*Thomas Tulinski,Jorge Fernandez-De-Cossio-Diaz,Simona Cocco,Rémi Monasson*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究为玻尔兹曼机（Boltzmann machines）的集成学习（ensemble learning）提供了分析框架，揭示了集成学习与自旋玻璃模型（spin glass models）中自由能大偏差（large deviations of the free energy）的对偶关系，并通过副本计算（replica calculations）和数值模拟验证了集成学习优于标准损失最小化的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习训练通常寻找单个最小化数据依赖损失（data-dependent loss）的模型，但实证研究表明集成学习（ensemble learning）能提升性能。本文旨在为玻尔兹曼机提供分析框架来理解这一现象。

Method: 利用集成学习与自旋玻璃模型中自由能大偏差的对偶关系，通过副本计算（replica calculations）完全求解球形玻尔兹曼机集成（spherical Boltzmann machine ensembles）的情况。特别关注近有限维数据（nearly finite-dimensional data）的情况，并用深度网络数值模拟验证。

Result: 副本计算阐明了集成学习何时优于标准损失最小化。对于近有限维数据，副本预测在数据点数量相对于（大的）嵌入维度（embedding dimension）任意大时仍然有效。数值模拟证实了这些发现。

Conclusion: 该研究为玻尔兹曼机集成学习提供了理论分析框架，揭示了其与自旋玻璃物理的对偶关系，并确定了集成学习提供性能提升的条件，为理解机器学习中的集成方法提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Training in machine learning generally consists in finding one model, whose parameters minimize a data-dependent loss. Yet, empirical work shows that ensemble learning, an approach in which multiple models are sampled, can improve performance. Here, we provide an analytical framework to understand these observations in the case of Boltzmann machines, exploiting a duality between ensemble learning and large deviations of the free energy in spin-glass models. Replica calculations allow us to fully solve the case of spherical Boltzmann machine ensembles, and clarify when ensemble learning improves over standard loss minimization. Our findings are corroborated by numerical simulations on deep networks. Special care is brought to the case of nearly finite-dimensional data, for which we show that replica predictions are valid for arbitrarily large number of data points compared to the (large) embedding dimension.

</details>


### [5] [Intrinsic Neuro-Synaptic Spiking Dynamics and Resonance in Memristive Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18015)
*Yinhao Xu,Georg A. Gottwald,Zdenka Kuncic*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 忆阻自组织网络（self-organizing memristive networks）在特定频率输入下产生类似生物神经系统的群体放电动态，其计算最优频率出现在共振发生前的最大频率处。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索忆阻自组织网络的固有和涌现动态特性，这类物理电路能够根据外部输入信号动态重构其电路结构，其自适应行为源于内在神经突触动态与异质网络拓扑的结合。

Method: 通过数学分析和数值模拟方法，研究忆阻网络在直流（DC）和交流（AC）输入信号下的动态行为，特别关注输入驱动信号频率与网络固有动态时间尺度的匹配情况。

Result: 当输入信号频率与网络固有动态时间尺度匹配时，非线性共振（nonlinear resonance）现象出现，此时非线性尖峰状特征最大化；计算最优频率被确定为共振发生前的最大频率。

Conclusion: 忆阻自组织网络能够自然产生类似生物神经系统的神经元群体放电动态，其计算性能在特定频率条件下达到最优，这为神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）提供了物理实现基础。

Abstract: Self-organizing memristive networks are physical circuits that dynamically reconfigure their circuitry in response to external input signals. Their adaptive behavior arises from intrinsic neuro-synaptic dynamics combined with a heterogeneous network topology. In this work, we demonstrate that such networks naturally generate neuronal population spiking dynamics similar to those observed in biological neuronal systems. This study investigates the intrinsic and emergent dynamics of memristive networks mathematically and numerically for both DC and AC input signals. Nonlinear spike-like features are maximized when the frequency of the input driving signal matches the network's intrinsic dynamical timescale, where nonlinear resonance is observed. Furthermore, the optimal frequency for computation is found to be the maximal frequency before the onset of resonance.

</details>


### [6] [Transition path sampling in Ising models on heterogeneous graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18412)
*Riccardo Cipolloni,Federico Ricci-Tersenghi,Francesco Zamponi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究使用过渡路径采样（transition path sampling）方法分析有限稀疏随机图上伊辛模型（Ising model）铁磁态间的跃迁概率，通过三态动力学描述解释过渡概率曲线的瞬态起始，并在不同类型网络上验证方法，揭示了淬火拓扑无序（quenched topological disorder）对动力学速率的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激活跃迁（activated transitions）的速率通常随系统尺寸呈指数衰减，在实际中提取相关激活势垒（activation barriers）具有挑战性，特别是在深度亚稳态（deeply metastable regimes）和存在无序（disorder）的情况下。研究旨在解决这一难题。

Method: 采用过渡路径采样（transition path sampling）方法评估有限稀疏随机图上伊辛模型铁磁态间的跃迁概率；引入最小三态动力学描述（minimal three-state kinetic description）解释过渡概率曲线的瞬态起始；在异质Zachary Karate Club网络、随机正则图（random regular graphs）和Erdős-Rényi图上验证和应用该方法。

Result: 在随机正则图中样本间波动较弱，而在Erdős-Rényi图中淬火拓扑无序（quenched topological disorder）导致显著的实例变异性（instance variability）；针对Erdős-Rényi图引入实例依赖的温度重标度（instance-dependent temperature rescaling），恢复了动力学速率的一致有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling），实现了与相应静态自由能势垒（static free-energy barrier）的直接比较。

Conclusion: 该方法成功应用于无序系统中的亚稳态跃迁分析，揭示了拓扑无序对动力学行为的影响，并通过温度重标度技术建立了动力学速率与静态自由能势垒之间的联系，为研究复杂网络中的激活跃迁提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Activated transitions have rates that are often exponentially small in system size. Extracting the associated activation barriers is challenging in practice, especially in the deeply metastable regimes and in the presence of disorder. Here, we use transition path sampling to evaluate transition probabilities between ferromagnetic states in the Ising model on finite sparse random graphs, which are perhaps the simplest example of a disordered system with metastable states. To interpret the transient onset of the transition probability curve, we introduce a minimal three-state kinetic description that highlights the role of intermediate configurations. We validate the method on the heterogeneous Zachary Karate Club network, where distinct dynamical regimes emerge as temperature varies. We then apply the method to random regular graphs and Erdős-Rényi graphs, showing that sample-to-sample fluctuations are weak in the former but that quenched topological disorder induces sizable instance variability in the latter. For Erdős-Rényi graphs, we introduce an instance-dependent temperature rescaling that restores a consistent finite-size scaling of dynamical rates and enables a direct comparison with the corresponding static free-energy barrier.

</details>


### [7] [BBP transition and the leading eigenvector of the spiked Wigner model with inhomogeneous noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18523)
*Leonardo S. Ferreira,Fernando L. Metz*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有非均匀噪声的尖峰Wigner模型（spiked Wigner model）的谱特性，推导了谱边缘、离群特征值及其特征向量分布的精确方程，揭示了非单调的BBP相变线（BBP transition line），表明非均匀噪声可增强信号可检测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尖峰Wigner系综（spiked Wigner ensemble）是高维推断的原型模型。本研究旨在探索噪声矩阵每个条目的方差本身是随机变量的非均匀秩一尖峰Wigner模型的谱性质。

Method: 在高维极限下，推导了谱边缘（spectral edges）、离群特征值（outlier eigenvalue）以及离群特征向量（outlier eigenvector）分量分布的精确方程。这些方程确定了区分有隙相（gapped phase）和无隙相（gapless phase）的BBP相变线（BBP transition line）。

Result: 对于方差由截断幂律分布（truncated power-law distribution）生成的噪声矩阵，求解了相关方程。结果显示BBP相变线是非单调的，表明非均匀噪声可以增强信号可检测性（signal detectability）。在有隙区域，离群特征向量的分布提供了尖峰（spike）的自然估计器。

Conclusion: 非均匀噪声结构能够改变信号检测的相变行为，产生非单调的BBP相变线，这为高维推断中的信号检测问题提供了新的理论见解。

Abstract: The spiked Wigner ensemble is a prototypical model for high-dimensional inference. We study the spectral properties of an inhomogeneous rank-one spiked Wigner model in which the variance of each entry of the noise matrix is itself a random variable. In the high-dimensional limit, we derive exact equations for the spectral edges, the outlier eigenvalue, and the distribution of the components of the outlier eigenvector. These equations determine the BBP transition line that separates the gapped phase, where the signal is detectable, from the gapless phase. In the gapped regime, the distribution of the outlier eigenvector provides a natural estimator of the spike. We solve the equations for a noise matrix whose variances are generated from a truncated power-law distribution. In this case, the BBP transition line is non-monotonic, showing that an inhomogeneous noise can enhance signal detectability.

</details>


<div id='math.DS'></div>

# math.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Gibbs Measures on Symbolic Spaces: A Unified Treatment of Five Characterizations with Explicit Constants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17528)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明了有限型拓扑混合子移位上Hölder势能的吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure）五种刻画等价性，包括雅可比条件、经典柱状吉布斯性质、Ruelle转移算子的本征测度、变分平衡态和大偏差率函数最小化。证明提供了显式常数估计和谱隙分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于统一有限型拓扑混合子移位（topologically mixing subshifts of finite type）上Hölder势能的吉布斯测度多种等价刻画，建立包含显式常数的单一理论框架，并为后续六部曲系列研究双曲动力系统（hyperbolic dynamical systems）的热力学形式奠定基础。

Method: 采用Birkhoff锥收缩技术（Birkhoff cone contraction technique）获得转移算子的显式谱隙估计，通过分析雅可比条件（Jacobian condition）、柱状吉布斯性质（cylinder-based Gibbs property）、Ruelle转移算子（Ruelle transfer operator）本征测度、变分平衡态（variational equilibrium state）和大偏差率函数（large deviations rate function）最小化之间的等价关系。

Result: 建立了五种吉布斯测度刻画的等价性定理，提供了以Hölder指数、势能范数、字母表大小和混合时间为参数的显式常数表达式。获得了势能扰动下吉布斯测度在Wasserstein距离中的Lipschitz稳定性，以及包含Berry-Esseen界限的中心极限定理和大偏差原理等统计极限定理。

Conclusion: 本文成功证明了有限型拓扑混合子移位上Hölder势能吉布斯测度五种刻画的等价性，为双曲动力系统的热力学形式研究提供了统一的理论框架和显式估计工具，这是关于双曲动力系统热力学形式六部曲系列的第一部分。

Abstract: We prove that five characterizations of Gibbs measures for Hölder potentials on topologically mixing subshifts of finite type are equivalent: the Jacobian condition, the classical cylinder-based Gibbs property, the eigenmeasure of the Ruelle transfer operator, the variational equilibrium state, and the minimizer of the large deviations rate function. The equivalence is established in a single theorem with explicit constants expressed in terms of the Hölder exponent, the potential norm, the alphabet size, and the mixing time. The proof yields explicit spectral gap estimates for the transfer operator via the Birkhoff cone contraction technique, Lipschitz stability of the Gibbs measure in Wasserstein distance under perturbation of the potential, and statistical limit theorems including a central limit theorem with Berry-Esseen bounds and a large deviations principle. This paper constitutes Part I of a six-part series on the thermodynamic formalism for hyperbolic dynamical systems.

</details>


### [9] [The Geometry of Thermodynamic Equilibrium: Pressure, Tangent Functionals, and Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17531)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文建立了紧致度量空间上连续映射热力学形式主义的凸分析结构，证明了压力泛函是负熵的Legendre-Fenchel变换，并建立了完全对偶性。通过凸泛函的统一变分原理整合了加性、次加性和相对变分原理，并将结果推广到具有specification性质的系统和非紧致空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在发展紧致度量空间上连续映射的热力学形式主义（thermodynamic formalism）的凸分析结构。研究动机在于建立压力泛函与熵之间的完整对偶关系，并统一处理不同类型的变分原理。

Method: 采用凸分析（convex analysis）方法，将压力泛函构造为负熵的Legendre-Fenchel变换。通过满足凸性、下半连续性、强制性和上循环不变性的凸泛函的统一变分原理，整合了经典变分原理。方法扩展到具有specification性质的系统，并在强制性条件下推广到非紧致空间。

Result: 证明了压力泛函是负熵的Legendre-Fenchel变换，熵的双共轭恢复建立了完全对偶性。平衡态是压力的次微分元素，平衡态唯一性对应Gâteaux可微性，一阶相变对应不可微性。对于具有specification性质和Hölder势的系统，压力在Hölder范数下是Fréchet可微的，其二阶导数等于Birkhoff和的渐近方差。

Conclusion: 本文建立了热力学形式主义的完整凸分析框架，通过统一变分原理整合了经典变分原理。结果可推广到具有specification性质的系统和非紧致空间，并通过Sarig的回归分类应用于可数Markov移位。该论文是双曲动力系统热力学形式主义六部系列的第二部分。

Abstract: We develop the convex-analytic structure of the thermodynamic formalism for continuous maps on compact metric spaces. The pressure functional is the Legendre-Fenchel transform of the negative entropy, and the biconjugate recovery of the entropy from the pressure establishes a complete duality. Equilibrium states are elements of the subdifferential of the pressure, uniqueness of equilibrium states corresponds to Gâteaux differentiability, and first-order phase transitions correspond to non-differentiability. For systems with specification and Hölder potentials, the pressure is Fréchet differentiable in the Hölder norm, and the second derivative of the pressure equals the asymptotic variance of the Birkhoff sums. We prove a universal variational principle that unifies the classical additive, the subadditive, and the relative variational principles through a single theorem on convex functionals satisfying convexity, lower semi-continuity, coercivity, and cocycle invariance. Extensions to systems with the specification property and to non-compact spaces under coercivity conditions are included, with applications to countable Markov shifts via Sarig's recurrence classification. This paper constitutes Part II of a six-part series on the thermodynamic formalism for hyperbolic dynamical systems.

</details>


### [10] [Uniform Hyperbolicity and Symbolic Dynamics: Markov Partitions, Shadowing, and the Coding of Axiom A Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17608)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 该论文建立了具有显式定量界限的一致双曲集几何理论，包含五个主要定理：稳定流形定理、谱分解定理、跟踪引理、马尔可夫分割存在性以及编码映射构造，为将符号谱理论和变分理论转移到光滑环境提供了定量基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立具有显式定量界限的双曲集几何理论，为将符号谱理论（Part I）和变分理论（Part II）转移到光滑环境提供必要的定量基础设施。这是关于双曲动力系统热力学形式主义的六部分系列论文中的第三部分。

Method: 采用向后图变换（backward graph transform）证明稳定流形定理，包含完整的纤维收缩论证以获得C^r正则性和局部稳定/不稳定流形对基点的Hölder依赖性。通过构造性方法建立任意小直径的马尔可夫分割，并构建从有限型子移位到双曲集的编码映射。

Result: 证明了五个主要定理：稳定流形定理（含显式流形尺寸估计）、谱分解定理（含显式混合速率）、跟踪引理（含显式误差界）、马尔可夫分割存在性（含显式直径界）以及Hölder连续编码映射构造。所有常数均以收缩率、导数的Hölder指数、流形维数和单射半径表示。

Conclusion: 该论文建立了具有完整定量控制的双曲集几何理论，为将符号动力学和变分方法应用于光滑双曲动力系统提供了必要的数学基础设施。这项工作构成了双曲动力系统热力学形式主义系列研究的核心定量基础部分。

Abstract: This paper establishes the geometric theory of uniformly hyperbolic sets with explicit quantitative bounds throughout, and contains five main theorems. The Stable Manifold Theorem is proved via the backward graph transform, with a complete fiber-contraction argument yielding $C^r$ regularity and Hölder dependence of the local stable and unstable manifolds on the base point, with explicit manifold-size estimate in terms of the contraction rate $λ$ and the second-derivative bound of the diffeomorphism. The Spectral Decomposition Theorem gives the unique decomposition of the nonwandering set into basic sets, with explicit mixing rates for the topologically mixing factors. The Shadowing Lemma provides explicit error bounds controlling how far a pseudo-orbit deviates from a tracking true orbit. The existence of Markov partitions of arbitrarily small diameter is established constructively, with explicit diameter bounds expressed in terms of the shadowing constants. Finally, the coding map from the subshift of finite type to the hyperbolic set is constructed and shown to be Hölder continuous with quantitative control on the exceptional set where it fails to be injective. Along the way we establish canonical coordinates through the bracket map with quantitative bounds. All constants are expressed in terms of the contraction rate, the Hölder exponent of the derivative, the manifold dimension, and the injectivity radius, providing the quantitative infrastructure required to transfer the symbolic spectral theory of Part I and the variational theory of Part II to the smooth setting. This paper constitutes Part III of a six-part series on the thermodynamic formalism for hyperbolic dynamical systems.

### [11] [Morita equivalence for quantum graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18065)
*Alexandros Chatzinikolaou,Gage Hoefer,Nikolaos Koutsonikos-Kouloumpis,Ioannis Apollon Paraskevas*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 该论文建立了量子图（quantum graphs）的Morita等价性（Morita equivalence）的算子代数框架，证明了不可约量子图的Morita等价性条件，并展示了多种图论不变量在该等价性下的不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为量子图的Morita等价性建立一个算子代数框架，将Eleftherakis、Kakariadis和Todorov提出的图算子系统的Δ-等价性（Δ-equivalence）扩展到量子图（quantum graphs）设置中。

Method: 采用Weaver的视角，将量子图视为量子关系（quantum relations），即在冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra）交换子上具有双模结构的算子系统。在此框架下，通过构造不可约量子图的真孪生约化（true-twin reduction）类似物，并利用算子系统的Δ-等价性理论进行研究。

Result: 证明了两个不可约量子图是Morita等价的当且仅当它们都是某个共同量子图的完全拉回（full pullbacks）。进一步刻画了量子图及其关联代数同时具有TRO-等价性（TRO-equivalence）的更强Morita等价概念。在非交换图（noncommutative graphs）的特殊情况下，两种概念重合。

Conclusion: 研究展示了连通性、独立数（independence number）、香农容量（Shannon capacity）、量子复杂度（quantum complexity）和子复杂度（subcomplexity）、Haemers界以及Lovász数（Lovász number）在Morita等价性下都是不变的，为量子图理论提供了重要的结构不变性结果。

Abstract: We introduce an operator-algebraic framework for Morita equivalence of quantum graphs based on $Δ$-equivalence of operator systems introduced by Eleftherakis, Kakariadis and Todorov. Adopting the perspective of Weaver, we view quantum graphs as quantum relations, that is, operator systems endowed with a bimodule structure over the commutant of a von Neumann algebra. Within this framework, we show that two irreducibly acting quantum graphs are Morita equivalent if and only if they are both full pullbacks of a common quantum graph. This extends a result of Eleftherakis, Kakariadis and Todorov for graph operator systems to the quantum graph setting. In passing we construct a true-twin reduction analogue for an irreducibly acting quantum graph. We further characterise the case where we have simultaneous TRO-equivalence of the quantum graphs and their associated algebras, thus giving a second, stronger notion of Morita equivalence. In the special case of noncommutative graphs, corresponding to the zero-error quantum communication setting, the two notions coincide and we obtain a characterisation in terms of strong co-homomorphisms of noncommutative graphs. Finally, we show that connectivity, the independence number, Shannon capacity, quantum complexity and subcomplexity, Haemers bound, and the Lovász number are invariant under Morita equivalence.

</details>

Result: 研究结果包括：1）建立了更一般的线性/非线性对应框架，其中Fritz的工作是特例；2）对一类推广对象进行了分类；3）在诺特定理非线性类比方向上取得了一些进展。

Conclusion: 本文系统研究了自分配结构在物理学中的推广，扩展了李拟群理论框架，为诺特定理的非线性类比提供了理论基础，深化了对物理系统中非线性代数结构的理解。

Abstract: In [Self-distributive structures in physics. Internat. J. Theoret. Phys. 64 (2025), no. 3, Paper No. 73], Fritz was motivated by the structure of Hamiltonian/Heisenberg mechanics to define the notion of "Lie Quandle", which he argued are nonlinear generalizations of finite dimensional real Lie algebras. In this article, we will investigate a linear/nonlinear correspondence to which Fritz' is a special case, classify a class of generalizations of these objects, as well as describe some results in the direction of a nonlinear analogue of Noether's first theorem first described by Fritz.

### [13] [Parametric Resonance and RF-to-THz Frequency Conversion in Semiconductor Plasmonic Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16510)
*G. R. Aizin,J. Mikalopas,M. Shur*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新型等离子体激发——"rotonic plasmons"，存在于具有周期性栅极/非栅极区域的纳米场效应晶体管结构中。这些激发具有抛物线色散关系和有限有效质量，类似于rotons，可通过栅极电压泵浦高效驱动，应用于太赫兹频率产生和检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统栅极和非栅极区域的等离子体激发分别具有线性色散和平方根色散关系，而纳米尺度场效应晶体管结构中周期性交替的栅极/非栅极区域（等离子体晶体）的等离子体激发展现出根本不同的特性。研究这些新型激发对于开发紧凑、可调谐的太赫兹源和探测器具有重要意义，特别是在新兴6G通信和传感应用中。

Method: 基于具有二维电子气的耦合栅极-非栅极区域等离子体晶体的一般色散关系，推导出抛物线（"rotonic"）等离子体谱，并建立其与roton-like激发的类比。通过广义Mathieu方程描述rotonic plasmons的动力学，分析其在栅极电压泵浦下的参数不稳定性，特别针对III-N和III-V等离子体晶体系统。

Result: 研究发现rotonic plasmons具有抛物线色散关系和有限有效质量，与传统的线性或平方根色散关系有本质区别。栅极电压泵浦能够高效驱动这些非线性共振，避免电流驱动激发中的空间非均匀性和电子漂移速度饱和效应，实现更高的太赫兹功率水平。理论预测了III-N和III-V等离子体晶体在栅极电压泵浦下的参数不稳定性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了rotonic plasmons的统一理论，证明这些系统可作为可调谐、紧凑的太赫兹源和探测器，适用于新兴6G通信和传感应用。栅极电压泵浦在大面积晶体管或晶体管阵列中具有相同的栅极电压摆幅，为射频到太赫兹频率倍频和太赫兹产生提供了新途径。

Abstract: We show that plasma excitations in nanoscale field-effect transistor structures with periodic alternation of gated and ungated regions (plasmonic crystals) differ fundamentally from conventional plasmons in isolated gated or ungated regions. In contrast to the linear dispersion of purely gated plasmons and the square-root dispersion of ungated plasmons, these collective modes also exhibit a parabolic dispersion law characterized by a finite effective mass. We call these excitations "rotonic plasmons" emphasizing the analogy to roton-like excitations. The dynamics of rotonic plasmons are governed by a generalized Mathieu equation, describing either resonant or non-resonant parametric excitations of rotonic plasmons depending on damping. These nonlinear resonances can be efficiently driven by gate-voltage pumping, avoiding the spatial nonuniformities and electron drift velocity saturation effects associated with current-driven excitation. Gate-voltage pumping enables much higher terahertz (THz) power levels in plasmonic crystals. More importantly, in contrast to source-drain excitation, gate voltage pumping has the same gate voltage swing over large area transistors or transistor arrays. We develop a unified theory of rotonic plasmons and demonstrate their application for RF to THz frequency multiplication and THz generation. Starting from the general dispersion relation in plasmonic crystals based on coupled gated-ungated regions with two-dimensional electron gas, we derive the parabolic ("rotonic") plasmon spectrum and establish its analogy with roton-like excitations. The analysis predicts parametric instabilities in III-N and III-V plasmonic crystals under gate-voltage pumping. The results confirm that these systems can function as tunable, compact THz sources and detectors suitable for emerging 6G communications and sensing applications.

</details>


### [14] [Unveiling Topological Fusion in Quantum Hall Systems from Microscopic Principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16525)
*Arkadiusz Bochniak,Shinsei Ryu,Jürgen Fuchs,Gerardo Ortiz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立分数量子霍尔流体中任意子准粒子的融合规则对于理解其底层拓扑序至关重要。该研究基于一个猜想：关键拓扑性质编码在候选多体波函数的"DNA"中，即限制在有限个最低朗道能级的主导轨道占据模式。

Method: 通过扩展Schrieffer计数论证并引入拓扑激发类别，该研究提出了一个组合框架，直接从微观数据推导融合规则。该框架为阿贝尔和非阿贝尔激发提供了统一的融合规则推导路径。

Result: 该框架能够从第一性原理阐明拓扑特征在费米子和玻色子系统中的涌现。它提供了一种直接从候选波函数的轨道占据模式推导任意子融合规则的方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的组合框架为理解分数量子霍尔流体中的拓扑序提供了新视角，直接从微观数据推导融合规则，统一处理了阿贝尔和非阿贝尔激发的情况。

Abstract: Establishing the fusion rules of anyonic quasiparticles in fractional quantum Hall fluids is essential for understanding their underlying topological order. Building on the conjecture that key topological properties are encoded in the "DNA" of candidate many-body wave functions - that is, the pattern of dominant orbital occupations restricted to a finite number of lowest Landau levels - we propose a combinatorial framework that derives these fusion rules directly from microscopic data. By extending Schrieffer's counting argument and introducing classes of topological excitations, our framework provides a unified route to the fusion rules for both Abelian and non-Abelian excitations. This approach elucidates the emergence of topological features from first principles in both fermionic and bosonic systems.

### [15] [Nonequilibrium Cooper quartet generation in superconducting devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16647)
*Luca Chirolli,Alessandro Braggio,Michele Governale*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在双量子点系统中隔离和探测库珀四重态（Cooper quartets）的方法，通过非平衡驱动实现真空态与四电子态之间的共振，并观察到与四重态耦合相关的安德烈夫电流峰和独特的电流关联特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 库珀四重态（Cooper quartets）作为四个电子的聚集体，扩展了库珀对（Cooper pairs）的概念，其研究可为关联物质和多体物理（many-body physics）开辟新视角。然而，需要实验可访问的平台来探索四重态关联和多费米子关联态。

Method: 提出在耦合到常规超导引线（superconducting leads）和正常引线（normal leads）的双量子点系统（double-quantum-dot system）中隔离库珀四重态。通过将系统驱动至非平衡态，在高偏压（high bias voltage）条件下实现真空态|0⟩与四电子态|4e⟩之间的共振，该过程涉及双库珀对交换（two-Cooper pair exchange）并具有有限四重态关联。

Result: 在高偏压条件下观察到安德烈夫电流（Andreev current）峰值，其宽度与四重态耦合强度Γ₄ₑ成比例，该耦合可通过附加超导引线的相位进行调控。电流-电流关联（current-current correlations）和法诺因子（Fano factor）分析显示存在自关联与交叉关联相等的区域，这被解释为量子点与超导引线之间快速相干双库珀对振荡的明确特征。

Conclusion: 所提出的平台在量子固态实验室中具有实验可访问性，为探索四重态关联（quartet correlations）和多费米子关联态（multifermion-correlated states）提供了有效途径，为相关物质研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Cooper quartets are aggregates of four electrons that generalize the concept of Cooper pairs, and their study can unfold unexplored perspectives in correlated matter and many-body physics. We propose a method to isolate them in a double-quantum-dot system coupled to conventional superconducting and normal leads. By driving the system out of equilibrium, we show that a resonance between the vacuum $|0\rangle$ and the four-electron state $|4e\rangle$ emerges in the high bias voltage regime, which involves a two-Cooper pair exchange process and is characterized by finite quartet correlations. We study the transport properties of the system and show that a peak in the Andreev current at high bias voltage has a width that scales with the magnitude of the quartet coupling $Γ_{4e}$, which can be tuned by the phase of additional superconducting leads, yielding distinctive signatures. By further studying the current-current correlations and the Fano factor, we establish a regime characterized by equal auto- and cross-correlations, which we interpret as a definitive signature of fast coherent two-Cooper-pair oscillations between the dots and the superconducting leads. The proposed platform, experimentally accessible in a quantum solid-state laboratory, enables exploration of quartet correlations and multifermion-correlated states of matter.

</details>


### [16] [Anisotropic spin-valley coupling in SiMOS and Si/SiGe quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16713)
*N. Tobias Jacobson,Natalie D. Foster,Ryan M. Jock,Andrew M. Mounce,Daniel R. Ward,Malcolm S. Carroll,Dwight R. Luhman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究测量了硅基量子点中界面自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）的角度依赖性，比较了SiMOS和Si/SiGe两种材料平台的自旋-谷耦合强度，发现SiMOS量子点的自旋-谷耦合比Si/SiGe大一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然体硅的自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）较弱，但在硅异质界面量子点（quantum dots）中SOC显著增强，这会影响电子自旋量子比特（electron spin qubits）的性能。自旋-谷耦合（spin-valley coupling）可能导致不期望的自旋弛豫，特别是在谷分裂（valley splitting）与塞曼能量（Zeeman energy）共振时。

Method: 研究测量了SiMOS和Si/SiGe异质结构中界面自旋-轨道相互作用的角度依赖性，作为外加磁场方向和强度的函数。通过构建物理模型，从数据拟合中准确推断出谷内（intravalley）和谷间（intervalley）SOC物理特性。

Result: 对于所测量的器件，虽然g因子差异相当，但SiMOS量子点表现出比Si/SiGe大一个数量级的自旋-谷耦合。两种器件的自旋-谷耦合角度依赖性相似，具有相似的磁场方向可以最小化自旋-谷耦合。

Conclusion: 该工作指出了优化自旋-谷耦合的操作方案，以避免或利用这种机制进行量子比特操作，为硅自旋量子比特的材料平台选择提供了重要参考。

Abstract: While bulk silicon has long been understood to exhibit relatively weak spin-orbit coupling (SOC), confinement of electrons to quantum dots (QDs) at a silicon heterointerface results in significantly larger SOC. This is a concern for electron spin qubit performance, as intravalley and intervalley SOC can significantly perturb the operation of electron spin qubits. While these interactions can be harnessed to drive coherent rotations in a singlet-triplet qubit, coupling to low-lying excited valley states can lead to undesirable spin relaxation when valley splitting is on resonance with the Zeeman energy. In this work, we measure the angular dependence of the interfacial spin-orbit interaction as a function of the direction and magnitude of an applied external magnetic field in SiMOS and Si/SiGe heterostructures, two common material platforms for silicon spin qubits. We construct a physical model that accurately infers intra- and inter-valley SOC physics from fits to the data, allowing for a direct comparison between these two material systems. For the devices measured we find that, while the $g$-factor differences are comparable, the SiMOS QDs exhibit an order of magnitude larger spin-valley coupling than for Si/SiGe. Moreover, we find that the angular dependence of the spin-valley coupling is similar for both devices, with similar magnetic field orientations minimizing the spin-valley coupling. Our work points towards operational schemes for optimizing spin-valley coupling to avoid or exploit this mechanism for qubit operation.

</details>


### [17] [Charge-Density Waves of Single and Double NbS$_{3}$ Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16837)
*S. Tanda,S. Kashimoto,H. Yamamoto,K. Inagaki,H. Nobukane,Y. Fukuda*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 首次在真正的单链和双链NbS₃系统中观测到电荷密度波（CDW），发现单链中出现了与体材料不同的(1/4)b* CDW，双链中则存在(1/2)b*二聚体结构与(1/3)b* CDW共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真正的准一维系统（genuinely one-dimensional system）中电子态物理仍不明确，因为以往实验均在准一维（quasi-one-dimensional）体晶体中进行，无法直接反映真正一维电子态。传统认为费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）驱动的电荷密度波（charge-density waves, CDWs）会在一维电子-晶格系统中出现，但迄今观测到的CDW转变都发生在准一维系统中。

Method: 采用碳纳米管鞘法（carbon-nanotube-sheath method）首次研究了孤立的单链和双链NbS₃样品，从而避免了传统体材料研究的局限性。

Result: 在单链系统中意外观测到(1/4)b* CDW，与体材料中常见的(1/3)b* CDW不同；在双链系统中确认了(1/2)b*二聚体结构（dimer structure）与(1/3)b* CDW的共存现象。

Conclusion: 这一发现代表了低维物理（low-dimensional physics）领域的重要进展，超越了以往体材料研究的局限性，首次揭示了真正一维系统中的CDW行为。

Abstract: The physics of a genuine one-dimensional system in which electrons are confined in one direction remains unclear. The actual electronic state of such a genuinely one-dimensional system has not been investigated in previous experiments, for they have all been conducted on quasi-one-dimensional specimens, namely in strongly anisotropic bulk crystals. Conventionally, charge-density waves (CDWs) driven by Fermi surface nesting have been considered to appear in one-dimensional electron-lattice systems. However, the CDW transitions actually observed to date have all occurred in quasi-one-dimensional systems and therefore do not directly indicate a genuine one-dimensional electronic state.
  We investigated, for the first time, isolated single and double-chain NbS$_{3}$ samples using the carbon-nanotube-sheath method and discovered CDWs in both systems. In the single-chain, surprisingly, a $(1/4)b^*$ CDW was observed, in contrast to the $(1/3)b^*$ CDW that has been observed in bulk samples. In the double-chain, the coexistence of a $(1/2)b^*$ dimer structure and a $(1/3)b^*$ CDW was confirmed. This discovery represents a significant advancement in the field of low-dimensional physics, surpassing the limitations of previous studies on bulk systems.

### [18] [Evolution of topological phases in atomically thin WTe2 films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16860)
*Changcang Qiao,Chen-Chia Hsu,Tao Zhang,Zhiming Sun,Dong Qian,Yang-hao Chan,Peng Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）和第一性原理计算，揭示了WTe2从单层到块体的拓扑性质随厚度变化的非单调演化规律，发现层间耦合诱导的能带重构导致拓扑相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑材料（如拓扑绝缘体和半金属）展现出许多新颖量子现象，不同拓扑相之间的转变引起了广泛研究兴趣。本研究旨在探索WTe2材料随层数变化的拓扑性质演化规律。

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）技术对WTe2从单层到块体进行测量，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析拓扑性质随厚度的变化。

Result: 单层WTe2存在能隙，而三层系统能隙被抑制变为金属性。拓扑Z2不变量随层数增加在1和0之间振荡，源于层间耦合（interlayer coupling）引起的能带交叉变化。当导带和价带在费米能级附近接触时，系统演化为外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal），其拓扑性质由陈数（Chern number）描述。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明拓扑态对维度的依赖具有非单调性（non-monotonic dependence），层驱动的电子能带重构（layer-driven electronic band reconfiguration）导致了固体中的相变（phase transitions）。

Abstract: Topological materials ranging from topological insulators to semimetals host many novel quantum phenomena including quantum spin Hall effect and topological Fermi arcs. Transitions between these topological phases have attracted much research interest. We performed angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) on WTe2 ranging from a monolayer to the bulk and reveal the evolution of the electronic structure and the band gap. Notably, the gap observed in the monolayer system is suppressed in the three layers, where the film becomes metallic. Variations in the topological properties with thickness are demonstrated by the first-principles calculations. Topological Z2 invariant is shown to oscillate between 1 and 0 with the addition of layers, originating from the interlayer coupling-induced change in band crossing. The system evolves into a Weyl semimetal when the conduction and valence bands touch near the Fermi level and the topological nature is described by the Chern number. Our findings demonstrate the non-monotonic dependence of topological states on dimensionality and how layer-driven electronic band reconfiguration leads to phase transitions in solids.

### [19] [Wave Packet Propagation in Tilted Weyl Semimetals for Black Hole Analog Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16927)
*M. A. Lozande,E. A. Fajardo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过比较两种具有不同光谱特性的模型，在倾斜外尔半金属中实现了不同的类比黑洞视界。研究发现空间变化的外尔锥倾斜会产生类似引力黑洞视界附近光锥倾斜的效应，揭示了两种根本不同类型的类比视界：一种完全反射波包，另一种允许波包穿越视界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索倾斜外尔半金属作为实现类比黑洞视界的平台，通过比较具有不同光谱特性的模型来揭示不同类型的量子效应和信息动力学。

Method: 通过分析两种具有对比光谱特性的模型中的波包动力学，研究空间变化的外尔锥倾斜如何产生类似引力黑洞视界附近光锥倾斜的效应。

Result: 揭示了两种根本不同类型的类比视界：第一种模型表现出完全的波包反射，模拟不可穿透的屏障；第二种模型允许波包穿越视界。零动量波包经历最强的视界效应，表现为显著减速和在视界区域更长的停留时间。

Conclusion: 倾斜外尔半金属为研究与非平凡量子效应和信息动力学相关的类比黑洞视界提供了一个丰富且可调控的平台，两种系统都表现出显著的概率损失，这与波包在视界附近的停留时间直接相关。

Abstract: We explore the realization of distinct analog black hole horizons within tilted Weyl semimetals by comparing two models with contrasting spectral properties. We demonstrate that a spatially varying tilt in the Weyl cone structure creates an effect analogous to the tilting of light cones near a gravitational black hole horizon. By analyzing wave packet dynamics in both models, we reveal two fundamentally different types of analog horizons. The first model exhibits complete wave packet reflection, effectively mimicking an impenetrable barrier. In contrast, the second model permits wave packet transmission across the horizon. Critically, for both models, wave packets initialized with zero momentum ($k_0=0.0$) experience the strongest horizon effects, characterized by a dramatic slowing and significantly longer dwell times at the horizon region. Finally, we find that both systems exhibit substantial probability loss, which we demonstrate is directly correlated with the wave packet's dwell time near the horizon. Our findings establish tilted Weyl semimetals as a rich, tunable platform for investigating non-trivial quantum effects and information dynamics associated with analog black hole horizons.

### [20] [Crystallography, Lorentz violation, and the Standard-Model Extension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17646)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在有效理论层面，利用晶体学和磁点群（magnetic point groups）作为数学工具，展示不同晶体结构的电磁特性如何在SME框架中被参数化，并对双折射（birefringent）和磁电介质（magnetoelectric media）进行专门研究。

Result: 研究发现，在SME语言中重新表达了一些在现代文献中未被系统描述的磁电介质的有趣效应，并建立了具有特定对称性（如双折射或多铁性晶体）的材料作为SME效应的凝聚态类比物。

Conclusion: 基于所建立的对应关系，研究能够提出具有特殊光学性质的材料，这些材料在近期研究中尚未得到充分探索，为SME效应提供了凝聚态物理的类比系统。

Abstract: The motivation behind the present work is to adopt methodology from field theory and high-energy physics to crystallography. In particular, we establish a relationship between the electromagnetic sector of the Standard-Model Extension (SME) for Lorentz invariance violation and optical media. At an effective level, electromagnetic properties associated with different crystal structures are demonstrated to be parametrized in the SME. Crystallographic and magnetic point groups provide the mathematical tools to show this correspondence. Birefringent and magnetoelectric media merit a dedicated study. Intriguing effects, which have not been described systematically in the modern literature, are rediscovered for the latter and expressed in SME language. With the setting developed at our disposal, materials with specific symmetries such as birefringent or multiferroic crystals serve as condensed-matter analogs for SME effects. It enables us to propose materials with unusual optical properties, which have not been thoroughly looked at in recent times.

Method: 本文采用批判性综述方法，系统评估了关于TMDCs中SPEs原子起源的现有理论提案。同时进行了关键趋势分析，评估了基于TMDC的SPEs的不同性能指标（figures of merit），并提出了标准化的表征方法以规范报告流程。

In this paper, we critically review these existing proposals to elucidate their origin. Further, we perform a critical trend analysis for different figures of merit of TMDC-based SPEs, and propose a characterization methodology to streamline the reporting process. Finally, we review several quantum technology implementations where solid state SPEs are being used, and identify the advancements required in TMDC-based SPEs for their successful adoption in these technologies.

By explicitly deriving the Raman scattering cross-section, we establish that for the two-level atomic system in the near-field zone of the carbon nanotube metasurface the effect can be enhanced by a factor of up to 10^4, not only for p-polarized but for s-polarized light as well.

### [23] [Quantum higher-spin Hall insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17479)
*Takuto Kawakami,Igor Kuzmenko,Yshai Avishai,Yigal Meir,Masatoshi Sato*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了任意自旋J的量子自旋霍尔绝缘体理论，揭示了其支持J+1/2对螺旋边缘模式，这些模式受非平庸镜面陈数保护，并展现出高阶色散和非线性输运响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是将量子自旋霍尔（quantum spin Hall）物理扩展到更高自旋系统，探索在任意自旋J下的拓扑绝缘体行为，为在超冷原子气体等平台中的实现提供理论基础。

Method: 通过理论分析建立了任意自旋J的量子自旋霍尔绝缘体理论框架，利用镜面陈数（mirror Chern numbers）作为拓扑不变量来保护边缘模式，并研究了外加磁场对边缘谱的影响。

Result: 研究发现此类系统支持J+1/2对螺旋边缘模式（helical edge modes），其边缘理论由具有高阶色散（higher-order dispersion）的广义狄拉克费米子描述，产生非线性电压输运响应。面内磁场可在边缘谱中打开质量隙，磁畴壁则承载J+1/2重简并束缚态。

Conclusion: 该工作成功将量子自旋霍尔物理推广到高自旋系统，揭示了新的拓扑边缘态特征和非线性输运行为，为在超冷原子气体等实验平台中实现此类系统提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We develop a theory of quantum spin Hall insulators with arbitrary spin $J$. Our analysis demonstrates that such systems support $J+\tfrac{1}{2}$ pairs of helical edge modes protected by nontrivial mirror Chern numbers. We establish that the corresponding edge theory is described by a generalized Dirac fermion with higher-order dispersion. These modes produce unique transport responses that are non-linear with voltage. An in-plane magnetic field opens a mass gap in the edge spectrum, and magnetic domain walls host $(J+\tfrac{1}{2})$-fold degenerate bound states characterized by nontrivial winding numbers. Our results extend quantum spin Hall physics to higher-spin systems and suggest possible realizations in ultracold atomic gases.

### [24] [Photocurrent at oblique illumination and reconstruction of wavefront direction with 2d photodetectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17591)
*Kirill Kapralov,Vladislav Atlasov,Alina Khisameeva,Viacheslav Muravev,Weiwei Cai,Dmitry Svintsov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文展示了一种基于金属-二维电子系统（2DES）对称结的光电探测器，能够实现零偏压光电流并重建光入射方向，突破了传统探测器仅能测量光强、光谱和偏振的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管当代光电探测器已能实现光谱和偏振的单像素重建，但光入射方向的重建尚未实现。本研究旨在开发能够确定光入射方向的重构型探测器，填补这一技术空白。

Method: 采用基于金属与二维电子系统（2DES）对称结的光电探测器，利用金属接触2DES的特殊电动力学特性，其中入射场相位的空间变化转化为局部场振幅的强烈变化。通过可变载流子密度下的光电流测量实现入射方向重建。

Result: 该探测器实现了斜入射下的零偏压光电流，且光电流方向唯一确定了光入射的象限。在可变载流子密度下的二维等离子体激元（2d plasmon）共振条件下，可以实现入射角的定量确定，因为斜入射辐射激发了非对称等离子体激元模式。

Conclusion: 基于金属-2DES对称结的光电探测器首次实现了光入射方向的重建能力，通过零偏压光电流效应和可变载流子密度下的等离子体激元共振，为全光信息重建提供了新途径。

Abstract: Many contemporary photodetectors operate beyond the readout of light intensity and enable the reconstruction of spectrum and polarization at the single-pixel level. However, the determination of light incidence direction with reconstructive detectors has not been realized so far. We show that photodetectors based on symmetric junctions of metals and 2d electron systems (2DES) enable (1) zero-bias photocurrent at oblique light incidence (2) reconstruction of incidence direction based on photocurrent measurements at variable carrier density. The former effect is based on peculiar electrodynamics of metal-contacted 2DES, where spatial variations of incident field phase translate into strong variations of local field amplitude. The local absorbances at two opposite metal-2DES junctions at oblique incidence are dissimilar, which results in finite photocurrent independent of microscopic rectification mechanism at these junctions. The direction of photocurrent uniquely determines the quadrant of light incidence. Quantitative determination of incidence angle becomes possible under conditions of 2d plasmon resonance at variable carrier density. In such a case, obliquely incident radiation excites the asymmetric plasmon modes, which amplitude carries unique information about angle of incidence.

</details>


### [25] [Microscopic Theory of Acoustic Phonon Scattering by Charge-Density-Wave Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17655)
*Han Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究发展了一个格林函数理论，统一描述电荷密度波（CDW）材料中的声子软化、热输运异常和软模光谱现象，通过直接与2H-TaSe₂的实验数据比较验证了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）序在关联金属中源于特定波矢处的电子响应峰值，其前驱涨落会衰减载热声子。现有理论需要统一解释衍射、软模光谱和热输运实验现象。

Method: 发展了一个格林函数理论，其中包含：1）CDW-晶格软模的阻尼谐振子传播子；2）从电子回路获得的应变-强度顶点。该理论识别了两个散射通道：局部强度通道和纹理（梯度）通道。

Result: 理论框架统一了衍射、软模光谱和热输运测量，能够描述CDW-声子软极点的晶格投影，并识别出欠阻尼到过阻尼的交叉转变。通过直接与2H-TaSe₂的非弹性X射线散射声子软化和异常热输运实验数据比较验证了理论。

Conclusion: 该理论框架具有广泛适用性，可应用于多种CDW材料体系，包括过渡金属二硫化物、稀土三碲化物、kagome CDW化合物和铜氧化物中的涨落电荷序区域。

Abstract: Charge-density-wave (CDW) order in correlated metals originates in a peaked electronic susceptibility at a finite wavevector $\mathbf Q_0$, set either by Fermi-surface features (nesting or saddle-point singularities) or by momentum-resolved electron-phonon coupling, or by a combination of the two. CDW precursor fluctuations can attenuate heat-carrying acoustic phonons even when long-range order is absent. We develop a Green's-function theory in which a damped-harmonic-oscillator propagator for a hybrid CDW--lattice soft mode at the ordering wavevector $\mathbf Q_0$ and a strain--intensity vertex obtained from an electron loop combine to give the acoustic phonon self-energy. The theory identifies two scattering channels: a local-intensity channel, controlled by a retarded composite CDW response and giving a narrow critical contribution when the CDW correlation length is large, and a texture (gradient) channel, which couples acoustic strain to spatial variations of the CDW envelope and, in a frozen-texture limit, reduces to a phenomenological form set by the measured diffraction peak weight and width. The same propagator fixes the lattice projection of a hybrid CDW--phonon soft pole measured by inelastic X-ray scattering, with an underdamped-to-overdamped crossover controlled by the distance to the CDW instability and a mass-tracking identity for the slow overdamped relaxation rate. The framework unifies diffraction, soft-mode spectroscopy, and thermal transport and applies broadly across CDW materials, including the transition-metal dichalcogenides, rare-earth tritellurides, kagome CDW compounds, and the cuprate fluctuating charge-order regime; we illustrate it by direct comparison with experimental IXS phonon softening and anomalous thermal transport in 2H-TaSe$_2$ at elevated temperatures.

</details>


### [26] [Magnetoresistance from decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17672)
*Xian-Peng Zhang,Yan-Qing Feng,Haiwen Liu,Yugui Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了一种新的磁阻（magnetoresistance）机制，其中量子退相干（quantum decoherence）而非传统的动量弛豫（momentum relaxation）成为主导因素，导致电导率（conductivity）与杂质密度呈线性关系而非反比关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁阻微观理论主要关注巡游电子的动量弛豫和等离子体频率（plasma frequency）。本研究旨在探索一种不同的机制，即量子退相干在整个费米海（Fermi sea）中的作用如何影响磁阻。

Method: 通过分析密度矩阵（density matrix）的非对角分量衰减来研究量子退相干机制。该方法使用两个复退相干时间（complex decoherence times）参数化电导率，并与外部磁场和交换场（exchange field）的相互作用相结合。

Result: 发现电导率与杂质密度呈线性标度关系，这与传统Drude图像中电导率与杂质密度成反比形成鲜明对比。此外，观察到丰富的磁输运现象，包括温度驱动的正负磁阻交叉和非单调温度依赖性，后者表现出类似近藤效应（Kondo effect）的电导率最大值。

Conclusion: 量子退相干被确立为磁阻的关键因素，这一发现为探测量子退相干提供了直接的电学探针，并有望对涉及磁阻的基础研究和新兴纳米技术应用产生前所未有的影响。

Abstract: Microscopic theories of magnetoresistance have traditionally focused on momentum relaxation and the plasma frequency of itinerant electrons. Here, we uncover a distinct mechanism in which magnetoresistance originates from quantum decoherence throughout the whole Fermi sea, specifically the decay of the off-diagonal components of the density matrix. The resulting conductivity, parameterized by two complex decoherence times, scales linearly with impurity density-markedly contrasting the conventional Drude picture, where conductivity is governed by momentum relaxation of Ferm-surface quasiparticles and is inversely proportional to impurity density. This unconventional scaling provides a direct electrical probe of quantum decoherence, a quantity central to both fundamental studies and emerging nanoscale technologies. Furthermore, the interplay between the external magnetic field and the exchange field gives rise to rich magnetotransport phenomena, including temperature-drive crossover from positive to negative magnetoresistance and a nonmonotonic temperature dependence with a conductivity maximum reminiscent of the Kondo effect. Our results establish quantum decoherence as a key ingredient in magnetoresistance and our findings should have an unprecedented impact on advancing research and applications involving magnetoresistance.

</details>


### [27] [Dynamical spin-nematic order in a transverse field Ising chain with non-Hermitian Gamma interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17700)
*Yu-Hong Yan,Ran Wang,Kun-Liang Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了非厄米Gamma相互作用对横场伊辛链相变和磁关联的影响，揭示了由宇称-时间对称性破缺诱导的自旋向列序（spin-nematic order）及其在非平衡动力学中的表征方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非厄米Gamma相互作用与伊辛相互作用、横场之间的竞争如何影响量子相变和磁关联，探索在自旋链中产生自旋向列序的新机制。

Method: 通过分析横场伊辛链（transverse field Ising chain）中非厄米Gamma相互作用的影响，研究系统的相变行为和磁关联特性。

Result: 发现系统除了有能隙的铁磁相和顺磁相外，还存在无能隙相，其中宇称-时间对称性破缺（parity-time symmetry breaking）诱导了长程自旋向列序；同时揭示了动力学自旋向列序的出现，为通过非平衡动力学表征自旋向列相图提供了途径。

Conclusion: 非厄米Gamma相互作用与伊辛相互作用、横场的竞争产生了丰富的量子相，并为在自旋链中生成自旋向列序提供了一种方案。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of non-Hermitian Gamma interaction on the phase transitions and magnetic correlations for the transverse field Ising chain. We demonstrate that apart from the gapped ferromagnetic and paramagnetic phases, there is a gapless phase, where the system exhibits long-range spin-nematic order induced by parity-time symmetry breaking. Furthermore, we reveal that the parity-time symmetry breaking leads to the emergence of dynamical spin-nematic order, which also suggests a way of characterizing the spin-nematic phase diagram through non-equilibrium dynamics. Our findings show rich quantum phases stem from the competition among the Ising interaction, transverse field and non-Hermitian Gamma interaction, as well as providing a scheme for generating spin-nematic order in the spin chain.

### [28] [Propagation, generation, and utilization of topologically trivial magnetic solitons in magnetic nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17992)
*Kai-Tao Huang,X. S. Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论和数值方法研究了一维拓扑平凡磁孤子在铁磁纳米线中的特性与生成机制，验证了近似解析解，发现了孤子在异质界面上的非线性反射折射现象，并提出通过交替磁场或自旋极化电流脉冲生成可控制孤子的方法，为自旋电子学应用提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁孤子（magnetic solitons）作为磁性系统中的非线性局域激发，在自旋电子学（spintronics）中具有重要应用潜力。研究旨在探索一维拓扑平凡磁孤子的特性及其在铁磁纳米线中的生成机制，以推动其在信息存储和处理中的应用。

Method: 采用理论分析与数值模拟相结合的方法：首先推导出由两个自由参数描述的近似解析孤子解，然后通过微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）进行验证。研究还通过交替施加磁场或自旋极化电流脉冲（spin-polarized current pulses）来生成孤子对。

Result: 验证了近似解析孤子解的有效性；发现孤子在异质各向异性界面上的反射和折射呈现高度非线性特性，与线性自旋波（linear spin waves）显著不同；成功生成了反向传播的孤子对，且每个孤子都可通过生成过程进行控制；这些孤子可用于驱动畴壁（domain wall）运动，实现与信息技术数字特性兼容的离散操控。

Conclusion: 研究证实了一维拓扑平凡磁孤子在铁磁纳米线中的可控生成与非线性传播特性，为利用孤子驱动畴壁运动提供了理论基础。这些发现为拓扑平凡孤子在自旋电子学中的应用开辟了新途径，特别是在数字信息处理领域具有潜在价值。

Abstract: Magnetic solitons are nonlinear, local excitations in magnetic systems. In this study, we theoretically and numerically investigate the properties and generation of one-dimensional (1D) topologically trivial magnetic solitons in ferromagnetic nanowires. An approximate analytical soliton solution described by two free parameters is validated by comparing with the micromagnetic simulation. Across an interface between two media of different anisotropy, the reflection and refraction of a soliton are highly nonlinear that are different from the linear spin waves. A pair of magnetic solitons that propagate in opposite directions can be generated by alternately applying magnetic field or spin-polarized current pulses of opposite directions to at least two successive regions. Each soliton falls into a soliton solution that can be controlled by the generation process. These magnetic solitons can be used to drive domain wall motion over a certain distance determined by the soliton magnitude, allowing for discrete manipulation of domain walls compatible with the digital nature of information technology. Our findings pave the way for the application of topologically trivial solitons in spintronics.

### [29] [Generic skyrmion phase diagram in ferrimagnetic films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18079)
*M. V. Wijethunga,X. R. Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了亚铁磁斯格明子（ferrimagnetic skyrmions）的稳定性如何受亚晶格间交换耦合强度J的影响，并引入无量纲参数ζ_eff来描述强耦合与弱耦合之间的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚铁磁斯格明子因反铁磁耦合亚晶格和降低的净磁化强度而具有增强的可调性。然而，传统用于表征斯格明子稳定性的无量纲参数κ在亚铁磁系统中的适用性尚不明确，因为大多数研究假设固定的强亚晶格间交换耦合J。

Method: 研究通过改变亚晶格间交换耦合J来探究其对弛豫稳定和亚稳态亚铁磁斯格明子构型的影响，并引入无量纲参数ζ_eff来表征强耦合与弱耦合之间的转变。

Result: 在强耦合区域，亚晶格间锁定使得斯格明子能在本征Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）缺失的亚晶格中稳定，而另一亚晶格具有有限DMI，从而产生无DMI的亚铁磁斯格明子。随着J减小，这种锁定被破坏，导致亚晶格独立行为，使得基于有效κ的描述失效。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个统一框架，将亚晶格间交换耦合与亚铁磁系统中斯格明子相稳定性联系起来，为理解亚铁磁斯格明子的稳定机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Ferrimagnetic skyrmions offer enhanced tunability due to antiferromagnetically coupled sublattices and reduced net magnetization. In chiral magnetic films at zero magnetic field, skyrmion stability is commonly characterized by a dimensionless parameter $κ$, yet its applicability to ferrimagnetic systems remains unclear, as most studies assume a fixed, strong inter-sublattice exchange coupling $J$. Here we investigate how variations in $J$ govern relaxed stable and metastable ferrimagnetic skyrmion configurations and introduce a dimensionless parameter $ζ_{eff}$ to characterize the crossover between strong and weak inter-sublattice locking. In the strong-coupling regime, inter-sublattice locking enables stabilization of skyrmion in a sublattice where intrinsic Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction is absent while the other sublattice has finite DMI, yielding a sublattice with DMI-free ferrimagnetic skyrmions. As $J$ decreases, this locking breaks down, leading to independent sublattice behavior and the failure of an effective $κ$-based description. Our results establish a unified framework linking inter-sublattice exchange and skyrmion phase stability in ferrimagnetic systems.

</details>


### [30] [Asymmetric Scattering-Induced Neel Spin-Orbit Torque in Antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18097)
*Sayan Sarkar,Amit Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了反铁磁体中一种新的反常斜散射（anomalous skew-scattering）机制，该机制通过非对称杂质散射与布洛赫电子的反常自旋极化率（ASP）耦合，产生额外的PT奇性自旋极化，为奈尔自旋轨道矩（NSOT）提供了新的能带几何驱动机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体中的磁开关依赖于奈尔自旋轨道矩（NSOT），该效应源于传导电子的电流诱导交错自旋极化。传统上认为这种响应需要自旋磁化率在时空反演对称性（PT）下为奇性，并归因于对称散射过程。然而，非对称杂质散射与能带几何的相互作用可能产生新的贡献机制。

Method: 研究采用四方CuMnAs的最小模型，分析非对称杂质散射与布洛赫电子的反常自旋极化率（ASP）的耦合效应。通过结合反对称高阶散射过程和能带几何，将原本PT偶性的磁化率转化为交错自旋极化。

Result: 研究表明，这种反常斜散射（anomalous skew-scattering）贡献可与传统的对称散射（Drude）贡献相当，且在足够高的杂质密度下甚至可能超过后者。该机制有效地将PT偶性磁化率转化为交错自旋极化，为NSOT提供了新的能带几何驱动来源。

Conclusion: 该工作发现了一种新的能带几何驱动机制用于产生奈尔自旋轨道矩（NSOT），并确立了一种高效的电控反铁磁体途径。反常斜散射贡献的识别扩展了对反铁磁体自旋轨道矩物理起源的理解。

Abstract: Magnetic switching in antiferromagnets relies on Neel spin orbit torque (NSOT), which originates from a current-induced staggered spin polarization of itinerant electrons. In collinear antiferromagnets, such a response requires the spin susceptibility to be odd under combined space-time inversion symmetry (PT), and is conventionally attributed to symmetric scattering processes. Here, we demonstrate that asymmetric impurity scattering generates an additional PT-odd spin polarization when coupled with the anomalous spin polarizability (ASP) of Bloch electrons. This extrinsic contribution arises from the interplay between antisymmetric higher-order scattering processes and band geometry, effectively converting an otherwise PT-even susceptibility into a staggered spin polarization. Using a minimal model of tetragonal CuMnAs, we show that this anomalous skew-scattering contribution can be comparable to, and with sufficient impurity density even exceed, the conventional symmetric scattering (Drude) contribution. Our results identify a new band-geometry-driven mechanism for NSOT and establish an efficient route for electrical control of antiferromagnets.

</details>

Method: 研究基于IceCube中微子天文台的观测数据，该设施能够测量宽能区范围内的中微子。通过分析中微子事件，研究团队进行了多种物理分析，包括源识别、味成分分析和暗物质搜寻。

Abstract: The IceCube Neutrino Observatory has opened a new window into the high-energy Universe, providing measurements of neutrinos over a broad energy range. This contribution presents recent results, including a follow-up on the first identification of a steady neutrino source NGC 1068, measurements of the flavor composition of the diffuse astrophysical flux, limits on prompt atmospheric neutrinos, and searches for neutrinos from dark matter annihilation in the Sun. These measurements probe neutrino production mechanisms, fundamental particle interactions, and physics beyond the Standard Model. Looking forward, the recently deployed IceCube Upgrade will enhance sensitivity to lower-energy neutrinos and reduce systematic uncertainties, while the planned IceCube-Gen2 will expand the detector volume, increase the neutrino detection rate, and extend energy reach, enabling more detailed studies of cosmic sources and high-energy particle physics.

### [32] [Neutron star atmospheres composed of fusion ashes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16650)
*Valery F. Suleimanov,Juri Poutanen,Klaus Werner*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究建立了包含不同化学成分热核灰烬的热中子星大气模型，用于研究X射线暴中核燃烧产物输运到恒星表面的过程。模型考虑了多种不透明度源，包括激发态光致电离和大量谱线，并开发了同时处理康普顿散射与谱线的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立热中子星大气模型，以研究X射线暴中核燃烧灰烬输运到恒星表面的过程。这些模型对于理解热核闪（thermonuclear flashes）在X射线暴中子星中的物理机制至关重要。

Method: 研究考虑了四种不同化学混合物，分别以氦、铬、铁或镍为主。除了先前中子星大气建模中使用的不透明度源外，还纳入了激发态离子的光致电离（photoionization from excited ionic states）以及约5000条谱线。开发了一种能够同时处理康普顿散射（Compton scattering）和大量谱线的方法。

Result: 模型显示中子星大气在光学薄与光学厚过渡区域存在辐射压力显著增加的层。这种增强的力为给定表面重力和化学成分设定了最大可达到的辐射通量上限。计算大气产生的光谱显示出明显的吸收边（absorption edges），其能量由主要化学物种决定。

Conclusion: 研究通过单一吸收边修正的稀释黑体拟合模型光谱，并探讨了拟合参数如何依赖于相对辐射通量和大气化学成分。最后讨论了在HETE J1900.1-2455和GRS 1747-312系统中观测到的具有吸收边的X射线暴特性对这些模型的约束。

Abstract: Here we present models of hot neutron star (NS) atmospheres consisting of thermonuclear ashes of various chemical compositions. These models are essential for studying thermonuclear flashes in X-ray bursting NSs in which nuclear-burning ashes are transported to the stellar surface. We consider four different mixtures, each dominated by helium, chromium, iron, or nickel. In addition to the opacity sources previously used in NS atmosphere modeling, we include photoionization from excited ionic states as well as approximately 5000 spectral lines. We also develop a method that enables the simultaneous treatment of Compton scattering and a large number of spectral lines. A key feature of the modeled NS atmospheres is the presence of a layer in the transition region between the optically thin and optically thick parts of the atmosphere where the radiation-pressure force increases significantly. This enhanced force sets an upper limit on the maximum attainable bolometric flux for a given surface gravity and chemical composition. The emergent spectra from the computed atmospheres display pronounced absorption edges, whose energies are determined by the dominant chemical species. We fit the model spectra using a diluted blackbody modified by a single absorption edge, and we investigate how the fit parameters depend on both the relative bolometric flux and the chemical composition of the atmosphere. Finally, we discuss constraints on these models imposed by the properties of X-ray bursts that exhibit absorption edges in their spectra, as observed in the systems HETE~J1900.1$-$2455 and GRS~1747$-$312.

</details>


### [33] [Superfluid $^3$He aerogel experiments as a laboratory neutron star analogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18016)
*Samuli Autti,Vanessa Graber,Brynmor Haskell*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究提出将气凝胶中的超流体涡旋实验作为中子星物理的类比系统，通过点涡旋模拟揭示了两种不同的涡旋钉扎机制，为理解中子星自转突增现象提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星为千米尺度量子物理提供了独特的天体物理测试平台，其自转突增（glitches）现象常归因于星体内部超流体相中量子化涡旋的钉扎动力学。实验室超流体涡旋实验虽启发了中子星理论，但气凝胶中的涡旋实验现象作为高度相关但尚未充分探索的类比系统，具有重要研究价值。

Method: 研究构建了点涡旋模拟（point-vortex simulation），用于分析在类地壳（crust-like）和类核心（core-like）气凝胶中的实验。该方法能够提取两种不同的涡旋钉扎（vortex pinning）动力学机制，并验证微观层面的强涡旋钉扎图像。

Result: 在类地壳气凝胶中，当环境超流速度足够快时，涡旋会发生脱钉（depinned）；而在类核心气凝胶中，钉扎涡旋永不释放，旋转速度变化通过雪崩式（avalanche-like）产生新涡旋来适应。这些概念同样适用于中子星，可能彻底改变中子星观测数据的分析方式。

Conclusion: 气凝胶中的超流体涡旋实验现象为中子星物理提供了极具吸引力但尚未充分探索的类比系统。研究揭示的两种涡旋钉扎机制应同样适用于中子星，可能革新对中子星观测的分析理解。

Abstract: Neutron stars make a unique astrophysical test bench for our understanding of quantum physics at kilometre scales. The rotation of a neutron star features glitches, sudden spin-ups that interrupt the otherwise regular stellar spin-down, which are often attributed to the dynamics of pinned quantised vortices in one or several of the superfluid phases inside the star. Laboratory experiments probing superfluid vortices have inspired neutron star theory and simulations from the beginning. Here we argue that vortex experiments in superfluids contained in aerogels show phenomenology that offers a highly appealing but vastly unexplored analogue for neutron star physics. We build a point-vortex simulation that allows analysing experiments in a crust-like and a core-like aerogel, extracting two different regimes of pinned vortex (non-)dynamics and validating a microscopic picture of very strong vortex pinning. In the crust-like aerogel, vortices get depinned once the ambient superflow is fast enough, while in the core-like aerogel pinned vortices are never released and rotational velocity changes are accommodated by the avalanche-like production of new vortices instead. Finally, we show that these concepts should apply also in neutron stars and may thus revolutionise the analysis of neutron star observations.

</details>


<div id='math.DG'></div>

# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [34] [Geometric Stability of the Schoen-Yau Zero Mass Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17599)
*Christina Sormani*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文回顾了Schoen-Yau正质量定理（Positive Mass Theorem）几何稳定性问题的研究进展与开放性问题，重点关注当渐近平坦黎曼流形（asymptotically flat Riemannian manifold）的质量趋近于零时，其几何结构如何趋近于欧几里得空间（Euclidean space）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨Schoen-Yau正质量定理中零质量刚性定理（zero mass rigidity theorem）的几何稳定性问题：当渐近平坦黎曼流形具有几乎为零的质量时，其几何结构在何种程度上接近欧几里得空间。这是一个重要的未解决问题，即使在三维情况下也尚未完全解决。

Method: 论文采用综述性方法，回顾了相关研究结果和开放性问题，包括分析这类空间的几何性质、构建质量趋近于零的空间序列示例，以及探讨多种几何收敛（geometric convergence）概念。

Result: 尽管已有显著进展，但核心问题仍未解决：在三维及更高维度中，究竟哪种几何收敛概念最能有效刻画该刚性定理的几何稳定性。论文总结了现有研究成果，但强调这仍然是一个开放性问题。

Conclusion: Schoen-Yau正质量定理的几何稳定性问题仍然开放，需要进一步研究来确定最能描述质量趋近于零时几何结构趋近于欧几里得空间的收敛概念。该问题在广义相对论和微分几何中具有重要意义。

Abstract: In 1979, Schoen and Yau proved their famous Positive Mass Theorem which is a combination of a comparison theorem: {\em a three dimensional asymptotically flat Riemannian manifold with nonnegative scalar curvature has nonnegative ADM mass}, and a rigidity theorem: {\em if such a manifold has zero ADM mass then it is isometric to Euclidean space}. Here we review results and open questions on the geometric stability of their zero mass rigidity theorem: {\em if such a manifold has almost zero mass, how close is its geometry to that of Euclidean space}? We review the geometry of these spaces, examples of sequences of such spaces with mass approaching zero, and a variety of geometric notions of convergence. Although there has been much progress, it is still an open question (even in dimension three): exactly which geometric notion of convergence works best to capture the geometric stability of this famous rigidity theorem.

</details>

Method: 方法包括提出并实现系统性的延拓程序，专门针对基灵二张量进行处理。该方法特别关注局部对称情形，并利用所得工具分析对称空间上的数学结构。

Result: 主要成果是成功实现了基灵二张量的延拓程序，并利用该工具阐明了在紧型不可约局部对称空间上，从基灵场到基灵二张量的自然二次映射关系。

Conclusion: 结论表明所提出的延拓程序为处理基灵二张量提供了有效工具，特别是在局部对称情形下，并成功揭示了对称空间上基灵场与基灵二张量之间的二次映射关系。

Abstract: We present a systematic prolongation procedure and its implementation for Killing two-tensors, especially in the locally symmetric case. We use the resulting machinery to elucidate the natural quadratic mapping from Killing fields to Killing two-tensors on irreducible locally symmetric spaces of compact type.

### [36] [DMRadio-Core: A new approach for GUT-scale axion searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16602)
*V. Ankel,C. Bartram,J. Begin,C. Bell,S. Chaudhuri,H. -M. Cho,J. Corbin,W. Craddock,S. Cuadra,A. Droster,J. Echevers,E. Engelhardt,J. T. Fry,K. D. Irwin,A. Keller,R. Kolevatov,A. Kunder,N. Kurita,N. Otto,E. Pariset,S. Puranam,P. Quassolo,N. M. Rapidis,C. P. Salemi,M. Simanovskaia,J. Singh,P. Stark,E. C. van Assendelft,K. van Bibber,K. J. Vetter,K. Wells,J. Wiedemann,L. Winslow,D. Wright,A. K. Yi,B. F. Zemenu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于窄孔径分段螺线管的新型实验几何结构，用于探测neV/c²质量范围的QCD轴子，通过优化LC谐振器信号收集显著降低所需磁场储能，实现从30-200 MHz到100 kHz-30 MHz范围的分阶段可扩展实验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测neV/c²质量范围的QCD轴子（QCD axions）具有强烈动机，因其与大统一理论（GUT scale）尺度的新物理以及合理的暴胀前轴子对称性破缺尺度相关。然而该参数空间因轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon couplings）微弱而难以探测，通常需要具有大量储能的大型高场磁体。

Method: 提出一种新型实验几何结构，基于窄孔径分段螺线管（narrow-bore, segmented solenoid），通过在磁体孔径高场区域外部使用LC谐振器（LC resonators）来优化轴子诱导信号的收集。这种替代优化方法在保持灵敏度的同时显著降低所需磁场储能。

Result: 该设计可实现近期在30-200 MHz（120-830 neV/c²）频率范围内的实验，并具有成本效益的分阶段扩展能力，最终可扩展至大统一理论尺度实验，覆盖100 kHz-30 MHz（0.4-120 neV/c²）范围。

Conclusion: 提出的新型实验几何结构通过优化信号收集和降低磁场储能需求，为探测neV/c²质量范围的QCD轴子提供了可行且可扩展的实验方案，能够覆盖从近期实验到大统一理论尺度实验的广泛参数空间。

Abstract: Searches for QCD axions with masses in the neV/$c^2$ mass range are strongly motivated by new physics at the GUT scale and by well-motivated pre-inflationary axion symmetry breaking scales. This parameter space is challenging to probe due to the small axion-photon couplings, which typically require large, high-field magnets with substantial stored energy. In this paper, we propose a new experimental geometry based on a narrow-bore, segmented solenoid that optimizes the collection of the axion-induced signal using LC resonators outside the high-field region of the magnet bore. This alternative optimization significantly reduces the required stored magnetic energy while preserving sensitivity, enabling a near-term experiment in the 30-200 MHz (120-830 neV/$c^2$) range, with a cost-effective, staged scaling to a GUT-scale experiment in the 100 kHz-30 MHz (0.4-120 neV/$c^2$) range.

</details>


### [37] [Searches for massive, long-lived particles in events with displaced vertices with ATLAS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16789)
*David Rousso*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究介绍了ATLAS实验在LHC上进行的两个长寿命粒子（long-lived particle）搜索：一个使用模糊顶点重建算法（fuzzy displaced vertex reconstruction algorithm）在缺失横向能量触发的事件中寻找位移顶点（displaced vertices），另一个使用新型位移μ子触发（displaced muon trigger）在μ子触发的事件中寻找位移顶点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHC近期致力于搜索非即时衰变的长寿命新粒子（new long-lived particles），这些粒子在探测器中飞行一定距离后才衰变为多个可见径迹，形成位移顶点（displaced vertices, DV）这一奇异特征。

Method: 研究采用两种不同方法：Run 2搜索使用新型"模糊"位移顶点重建算法（fuzzy displaced vertex reconstruction algorithm）处理长寿命粒子衰变为重夸克（heavy quarks）的情况，该算法与标准算法并行使用；Run 3搜索则首次应用新型位移μ子触发（displaced muon trigger）来识别相关事件。

Result: Run 2搜索对希格斯门户（Higgs Portal）、超对称（SUSY）和DFSZ轴微子（DFSZ axino）模型设定了限制；Run 3搜索则对R-宇称破缺超对称（RPV SUSY）模型设定了限制。两个搜索均为首次应用各自的新技术。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了ATLAS实验通过创新算法和触发技术，在长寿命粒子搜索方面取得的进展，特别是在处理复杂衰变拓扑（如重夸克衰变）和利用新型触发策略方面的突破。

Abstract: Many recent efforts at the LHC have been made to search for new particles that do not decay promptly but are instead long-lived. This has been done via many different exotic signatures, including searches performed at ATLAS for displaced vertices (DV), where the new long-lived particle decays into multiple visible tracks after having traveled a certain distance into the detector. This talk covers two such searches: a Run 2 search for DVs in events triggered by missing transverse energy, and a Run 3 search for DVs in events triggered by muons. The former search is the first to use a new "fuzzy" displaced vertex reconstruction algorithm, alongside the standard one, to effectively reconstruct cases where the long-lived particle decays into heavy quarks that are themselves slightly long-lived, hence causing the final visible decay products to not point back exactly to the same vertex, setting limits on Higgs Portal, SUSY, and DFSZ axino models. The latter search is the first to use a new displaced muon trigger, setting limits on RPV SUSY models.

</details>

Abstract: This contribution discusses the physics potential of a future muon collider operating at a center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s} = 10$ TeV for precision studies in the Higgs sector. Using a detailed detector simulation that incorporates the dominant sources of machine-induced background, the expected sensitivity to key Higgs processes is evaluated. These include the measurement of production cross sections for $H\to b\bar{b}$, $H\to WW^*$, and double-Higgs production $H\!H\to b\bar{b}b\bar{b}$. A central focus of the study is the determination of the Higgs boson trilinear self-coupling, a critical parameter for understanding the structure of the Higgs potential and electroweak symmetry breaking. The analysis is based on the MUSIC multi-purpose detector concept, specifically optimized for the muon collider environment, and assumes an integrated luminosity of $10$ ab$^{-1}$ collected over five years. The results presented highlight the exceptional prospects of a multi-TeV muon collider for exploring the Higgs potential with a level of precision unattainable by any other proposed future collider within a comparable timeframe.

### [41] [Search for the single production of vector-like quarks decaying into a W boson and a b quark using single-lepton final states in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17564)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: CMS实验在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中搜索重矢量样夸克（VLQ）的单产生过程，未发现超出标准模型预言的显著信号，并给出了VLQ产生截面及其耦合常数κ_W的最严格上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在搜索重矢量样夸克（vector-like quark, VLQ）的单产生过程，这类粒子是超越标准模型（beyond the Standard Model）物理的重要候选者。通过分析VLQ衰变为W玻色子和b夸克的过程，可以探索新物理的存在及其与标准模型粒子的耦合强度。

Method: 分析使用CMS实验在CERN大型强子对撞机（LHC）收集的13 TeV质心能量质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度为138 fb⁻¹。搜索针对W玻色子轻子衰变的事件特征，包括一个电子或μ子、大的横向动量不平衡、至少一个来自b夸克碎裂的高横向动量喷流，以及至少一个探测器前向区域的喷流。

Result: 未观察到超出标准模型预言的显著超出信号。在95%置信水平下设置了VLQ产生截面及其与标准模型扇区耦合κ_W的上限。对于完全衰变为Wb的VLQ，κ_W上限随VLQ质量变化，在约1.4 TeV质量处达到低至0.086的值。当κ_W=0.2时，VLQ质量下限为2.4 TeV。

Conclusion: 本研究给出了迄今为止对衰变为Wb的VLQ单产生过程最严格的限制。这些结果对超越标准模型物理中重矢量样夸克的存在及其性质设定了重要约束，为未来更高能量对撞实验的搜索提供了基准。

Abstract: A search is performed for the single production of a heavy vector-like quark (VLQ), decaying into a W boson and a b quark. The analysis uses proton-proton collision data collected by the CMS experiment at the CERN LHC at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. The search targets events with leptonic W boson decays. The event signature consists of one electron or muon, large transverse momentum imbalance, at least one jet consistent with coming from the fragmentation of a b quark and having large transverse momentum, and at least one jet in the forward region of the detector. No significant excess over the standard model prediction is observed. Upper limits are set at the 95% confidence level on the production cross section of a VLQ and its coupling $κ_\mathrm{W}$ to the standard model sector. For a VLQ decaying exclusively into Wb, the upper limit on $κ_\mathrm{W}$ depends on the VLQ mass and reaches values as low as 0.086 for masses around 1.4 TeV. For $κ_\mathrm{W}$ = 0.2 the lower limit on the VLQ mass is 2.4 TeV. These are the most stringent limits to date on the single production of VLQs decaying into Wb.

</details>


### [42] [Measurements of electroweak penguins and $B$ decays to final states with missing energy at Belle and Belle II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17644)
*Valerio Bertacchi*

Conclusion: Belle和Belle II实验积累的大规模数据集为研究稀有电弱企鹅B衰变，特别是那些涉及末态缺失能量的过程提供了重要平台，相关结果有助于检验标准模型（Standard Model）和寻找新物理（new physics）迹象。

Abstract: The Belle and Belle II experiments have collected a 1.3 ab$^{-1}$ sample of $e^+e^-\to B\bar B$ collisions at $Υ(4S)$ centre-of-mass energy. Results on these datasets of $b\to s \ell^+\ell^-$ $(\ell=e,μ)$, $b\to sτ^+τ^-$, and $b\to sν\bar ν$ transitions are presented.

For user experiments, the facility is equipped with a high-precision proton telescope offering a positioning resolution of 10 $μ$m, and a Time-of-Flight (TOF) spectrometer achieving an energy resolution of 1%. Furthermore, a compatible trigger logic unit have been designed to provide precise event tagging, which is essential for data alignment. This paper presents an overview of the detector systems within HPES, discusses their design considerations, and outlines the future prospects of the facility.

*Yuan Wang,Ran Li,Bin Zhong,Yaqian Wang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过联合分析LHCb、ATLAS和CMS实验的双J/ψ质量谱数据，显著增强了X(7200)态的证据，并改进了X(6900)共振参数的测量精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过联合分析多个实验数据，提高对全粲四夸克态（fully-charmed tetraquark）X(6900)和X(7200)的测量精度，并深入理解干涉效应在四夸克谱学中的重要作用。

Method: 方法是对LHCb、ATLAS和CMS三个实验的双J/ψ（di-J/ψ）质量谱数据进行联合分析，采用同时拟合（simultaneous fits）技术，并比较多个干涉模型（interference models）以评估信号显著性。

Result: 结果发现X(6900)具有极高显著性（>12σ），其质量和宽度测量精度显著提高；X(7200)在不同干涉模型中均显示一致信号，显著性范围为3.7σ至6.6σ，其中CMS三共振方案（three-resonance scheme）的最佳拟合模型达到6.6σ显著性。

Conclusion: 结论强调干涉效应在全粲四夸克谱学中的关键作用，并为LHC上这些态的产生机制提供了新的约束条件，显著增强了X(7200)态存在的证据。

Abstract: We report enhanced evidence for the $X(7200)$ state and significantly improved measurements of the $X(6900)$ resonance parameters through a combined analysis of the di-$J/ψ$ mass spectrum using published data from LHCb, ATLAS, and CMS. By performing simultaneous fits to all three experiments, we observe the $X(6900)$ with overwhelming significance ($>12σ$) and determine its mass and width with improved precision. For the $X(7200)$, we find consistent signals across multiple interference models, with significances ranging from $3.7σ$ to $6.6σ$; the best-fit model (adopting the CMS three-resonance scheme) yields $6.6σ$ significance, providing substantially strengthened evidence for this state. Our results underscore the essential role of interference effects in fully-charmed tetraquark spectroscopy and offer new constraints on their production mechanisms at the LHC.

### [46] [Lights, Camera, Axion: Tracing Axions from Supernovae in the Diffuse $γ$-ray Sky](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01277)
*Brijesh Kanodia,Debajit Bose,Subhadip Bouri,Ranjan Laha*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae）大量产生的轴子在传播过程中可通过轴子-光子转换（axion-photon conversion）产生光子，超新星宇宙群体的累积发射可能产生弥散伽马射线信号（diffuse gamma-ray signal）。

Method: 开发了一个综合框架，建模超新星中的轴子产生，并首次一致地考虑了轴子在所有相关磁场环境中的光子转换，包括前身星（progenitor）、宿主星系（host galaxy）、星系际介质（intergalactic medium）和银河系（Milky Way），同时结合更新的宇宙恒星形成率（cosmic star formation rate）。

Result: 利用COMPTEL、EGRET和Fermi-LAT对弥散伽马射线天空的测量，在广泛的轴子质量范围内推导出对轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）的竞争性约束。通过Fisher预测分析（Fisher forecast analysis）进一步预测了即将到来的MeV伽马射线望远镜对该弥散信号的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了计算超新星轴子转换产生的弥散伽马射线通量的完整框架，利用现有观测数据对轴子参数施加了约束，并为未来MeV伽马射线望远镜的探测能力提供了预测。

Abstract: Axions produced copiously in core-collapse supernovae can convert into photons as they propagate through various astrophysical magnetic fields. The cumulative emission from the cosmic population of supernovae can therefore generate a diffuse gamma-ray signal through axion-photon conversion. In this work, we develop a comprehensive framework to compute the diffuse gamma-ray flux by modeling axion production in supernovae and, \textit{for the first time}, consistently accounting for their conversion into photons across all relevant magnetic field environments - progenitor, host galaxy, intergalactic medium, and the Milky Way - together with an updated cosmic star formation rate. Using measurements of the diffuse gamma-ray sky from COMPTEL, EGRET, and \textit{Fermi}-LAT, we derive competitive constraints on the axion-photon coupling over a wide range of axion masses. We further forecast the sensitivity of upcoming MeV gamma-ray telescopes to this diffuse signal using a Fisher forecast analysis.

*Tommaso Armadillo,Eugenia Celada,Jaco ter Hoeve,Fabio Maltoni,Luca Mantani,Juan Rojo,Alejo N. Rossia,Simone Tentori,Marion O. A. Thomas,Eleni Vryonidou*

Method: 采用三种互补的分析框架：希格斯耦合修正因子（Higgs coupling modifiers）、有效希格斯和电弱耦合（effective Higgs and electroweak couplings）、以及全局标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）拟合。SMEFT分析包含重整化群演化（renormalisation-group evolution）、线性/二次贡献、以及可用的EFT截面NLO修正。
