Conclusion: 研究为未来高能对撞机实验提供了系统的灵敏度评估框架，通过多种互补方法解释测量结果，并为新物理探测建立了可复现的分析工具链，支持后续的扩展和定制化研究。

Abstract: We present projections for the sensitivity of future high-energy colliders to new physics through precision measurements of the Standard Model (SM) interactions, focusing on near-term electron-positron facilities: FCC-ee, LEP3, and the Linear Collider Facility. We interpret these projections in three complementary frameworks: Higgs coupling modifiers, effective Higgs and electroweak couplings, and global SMEFT fits. The SMEFT analysis includes renormalisation-group evolution, linear/quadratic contributions, and NLO corrections to EFT cross sections where available. By matching the EFT to UV-complete models, we also quantify the sensitivity of future colliders to representative benchmark scenarios, including composite Higgs models and single-particle SM extensions. In parallel, we release an updated version of the open-source SMEFiT framework, enabling the results presented here to be fully reproduced, extended, and customised.

### [48] [Four-fermion operators, $Z$-boson exchange, and $τ$ lepton dipole moments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16598)
*Joël Gogniat,Martin Hoferichter,Gabriele Levati*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了在$e^+e^-\toτ^+τ^-$过程中通过不对称性测量来约束τ子偶极矩（包括反常磁矩$a_τ$和电偶极矩$d_τ$）的潜力，特别关注了未来SuperKEKB对撞机极化升级后的前景，并评估了电弱效应和四费米子算符等次领头阶修正的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $e^+e^-\toτ^+τ^-$过程中的不对称性测量为约束τ子的偶极矩（dipole moments）——包括反常磁矩（anomalous magnetic moment）$a_τ$和电偶极矩（electric dipole moment）$d_τ$——提供了有前景的途径。特别是在未来SuperKEKB对撞机可能实现的极化电子束（polarized electron beam）升级后，这种方法将更具竞争力。

Method: 研究分析了次领头阶（subleading orders）的电弱效应（electroweak effects）和四费米子算符（four-fermion operators）的影响，这些算符参数化了超出标准模型（beyond-the-Standard-Model）的场景。通过理论计算评估了Z玻色子贡献和四费米子算符的最大可能效应。

Result: Z玻色子贡献出现在$\simeq 3\times 10^{-6}$的水平，而四费米子算符的最大可能效应估计为$\simeq 10^{-5} C \, v^2/Λ^2$。研究还发现，四费米子算符在圈图水平（loop level）的插入可以探测那些原本无法直接约束的威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients），而偶极算符在圈图水平产生的虚部为无需极化电子束即可确定$a_τ$提供了另一潜在途径。

Conclusion: 尽管存在固有的圈图压制（loop suppression），但将所需的正规不对称性（normal asymmetry）$A_N^\pm$测量精度提高到$\lesssim 10^{-5}$将允许探测施温格项（Schwinger term），这可以定义为在Belle II当前设置下实现的中间目标。这表明不对称性测量为约束τ子偶极矩提供了有前景的方法，特别是在未来极化升级的背景下。

Abstract: Asymmetry measurements in $e^+e^-\toτ^+τ^-$ constitute a promising avenue to obtain competitive constraints on the $τ$ dipole moments, the anomalous magnetic moment $a_τ$ and the electric dipole moment $d_τ$, especially, once a polarized electron beam becomes available, as possible at a future polarization upgrade of the SuperKEKB collider. While the main challenges concern the measurement of these asymmetries and the calculation of radiative corrections at the relevant level of precision, at subleading orders also electroweak effects and the potential impact of four-fermion operators parameterizing other beyond-the-Standard-Model scenarios besides those described by dipole operators need to be taken into consideration. Here, we show that $Z$-boson contributions arise at the level of $\simeq 3\times 10^{-6}$, while we estimate the largest possible effect from four-fermion operators as $\simeq 10^{-5} C \, v^2/Λ^2$. In addition, we observe that four-fermion-operator insertions at the loop level can probe Wilson coefficients that are otherwise not constrained directly, and that the imaginary part generated by insertions of the dipole operator at loop level opens another potential avenue towards a determination of $a_τ$ without the need for a polarized electron beam. Despite the inherent loop suppression, a measurement of the required normal asymmetry $A_N^\pm$ with a precision of $\lesssim 10^{-5}$ would allow one to probe the Schwinger term, which could define an intermediate goal to be realized in the current setting at Belle II.

</details>


### [49] [Investigating the Neutrino Mass Ordering Problem via Ternary Plots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16652)
*Alexander Migala,Kate Scholberg*

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析超新星爆发中微子在现代探测器中的观测数据，探索如何区分中微子质量顺序（normal vs. inverted ordering）。研究采用三元图（ternary plots）可视化SNEWPY软件包中不同超新星中微子通量模型的风味组成（flavor composition）随时间演化，并通过简化反演过程（unfolding process）识别两种质量顺序的判别特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法采用SNEWPY软件包中的多个超新星中微子通量模型，创新性地使用三元图（ternary plots）可视化中微子风味组成的时间演化。通过简化的反演过程（unfolding process）分析不同模型，探索正常质量顺序（normal mass ordering）与倒置质量顺序（inverted mass ordering）之间的判别特征。

Result: 研究发现正常质量顺序与倒置质量顺序在不同模型中倾向于占据三元空间（ternary space）的不同区域。通过分析多个模型，研究探索了区分两种质量顺序的潜在稳健判别因子（robust discriminants）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过分析超新星爆发中微子的风味组成时间演化，可以区分正常与倒置质量顺序。不同质量顺序在三元空间中占据不同区域的特征为未来实验观测提供了有价值的理论依据。

Abstract: We explore what may be deduced about the neutrino mass ordering problem from the observation of core-collapse supernova burst neutrinos in modern terrestrial detectors. We employ ternary plots in a novel way to visualize the time evolution of the flavor composition of various supernova neutrino flux models from the SNEWPY software package. Through our analysis of several models using a simplified unfolding process, we have explored potential robust discriminants between the normal and inverted mass orderings. We find that the normal and inverted mass orderings tend to occupy different regions in ternary space across different models.

### [50] [Cavity-mode couplings in axion dark matter searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16891)
*Byeong Rok Ko*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了用于轴子暗物质搜索的双端口微波腔系统中腔模耦合效应，发现弱耦合端口的测量对于消除系统不确定性至关重要，可恢复约10%的实验灵敏度损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子暗物质搜索实验通常使用双端口微波腔系统，其中一个端口强耦合用于信号拾取，另一个端口弱耦合用于腔体表征。研究旨在分析这种配置下腔模耦合对实验的影响，特别是对系统不确定性的贡献。

Method: 研究通过理论分析双端口腔系统中的腔模耦合效应，考察强耦合端口和弱耦合端口之间的相互依赖性，并评估其对轴子暗物质搜索实验关键参数的影响。

Result: 研究发现双端口系统中一个端口的测量耦合强度依赖于另一个端口，导致腔模无载品质因数（unloaded quality factor）关系中的耦合系数随测量值显著变化。扫描速率（scanning rate）作为轴子暗物质搜索的品质因数（figure-of-merit），能消除强耦合端口的系统贡献，剩余系统不确定性仅来自弱耦合端口。

Conclusion: 建议测量弱耦合端口的耦合强度以消除系统不确定性，从而恢复可能损失的实验灵敏度。例如，当弱耦合端口耦合强度为0.05时，可恢复约10%的灵敏度损失。

Abstract: Axion dark matter searches use a microwave cavity for the resonant conversion of axions into photons to enhance experimental sensitivity, with the cavity generally configured as a two-port system for both signal pickup and cavity characterization measurements. In this study, we investigated cavity-mode couplings in such a two-port system and examined their impact on axion dark matter search experiments, which typically use one strongly coupled port and one weakly coupled port. We found that, in such a two-port cavity system, the measured coupling strength of one port depends on that of the other; hence, the coupling coefficients appearing in the relation for the unloaded quality factor of the cavity mode can vary substantially with the measured coupling strengths. Meanwhile, the scanning rate, the figure-of-merit for axion dark matter searches, cancels the systematic contribution from the strongly coupled port; hence, the remaining systematic uncertainty arises only from the weakly coupled port and may be negligible, depending on its coupling strength. Nevertheless, we recommend measuring the coupling strength of the weakly coupled port to eliminate this systematic uncertainty and thereby recover any experimental sensitivity that may have been lost, for example by approximately 10\% when the coupling strength of the weakly coupled port is 0.05.

</details>


### [51] [Deciphering the universal scaling of particle transverse momentum spectra in heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17345)
*Xi-Yao Guo,Hua Zheng,Wenchao Zhang,Li-Lin Zhu,Xing-Quan Liu,Zhi-Guang Tan,Dai-Mei Zhou,Ben-Hao Sa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了RHIC能量下重离子碰撞中π介子、K介子和质子的横向动量谱标度性质，发现了基于平均总粒子多重数和平均横向动量的普适标度行为，并与LHC的ExTrEMe合作组发现以及Hwa-Yang标度建立了等价关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于系统性地探究相对论重离子对撞机（Relativistic Heavy Ion Collider, RHIC）不同能量和中心度下粒子横向动量谱的标度性质，验证大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）ExTrEMe合作组最近发现的标度行为是否具有普适性。

Method: 研究方法包括：使用RHIC实验数据，分析Au+Au碰撞在$\sqrt{s_{NN}}$ = 7.7-200 GeV以及U+U碰撞在193 GeV下不同中心度类别的π介子、K介子和质子横向动量谱；通过全局物理量（平均总粒子多重数和平均横向动量）对谱进行标度化处理。

Result: 研究发现：当用全局物理量标度化粒子横向动量谱时，出现了普适标度行为，证实了LHC ExTrEMe合作组的标度发现；该标度行为在高横向动量（high $p_{T}$）区域和边缘碰撞（peripheral collisions）中失效；通过流体力学中强子化使用的Cooper-Frye公式为这些观测提供了自然解释。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明：RHIC数据中发现的标度行为与LHC ExTrEMe合作组的发现一致，并证明了该标度与二十年前提出的Hwa-Yang标度（Hwa-Yang scaling）具有等价性，为理解重离子碰撞中的粒子产生机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We systematically investigate the scaling properties of the transverse momentum spectra for pions, kaons, and protons in Au+Au collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$ = 7.7, 11.5, 14.5, 19.6, 27, 39, 62.4, and 200 GeV, as well as in U+U collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$ = 193 GeV, across different centrality classes, using experimental data from the collaborations at the Relativistic Heavy Ion Collider (RHIC). Universal scaling emerges when the particle transverse momentum spectra are scaled by global physical quantities, i.e., the average total particle multiplicity and mean transverse momentum, confirming recent scaling findings from the data at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) by the ExTrEMe collaboration. The scaling behavior breaks down in the high $p_{T}$ region and in peripheral collisions. We provide a natural explanation for these observations by invoking the Cooper-Frye formula, which is used for hadronization in hydrodynamics. Furthermore, we demonstrate the equivalence between the scaling found by the ExTrEMe collaboration and the Hwa-Yang scaling which was proposed two decades ago.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 测试结果显示锥隔离和球度形成了"剪刀约束"：Comover相互作用模型的局域解读与锥数据存在张力，其全局解读与球度数据不符。非即时产生的平坦性要求机制在早期本征时间起作用。

Conclusion: 现有强子或弦基框架均无法同时满足四项约束，唯一存活的机制类别是与部分子自由度一致的早期全局关联介质，该介质与ALICE奇异增强、长程脊结构等现象共存，且密度窗口符合Campanini & Ferri状态方程。

Abstract: The multiplicity-dependent suppression of $Υ(n\mathrm{S})$ states measured by CMS in $pp$ at $\sqrt s=7\,$TeV \cite{CMS2020}, and of $ψ(2S)\big/J/ψ$ measured by LHCb at $\sqrt s=13\,$TeV \cite{LHCb2024}, is subjected to four multi-differential tests: \emph{cone isolation}, \emph{azimuthal sectors}, \emph{transverse sphericity}, and \emph{prompt vs. non-prompt}. Cone and sphericity close a \emph{scissors constraint}: the local reading of the Comover Interaction Model is in tension with the cone data, its global reading with the sphericity data. The non-prompt flatness forces the mechanism to act at early proper times. None of the considered hadronic or string-based frameworks -- CIM local or global, PYTHIA 8 MPI \cite{Sjostrand2015}, rope hadronisation \cite{Bierlich2015}, CGC \cite{Ma2015}, Trainor TCM \cite{Trainor2008} -- naturally satisfies the four constraints simultaneously in its published form. The surviving class is an early, globally correlated medium consistent with partonic degrees of freedom, co-occurring with the ALICE strangeness enhancement \cite{ALICE_SE}, the long-range ridge \cite{CMS_ridge}, and below the threshold of the partonic baryon-meson $v_2$ \cite{ALICE_v2}, in a density window compatible with the Campanini \& Ferri equation of state \cite{Campanini2011}.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过推导固定局域极化下共轭度的上界（upper bound），建立极化与纠缠的定量关系。进一步考虑宇称破坏过程$e^+e^- \to Z^0 \to q\bar{q}$作为具体物理应用，分析末态自旋极化的生成。

Result: 研究发现增加局域极化会约束最大可达到的纠缠，该上界在某些情况下可由纯态饱和。在$e^+e^- \to Z^0 \to q\bar{q$过程中，最大共轭度在特定运动学区域达到，且相对于非极化情况显著降低。

Abstract: We establish a quantitative relation between local spin polarization and quantum entanglement in two-qubit systems by deriving an upper bound on the concurrence at fixed local polarization, showing that increasing polarization constrains the maximum achievable entanglement. We further demonstrate that this bound is saturated by pure states in certain cases. As a concrete physical application, we consider the parity-violating process $e^+e^- \to Z^0 \to q\bar{q}$, which generates final-state spin polarization. We show that the maximal concurrence is attained in specific kinematic regions and is significantly reduced relative to the unpolarized case. These results establish a general, process-independent framework connecting local polarization, maximal entanglement, and the role of pure states.

Abstract: Motivated by the first observation of CP violation in $b$-baryon decays, the search for baryonic decays exhibiting large CP violation will be a primary focus in the coming years. We propose that significant CP-violating effects exist in the decay $Λ_b \to ΛD$, where $D$ denotes a CP eigenstate of the $D^0 - \bar{D}^0$ system. Additionally, we predict for the first time several nonzero CP-violating observables associated with angular distribution parameters, providing valuable complementary information in the search for CP violation in baryon decays. Furthermore, we propose a novel strategy to extract the CKM angle $γ$ by combining data on angular distribution parameters and decay rates from the relevant channels. We emphasize that $Λ_b \rightarrow ΛD$ decays are among the most promising candidates for determining $γ$ in the baryon sector. Our findings may offer new insights for future theoretical and experimental investigations.

### [57] [Two-body charmed anti-charmed baryonic $B$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18366)

TL;DR: 该研究使用拓扑振幅方法分析B介子衰变为含粲反粲重子对的过程，系统分解了不同味表示组合的衰变振幅，并考虑了SU(3)味对称性破缺效应，对多个衰变道的分支比进行了预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用拓扑振幅方法，将所有$\overline B\to {\bf B}_c \overline {\bf B}_c$衰变振幅按重子的味表示（flavor representation）进行分解，包括$\bf {\bar 3_f}$、$\bf {3_f}$、$\bf {6_f}$、$\bf {\bar 6_f}$等不同组合。模型化了多种依赖于s夸克线位置的SU(3)破缺效应，并利用现有实验数据作为输入参数。

Conclusion: 测量这些衰变道的分支比能够为理解SU(3)味对称性破缺效应提供重要信息。当前预测的不确定性较大，需要通过实验测量来约束相关理论参数，深化对重子衰变中非微扰QCD效应的认识。

Abstract: We study the rates of two-body charmed anti-charmed baryonic $\overline B\to {\bf B}_c \overline {\bf B}_c$ decays using the topological amplitude approach. (i) In the low-lying $\overline B\to {\bf B}_c(\bf {\bar 3_f}) \overline {\bf B}_c(\bf { 3_f})$ decays, we find that the exchange diagram is sizable. Furthermore, there is a large cancellation between internal $W$-tree and exchange-$W$-tree amplitudes. The SU(3) breaking is sizable, 35% SU(3) breaking effects are needed, and they work differently in different amplitudes. The rates of $\overline B\to {\bf B}_c(\bf {\bar 3_f}) \overline {\bf B}_c(\bf { 3_f})$ decays with some excited ${\bf B}_c(\bf {\bar 3_f})$ are also studied. (ii) The $\overline B\to {\bf B}_c(\bf 6_f) \overline {\bf B}_c(\bf { 3_f})$ decays, with low-lying $ \overline {\bf B}_c(\bf { 3_f})$ and low-lying and some excited ${\bf B}_c(\bf 6_f)$ baryons are studied with some predictions on rates. (iii) The $\overline B\to {\bf B}_c(\bf {\bar 3_f}) \overline {\bf B}_c(\bf {\bar 6_f})$ decays with low-lying charmed anti-charmed baryons are studied with some predictions on rates. (iv) Uncertainties in most predicted rates are large, reflecting our current poor understanding of the related SU(3) breaking effects. Measuring these rates can provide very useful information about these effects.

### [58] [Hydrodynamics of Filtered Dark Matter: A Two-Component Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17383)
*Juntaro Wada*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了过滤暗物质（Filtered DM）在一级相变（FOPT）期间的流体动力学行为，发现气泡壁对暗物质流体高度反射但对辐射透明，导致不同于电弱相变的流体动力学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究过滤暗物质（Filtered DM）在一级相变（first-order phase transition, FOPT）期间的流体动力学行为，其独特之处在于气泡壁对暗物质流体高度反射但对辐射透明，这与电弱相变（electroweak FOPT）的流体动力学问题有本质区别。

Method: 将系统建模为由暗物质和辐射组成的双组分流体（two-component fluid），分别在弹道区域（ballistic regime）和局域热平衡区域（local thermal equilibrium, LTE regime）分析流体动力学解。

Result: 流体动力学解可分为类爆轰（detonation-like）和类爆燃（deflagration-like）分支；在弹道区域，无法进入壁的暗物质能量-动量表现为反射模式，而在LTE区域则弛豫为辐射能量-动量；这种差异导致暗物质和辐射流体表现出不同的流体动力学行为，特别是类爆燃分支解的存在条件不同。

Conclusion: 流体动力学效应对过滤暗物质遗迹丰度（relic abundance）产生影响，并改变了丰度值；从双流体系统视角讨论了熵流（entropy current）的非守恒性，并简要评述了过滤暗物质系统与信息热力学系统（information-thermodynamic systems）的相似性。

Abstract: We study the hydrodynamics of the Filtered Dark Matter (Filtered DM) scenario during a first-order phase transition (FOPT). In this scenario, the bubble wall is highly reflective of the dark matter (DM) fluid but transparent to radiation, making the hydrodynamic problem fundamentally different from that of the electroweak FOPT. Motivated by this property, we formulate the hydrodynamics of this system as a two-component fluid composed of DM and radiation, and find that the solutions can be classified into detonation-like and deflagration-like branches in the ballistic regime and in the local thermal equilibrium (LTE) regime. In the ballistic regime, the energy--momentum of DM that cannot enter the wall appears as a reflected mode, while in the LTE regime, it relaxes into the energy--momentum of radiation. We find that this difference in the fate of the DM fluid that cannot enter the interior of the wall leads to different hydrodynamic behaviors in the DM and radiation fluids independently and, in particular, results in different existence conditions for solutions in the deflagration-like branch. Based on these results, we further revisit the impact of hydrodynamic effects on the relic abundance of Filtered DM and demonstrate the change in the abundance induced by hydrodynamic effects. In addition, we also discuss the non-conservation of the entropy current from the viewpoint of the two-fluid system, and briefly comment on the similarity between the Filtered DM system and information-thermodynamic systems.

Conclusion: 本文提出的改进Bogoliubov方法能够稳定计算原初引力波全谱，揭示了暴胀子振荡非简谐性对高频引力波谱的影响。相关数值代码已在GitHub上公开，便于后续研究使用。

The improved method allows us to demonstrate that anharmonicity of inflaton oscillations can leave interesting fingerprints on the high-frequency part of the GW spectrum. The improved method allows us to demonstrate that anharmonicity of inflaton oscillations can leave interesting fingerprints on the high-frequency part of the GW spectrum. ### [60] [New physics in the $ZZh$ vertex: One-loop contributions from a radiative seesaw model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17666)
*Héctor Novales-Sánchez,Humberto Vázquez-Castro,Mónica Salinas*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确希格斯物理为超越标准模型（Standard Model）的物理提供了敏感窗口，而中微子振荡实验证实了非零中微子质量的存在，暗示了新物理的存在。这些事实促使研究者探索中微子对希格斯物理的贡献。

Method: 在I型跷跷板机制（type-I seesaw mechanism）的变体中，轻中微子质量在树图水平为零并通过辐射修正产生，研究者计算了轻型和重型马约拉纳中微子（Majorana neutrinos）对ZZh顶点的单圈贡献。分析了表征ZZh顶点的CP守恒和CP破坏异常耦合，并研究了在未来轻子对撞机中两种相关运动学情景下的现象学意义：希格斯辐射产生（Higgsstrahlung production）和通过中性流矢量玻色子融合（neutral-current vector-boson fusion）的希格斯产生。

Result: 研究发现CP守恒效应可以达到约10^{-3}的量级，这可能在未来实验灵敏度范围内；而CP破坏贡献则被强烈压制，远低于此类预测的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 在研究的跷跷板机制框架下，马约拉纳中微子对ZZh顶点的贡献中，CP守恒效应可能在未来实验中被探测到，而CP破坏效应则极其微弱。这为通过精确希格斯测量探测中微子质量生成机制提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Precision Higgs physics offers a sensitive window into physics beyond the Standard Model. In parallel, neutrino-oscillation experiments have established the existence of nonzero neutrino masses, thus implying the presence of new physics. Motivated by these facts, we investigate the one-loop contributions of light and heavy Majorana neutrinos to the $ZZh$ vertex within a variant of the type-I seesaw mechanism in which light-neutrino masses vanish at tree level and are then generated radiatively. We analyze the $CP$-conserving and $CP$-violating anomalous couplings which characterize the $ZZh$ vertex and study their phenomenological implications in two relevant kinematic scenarios at future lepton colliders: Higgsstrahlung production and Higgs production via neutral-current vector-boson fusion. We find that $CP$-conserving effects can reach magnitudes of order $10^{-3}$, potentially within projected future experimental sensitivities, whereas $CP$-violating contributions are strongly suppressed, lying well beyond such projections.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We reevaluate the vacuum polarization functions for electroweak gauge bosons at three loops in QCD, employing state-of-the-art perturbative techniques. We apply these results to determine the ${\mathcal{O}}(αα_s^2)$ corrections to the electroweak radiative parameters $Δρ$, $Δr$ and $Δκ$. We improve the accuracy of the calculation at this perturbative order, compared to the existing literature, and present some phenomenological implications of these results. We find a shift in the prediction of the $W$ boson mass, significant in view of the FCC precision targets. We improve the prediction of the $\overline{\mathrm{MS}}$ electric charge at $q^2=m_Z^2$ with the inclusion of these ${\mathcal{O}}(αα_s^2)$ corrections.

Result: 对于特定范围的Riesz指数（Riesz exponents），证明了优化集收敛于球体（ball），同时在不相交凸集并集的优化问题上获得了新的研究成果。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在截断参数趋于无穷的渐近极限下，拉普拉斯特征值Riesz平均的优化问题中，最优几何形状在一定指数范围内收敛于球体，这一结论为理解特征值优化问题的几何结构提供了重要见解。

Result: 证明了在温和的附加假设下，满足Szegö条件的雅可比矩阵的波算子存在且完备，为这类算子的散射理论建立了严格数学基础。

### [64] [Muscle-inspired magnetic actuators that push, pull, crawl, and grasp](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18090)

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该研究通过激光粉末床熔融技术制备了肌肉启发的磁性驱动器，通过调控激光能量精确控制机械刚度和磁响应，实现了可逆弯曲、线性收缩和抓取功能，为下一代自适应软机器人提供了新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具备大变形、承载能力和多功能运动的磁性复合材料对于下一代自适应软机器人至关重要。现有技术需要在单一材料系统中同时编程刚度和磁化强度，以实现远程驱动、可重构且耐疲劳的软驱动器。

Method: 采用激光粉末床熔融技术增材制造热塑性/永磁聚氨酯/Nd2Fe14B复合材料。通过将激光能量尺度调谐在1.0至3.0之间，精确控制机械刚度和磁响应。该方法能够制造0.5毫米厚的弯曲铰链，并在中等磁场下实现可逆弯曲和折叠。

Result: 拉伸强度从0.28 MPa增加到0.99 MPa，同时保持30-45%的断裂伸长率。两种驱动器展示了系统多功能性：伸长型驱动器在500 mT磁场下实现线性收缩，提升50克负载（32倍自重）；可扩展型驱动器在300 mT磁场下可逆开合，可靠抓取不同物体。磁性爬行机器人在纹理基底上达到100%运动成功率。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了基于激光粉末床熔融的策略，可在单一材料系统中同时编程刚度和磁化强度，实现远程驱动、可重构且耐疲劳的软驱动器。该方法为力控、多功能磁性软机器人在自适应抓取、运动和生物医学工具微创操作方面开辟了新可能性。

Abstract: Functional magnetic composites capable of large deformation, load bearing, and multifunctional motion are essential for next-generation adaptive soft robots. Here, we present muscle-inspired magnetic actuators (MMA), additively manufactured from a thermoplastic/permanent magnet polyurethane/Nd2Fe14B (TPU/MQP-S) composite using laser powder bed fusion (LPBF). By tuning the laser-energy scale between 1.0 and 3.0, both mechanical stiffness and magnetic response are precisely controlled: the tensile strength increases from 0.28 to 0.99 MPa while maintaining 30-45% elongation at break. This process enables the creation of 0.5 mm-thick flexural hinges, which reversibly bend and fold under moderate magnetic fields without damage. Two actuator types are reported showing the system versatility. The elongated actuator with self-weight of 1.57 g, magnetized in its contracted state, achieves linear contraction under a 500 mT field, lifting 50 g (32x its own weight) and sustaining performance over at least 50 cycles. Equipped with anisotropic frictional feet, it supports movement of a magnetic crawling robot that achieves up to 100% locomotion success on textured substrates. The expandable actuator exhibits reversible opening and closing under a 300 mT field, reliably grasping and releasing different objects, including soft berries and rigid 3D printed geometries. It can also anchor in a tube while holding suspended 50 g loads. This work demonstrates a LPBF-based strategy to program both stiffness and magnetization within a single material system, enabling remotely driven, reconfigurable, and fatigue-resistant soft actuators. The approach opens new possibilities for force controlled, multifunctional magnetic soft robots for adaptive gripping, locomotion, and minimally invasive manipulation of biomedical tools.

### [65] [Reevaluating Quantum Geometric Criteria for Itinerant Magnetic Instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16782)
*Min-Fong Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了量子几何与磁不稳定性之间的理论关联，通过建立基于通道表示的矩阵不稳定性判据，揭示了磁相变由裸磁化率张量与自旋相互作用矩阵共同决定，而非仅由单通道量子几何结构预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何与电子关联的相互作用已成为量子多体物理中的重要范式，近期研究强调量子几何在巡游电子系统中识别磁不稳定性的诊断效用。本研究旨在批判性地重新审视这些理论提案。

Method: 采用Ginzburg-Landau框架下的Hartree-Fock平均场近似，考虑多通道磁有序化，为一般双轨道系统在通道表示中建立了严格的矩阵不稳定性判据。

Result: 研究结果表明磁相变由裸磁化率张量与自旋相互作用矩阵之间的复杂相互作用共同决定。先前关于仅从单通道磁化率的量子几何结构预测不稳定性的论断，仅在相互作用矩阵和磁化率矩阵完全通道解耦时才成立。

Conclusion: 通过采用通道表示，该公式相比传统的轨道空间方法具有更高的物理透明度和计算可行性，为复杂多轨道系统的理论研究提供了有前景的替代方案。

Abstract: The interplay between quantum geometry and electron correlation has emerged as a compelling paradigm in quantum many-body physics. Recent studies have highlighted the diagnostic utility of quantum geometry in identifying magnetic instabilities within itinerant electron systems. In the present work, we critically re-examine these theoretical proposals. Using the Ginzburg-Landau framework within the Hartree-Fock mean-field approximation and accounting for multiple channels of magnetic ordering, we formulate a rigorous matrix-based instability criterion in the channel representation for generic two-orbital systems. Our results demonstrate that magnetic phase transitions are intricately governed by the interplay between the bare susceptibility tensor and the spin interaction matrix. Consequently, prior assertions that instabilities can be predicted solely from the quantum geometric structure of a single-channel susceptibility are valid only under complete channel decoupling in both the interaction and susceptibility matrices. By adopting the channel representation, our formulation achieves greater physical transparency and computational tractability compared to the conventional orbital-space approach, thereby furnishing a promising alternative for advancing theoretical studies of complex multi-orbital systems.

Even through the need for collaboration among theory, numerics and experiment to understand the complex phases of quantum magnets is well established, yet, in our view there remains a persistent perception from experts in one area that the other two serve merely as supporting tool, primarily useful for validating the dominant ideas of one specialty, and less relevant to shaping the underlying scientific narrative. In this article, we advocate for a different, more integrated approach to overcome the challenges faced by quantum magnetism researchers. We argue that this alternative mindset has already started to advance the understanding of several important quantum magnetic models and their materials realizations.

### [67] [UCd$_{11}$: A strongly localized 5$f^3$ material](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16844)
*Martin Sundermann,Naoki Ito,Daisuke Takegami,Chun-Fu Chang,Sheng-Huai Chen,Chang-Yang Kuo,Simone G. Altendorf,Andrei Gloskovskii,Hlynur Gretarsson,Eric D. Bauer,Jan Kuneš,Liu Hao Tjeng,Andrea Severing,Atsushi Hariki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过DFT+DMFT计算揭示UCd₁₁为高度局域化的铀5f³系统，并挑战了卫星特征作为强关联或巡游5f行为可靠指标的传统观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UCd₁₁作为反铁磁铀金属间化合物，其铀-铀间距接近希尔极限的两倍，暗示弱杂化的5f电子特性。尽管X射线光谱显示铀采用U³⁺ 5f³构型，但芯能级光电子能谱仅显示弱卫星特征，这与巡游行为的典型解释相矛盾，需要澄清其电子特性。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）结合动力学平均场理论（DMFT）计算UCd₁₁，使用材料特定参数调整以重现不同光子能量下的价带光电子能谱（PES）谱，利用光电离截面的能量依赖性。同时通过DFT+DMFT安德森杂质模型获得芯能级谱。

Result: 计算结果表明UCd₁₁是高度局域化的铀5f³系统。芯能级谱分析显示，与传统假设相反，卫星结构的存在或缺失并非强关联或巡游5f行为的可靠指标。

Conclusion: 该研究明确证实UCd₁₁为高度局域化系统，并挑战了基于卫星特征判断电子特性的传统范式，指出需要更谨慎地解释光谱特征与电子行为之间的关系。

Abstract: UCd$_{11}$ is an antiferromagnetic uranium intermetallic compound ($T_{\rm N}$ = 5.3K) with enhanced electron mass and uranium-uranium spacings nearly twice the Hill limit, suggesting a weakly hybridized 5$f$ electronic character. Various x-ray spectroscopy techniques indicate that uranium in UCd$_{11}$ adopts the formal U$^{3+}$ 5$f^3$ configuration, while core-level photoemission spectroscopy (PES) data of UCd$_{11}$ reveal only a weak satellite feature, typically interpreted as a signature of itinerancy. In this work, we present density functional theory (DFT) combined with dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) calculations of UCd$_{11}$, using material-specific parameters tuned to reproduce valence-band PES spectra at different photon energies, thereby exploiting the energy dependence of photoionization cross sections. Our results demonstrate that UCd$_{11}$ is a highly localized uranium 5$f^3$ system. Furthermore, core-level spectra obtained from a DFT+DMFT Anderson impurity model reveal that, contrary to common assumptions, the presence or absence of satellite structures is not a reliable indicator of strong correlations or itinerant 5$f$ behavior.

</details>


### [68] [Band mixing and particle-hole asymmetry in moiré fractional Chern insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16847)
*Nicolás Morales-Durán,Jingtian Shi,Cristian Voinea,Paweł Potasz,Jennifer Cano*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了远程能带混合（remote band mixing）对分数陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator）稳定性的影响，解释了魔角MoTe₂中ν=1/3和ν=2/3填充率下实验观测到的不对称性，并阐明了ν>1/2时重入整数量子反常霍尔态（re-entrant integer quantum anomalous Hall states）的起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释魔角材料（moiré materials）中观察到的实验不对称性，特别是在扭曲MoTe₂中ν=1/3和ν=2/3填充率下分数陈绝缘体稳定性的差异。该研究试图揭示远程能带混合如何影响不同量子相之间的竞争。

Method: 研究采用一系列近似连续介质描述的魔角材料模型，分析远程能带混合对分数陈绝缘体稳定性的影响。通过比较不同填充率下电子维格纳晶体（electron Wigner crystal）、空穴维格纳晶体（hole Wigner crystal）和分数陈绝缘体之间的能量竞争来探究相稳定性。

Result: 研究发现，在无能带混合时，ν=1/3的主要不稳定性是电子晶体，而ν=2/3的主要竞争相是空穴晶体。远程能带混合显著降低电子晶体能量，但对空穴晶体影响微弱，因此对ν=1/3分数陈绝缘体的破坏作用强于ν=2/3，解释了实验观测的不对称性。

Conclusion: 远程能带混合通过不对称地影响电子和空穴维格纳晶体的能量，导致分数陈绝缘体在不同填充率下的稳定性差异。这一机制不仅解释了ν=1/3和ν=2/3的不对称性，也为魔角MoTe₂中ν>1/2时重入整数量子反常霍尔态的出现提供了理论解释。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of remote band mixing on the stability of fractional Chern insulators in a family of models that approximate continuum descriptions of moiré materials. Our results suggest that the experimentally observed asymmetry between filling fractions $ν=1/3$ and $ν=2/3$ in twisted MoTe$_2$ originates from a competition between a fractional Chern insulator, an electron Wigner crystal, and a hole Wigner crystal. In the absence of band mixing, the leading instability at $ν= 1/3$ is the electron crystal, whereas at $ν= 2/3$ the main competing phase is the hole crystal. Remote band mixing substantially lowers the energy of the electron crystal but has only a weak effect on the hole crystal. Consequently, it destabilizes the fractional Chern insulator at $ν=1/3$ more strongly than at $ν=2/3$. This mechanism also provides an explanation for the emergence of re-entrant integer quantum anomalous Hall states in moiré MoTe$_2$ for fillings $ν>1/2$.

### [69] [Experimental Signatures of Topological Transport in Polycrystalline FeSi Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17103)
*R. Mantovan,A. Bozhko,V. Zhurkin,A. Bogach,A. Khanas,S. Zarubin,A. Zenkevich,V. Glushkov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究在65纳米厚的多晶ε-FeSi薄膜中意外发现了清晰的拓扑特征，证明了其作为高温、无贵金属的Weyl半金属（Weyl semimetal）的潜力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过固态反应（solid-state reaction）在Si(100)衬底上沉积Fe，制备了65纳米厚的多晶ε-FeSi薄膜。通过测量温度无关的反常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）σ_{xy}^{AHE}、各向异性纵向磁阻（anisotropic longitudinal magnetoresistance）和平面霍尔效应（planar Hall effect）来探测拓扑特征。

Result: 在200K以下观测到温度无关的反常霍尔电导σ_{xy}^{AHE} ≈ 14 μS/sq.，证明反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）是内禀的，源于非平庸贝里相位（non-trivial Berry phase）。该标度关系在约40纳米的多晶结构中占主导，且对体态与表面态电子输运的温度交叉具有鲁棒性。通过手征反常（chiral anomaly）进一步确认了ε-FeSi的非平庸拓扑态，并估算出两个Weyl点（Weyl points）的间距为(k_{+}^{W}-k_{-}^{W})/(2π) ≈ 0.36。

Conclusion: 研究证实了多晶ε-FeSi薄膜中电子输运的拓扑起源，并发现其作为一种新型高温、无贵金属的Weyl半金属的潜力，挑战了无序会破坏拓扑特征的固有观念。

Abstract: Disorder in any form is considered to be highly detrimental to the experimental exploration of novel phenomena in quantum materials with non-trivial band topology. Contrary to established belief, clear topological features are reliably detected in the electron transport of polycrystalline 65-nm-thick ε-FeSi films grown via solid-state reaction of Fe deposited on a Si(100) substrate. The observation of temperature-independent anomalous Hall conductivity σ_{xy}^{AHE} \sim const (σ_{xx)) (σ_{xy}^{AHE} \approx 14 uS/sq.) below 200 K firmly proves the anomalous Hall effect in this compound to be intrinsic and originating from a non-trivial Berry phase. The discovered scaling dominates over the nanoscale (\sim 40 nm) polycrystalline texture and is robust to temperature crossover between bulk and surface modes of electron transport. The non-trivial topological state of ε-FeSi is also confirmed by a chiral anomaly both in anisotropic longitudinal magnetoresistance and planar Hall effect specific for Weyl semimetals. Relating scaled anomalous Hall conductance to a "quantized" Hall response of a Weyl semimetal the distance between two Weyl points has been estimated as (k_{+}^{W}-k_{-}^{W})/(2π) \approx 0.36. Our findings confirm the topological origin of electron transport in the polycrystalline ε-FeSi thin films and discover its potential as a new high temperature and noble metal-free Weyl semimetal.

Although the NQR spectra show no detectable change across $T_{\rm N}$, the nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate, $1/T_1$, exhibits a clear anomaly at $T_{\rm N}$. An analysis based on the alignment of the Nd moments demonstrates that the internal magnetic fields generated by these moments cancel each other at the Co sites. If the nearest-neighbor Nd moments align antiferromagnetically, this finding suggests that Ga substitution removes magnetic frustration, thereby increasing $T_{\rm N}$.

### [71] [Orbital glass conceals missing magnetic entropy in a relativistic Mott insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17540)
*Ilija K. Nikolov,Rong Cong,Adrien Rosuel,Stephen Carr,Ian R. Fisher,Dmitri E. Feldman,Adrian Del Maestro,Chandrasekhar Ramanathan,Vesna F. Mitrović*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子材料中不同自由度（degrees of freedom, DOF）的耦合会产生具有复杂竞争序参量和涌现激发的奇异物相。然而，不同序参量在传统实验探测中相互掩盖，阻碍了对这些序参量及其相互关系的微观理解。

Method: 采用相位敏感技术（phase sensitive technique），通过独立解析不同对称性的相互作用来测量基态性质，从而能够区分源自自旋与轨道自由度耦合的不同序参量响应。

Result: 在5d¹相对论性莫特绝缘体（relativistic Mott insulator）Ba₂NaOsO₆中直接探测到由竞争相互作用引起的轨道玻璃态（orbital glass state）。观察到高达380 K的短程轨道序（short-range orbital order），以及在磁相变附近轨道色散的急剧增加，后者形成了破坏晶体旋转对称性的轨道向列态（orbital nematic state）。

Conclusion: 轨道向列态诱导了磁有序（magnetic ordering）的形成。短程轨道序在远高于磁相变的温度下存在，解决了该材料长期存在的熵缺失（missing entropy）难题。

Abstract: Coupling between different degrees of freedom (DOF) in an electronic material leads to exotic phases of matter characterized by complex and competing order parameters as well as emergent excitations. Building a microscopic understanding of these order parameters and their mutual relationship is hindered by the fact that different orders often mask each others' response to conventional experimental probes. Here, we reveal how to disentangle responses from distinct orders that arise from the coupling between the spin and orbital DOF. Our method uses a phase sensitive technique that measures ground state properties by independently resolving interactions of different symmetries. This allows us to directly detect an orbital glass state caused by competing interactions in the $5d^1$ relativistic Mott insulator Ba$_2$NaOsO$_6$. We observe short-range orbital order up to 380 K and a dramatic increase of orbital dispersion near the magnetic phase transition. This orbital dispersion generates a directional ordering, $\textit{i.e.}$, it forms an orbital nematic state which breaks the rotational symmetry of the crystal. We establish that the orbital nematic state induces the magnetic ordering. The presence of this short-range orbital order well above the magnetic phase transition solves the long-standing puzzle of missing entropy in this material.

Abstract: We study an effective low-energy Kondo model on the triangular lattice in which itinerant electrons occupy a valence pocket at $Γ$ and three conduction pockets at the $M$ points of the Brillouin zone. This construction has a Fermi-surface nesting structure that favors triple-$Q$ magnetic order while only assuming the low-energy band-structure. Treating the local moments as classical spins on a four-sublattice magnetic unit cell, we find extended regions of non-coplanar order, including tetrahedral and related canted tetrahedral states, in addition to ferromagnetic and coplanar phases. The chiral phases remain stable over a broad range of inter-pocket Kondo couplings and persist in the presence of an external magnetic field. For certain chiral orders, the electronic bands can become gapped and host a quantum anomalous Hall state with $σ_{xy}=4\,e^2/h$. These results show that chiral magnetism and a quantized anomalous Hall effect on the triangular lattice do not rely on a specific tight-binding band structure, but can arise more generally from low-energy nested pockets at $Γ$ and $M$.

### [75] [Magnetic-fluctuation-driven suppression of spin-orbit hybridization in the surface ferromagnet GdAg$_2$/Ag(111)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18009)

We find that spin fluctuations preserve the nodal-line-derived band crossings even above the Curie temperature, while SOC-induced hybridization develops only at low temperatures, as evidenced by spectral-weight redistribution. Motivation: 研究旨在探索三维Hubbard-Holstein模型中电子关联与电子-声子耦合的相互作用，特别是在半填充条件下对磁输运性质的影响，以理解强关联材料中竞争相之间的邻近效应。

Result: 低温相图显示存在反铁磁绝缘相和电荷有序绝缘相，由一级相变分隔；在U~带宽条件下，V-T相图呈现多种相态，包括Mott-Hubbard绝缘体、双极化子绝缘体和两种双极化子金属态；在相边界附近观察到强邻近效应。

Conclusion: 三维Hubbard-Holstein模型展现出丰富的相行为，竞争相之间的强邻近效应为调控关联材料和探索涌现电子态提供了可能途径。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetotransport properties of the one-band Hubbard-Holstein model at half-filling in three dimensions (3D) using exact diagonalization based semi-classical Monte Carlo simulations with phonons treated in the adiabatic limit. The low-temperature electronic correlation $U$ vs electron-phonon coupling $V$ phase diagram reveals two insulating phases--antiferromagnetic (AF-I) and charge-ordered (CO-I)--separated by a first-order transition, with no metallic phase observed at their intersection, indicating robustness of these phases in 3D. For $U \sim bandwidth$, the $V$ vs temperature $T$ phase diagram exhibits multiple phases including AF-I, CO-I, Mott-Hubbard insulator, bipolaronic insulator, and two bipolaronic metallic states. Several first-order transitions occur near $V \sim 3.75$. Above the ordering temperature, the density of states shows universal behavior dominated by electronic contribution, while susceptibility and DOS analyses reveal pseudogap features. Magnetic and transport properties along the phase boundary highlight strong proximity effects between competing phases, suggesting routes for tuning correlated materials and emergent electronic states.

Abstract: We show that a three-dimensional superconductor with a non-Abelian SU(2) order parameter can support an extended resistive regime a Bose metal, in which transport is carried by bosonic electron-Majorana bound states - separating a uniform superconductor from a pair-density-wave (PDW) phase. The setting is a solvable Kondo lattice model introduced previously by the present authors, in which Kondo screening of a Yao-Lee $\mathbb{Z}_2$ spin liquid generates an order parameter with SU(2), rather than conventional U(1), symmetry, containing both superconducting and spin-density-wave components. Two effects cooperate to make fluctuations anomalously strong in three dimensions: the vanishing of the quadratic superconducting stiffness near the Lifshitz point where the optimal pairing momentum shifts from zero to finite $Q$, and the enlarged SU(2) order-parameter manifold. Building on our prior result that doping away from half-filling drives amplitude-modulated PDW order via finite-momentum electron-Majorana condensation, we analyze the fluctuation-dominated regime above that phase using a nonlinear sigma model. We find that the order-parameter propagator develops a ring of soft modes throughout the disordered phase, and that the resulting resistivity scales approximately as $R \sim T^3$ in three dimensions.

### [78] [Photoinduced orbital polarization and Jahn-Teller effect in RNiO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18524)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀土镍酸盐中轨道自由度通常在温度驱动的金属-绝缘体转变中保持惰性，系统形成两个不等价的Ni位点。研究旨在探索通过光学激发激活轨道极化，以访问隐藏的非热相并实现轨道序的相干控制。

Method: 采用相互作用的紧束缚多带模型（interacting multiband tight-binding model），结合电子-离子-自旋动力学的实时模拟（real-time simulations of coupled electron-ion-spin dynamics）。通过调节光偏振实现轨道选择性激发。

Result: 光诱导的d-d跃迁降低了Ni位点的局域磁矩，有效抑制了激发态中的洪德耦合（Hund's coupling）。偏振调控使激发具有强轨道选择性，导致e_g轨道占据数不平衡，驱动Jahn-Teller畸变的结构弛豫。

Conclusion: 偏振控制的光学激发为访问具有涌现轨道序的隐藏非热相提供了途径，实现了在超快时间尺度上对耦合的电荷、自旋和晶格自由度的相干控制。

Abstract: The orbital degree of freedom in rare-earth nickelates is typically inactive across the temperature-driven metal-insulator transition, where the system develops two inequivalent Ni sites associated with Ni-O bond disproportionation and breathing-mode distortions of NiO$_6$ octahedra. Here, we show that orbital polarization can be induced by optical excitation with linearly polarized light. Using an interacting multiband tight-binding model combined with real-time simulations of coupled electron-ion-spin dynamics, we find that photoinduced $d$-$d$ transitions reduce the local magnetic moments at Ni sites and effectively suppress Hund's coupling $J$ in the excited state. Importantly, these transitions can be made strongly orbital-selective by tuning the light polarization, leading to an imbalance in $e_g$ orbital occupancies. The resulting nonequilibrium state, characterized by reduced effective $J$ and unequal orbital populations, becomes unstable toward Jahn-Teller (JT) distortions, driving structural relaxation along coherently excited JT modes. Our results demonstrate that polarization-controlled optical excitation provides a pathway to access hidden nonthermal phases with emergent orbital order, enabling coherent control of coupled charge, spin, and lattice degrees of freedom on ultrafast timescales.

### [79] [Fingerprints of preformed pairs in two-electron angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18560)
*Janez Bonča,Andrea Damascelli,Mona Berciu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究使用变分精确对角化方法计算Hubbard-Holstein模型中双电子移除谱权重，提出该谱权重可作为双电子角分辨光电子能谱强度的有效代理。研究发现来自同一电子对的信号与来自不同电子对的信号在能量和动量依赖上具有明显差异，这些特征可用于确认电子对的存在并区分其相干性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用变分精确对角化（variational exact diagonalization, VED）方法计算一维链上Hubbard-Holstein模型的双电子移除谱权重。该方法从基态（包含两个电子）出发，分析谱权重作为2eARPES过程强度的有效代理。

Result: 研究结果显示：来自同一电子对的信号（较弱）与来自不同电子对的信号（较强）在能量上分离，前者出现在较低结合能处；两者具有不同的动量依赖特征和对称性。这些特征在不同对称性的电子对中均出现，且源于动量和能量守恒，因此是电子-玻色子耦合模型中电子对形成的普适特征。

Conclusion: 实验观测这些特征可确认电子对的存在，且动量依赖图谱能够区分电子对是否具有相干性（超导性）。这些结论可推广至有限但低电子浓度、有限温度及更高维度的情况，为实验探测电子对提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We use variational exact diagonalization (VED) to calculate the two-electron removal spectral weight for the Hubbard-Holstein model, starting from the ground-state with two electrons on a one-dimensional chain. We argue that this spectral weight provides a valuable proxy for the intensity of 2eARPES processes. Our results show that when contrasted to the presumably larger signal due to two electrons ejected from two different pairs, the presumably weaker signal due to two electrons ejected from the same pair (i) is segregated in energy, appearing at a lower binding energy, and (ii) has a very characteristic momentum dependence, with a different symmetry than that of the signal corresponding to two electrons emitted from two different pairs. We verify that these fingerprints appear for pairs with different symmetries, and prove that they arise as a direct consequence of momentum and energy conservation, therefore they are generic for any model with electron-boson coupling that can lead to formation of electron pairs. Experimental observation of these fingerprints will confirm the existence of pairs. Moreover, the momentum dependence map allows one to distinguish whether the pairs are coherent (superconducting) or not. Finally, we argue that these considerations generalize to finite but low electron concentrations, finite temperatures and higher dimensions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 静态非局域磁化率在波矢Q=(π,π)处出现峰值，顶点修正显著增强该峰值导致磁不稳定性；d波和s±序参数之间存在激烈竞争，梯子DFT+DMFT方法中s±不稳定性占主导。

Abstract: By employing a combined method of density functional theory and dynamical mean field theory (DFT+DMFT) we investigate the effect of electronic correlations on the magnetic and superconducting properties of the iron-based parent compound LaFeAsO. We find that the static non-local susceptibility $χ({\bf q})$ exhibits a peak at the in-plane wave vector ${\mathbf Q}=(π,π)$, which is strongly enhanced upon inclusion of the vertex corrections in the ladder approximation, leading to magnetic instability. Considering the eigenfunctions of the Bethe-Salpeter equation with the vertex, obtained within the second order perturbation theory, as well as the ladder approach containing dynamic interaction vertices, in agreement with earlier weak-coupling-based studies of LaFeAsO, we obtain a close competition between $d$-wave and $s_{\pm}$ order parameters, dominating in the second-order and ladder approach, respectively. We argue that the dominating $s_{\pm}$ instability in the ladder DFT+DMFT approach is related to the reduced degree of magnetic frustration by itinerant degrees of freedom due to only partially formed local magnetic moments. Our study shows that dynamic correlation effects do not change the type of the leading superconducting instability in LaFeAsO.

### [81] [Dimensional Criticality at Grokking Across MLPs and Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16431)
*Ping Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出TDU-OFC方法，通过分析梯度快照的级联统计量，发现深度神经网络在"顿悟"（grokking）过程中存在从记忆到泛化的宏观相变特征，表现为有效级联维度D(t)在泛化转变时穿越高斯扩散基线D=1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂系统中不同动力学状态间的急剧转变是普遍现象，深度神经网络中的"顿悟"现象提供了典型例证——训练精度饱和后长时间才出现从记忆到泛化的急剧转变。然而，这种转变的稳健宏观特征仍然难以捉摸。

Method: 引入TDU-OFC（阈值化扩散更新-Olami-Feder-Christensen）离线雪崩探针，将梯度快照转换为级联统计量，并通过与顿悟对齐的有限尺寸标度提取宏观可观测量——时间分辨的有效级联维度D(t)。

Result: 在Transformer（模加法任务）和MLP（XOR任务）中发现，有效级联维度D(t)在泛化转变时精确穿越高斯扩散基线D=1，且穿越方向具有任务依赖性。雪崩分布呈现重尾特征，有限尺寸标度与从D(t)提取的维度指数一致。

Conclusion: D(t)作为非侵入性探针，能够提前100-200个训练周期预测顿悟行为转变，揭示了深度神经网络中从记忆到泛化转变的临界动力学特征，支持向候选共享临界流形吸引的机制解释。

Abstract: Abrupt transitions between distinct dynamical regimes are a hallmark of complex systems. Grokking in deep neural networks provides a striking example -- an abrupt transition from memorization to generalization long after training accuracy saturates -- yet robust macroscopic signatures of this transition remain elusive. Here we introduce \textbf{TDU--OFC} (Thresholded Diffusion Update--Olami-Feder-Christensen), an offline avalanche probe that converts gradient snapshots into cascade statistics and extracts a \emph{macroscopic observable} -- the time-resolved effective cascade dimension $D(t)$ -- via grokking-aligned finite-size scaling. Across Transformers trained on modular addition and MLPs trained on XOR, we discover a localized dynamical crossing of the Gaussian diffusion baseline $D=1$ precisely at the generalization transition. The crossing direction is task-dependent: modular addition descends through $D=1$ (approaching from $D>1$), while XOR ascends (from $D<1$). This opposite-direction convergence is consistent with attraction toward a candidate shared critical manifold, rather than trivial residence near $D \approx 1$. Negative controls confirm this picture: ungrokked runs remain supercritical ($D>1$) and never enter the post-transition regime. In addition, avalanche distributions exhibit heavy tails and finite-size scaling consistent with the dimensional exponent extracted from $D(t)$. Shadow-probe controls ($α_{\mathrm{train}}=0$) confirm that $D(t)$ is non-invasive, and grokked trajectories diverge from ungrokked ones in $D(t)$ some $100$--$200$ epochs before the behavioral transition.

</details>


### [82] [Multi-Label Phase Diagram Prediction in Complex Alloys via Physics-Informed Graph Attention Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16468)
*Eunjeong Park,Amrita Basak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种物理信息图注意力网络（physics-informed graph attention network），用于快速预测Ag-Bi-Cu-Sn合金系统的相平衡，通过结合元素感知表示和热力学约束，实现了高精度相图映射和合金筛选。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相平衡（phase equilibria）是合金设计的基础，但传统CALPHAD方法在多组分成分-温度空间中的计算成本高昂且通常局限于稀疏截面。需要开发快速相映射和合金筛选方法以克服这些限制。

Method: 采用物理信息图注意力网络（GAT），将每个成分-温度点表示为四节点元素图，以原子分数和元素描述符作为节点特征。模型结合图注意力、全局池化和多层感知器预测九个相关相，并引入热力学约束作为训练惩罚或推理时投影。

Result: 在六个二元和三个三元子系统中，基线模型获得0.951的宏观F1分数和93.98%的精确集匹配率。物理信息解码提高了鲁棒性，在密集域内网格上将精确集准确率提升至约96%。模型在未见三元截面和700°C四元截面分别达到99.32%和91.78%的准确率。

Conclusion: 基于注意力的图学习与热力学约束强制相结合，为高分辨率相映射和外推合金筛选提供了有效且物理一致的替代模型，显著提高了相平衡预测的效率和准确性。

Abstract: Accurate phase equilibria are foundational to alloy design because they encode the underlying thermodynamics governing stability, transformations, and processing windows. However, while the CALculation of Phase Diagrams (CALPHAD) provides a rigorous thermodynamic framework, exploring multicomponent composition-temperature space remains computationally expensive and is typically limited to sparse section. To enable rapid phase mapping and alloy screening, we propose a physics-informed graph attention network (GAT) that learns element-aware representations and couples them with thermodynamic constraints for multi-label phase-set prediction in the Ag-Bi-Cu-Sn alloy system. Using about 25,000 equilibrium states generated with pycalphad, each composition-temperature point is represented as a four-node element graph with atomic fractions and elemental descriptors as node features. The model combines graph attention, global pooling, and a multilayer perceptron to predict nine relevant phases. To improve physical consistency, we incorporate thermodynamic constraints, applied as training penalties or as an inference-time projection. Across six binary and three ternary subsystems, the baseline model achieves a macro-F1 score of 0.951 and 93.98% exact-set match, while physics-informed decoding improves robustness and raises exact-set accuracy to about 96% on dense in-domain grids. The surrogate also generalizes to an unseen ternary section with 99.32% exact-set accuracy and to a quaternary section at 700 °C with 91.78% accuracy. These results demonstrate that attention-based graph learning coupled with thermodynamic constraint enforcement provides an effective and physically consistent surrogate for high-resolution phase mapping and extrapolative alloy screening.

### [83] [Do time delay effects explain galactic velocity profiles?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18132)
*L. Benkoula,K. Chima,J. Kingsbury,K. Marroquin,M. Yim,T. Curtright*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 基于引力-电磁类比，本文批判了用时间延迟效应（"延迟引力"）解释星系速度曲线的理论，证明在各项同性、时间依赖的物质流情况下，作用在轨道天体上的力是牛顿式的，仅由瞬时环境物质分布决定，不存在时间延迟效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在批判那些利用时间延迟效应（time delay effects）或"延迟引力（retarded gravity）"来解释星系速度曲线（galactic velocity profiles）的理论。研究动机源于对弱引力场（weak gravitational fields）中引力-电磁类比（gravitoelectromagnetic analogy）框架下此类解释的有效性质疑。

Method: 研究方法采用弱引力场下的引力-电磁类比框架。针对各项同性、时间依赖的物质流（isotropic, time-dependent matter currents），在该理论框架内进行分析和推导。

Result: 研究结果表明，对于各项同性、时间依赖的物质流，作用在轨道天体上的力是牛顿式的（Newtonian），且仅由瞬时环境物质配置（instantaneous ambient matter configuration）决定。在此类情况下不存在时间延迟效应。

Conclusion: 结论指出，在引力-电磁类比框架下，对于各项同性、时间依赖的物质流，星系速度曲线不能用时间延迟效应解释，因为作用力本质上是牛顿式的且仅依赖于瞬时物质分布。

Abstract: Using the gravitoelectromagnetic analogy for weak gravitational fields, we critique explanations of galactic velocity profiles that invoke time delay effects (i.e. "retarded gravity"). For isotropic, time-dependent matter currents, we show within this framework that the force exerted on an orbiting body is Newtonian and due only to the instantaneous ambient matter configuration -- there are no time delay effects in such situations.

Method: 通过溶胶-凝胶（sol-gel）、煅烧（calcination）、液滴挤出（droplet extrusion）和烧结（sintering）工艺制备了bredigite（Ca7MgSi4O16）、akermanite（Ca2MgSi2O7）和diopside（CaMgSi2O6）三种载体，随后浸渍负载万古霉素。使用X射线衍射（XRD）和扫描电子显微镜（SEM）分别验证了陶瓷晶相形成和载体的大孔特性。

Result: 基于MTT检测，负载抗生素的bredigite、akermanite和diopside装置分别表现出最低、中等和最高水平的人骨髓间充质干细胞（hBM-MSCs）活力与增殖。XRD和SEM分析证实了所需陶瓷晶相的形成和载体的大孔特性。

Conclusion: 研究得出结论：在决定装置的细胞生物相容性时，载体生物吸收动力学（bioresorption kinetics）的作用超过了药物递送动力学（drug delivery kinetics）的影响。

Abstract: Bioceramic porous microspheres are promising substances for dental and orthopedic bone void filling, tissue engineering and drug delivery applications. In this research, the structure and cytocompatibility of bioactive magnesium-calcium silicate macroporous microspheres loaded with vancomycin hydrochloride, an antibiotic drug, were studied. In this regard, bredigite (Ca7MgSi4O16), akermanite (Ca2MgSi2O7) and diopside (CaMgSi2O6) carriers were fabricated through a sequence of sol-gel, calcination, droplet extrusion and sintering processes, followed by impregnated with vancomycin. X-ray diffraction (XRD) and scanning electron microscopy verified the formation of the desired ceramic crystalline phases and macroporous characteristics of the carriers, respectively. Based on the MTT assay, the antibiotic-loaded bredigite, akermanite and diopside devices comparatively exhibited the lowest, intermediate and highest levels of human bone marrow mesenchymal stem cells (hBM-MSCs) viability and proliferation, respectively. It was concluded that the role of the carrier bioresorption kinetics prevails over the drug delivery kinetics in determining the cell biocompatibility of the devices.

</details>


### [85] [Drug-delivery Ca-Mg silicate scaffolds encapsulated in PLGA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16455)
*A. Jadidi,E. Salahinejad,E. Sharifi,L. Tayebi*

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种具有骨组织再生和局部抗生素递送双重功能的支架。通过泡沫复制法制备可生物降解的bredigite多孔支架，负载万古霉素并用PLGA涂层封装，改善了药物释放动力学和细胞相容性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在开发兼具骨组织再生和局部抗生素递送双重功能的支架，以解决骨缺损修复过程中感染控制和组织再生同步的需求。

Result: 未涂层样品因bredigite快速生物降解而表现出万古霉素突释（burst release）和对牙髓干细胞的低生物相容性。PLGA涂层在保持组织工程所需孔隙特性的同时，改善了药物释放动力学，缓冲了生理pH值，显著提高了负载万古霉素支架的细胞活力。

Conclusion: PLGA涂层封装的bredigite多孔支架成功实现了药物释放动力学的调控和细胞相容性的改善，为骨组织再生和局部抗生素递送的双功能应用提供了有效策略。

Abstract: The aim of this work is to develop dual-functional scaffolds for bone tissue regeneration and local antibiotic delivery applications. In this respect, bioresorbable bredigite (Ca7MgSi4O16) porous scaffolds were fabricated by a foam replica method, loaded with vancomycin hydrochloride and encapsulated in poly lactic-co-glycolic acid (PLGA) coatings. Field emission scanning electron microscopy, Archimedes porosimetry and Fourier-transform infrared spectroscopy were used to characterize the structure of the scaffolds. The drug delivery kinetics and cytocompatibility of the prepared scaffolds were also studied in vitro. The bare sample exhibited a burst release of vancomycin and low biocompatibility with respect to dental pulp stem cells based on the MTT assay due to the fast bioresorption of bredigite. While keeping the desirable characteristics of pores for tissue engineering, the biodegradable PLGA coatings modified the drug release kinetics, buffered physiological pH and hence improved the cell viability of the vancomycin-loaded scaffolds considerably.

### [86] [AI--Assisted Exploration: DHOST Theories without Quantum Ghosts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16531)
*Ginevra Braga,Raul Jimenez,Sabino Matarrese*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明了标量张量有效场论（EFTs）中高阶导数量子修正的规范对称性与哈密顿稳定性之间的等价性，为构建无鬼（ghost-free）引力有效场论提供了实用工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶导数量子修正是标量张量有效场论（scalar tensor effective field theories, EFTs）的关键组成部分，但通常会重新引入奥斯特罗格拉茨基鬼不稳定性（Ostrogradsky ghost instability），而经典理论原本设计来规避这一问题。本文旨在解决这一基本矛盾。

Method: 研究分析了由高斯-博内（Gauss Bonnet）和外尔平方（Weyl squared）算符增强的一般DHOST理论，其系数是标量场及其动能项的任意函数。通过两条独立路径：首先，要求完整作用量在经典理论的保护性规范对称性（protective gauge symmetry）下保持不变，推导出系数的微分方程组；其次，使用ADM形式（ADM formalism）进行第一性原理哈密顿分析，通过施加消除鬼所需的主要和次要约束（primary and secondary constraints）推导出另一组条件。

Result: 核心结果表明，这两组条件（一组代数条件，一组动力学条件）在数学上是完全相同的。这种等价性证明了规范对称性是量子修正理论中哈密顿稳定性（Hamiltonian stability）的根本起源。

Conclusion: 规范对称性原理被确立为构建一致、无鬼（ghost-free）引力有效场论（gravitational EFTs）的强大实用工具，无需进行完整的哈密顿分析。这为解决高阶导数量子修正中的鬼不稳定性问题提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Higher derivative quantum corrections are essential components of scalar tensor effective field theories (EFTs), yet they typically reintroduce the Ostrogradsky ghost instability that the classical theory was designed to evade. This paper resolves this fundamental tension by establishing a rigorous equivalence between two distinct criteria for theoretical consistency. We analyze a general DHOST theory augmented by Gauss Bonnet and Weyl squared operators with coefficients that are arbitrary functions of the scalar field and its kinetic term. We then pursue two independent paths: first, we derive a set of differential equations for these coefficients by demanding that the full action remains invariant under the protective gauge symmetry of the classical theory. Second, we perform a first principles Hamiltonian analysis using the ADM formalism, deriving a separate set of conditions by imposing the primary and secondary constraints required to eliminate the ghost. Our central result is the proof that these two sets of conditions, one algebraic and one dynamical, are mathematically identical. This equivalence demonstrates that the gauge symmetry is the fundamental origin of Hamiltonian stability in the quantum corrected theory and establishes the symmetry principle as a powerful and practical tool for constructing consistent, ghost free gravitational EFTs without resorting to a full Hamiltonian analysis

</details>


### [87] [Testing cosmological isotropy with gravitational waves and gamma-ray bursts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17746)
*Brian H. Y. Cheng,Donniel C. Cruz,Otto A. Hannuksela,Davendra S. Hassan,Christian Heiderijk,Leo Q. Hu,Souvik Jana,Jinwon Kim,Albert K. H. Kong,Peony K. K. Lai,Samuel C. Lange,Samson H. W. Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究使用引力波（gravitational waves）和伽马射线暴（gamma-ray bursts）的最新数据集，通过多种统计方法检验宇宙学各向异性，未发现显著证据支持各向异性，结果与宇宙学原理（cosmological principle）一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学原理（cosmological principle）主张宇宙在大尺度上是均匀和各向同性的，但一些替代宇宙学模型可能通过局部不均匀性、各向异性演化或奇异物理引入各向异性。此外，已有研究提示超新星（SNe Ia）、宇宙微波背景（CMB）和伽马射线暴（GRB）数据中可能存在轻微的各向异性证据，但这些发现尚未得到确认。

Method: 研究采用LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组最新发布的O4a数据和GRBWeb数据库（包含1991年以来所有已知伽马射线暴），通过角功率谱（angular power spectra）和两点相关函数（two-point correlation functions）等统计方法分析引力波和伽马射线暴的天空定位、质量、光度、红移等特征。在修正选择偏差后，将结果与合成数据进行比较。

Result: 在当前引力波和伽马射线暴数据集中未发现各向异性的显著证据，这一结果与宇宙学原理保持一致。研究扩展了先前分析，纳入了最新数据集并采用了多种互补的统计检验方法。

Conclusion: 基于引力波和伽马射线暴数据的分析未支持宇宙各向异性的存在，为宇宙学原理提供了新的观测验证。研究强调了使用多种统计方法和最新数据集进行宇宙学各向异性检验的重要性。

Abstract: The cosmological principle asserts that the Universe is homogeneous and isotropic on large enough scales. However, alternative cosmological models can bring about anisotropies through local inhomogeneities, anisotropic evolution, or exotic physics. In addition, select studies have also hinted at mild evidence of anisotropies in SNe Ia, CMB, and GRB data, though these remain unconfirmed. In this work, we test for cosmological anisotropies using gravitational waves and gamma-ray bursts, adopting the latest O4a release from the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA collaboration and GRBWeb (including all known GRBs since 1991). If the cosmological principle holds, the sky localisation and the characteristics of the GRBs and GWs (masses, luminosities, redshifts) should be statistically isotropic when corrected for selection biases. We employ a couple statistical methods, including angular power spectra and two-point correlation functions, and compare the results against synthetic data. The work extends previous analyses by including the most recent datasets, and the use of multiple complementary statistical tests. We find no significant evidence for anisotropy in the current GW and GRB datasets, consistent with the cosmological principle.

### [88] [A barotropic alternative to Early Dark Energy for alleviating the $H_0$ tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18053)
*Youri Carloni,Orlando Luongo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的宇宙学模型Λ_{ω_s}CDM，引入具有正状态方程ω_s的额外正压流体（barotropic fluid），以缓解哈勃常数（Hubble constant）的张力问题。该模型通过修改早期宇宙膨胀历史来提高H_0的推断值，同时保持晚期宇宙中该流体的次要地位以符合观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决标准宇宙学模型中的哈勃常数张力（Hubble tension）问题。与早期暗能量（Early Dark Energy, EDE）方案不同，作者提出引入一种具有正状态方程的额外正压流体，以修改早期宇宙膨胀历史，从而提高哈勃常数的推断值。

Method: 作者提出了Λ_{ω_s}CDM模型框架，在背景和微扰层面研究其理论含义。采用修改版的CLASS玻尔兹曼代码（Boltzmann code）与MontePython接口，进行完整的贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis），结合普朗克2018年宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）数据、DESI DR2重子声学振荡（BAO）测量、Pantheon Ia型超新星（SNe Ia）数据以及SH0ES的H_0测定。

Result: 分析显示，包含SH0ES先验（H_0 = 73.04 ± 1.04 km/s/Mpc）时，数据倾向于存在非零的正压流体。对于CMB+BAO+Pantheon+SH0ES数据集组合，得到ω_s = 0.290^{+0.017}_{-0.007}和密度参数10^5Ω_s = 1.47^{+0.35}_{-0.62}；排除BAO数据时，ω_s = 0.302^{+0.024}_{-0.013}，10^5Ω_s = 1.21^{+0.31}_{-0.65}。与EDE框架相比，Λ_{ω_s}CDM模型在统计上未被强烈排除。

Conclusion: Λ_{ω_s}CDM模型为哈勃常数张力问题提供了可行的解决方案，该额外流体可解释为具有压力的物质。结果表明，当前最小化的标准宇宙学模型可能是不完整的，需要引入额外的正压流体成分来完善宇宙学描述。

Abstract: We propose a cosmological scenario in which, beyond matter and radiation, an additional barotropic fluid with positive equation of state $ω_s$ contributes to the cosmic energy budget, in contrast to Early Dark Energy (EDE). We investigate the theoretical implications of this framework, here dubbed the $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM model, at both the background and perturbative levels, exploring its impact on the expansion history and structure formation. We show that, while remaining subdominant at late times and therefore consistent with current observational bounds, the additional fluid modifies the early-time expansion rate, leading to a higher inferred value of the Hubble constant. Thus, we perform a full Bayesian analysis using a modified version of the \texttt{CLASS} Boltzmann code interfaced with \texttt{MontePython}, considering combinations of \textit{Planck} 2018 Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) data, DESI DR2 Baryon Acoustic Oscillations (BAO) measurements, Pantheon Type Ia supernovae (SNe Ia), and SH0ES determinations of $H_0$. We find that the inclusion of the SH0ES prior, $H_0 = 73.04 \pm 1.04\,\mathrm{km/s/Mpc}$, leads to a preference for a nonvanishing barotropic fluid. In particular, we obtain $ω_s = 0.290^{+0.017(0.021)}_{-0.007(0.028)}$ and density $10^5Ω_s = 1.47^{+0.35(1.14)}_{-0.62(0.94)}$ for the dataset combination CMB + BAO + Pantheon + SH0ES, and $ω_s = 0.302^{+0.024(0.034)}_{-0.013(0.038)}$ and $10^5Ω_s = 1.21^{+0.31(1.10)}_{-0.65(0.86)}$ when BAO data are excluded. We further compare our scenario with the EDE framework and show that, statistically, no strong evidence is found against the $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM model. Finally, we provide a physical interpretation of our fluid in terms of matter with pressure, indicating that the standard cosmological model may be incomplete in its current minimal formulation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用机器学习方法，分析铁基超导体中正常态电阻率与超导性之间的关联。该方法能够识别远高于超导转变温度（Tc）的温区（150-300K）中蕴含的预测信息。

Result: 研究发现正常态电阻率与超导性之间存在强相关性，且预测信息存在于150-300K的宽温区窗口，远高于该材料家族的Tc。进一步分析表明超导特征分布于多个散射通道中，而非局限于单一通道。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了铁基超导体中正常态与超导态之间的深层关联，表明超导特征广泛分布于多个散射通道且存在于远高于Tc的温区。这一发现需要进一步的理论研究来阐明其微观机制。

Abstract: Unconventional superconductivity remains one of the central unsolved problems in quantum materials, and revealing its connection to the normal state is widely believed to be key to uncovering the pairing mechanism. Previous efforts have largely focused on the temperature range immediately above the superconducting transition, where specific scattering channels-such as strange-metal transport-have been identified as sharing a possible microscopic origin with superconductivity. Here, using machine learning, we demonstrate a strong correlation between normal-state resistivity and superconductivity in Fe-based superconductors. Remarkably, the predictive information reside in a wide window of 150-300 K, far above $T_c$ of this family. We further show that the signatures of superconductivity are distributed across multiple scattering channels, which requires further theoretical investigation.

### [90] [Quantum Tunnelling and Room-Temperature Superconductivity of Hydride from Size Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16460)
*Xiaozhi Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究提出将极端压力下金属探针间微米级氢化物样品的超导现象解释为金属-氢化物-金属结构的宏观量子隧穿效应，通过调控压力调节能垒高度，并建议减小能垒宽度和样品厚度以实现室温超导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释极端压力下金属探针间微米级氢化物样品超导现象的物理机制，将其视为通过金属-氢化物-金属结构的宏观量子隧穿现象，为室温超导的实现提供理论框架。

Method: 通过压力调控氢化物的能垒高度，同时最小化金属探针尖端间的能垒宽度以限制电子隧穿的指数衰减，并考虑约1微米的薄样品厚度效应，优化量子隧穿条件。

Result: 分析表明氢化物的能垒高度可通过压力调节，而能垒宽度和样品厚度是影响量子隧穿效率的关键参数，较薄的氢化物样品（约1微米）有利于获得更高的超导转变温度。

Conclusion: 为实现室温超导，建议同时减小能垒宽度和样品厚度以确保最优的量子隧穿条件，这为极端压力下氢化物超导体的实验设计提供了重要指导原则。

Abstract: Superconductivity of a micron-sized hydride sample measured between metal probes under extreme pressure could be considered as a macroscopic quantum tunnelling phenomenon through metal-hydride-metal. The energy barrier height of hydride is regulated by pressure. The energy barrier width between tips of the metal probes should be minimized to limit the chance of exponential decay in electron tunnelling. There is also a thickness effect since thinner hydride samples around 1 micron are favoured for achieving higher superconductive temperatures. Hence, reduction in both barrier width and sample thickness is recommended to ensure optimum quantum tunnelling for realization of the room temperature superconductivity.

### [91] [Ultrafast Magneto-Pressure Spectroscopy and Control of Correlated Phases in a Trilayer Nickelate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16611)
*Zhi Xiang Chong,Joong-Mok Park,Shuyuan Huyan,Avinash Khatri,Martin Mootz,Xinglong Chen,Daniel P. Phelan,Liang Luo,Ilias E. Perakis,J. F. Mitchell,Sergey L. Bud'ko,Paul C. Canfield,Jigang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究开发了高压（40 GPa）、强磁场（7 T）、低温（5 K）飞秒光谱实验平台，用于探测三层镍酸盐Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀中的准粒子动力学。观察到电荷密度波转变处的临界减速现象，以及高压下可能的超导关联迹象，但磁场依赖性微弱表明该超导态可能为非体相、丝状或高度不均匀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同时施加高压和强磁场的超快光谱技术是研究压力驱动电子不稳定性、关联相以及极端条件下体相超导行为的重要工具。然而，此类实验平台尚未实现，阻碍了对非平衡超导电性和涡旋控制准粒子动力学的深入理解。

Method: 本研究开发了高压（可达40 GPa）、强磁场（可达7 T）、低温（低至5 K）飞秒光谱实验平台，并将其应用于探测三层镍酸盐Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀中的准粒子动力学随磁场和压力的演化。

Result: 在电荷密度波（charge-density-wave）转变处观察到准粒子弛豫的显著临界减速现象，该现象在施加压力后消失。在更高压力下，低温弛豫时间反而延长，这与初生超导关联一致。然而，高达7 T的磁场依赖性可忽略，且未观察到涡旋诱导的预瓶颈动力学，表明在当前压力条件下的任何超导态可能为非体相、丝状或高度不均匀。

Conclusion: 磁场-压力超快光谱能力为解决关联量子材料中压力诱导超导电性和交织序的未解问题开辟了新途径。该技术平台为研究极端条件下的非平衡超导电性和准粒子动力学提供了关键实验手段。

Abstract: Ultrafast spectroscopy under simultaneous high pressure and magnetic field provides a versatile approach for investigating pressure-driven electronic instabilities and correlated phases, and for probing potential bulk superconducting behavior under extreme conditions. However, such an experimental platform has yet to be implemented, standing as a roadblock to a fuller understanding of nonequilibrium superconductivity and vortex-controlled quasi-particle (QP) dynamics.
  Here, we bridge this capability gap by developing high pressure (up to 40 GPa), high magnetic field (up to 7 T), cryogenic (down to 5 K) femtosecond spectroscopy, and using it to probe magneto-pressure evolution of quasiparticle dynamics in the trilayer nickelate $\mathrm{Pr}_4\mathrm{Ni}_3\mathrm{O}_{10}$.
  We observe pronounced critical slowing down of QP relaxation at the charge-density-wave transition, which collapses under applied pressure. At higher pressures, the relaxation instead lengthens at low temperature, consistent with incipient superconducting correlations.
  However, the negligibel magnetic-field-dependence up to 7~T and absence of vortex-induced pre-bottleneck dynamics--robust signatures observed in our controlled bulk superconducting samples--indicates that any superconducting state under the present pressure conditions is likely non-bulk, filamentary, or strongly inhomogeneous.
  The magneto-pressure ultrafast capability opens a new avenue for resolving outstanding questions surrounding pressure-induced superconductivity and intertwined orders in correlated quantum materials.

</details>


### [92] [Pairing Mechanism in Bilayer Nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17181)
*Xianxin Wu,Tao Xiang,Jiangping Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究将"基因原理"和"协同费米面规则"应用于双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇超导体，揭示其s±波超导配对机制源于层间和层内两种反铁磁交换通道的协同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇在约80K温度下表现出超导性，为检验非常规高温超导的组织原理提供了新平台。研究旨在验证先前提出的"基因原理（gene principle）"和"协同费米面规则（collaborative Fermi-surface rule）"是否能统一解释这一多轨道双层系统的超导机制。

Method: 研究将统一框架扩展到双层多轨道系统，识别出两种主导配对力的反铁磁交换通道：层间轨道内最近邻交换J⊥（通过内顶端氧介导的dz²轨道间交换）和层内轨道间最近邻交换Jxz（通过面内氧介导的dz²与dx²-y²轨道间交换）。

Result: 两种交换通道协同产生稳健的s±超导态，在动量空间中镜像偶数和镜像奇数费米面口袋间存在内部符号反转。两个配对通道都在β口袋上最大化超导能隙，其动量空间形式因子为(coskx-cosky)²。

Conclusion: La₃Ni₂O₇被纳入非常规超导的统一框架，同时揭示了高Tc配对机制的独特电子环境。双层键合-反键合劈裂和dx²-y²轨道的B1g对称性使得两种交换通道能够协同作用。

Abstract: The recent discovery of superconductivity with $T_c \approx 80$~K in bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ provides a new setting in which to test the organizing principles of unconventional high-temperature superconductivity. We show that the gene principle and the collaborative Fermi-surface rule which were previously proposed to unify unconventional high temperature superconductors, extend naturally to this bilayer, multi-orbital system. We identify that there are two antiferromagnetic exchange channels that can provide the dominant pairing force: an interlayer intra-orbital nearest-neighbour exchange $J_\perp$ between $d_{z^2}$ orbitals mediated by the inner apical oxygen, and an intralayer inter-orbital nearest-neighbour exchange $J_{xz}$ between $d_{z^2}$ and $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbitals mediated by the in-plane oxygen. Owing to the bilayer bonding--antibonding splitting and the $B_{1g}$ symmetry of the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital, these two channels cooperate to produce a robust $s^\pm$ superconducting state with an internal sign reversal between mirror-even and mirror-odd Fermi-surface pockets in momentum space. Both pairing channels maximize the superconducting gap on the $β$ pocket with a form factor $(cosk_x-cosk_y)^2$ in momentum space. The result places La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ within a unified framework for unconventional superconductivity while revealing a distinct electronic environment for high-$T_c$ pairing.

</details>


### [93] [Collective Resonance of Superconducting/Normal Domain Walls in the Intermediate State of type-I superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17333)
*Mengju Yuan,Yugang Zhang,Ying Zhu,Jingchun Gao,Aifeng Wang,Mingquan He,Jun-Yi Ge,Yisheng Chai*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究利用交流磁致伸缩技术揭示了铅中间态中S/N界面（超导/正常界面）的集体振荡行为，发现了与德拜弛豫不同的准共振响应特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁测量方法因受表面势垒和过阻尼磁通过程主导，难以观测I类超导体中相边界（如超导/正常界面）的动力学行为，需要开发新的探测手段来揭示这些畴壁的体动力学特性。

Method: 采用交流磁致伸缩（ac magnetostriction）作为灵敏探针，研究铅中间态中S/N界面的体动力学行为，通过分析频率相关的响应特征来揭示界面运动机制。

Result: 发现了明显的准共振响应特征：虚部出现符号反转，实部随频率呈现非单调演化，这与磁化率中观察到的德拜型弛豫形成鲜明对比。该行为归因于正常畴内涡流驱动的S/N界面集体振荡。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了超导调制相中的基本动力学通道，并确立了交流磁致伸缩系数作为探测隐藏界面物理的有力工具，为研究相边界动力学提供了新方法。

Abstract: The dynamics of phase boundaries, such as superconducting/normal (S/N) interfaces in type-I superconductors, are typically obscured in conventional magnetic measurements, which are dominated by surface barriers and over-damped flux processes. Here, we employ ac magnetostriction as a sensitive probe to reveal the distinct bulk dynamics of these domain walls in the intermediate state of lead. In contrast to the Debye-type relaxation observed in magnetic susceptibility, we discover a pronounced quasiresonant response characterized by a sign reversal of the imaginary component and a non-monotonic evolution of the real part with frequency. We attribute this behavior to the collective oscillations of S/N interfaces driven by eddy currents generated within the normal domains. This work uncovers a fundamental dynamical channel in superconducting modulated phases and establishes ac magnetostrictive coefficient as a powerful tool for probing hidden interface physics.

</details>


### [94] [Anisotropic Superconducting Diode Effect in Planar Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17594)
*Abhishek Chilampankunnel Prasannan,Baris Pekerten,Nowar Alashkar,Alex Matos-Abiague*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该理论研究平面约瑟夫森结中具有共存Rashba和Dresselhaus自旋轨道耦合的超导二极管效应（SDE）的磁性和晶体各向异性。通过对称性分析、唯象模型和紧束缚模拟，揭示了SDE对磁场和晶体取向的依赖性，以及静电门控可诱导SDE极性反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解平面约瑟夫森结（planar Josephson junctions）中自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）与塞曼相互作用（Zeeman interaction）共同作用下超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect）的各向异性特性，为实验探测半导体基平面约瑟夫森结中的SDE机制提供理论指导。

Method: 采用对称性分析识别SDE抑制的几何约束条件，建立唯象模型描述二极管效率与自旋轨道场和磁场相对取向的关系，在窄结低场区域使用解析方法，并通过Bogoliubov-de Gennes方程的紧束缚模拟（tight-binding simulations）验证理论结果。

Result: 对称性分析确定了磁场和晶体取向的几何约束条件，在这些条件下SDE独立于磁场强度而被抑制。模拟显示静电门控（electrostatic gating）可在低场区域诱导SDE极性反转，即使仅存在Rashba SOC，并预测了特定场取向、结几何和SOC比例下的额外反转。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了各向异性非互易超导输运的起源，为实验探测半导体基平面约瑟夫森结中SDE的潜在机制提供了指导。结果与最近的实验趋势一致，揭示了SOC诱导的费米面畸变和各向异性库珀对动量（Cooper pair momentum）对二极管响应的贡献。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the magnetic and crystalline anisotropies of the superconducting diode effect (SDE) in proximitized planar Josephson junctions (JJs) with coexisting Rashba and Dresselhaus spin-orbit couplings (SOCs) under an in-plane magnetic field. A symmetry analysis identifies geometric constraints on magnetic-field and crystallographic orientations for which the SDE is suppressed independently of field strength, providing experimentally testable signatures of the interplay between SOC and Zeeman interaction. We develop a phenomenological model showing that the diode efficiency depends on the relative alignment between spin-orbit and magnetic fields, and corroborate this behavior in the narrow-junction, low-field regime using an analytical approach that links the anisotropy of the diode response to SOC-induced Fermi surface distortions and anisotropic Cooper pair momentum. These findings are supported by tight-binding simulations of the Bogoliubov-de Gennes equation, which reproduce recent experimental trends. The simulations reveal that electrostatic gating can induce polarity reversals of the SDE in the low-field regime even with only Rashba SOC, consistent with recent experiments, and predict additional reversals for specific field orientations, junction geometries, and SOC ratios. Our results elucidate the origin of anisotropic nonreciprocal superconducting transport and provide guidance for experimentally probing the mechanisms underlying the SDE in semiconductor-based planar JJs.

</details>


### [95] [Metal Atom (Dis)Order and Superconductivity in YCaH$_{n}$ ($n=8-20$) High-Pressure Superhydrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17712)
*Masashi W. Kimura,Seong Won Jang,Nisha Geng,Eva Zurek*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论计算，探索了Y-Ca超氢化物（YCaH₈₋₂₀）的结构与性质，发现金属原子无序排列对稳定性有重要影响，且掺杂可显著调控超导临界温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压超氢化物因其高超导临界温度（T_c）而备受关注，本研究旨在通过理论计算探索Y-Ca超氢化物的结构、性质以及金属原子无序和掺杂对T_c的增强效应。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，研究YCaH₈₋₂₀系列化合物的结构与性质，包括金属原子无序排列的潜在可能性，并利用各向同性Eliashberg形式主义评估超导临界温度。

Result: 研究发现YCaH₈存在多种金属原子排列近等焓的相，表明构型熵对稳定性至关重要；等摩尔金属比例使费米能级处于态密度峰值，在180 GPa下P4/mmm和Cmmm相的T_c分别达到149 K和170 K。YCaH₁₂的有序变体T_c范围广泛（105-253 K），显示掺杂可轻微增强或显著降低T_c。YCaH₁₈和YCaH₂₀仅预测到单一动态稳定超氢化物。

Conclusion: 金属原子无序排列在Y-Ca超氢化物的稳定性中起关键作用，通过金属原子掺杂可有效调控费米能级位置和态密度，从而显著增强超导临界温度，但掺杂效果取决于具体化合物结构。

Abstract: High-pressure superhydrides have attracted much attention due to their high superconducting critical temperatures ($T_\text{c}$s). Herein, density functional theory (DFT) calculations are used to study the structures and properties, including potential for metal atom disorder and doping-enhanced $T_\text{c}$, within Y-Ca superhydrides with YCaH$_{n}$ ($n=8-20$) compositions. For YCaH$_8$ numerous phases that differed in the arrangement of the metal atoms were found to be nearly isoenthalpic, suggesting the importance of configurational entropy on stability. The equimolar ratio of the two metal atoms brought the Fermi level to a peak in the density of states, enhancing $T_\text{c}$ to 149~K and 170~K for $P4/mmm$ and $Cmmm$ YCaH$_{8}$, respectively, at 180~GPa within the isotropic Eliashberg formalism. YCaH$_{12}$ was also predicted to be disordered, however the $T_\text{c}$s of the ordered variants spanned a wide range from 105-253~K at 200~GPa, showing that doping could either mildly enhance or drastically reduce $T_\text{c}$ from that of the parent compounds. For YCaH$_{18}$ and YCaH$_{20}$, only a single dynamically stable superhydride was predicted, which we attribute to the differences in the structures of the stable binary parents.

</details>


### [96] [Pairing properties of correlated three-leg ladders with strong interchain couplings near 1/3 filling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17812)
*Yushi Yamada,Tatsuya Kaneko,Masataka Kakoi,Ryota Ueda,Kazuhiko Kuroki*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了1/3填充附近关联三腿梯子（three-leg ladder）的基态性质，发现空穴掺杂能产生幂律衰减的配对关联，而电子掺杂则不会产生显著的配对关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解三腿梯子体系在1/3填充附近的电子性质，特别是配对性质，这为理解三层镍酸盐超导体（trilayer nickelate superconductors）的电子特性提供理论见解。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法研究具有强链间耦合的三腿t-J梯子模型，并与三腿哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）的空穴掺杂态进行比较。

Result: 当空穴掺杂到1/3填充的自旋能隙态时，配对关联呈现幂律衰减，而自旋关联呈指数衰减；相反，电子掺杂到1/3填充态不会产生显著的配对关联。

Conclusion: 数值计算结果表明三腿梯子体系在空穴掺杂下能形成配对态，这为理解三层镍酸盐超导体的电子性质提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state properties of correlated three-leg ladders near 1/3 filling. We apply the density-matrix renormalization group method to the three-leg t-J ladder with strong interchain couplings and evaluate its pairing nature. When holes are doped into the spin-gapped state at 1/3 filling, we find that pair correlations develop with power-law decays while spin correlations decay exponentially. On the other hand, doping of electrons into the 1/3-filled state does not give rise to substantial pair correlations. We also discuss the hole-doped state in the three-leg Hubbard model to compare it with the pairing state in the t-J model. Our numerical demonstrations provide insights into the electronic properties of trilayer nickelate superconductors.

### [97] [$0-π$ transitions in non-Hermitian magnetic Josephson junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17978)
*Roberto Capecelatro,Marco Marciani,Claudio Guarcello,Gabriele Campagnano,Procolo Lucignano,Roberta Citro*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非厄米磁性约瑟夫森结的输运特性，发现耗散效应会将0-π相变推向更高磁场，且外加磁场与库磁化方向的相对角度也可驱动相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解非厄米磁性约瑟夫森结（non-Hermitian magnetic Josephson junctions）的输运特性，特别是环境耦合如何影响0-π相变（0-π transitions）这一关键物理现象。

Method: 采用格林函数计算（Green's function calculations）结合限制在亚能隙安德列夫准束缚态（sub-gap Andreev quasi-bound states）的有效非厄米描述，研究超导体-量子点-超导体器件耦合到铁磁金属库的系统。

Result: 耗散效应使0-π相变向更高磁场偏移；固定磁场强度下，外加磁场与库磁化（reservoir magnetization）的相对角度也可驱动相变；这些效应完全归因于非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）复本征值的行为。

Conclusion: 非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）可作为工程化超导结电流-相位关系的新控制手段，为调控约瑟夫森结特性提供了额外自由度。

Abstract: We study the transport properties of non-Hermitian magnetic Josephson junctions, considering a superconductor-quantum dot-superconductor device coupled to a ferromagnetic metallic reservoir in the presence of an external magnetic field. We focus on the $0-π$ transitions that occur when the equilibrium phase difference between the superconductors shifts from $φ=0$ to $φ=π$ upon increasing the magnetic field amplitude. The coupling to the environment induces spin-dependent dissipation and leads to the broadening of the junction Andreev levels. By combining Green's function calculations with an effective non-Hermitian description restricted to the sub-gap Andreev quasi-bound states, we show that dissipation shifts the $0-π$ transition to higher magnetic fields. Remarkably, also the relative angle between the applied field and the reservoir magnetization can be used to drive the transition, at fixed field magnitude. We demonstrate that this effect can be entirely ascribed to the behavior of the complex eigenvalues of the non-Hermitian Hamiltonian. These findings highlight non-Hermiticity as a resource that can introduce new control knobs for engineering the current-phase relation in superconducting junctions.
