### [98] [Superconductivity in Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates: a review of recent progress, focusing on thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18385)
*Yang Zhang,Ling-Fang Lin,Thomas A. Maier,Elbio Dagotto*

Method: 本文采用综述方法，回顾Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐的实验和理论进展，特别关注超薄膜（thin films）研究，并讨论不同镍氧化物之间的异同。

Result: 双层La₃Ni₂O₇在高压下发现Tc~80 K的超导性，随后在高压下的三层La₄Ni₃O₁₀中也观察到超导现象。更重要的是，在提供压缩应变（compressive strain）的衬底上生长的La₃Ni₂O₇超薄膜中实现了常压超导。

Conclusion: 通过比较不同镍氧化物的异同，可为理解强关联电子系统中的高温超导机制提供新见解。本文旨在总结Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐的研究进展，并讨论未来展望和研究方向。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity with Tc ~ 80 K in the nickelate Ruddlesden-Popper bilayer La3Ni2O7 at high pressure has opened a new platform for unconventional superconductivity, followed by the subsequent observation of superconductivity in trilayer La4Ni3O10, also at high pressure. Remarkably, ambient-pressure superconductivity was also observed recently in La3Ni2O7 ultra-thin films when grown on substrates that provide compressive strain. This discovery significantly extends the type of experimental techniques that can be used in nickelates, previously limited due to the high-pressure constraint. Discussing the similarities and differences among these nickel oxides will provide new insights into understanding the mechanism of high-Tc superconductivity in correlated electron systems. In this paper, we review the experimental and theoretical progress on RuddlesdenPopper nickelates, with emphasis on thin films, and discuss future perspectives and research directions.

### [99] [Comment on "Extension of the adiabatic theorem"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16439)
*Jie Gu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一个关于量子淬火（quantum quench）的猜想不成立，即使淬火前后哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）在同一相（phase）内且通过对称性保持的能隙路径（symmetry-preserving gapped path）连接，也存在局部、平移不变、有能隙的自由费米子（free-fermion）反例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对Phys. Rev. B 113, 165102 (2026)提出的猜想——对于同一相内的量子淬火，初态基态（initial ground state）与淬火后本征态（postquench eigenstates）的重叠（overlap）在淬火后基态处最大，本文旨在检验该猜想的普适性。

Method: 通过构造一个显式的局部、平移不变、有能隙的自由费米子模型作为反例，证明该猜想在一般情况下不成立。该反例满足淬火前后哈密顿量通过对称性保持的能隙路径连接，且热力学极限（thermodynamic-limit）下的谱是连续的。

Result: 成功构造了反例，证明原猜想并非普遍有效。即使满足所有前提条件（同一相内淬火、对称性保持、能隙路径连接、连续谱），淬火后基态与初态基态的重叠也可能不是最大的。

Conclusion: 该工作推翻了先前关于量子淬火中初态-末态重叠最大化的猜想，表明即使在同一相内进行对称性保持的淬火，淬火后基态也不一定具有最大的初态重叠，这对理解量子淬火动力学有重要意义。

Abstract: Phys. Rev. B 113, 165102 (2026) proposed the conjecture that, for quantum quenches within the same phase, the overlap between the initial ground state and postquench eigenstates is maximal for the postquench ground state. We show that this conjecture is not valid in general. An explicit local, translationally invariant, gapped free-fermion counterexample exists even though the pre- and postquench Hamiltonians are connected by a symmetry-preserving gapped path and the thermodynamic-limit spectrum is continuous.

</details>


### [100] [Thermodynamic Curvature and the Widom Ridge in Interacting Spin Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16707)
*Eric R. Bittner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过定义在控制流形上的曲率场，为经典伊辛模型（Ising model）的热力学响应提供了几何表述。研究发现曲率场在临界点附近形成显著的山脊结构，将威德姆线（Widom line）识别为控制空间的几何特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立热力学响应的几何表述，探索控制变量选择对曲率存在性的影响，并揭示几何热力学与临界现象之间的直接联系。

Method: 通过定义在控制流形（由逆温度β和磁场h张成）上的曲率场，采用自由能的混合导数表达曲率，并使用蒙特卡洛采样（Monte Carlo sampling）评估曲率场。

Result: 研究发现(J,h)流形在固定温度下是可积的且曲率为零，而(β,h)流形支持由统计系综变化引起的有限曲率场。曲率场从临界点延伸到超临界区域形成显著的山脊结构，将威德姆线识别为控制空间中热力学响应最大的几何轨迹。

Conclusion: 该几何表述建立了几何热力学、临界现象与实验可观测量的直接联系，并表明热力学曲率可以通过循环驱动协议下所做的功测量来探测。

Abstract: We develop a geometric formulation of thermodynamic response in the classical Ising model by defining a curvature field over the control manifold spanned by inverse temperature $β$ and magnetic field $h$. We show that the existence of nontrivial curvature depends sensitively on the choice of control variables: while the $(J,h)$ manifold at fixed temperature is integrable and exhibits zero curvature, the $(β,h)$ manifold supports a finite curvature field arising from variations of the statistical ensemble. This curvature is given by a mixed derivative of the free energy and can be expressed directly as the covariance between energy and magnetization fluctuations. We evaluate the curvature field using Monte Carlo sampling and demonstrate that it develops a pronounced ridge structure extending from the critical point into the supercritical regime. This identifies the Widom line as a geometric feature of control space, corresponding to a locus of maximal thermodynamic response. More generally, the formulation provides a direct connection between geometric thermodynamics, critical phenomena, and experimentally accessible observables, and suggests that thermodynamic curvature may be probed through measurements of work performed under cyclic driving protocols.

</details>


### [101] [Quantum many-body operator cascade as a route to chaos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16720)
*Urban Duh,Marko Žnidarič*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了量子多体混沌（quantum many-body chaos）中算符演化的分形特性，建立了时间衰减率与空间分形维度之间的约束关系，提出了算符空间中的多体Kolmogorov级联（many-body Kolmogorov cascade）图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典混沌系统的动力学特性可通过初始平滑长波密度向分形短波密度的演化来理解，但量子多体混沌是否存在类似的分形特征尚不清楚。本研究旨在探索量子多体混沌中是否存在可表征的分形结构。

Method: 通过研究截断算符传播子（truncated operator propagator）的谱性质，分析其最慢衰减算符（leading Ruelle-Pollicott eigenvectors）的分形维度。研究在多种量子电路中验证预测：受击伊辛模型（kicked Ising model）、随机双量子比特门的砖墙电路（brickwall circuits）以及双幺正电路（dual-unitary circuits）。

Result: 研究发现最慢衰减算符具有非平凡分形维度（nontrivial fractal dimension），量化了其非局域性，并体现在其条件数的发散中。幺正性（unitarity）对局域关联的时间衰减率与算符空间分形维度施加了约束关系（近似等式）。

Conclusion: 量子多体混沌表现为局域算符随时间演化为具有可量化分形结构的非局域算符，在局域算符子空间上自然导致有效非幺正弛豫，形成了算符空间中的多体Kolmogorov级联图像。该框架为理解量子多体混沌提供了新的结构视角。

Abstract: Dynamical properties of classical chaotic systems, for instance relaxation, can be understood as emerging from the time evolution of initially smooth long-wavelength densities to ever finer short-wavelength densities with fractal structure. Whether there is any analogous fractality by which one could characterize quantum many-body chaos is not known. By studying the spectral properties of the truncated operator propagator, we provide such structures. Namely, we show that the slowest-decaying operators, i.e., the leading Ruelle-Pollicott eigenvectors, have a nontrivial fractal dimension quantifying their non-locality, visible also in the divergence of their condition numbers. Furthermore, we find that unitarity imposes a constraint, i.e., an (approximate) equality, between the temporal decay rate of local correlations and this spatial operator fractal dimension. With this insight, a scenario for many-body quantum chaos becomes clear: over time, local operators evolve towards increasingly non-local ones with a quantifiable fractal structure, thereby naturally leading to effective non-unitary relaxation on the subspace of local operators - a kind of many-body Kolmogorov cascade in the space of operators. Our predictions are demonstrated in various quantum circuits: the kicked Ising model, brickwall circuits with a random 2-qubit gate, and dual-unitary circuits, where our results are exact.

*De-Zhang Li,Xin Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Brascamp-Kunz边界条件下的正方晶格Ising模型是著名的精确可解晶格模型，但其精确解主要通过Pfaffian型方法推导。本文旨在通过转移矩阵形式下的Schultz-Mattis-Lieb方法提供另一种推导途径。

Method: 通过在边界设置特殊相互作用并取特定极限，将Brascamp-Kunz边界条件下的系统转化为环面边界条件下的系统。随后应用Schultz-Mattis-Lieb方法于映射后的系统，在费米子表示中精确求解配分函数。

Result: 解析计算了Fisher零点并确定了物理临界点。同时讨论了Brascamp-Kunz边界条件与环面边界条件下转移矩阵方法的差异，为不同边界条件下Ising模型的转移矩阵研究家族增添了新成员。

Conclusion: 本文成功通过Schultz-Mattis-Lieb方法在转移矩阵框架下推导了Brascamp-Kunz边界条件下Ising模型的精确解，扩展了该模型在不同边界条件下的研究方法体系。

Abstract: The square lattice Ising model under the Brascamp-Kunz boundary conditions is a well-known exactly solvable lattice model. The exact solution of this system has been derived within the framework of Pfaffian-type method. In this paper we provide a derivation for the solution by the Schultz-Mattis-Lieb method in the transfer matrix formalism. We set special interactions on the boundaries and take certain limit of these interactions, so that the system under the Brascamp-Kunz boundary conditions is transformed into another system under the toroidal boundary conditions. The Schultz-Mattis-Lieb method is applied to the mapping system and the partition function is exactly solved in the fermionic representation. The Fisher zeros are analytically calculated and the physical critical point is identified. We also discuss the difference between the transfer matrix approaches to the Brascamp-Kunz and to the toroidal boundary conditions. Our work introduces a member to the family of transfer-matrix-based studies for Ising model under various boundary conditions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超统计（superstatistics）作为描述非平衡稳态系统（如无碰撞等离子体、自引力系统等）的统计力学框架，其温度参数β的分布无法归因于相空间函数的涨落，且缺乏直接可观测性，这构成了需要解决的概念问题。

Method: 研究建立了超统计温度函数与基本温度（fundamental temperature）函数之间的映射关系，其中基本温度是依赖于能量的模型相关函数。该方法避免了拉普拉斯反演（Laplace inversion）的使用。

Result: 通过该映射关系，计算了q-正则系综（q-canonical ensemble）中给定能量条件下的逆温度条件分布，以及完整的逆温度分布。结果表明超统计温度函数与基本温度函数的期望值能够保持一致。

Conclusion: 该映射关系为解决超统计温度缺乏直接可观测性的概念问题提供了途径，建立了超统计温度与基本温度之间的理论联系，为超统计框架的应用提供了更坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Among the statistical mechanical frameworks able to describe systems in non-equilibrium steady states such as collisionless plasmas, self-gravitating systems and other complex systems, superstatistics have gained recent attention. Superstatistics postulates a superposition of canonical systems with inverse temperatures $β$ described by a probability distribution depending on the external conditions. Unfortunately, the uncertainty about $β$ cannot be attributed to fluctuations of a phase space function, and this suggests that the distribution of $β$ is purely of statistical nature and must be inferred rather than measured. This lack of direct observability of the superstatistical temperature then becomes a conceptual issue in need of resolution. In this work we address this issue, showing that a mapping exists between functions of the superstatistical temperature and functions of the recently proposed fundamental temperature, a model-dependent function of the energy, in such a way that their expectation values coincide. We illustrate the use of this mapping by computing the conditional distribution of inverse temperature given energy for the $q$-canonical ensemble, as well as the full inverse temperature distribution, without the use of Laplace inversion.

### [104] [Activation and Avalanche Length Scales in the Finite-Temperature Creep of an Elastic Interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17600)
*Giovanni Russo,Ezequiel E. Ferrero,Alejandro B. Kolton,Alberto Rosso,Damien Vandembroucq*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了有限温度下受驱弹性线蠕变动力学的双尺度机制：最优激活重排尺度ℓ_opt控制时间尺度，而热激活雪崩尺度ℓ_av控制空间关联，后者随温度降低而增长并遵循ℓ_av(T)∼T^{-ν_dep}标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解远低于脱钉（depinning）阈值的有限温度下受驱弹性线的蠕变（creep）动力学机制，特别是探索控制蠕变过程的不同长度尺度及其物理意义。

Method: 通过结合结构性和动力学可观测量，分析弹性线在有限温度下的蠕变行为，重点关注两个关键长度尺度：控制动力学瓶颈的最优激活重排尺度ℓ_opt和表征热激活雪崩空间范围的尺度ℓ_av。

Result: 研究发现ℓ_opt基本与温度无关，而ℓ_av随温度降低而增长，遵循ℓ_av(T)∼T^{-ν_dep}的标度关系；ℓ_av控制结构因子（structure factor）的交叉和四点动力学磁化率（four-point dynamical susceptibility）的增长，而弛豫时间仍由与ℓ_opt相关的大势垒激活过程控制。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了有限温度蠕变的统一图像：激活过程控制时间尺度，而脱钉临界性（depinning criticality）主导空间关联，雪崩尺度ℓ_av的标度行为在竞争的理论预测中选择了特定方案。

Abstract: We investigate the creep dynamics of a driven elastic line at finite temperature, well below the depinning threshold. We show that creep is governed by two distinct length scales. The first, $\ell_{\mathrm{opt}}$, corresponds to the optimal activated rearrangements that control the dynamics' bottleneck and remains essentially temperature-independent. The second, $\ell_{\mathrm{av}}$, characterizes the spatial extent of thermally activated avalanches and grows as temperature decreases. By combining structural and dynamical observables, we show that $\ell_{\mathrm{av}}$ governs both the crossover in the structure factor and the growth of the four-point dynamical susceptibility, while the relaxation time remains controlled by activation over large barriers associated with $\ell_{\mathrm{opt}}$. We find that the avalanche scale follows $\ell_{\mathrm{av}}(T)\sim T^{-ν_{\mathrm{dep}}}$, thereby selecting a unique scenario among competing theoretical predictions. These results establish a unified picture of finite-temperature creep in which activation controls temporal scales while depinning criticality governs spatial correlations.

### [105] [Self-averaging parameter estimation for coarse-grained particle models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18068)
*Carlos Monago,J. A. de la Torre,Pep Español*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用微观数据（特定微观可观测量（observables）的平均值和相关性）来估计粗粒度自由度（coarse-grained degrees of freedom）随机微分方程参数的方法，适用于静态和动态参数，并通过两个示例验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有参数估计方法通常局限于粗粒度动力学可逆部分中的静态参数，如自由能函数或平均力势（potential of mean force），而难以有效估计摩擦系数等动态参数。需要一种能够同时利用微观数据估计静态和动态参数的方法。

Method: 该方法将带有自由参数的随机微分方程与参数本身的动力学方程耦合。根据Anosov-Kifer定理，耦合系统能够自平均（self-averages），使得参数的最终状态能够确保所选微观和介观可观测量（observables）的平均值与相关性一致。

Result: 方法在两个示例中得到验证：谐波势中的布朗粒子（Brownian particle）和具有Rotne-Prager-Yamakawa迁移率张量（mobility tensor）相互作用的布朗粒子体系。后者展示了该方法不仅能确定系数，还能确定状态相关的输运性质（transport properties）——即迁移率张量的位置依赖形式。参数估计结果优异。

Conclusion: 该方法成功应用于研究双峰质量Lennard-Jones流体（bimodal-mass Lennard-Jones fluid），推断出重粒子间的平均力势及其流体动力学迁移率张量，证明了其在复杂体系参数估计中的适用性。

Abstract: We introduce a parameter estimation method that utilizes microscopic data, specifically averages and correlations of selected microscopic observables, to determine the parameters of a stochastic differential equation governing coarse-grained degrees of freedom. The method is not limited to static parameters found in the reversible part of the coarse-grained dynamics, such as those in the free energy function or potential of mean force, but also extends to dynamic parameters, including friction coefficients. The method couples the stochastic differential equation with free parameters to dynamic equations for the parameters. The coupled system self-averages, according to Anosov-Kifer's theorem, in such a way that the final state of the parameters gives coincidence between the microscopic and mesoscopic averages and correlations of selected observables. The method is validated in two examples: a Brownian particle in a harmonic potential, and a set of Brownian particles interacting hydrodynamically with the Rotne-Prager-Yamakawa mobility tensor. This latter case illustrates how the method can be used not only to determine coefficients but also state dependent transport properties - in this case, the position dependent form of the mobility tensor. The parameter estimation for these two models yields excellent results. Subsequently we use the methodology to study a bimodal-mass Lennard-Jones fluid for which we infer both the potential of mean force between the heavy particles and its hydrodynamic mobility tensor.

### [106] [Stability and breakdown of chiral motion in non-reciprocal flocking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18125)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明全局相干手性运动并非有限范围非互易集群运动的普适大尺度状态，因此本研究旨在探究在离散时间、度量、非互易的两物种Vicsek模型中，手性状态是否能够稳定存在及其所需条件。

Method: 采用具有种内对齐和不对称种间耦合的两物种Vicsek模型，其中一个物种与另一物种对齐，而后者则反对齐。研究通过调节种群平衡和运动性不平衡等参数来探索手性状态的形成条件。

Result: 在种群数量和运动性相等的情况下，手性状态仅存在于高密度、极低自推进速度以及系统尺寸相对于相互作用范围较小的受限窗口内。手性主要出现在对齐相互作用主导反对齐时，而更强的反对齐会导致物种分离并抑制手性。种群不平衡驱动从手性状态向多孔平行集群或反平行集群液体转变；运动性不平衡则引发异步振荡，极端情况下导致快速物种形成移动团簇而慢速粒子形成弥散背景。

Abstract: We study a two-species Vicsek model with intra-species alignment and asymmetric inter-species couplings, where one species aligns with the other while the latter anti-aligns. Motivated by recent results showing that globally coherent chiral motion is not a generic large-scale state of finite-range non-reciprocal flocking, we ask whether a chiral state can nevertheless be stabilized in the discrete-time, metric, non-reciprocal two-species Vicsek model, and if so, under what conditions. For equal populations and motilities, we show that such a state exists only within a restricted window characterized by high density, very low self-propulsion speed, and small system size relative to the interaction range. Within this window, we also find that chirality appears primarily when aligning interactions dominate over anti-alignment, whereas stronger anti-alignment leads to species segregation and suppresses chirality. Conversely, introducing species asymmetry through population imbalance drives transitions from chiral states to porous parallel-flocking or anti-parallel-flocking liquids; motility imbalance induces asynchronous oscillations and, in extreme cases, leads to segregation into moving clusters of the faster species within a more dispersed background of slower particles. Overall, these results indicate that chirality in the non-reciprocal two-species Vicsek model arises within a restricted regime set by density, motility, inter-species coupling, and system size, rather than being a generic outcome of non-reciprocal interactions.

Abstract: We determine the fully resolved equilibrium density profiles for two binary hard-sphere crystal structures using classical density functional theory through the White Bear II functional from fundamental measure theory. While for the substitutional crystal, in which some hard spheres are replaced by spheres of slightly smaller diameter, the density profiles are rather similar to the single-component case (narrow Gaussian peaks centered at fcc lattice sites), we observe a more complex behavior for the case of interstitial solid solutions, where the small species is fairly delocalized in the unit cell. Further, we compute the species-resolved inhomogeneous two-body direct correlation functions for these two types of binary crystals. The large-large components are mainly determined by the vacancy concentration $n_\text{vac}$ and show a characteristic magnitude $~1/n_\text{vac}$. Based on this observation, we propose a simple geometric picture of this six-dimensional function. The components of the direct correlation function involving the small spheres substantially differ in interstitial solid solutions from those of the substitutional crystal.

Method: 采用解析分析方法，首先研究具有幂律核函数表征的粘弹性记忆效应的活性粒子动力学行为，然后分析在均匀涡旋力、热噪声和粘性耗散（同样具有幂律核函数）作用下的粒子动力学，最后通过引入谐波约束力获得联合概率密度的解析解。

Result: 研究获得了两个不同时间区域（two distinct time regimes）的联合概率密度的解析解，为理解超流氦表面量子涡旋驱动的活性粒子扩散运动提供了理论框架。

Conclusion: 该研究通过解析方法成功描述了超流氦表面量子涡旋驱动的活性粒子在粘弹性记忆效应、均匀涡旋力、热噪声和粘性耗散共同作用下的扩散动力学，为相关实验观测提供了理论解释基础。

Abstract: We analytically investigate the diffusive motion inferred from experimental observations of active particles driven by quantum vortices on the surface of superfluid helium. We first study the dynamical behavior of an active particle subject to a viscoelastic memory effect characterized by a power-law kernel. We then analyze the dynamics of an active particle under a uniform vortex force, thermal noise, and viscous dissipation subject to a power-law kernel. Next, by including a harmonic confining force, we obtain analytical solutions for the joint probability density in two distinct time regimes.

</details>


### [109] [Emergent nonreciprocity in open thermodynamically-consistent chemical reaction networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18528)
*Daniel Evans,Yizhi Shen,Ahmad K. Omar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了化学恒化器（chemostat）诱导的昂萨格互易性（Onsager reciprocity）破缺如何在热力学一致的反应网络中产生振荡不稳定性，这些振荡仍能最小化自由能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解非互易性（nonreciprocity）这一非平衡系统特征如何通过化学恒化器诱导的昂萨格互易性破缺，在热力学一致的反应网络中产生振荡动力学。

Method: 通过分析开放、热力学一致的化学反应网络拓扑结构，研究局部平衡假设如何保持动力学耗散部分的变分结构，同时化学恒化器导致昂萨格互易性破缺。

Result: 数值结果证实，反应-扩散系统中的这种非互易性能够产生振荡动力学，但这些振荡仍能最小化自由能，揭示了拓扑结构在非平衡稳态附近产生振荡不稳定性的机制。

Conclusion: 化学反应网络的拓扑结构可在非平衡稳态附近引发振荡不稳定性，这种不稳定性源于化学恒化器诱导的昂萨格互易性破缺，同时局部平衡假设保持了耗散动力学的变分结构。

Abstract: Nonreciprocity, a hallmark of nonequilibrium systems, can generate dynamics not possible near thermodynamic equilibrium, including oscillatory and rotating patterns. The onset of temporal oscillations is often evident in linearized dynamics, where nonreciprocity appears as complex eigenvalues of an asymmetric Jacobian. Here, we show that the topology of open, thermodynamically-consistent chemical reaction networks can result in oscillatory instabilities near nonequilibrium steady states. These instabilities arise from chemostat-induced breaking of Onsager reciprocity, while the local equilibrium hypothesis preserves the variational structure of the dissipative part of the dynamics. Numerical results confirm that such nonreciprocity in reaction-diffusion systems produces oscillatory dynamics that nevertheless minimize a free energy.

### [110] [A First Investigation of Repeated-Signal Localization of Strongly Lensed Gravitational Waves for Multimessenger Astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16561)
*Alvin K. Y. Li,Otto A. Hannuksela*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了如何通过结合引力波（GW）强透镜事件的多重图像来改善天空定位精度，发现结合两个图像可使90%置信区域面积减少一个数量级，四图像系统能达到约10-100平方度的定位精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确的天空定位对于引力波天文学至关重要，特别是在多信使后续观测和宿主星系识别方面。对于强透镜引力波事件，达到约10平方度的定位精度对于将信号与透镜结构关联以及进行针对性搜索微弱图像至关重要。

Method: 研究使用模拟的透镜致密双星并合事件和BAYESTAR天空定位方法，评估了定位性能随图像多重性（image multiplicity）的变化。通过结合同一源的多重透镜图像来分析定位改进情况。

Result: 结合多重图像能系统性地改善定位精度，最大改进出现在结合两个图像时，通常使90%置信区域（credible region）面积减少一个数量级。四图像系统能达到约10-100平方度的定位面积。亚阈值图像（subthreshold images）也能提供适度且不降低精度的改进。

Conclusion: 强透镜引力波事件为改善定位精度提供了自然途径，并激励了用于检测微弱透镜图像的分层搜索策略（hierarchical search strategies）。这些发现支持在定位分析中安全地包含亚阈值图像。

Abstract: Accurate sky localization is essential for gravitational-wave (GW) astronomy, particularly for multimessenger follow-up and host galaxy identification. For strongly lensed GW events, achieving localization at the level of $\sim 10~\mathrm{deg}^2$ is critical for associating signals with their lensing structures and enabling targeted searches for additional faint images. We investigate how sky localization improves when combining multiple lensed images of the same source. Using simulated lensed compact binary coalescences and \textsc{BAYESTAR} sky localization, we evaluate localization performance as a function of image multiplicity. We find that combining multiple images leads to a systematic improvement in localization, with the largest gain occurring when combining two images, typically reducing the 90\% credible region area by an order of magnitude. Additional images provide further improvements, with four-image systems achieving localization areas of $\sim 10$--$100~\mathrm{deg}^2$. We also show that subthreshold images contribute modest but non-degrading improvements, enabling their safe inclusion in localization analyses. These results demonstrate that strongly lensed GW events provide a natural pathway to improved localization and motivate hierarchical search strategies for detecting faint lensed images.

### [111] [Clock Noise Cancellation in Heterodyne Links between Optical Cavities for Space-Borne Gravitational-Wave Telescopes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17766)
*Yutaro Enomoto,Subaru Shibai,Kiwamu Izumi*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对空间引力波望远镜中时钟抖动噪声的消除方案，通过利用臂腔入射和出射激光束产生的正负拍频信号进行加权组合，在不增加额外时钟调制的情况下实现时钟噪声消除，并保持引力波信号完整性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间引力波望远镜需要达到10⁻²²/√Hz的灵敏度水平，但外差干涉测量法（heterodyne interferometry）虽然能放宽臂长控制要求，却引入了对时钟抖动（clock jitter）的敏感性。在瞄准分赫兹（decihertz）频段的后向链接法布里-珀罗（back-linked Fabry-Perot, BLFP）干涉仪中，所需时钟稳定性超过当前空间合格振荡器一个数量级以上。

Method: 提出一种时钟噪声消除方案，利用臂腔（arm cavities）入射和出射激光束自然产生的两个具有正负拍频（beat-note frequencies）的外差信号，通过具有时间相关系数的加权组合来消除时钟抖动贡献，同时保留引力波信息。建立了理论框架，分析了实际臂长漂移下的性能，并使用B-DECIGO概念参数进行了时域模拟验证。

Result: 合成信号恢复了原始灵敏度，对于散粒噪声（shot noise）甚至将信噪比提高了√2倍。该方案有效解决了时钟抖动对分赫兹频段引力波探测的噪声限制问题。

Conclusion: 提出的时钟噪声消除方案能够在不增加额外时钟调制的情况下，有效消除外差干涉测量中的时钟抖动噪声，为空间引力波望远镜在分赫兹频段达到所需灵敏度提供了关键技术支撑。

Abstract: Space-borne gravitational-wave telescopes are key to extend the observation band below $10\,\mathrm{Hz}$. The use of inter-satellite optical cavities linked by heterodyne interferometry is a promising approach to reach the sensitivity level of $10^{-22}/\sqrt{\mathrm{Hz}}$ in the decihertz band. While heterodyne interferometry is advantageous for relaxing arm-length control requirements, it introduces susceptibility to clock jitter, which can be a significant noise source. In the back-linked Fabry--Perot (BLFP) interferometer aiming at the decihertz band, the required clock stability exceeds that of current space-qualified oscillators by more than an order of magnitude. We propose a clock noise cancellation scheme that uses two heterodyne signals with positive and negative beat-note frequencies, naturally obtained using both incoming and outgoing laser beams of arm cavities without additional clock modulation schemes. By forming a weighted combination of these signals with time-dependent coefficients, clock jitter contributions are eliminated while preserving gravitational-wave information. We present the theoretical framework, analyze performance under realistic arm-length drifts, and validate the approach through time-domain simulations using parameters from the B-DECIGO concept. Results show that the synthesized signal recovers the original sensitivity and even improves the signal-to-noise ratio by a factor of $\sqrt{2}$ for shot noise.

</details>

### [112] [ToFiE, a Topology-aware Fiber Extraction workflow for 3D reconstruction of dense and heterogeneous biological fiber networks from microscopy images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18230)
*Risa Togo,Sara Cardona,Irène Nagle,Gijsje H. Koenderink,Behrooz Fereidoonnezhad,Mathias Peirlinck*

TL;DR: ToFiE是一种开源的拓扑感知纤维提取工作流，能够从高分辨率显微图像中重建密集异质纤维网络，同时保持三维连通性，为多种纤维材料提供实用的半自动化网络信息提取框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纤维网络是生物学中普遍存在的结构组件，但当前分割方法无法保持网络拓扑结构，常依赖基于强度的阈值分割，这可能导致纤维断裂和连接点连通性失真，因此需要开发能够准确重建网络拓扑的方法。

Method: 研究团队开发了ToFiE（topology-aware fiber extraction）工作流，这是一种开源、拓扑感知的纤维提取方法，专门用于从高分辨率显微图像中重建密集异质纤维网络，同时保持三维连通性。

Result: 使用具有不同拓扑结构和信噪比的合成荧光显微图像验证了ToFiE的有效性，并进一步通过重建具有各种微观结构的胶原凝胶纤维网络库（使用共聚焦荧光显微镜成像）展示了其性能。

Conclusion: ToFiE被确立为一种实用的半自动化框架，能够从广泛的纤维材料成像数据中提取与力学相关的网络信息，解决了当前分割方法在保持网络拓扑方面的局限性。

Abstract: Fibrous networks are ubiquitous structural components in biology, spanning cellulose in plant cell walls, fibrin in blood clots, and collagen in the extracellular matrix of animal tissues. Theoretical models predict that network connectivity critically influences their mechanical behavior. However, accurately reconstructing network topology from 3D image data remains a major challenge as current segmentation methods are not designed to preserve network topology and often rely on intensity-based thresholding, which can fragment fibers and distort junction connectivity. Here, we introduce ToFiE, an open-source topology-aware fiber extraction workflow for reconstructing dense and heterogeneous fibrous networks from high resolution microscopy images while preserving connectivity in three dimensions. We validate ToFiE using synthetic fluorescence microscopy images of fiber networks with varying topologies and signal-to-noise ratios. We further demonstrate its performance by reconstructing the fiber networks of a library of collagen gels with various microstructures, imaged using confocal fluorescence microscopy. Altogether, the results establish ToFiE as a practical semi-automated framework for extracting mechanically relevant network information from imaging data across a broad range of fibrous materials.

### [113] [Boltzmann Machine Learning with a Parallel, Persistent Markov chain Monte Carlo method for Estimating Evolutionary Fields and Couplings from a Protein Multiple Sequence Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18022)
*Sanzo Miyazawa*

Main category: q-bio.BM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的逆Potts问题求解方法，用于从蛋白质多序列比对中估计进化单点场和成对耦合参数。通过采用并行持久马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛方法和随机梯度下降来加速计算，并引入基于蛋白质构象特性的超参数调整策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逆Potts问题（inverse Potts problem）在蛋白质结构和进化研究中仍是有用的方法，但现有方法在计算效率和超参数调整方面存在挑战。计算耗时且超参数调整缺乏敏感性是主要问题。

Method: 采用玻尔兹曼机方法（Boltzmann machine method），但为减少计算时间，使用了并行持久马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛方法（parallel, persistent Markov chain Monte Carlo method）来估计每个学习步骤中的单点和成对边际分布。同时采用随机梯度下降方法（stochastic gradient descent methods）加速学习过程。超参数调整方面，提出基于蛋白质构象特性的特定条件来调整两个正则化参数。

Result: 该方法已应用于八个蛋白质家族（eight protein families），通过基于构象特性的超参数调整策略解决了传统接触残基对预测精度对正则化参数不敏感的问题。

Conclusion: 提出的改进方法在保持玻尔兹曼机方法可重复性的同时，通过计算优化和基于蛋白质构象特性的超参数调整策略，有效提升了逆Potts问题求解的效率和适用性。

Abstract: The inverse Potts problem for estimating evolutionary single-site fields and pairwise couplings in homologous protein sequences from their single-site and pairwise amino acid frequencies observed in their multiple sequence alignment would be still one of useful methods in the studies of protein structure and evolution. Since the reproducibility of fields and couplings are the most important, the Boltzmann machine method is employed here, although it is computationally intensive. In order to reduce computational time required for the Boltzmann machine, parallel, persistent Markov chain Monte Carlo method is employed to estimate the single-site and pairwise marginal distributions in each learning step. Also, stochastic gradient descent methods are used to reduce computational time for each learning. Another problem is how to adjust the values of hyperparameters; there are two regularization parameters for evolutionary fields and couplings. The precision of contact residue pair prediction is often used to adjust the hyperparameters. However, it is not sensitive to these regularization parameters. Here, they are adjusted for the fields and couplings to satisfy a specific condition that is appropriate for protein conformations. This method has been applied to eight protein families.

### [114] [Energy conditions in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes and effective geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16545)
*Zi-Liang Wang,Emmanuele Battista*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了经典能量条件在静态球对称时空中的应用，开发了一种在特定条件下自动满足零能量条件的算法，并发现了一个包含对数修正的史瓦西度规，该度规可作为黑洞模拟器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探讨经典能量条件（classical energy conditions）在一般静态球对称时空中的表现，特别关注视界出现时对零能量条件（null energy condition）的影响以及标准近视界性质的破坏。

Method: 研究方法包括：分析非恒定$g_{tt} g_{rr}$设置下的视界出现情况；针对满足$g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1$的配置，设计系统算法生成爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）的解；从该族解中选择一个包含对数修正的史瓦西度规（Schwarzschild metric）。

Result: 研究结果显示：在特定条件下开发的算法能自动生成满足零能量条件的解；所选的对数修正史瓦西度规满足所有标准能量准则；该几何结构可作为包含视界和无视界致密天体的有效外部描述，并在某些情况下可作为黑洞模拟器（black hole mimicker）。

Conclusion: 结论表明，所研究的几何结构既能描述含视界的致密天体，也能描述无视界的致密天体，并在特定条件下具有作为黑洞模拟器的潜力，这为理解极端引力环境下的时空结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: Classical energy conditions are investigated in generic static and spherically symmetric spacetimes. In setups with nonconstant $g_{tt} g_{rr}$, the appearance of horizons can signal the violation of the null energy condition and the breakdown of some standard near-horizon properties. For configurations satisfying $g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1$, we devise a systematic algorithm to generate solutions of the Einstein field equations that automatically obey the null energy condition. Within this family, we select a particularly significant metric that incorporates a logarithmic correction to the Schwarzschild model and fulfills all standard energy criteria. We examine its main features, including the horizon structure, geodesic behavior, and junction conditions. Our analysis shows that this geometry can be interpreted as an effective exterior description for both horizon-bearing and horizonless compact objects, and suggests that it can potentially act, in certain regimes, as a black hole mimicker.

</details>


### [115] [Photon rings and shadows of black holes with non-minimal couplings between curvature and electromagnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16551)
*Zhixiang Yin,Changjun Gao,Yun-Long Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究具有电磁场与时空曲率非最小耦合（non-minimal couplings）的黑洞，分析其对事件视界、阴影和光子环的影响。三种耦合项产生不同的观测特征，可用于约束引力修正或寻找经典/量子效应证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究电磁场与时空曲率非最小耦合的黑洞，这种耦合可自然出现在经典有效引力场论和弯曲时空量子效应中。通过分析此类黑洞的事件视界、阴影和光子环特征，可探索引力修正的观测后果。

Method: 从包含三个独立耦合项的广义作用量出发，采用级数展开法（series expansion method）推导静态球对称黑洞解。通过向后光线追踪（backward ray tracing）生成黑洞图像，在可观测分辨率范围内验证理论特征。

Result: 所有耦合项均扩大事件视界和光子球（photon sphere）。$F^μ_{\ ν}F_{μρ}R^{νρ}$耦合轻微增大阴影尺寸和零阶-一阶光子环间距；$F_{μν}F_{σρ}R^{μνσρ}$耦合显著增大阴影和零阶-一阶环间距，但快速抑制高阶环间距；$F^2R$耦合减小阴影尺寸，使零阶和一阶环几乎重合（增强亮度），同时增大高阶环间距使其更易分辨。

Conclusion: 不同非最小耦合项产生特征性的观测信号差异，这些发现可用于对非最小耦合进行观测约束，或为经典/量子效应引起的引力修正提供新证据。

Abstract: We investigate black holes with non-minimal couplings between the electromagnetic field and spacetime curvature, focusing on their event horizons, shadows, and photon rings. Such couplings can naturally arise from both classical effective field theories of gravity and quantum effects in curved spacetime. Starting from a general action with three independent coupling terms, we derive static and spherically symmetric black hole solutions using a series expansion method. We find that all couplings enlarge the event horizon and photon sphere, while their observational consequences differ. The coupling $F^μ_{\ ν}F_{μρ}R^{νρ}$ slightly increases the shadow size and the separation between the zeroth- and first-order photon rings, leaving higher-order spacings nearly unchanged. The coupling $F_{μν}F_{σρ}R^{μνσρ}$ significantly enlarges the shadow and the zeroth-first ring separation, but rapidly suppresses the spacing between higher-order rings. In contrast, the $F^2R$ coupling reduces the shadow size and causes the zeroth- and first-order rings to nearly coincide, leading to an enhanced brightness, while increasing the separation of higher-order rings and leaving them easier to resolve observationally. We further generate black hole images via backward ray tracing and confirm these features within the observationally resolvable regime. These findings can make observational constraints on the non-minimal couplings or might provide new evidence for the modifications to gravity caused by classical or quantum effects.

</details>


### [116] [Shadow, Quasinormal Modes, Sparsity, and Energy Emission Rate of Euler-Heisenberg Black Hole Surrounded by Perfect Fluid Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16628)
*Edilberto O. Silva,Faizuddin Ahmed*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了浸没在完美流体暗物质（PFDM）背景中的欧拉-海森堡黑洞的光学、动力学和辐射特性，分析了光子球、阴影、准正规模谱、灰体因子、霍金辐射稀疏度及能量发射率，发现暗物质参数对观测现象有主导性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索欧拉-海森堡黑洞在完美流体暗物质（perfect fluid dark matter, PFDM）背景下的物理特性，旨在理解暗物质环境如何影响黑洞的光学、动力学和辐射现象，为通过黑洞观测探测暗物质效应提供理论基础。

Method: 研究方法包括分析光子球（photon sphere）和阴影（shadow）、在eikonal regime下的标量准正规模（quasinormal-mode）谱、通过eikonal QNM对应关系计算灰体因子（grey-body factor）、霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）稀疏度以及相应的能量发射率（energy emission rate）。

Result: 结果显示黑洞电荷和PFDM参数显著影响光子球、阴影尺寸、准正规模频率、霍金温度和发射剖面，而欧拉-海森堡（Euler-Heisenberg）修正在所探索参数范围内通常处于次要地位，但在强电荷区域对特定可观测量可能变得更为明显。

Conclusion: 结论表明暗物质环境对系统现象学提供了主导性印记，暗示在考虑的近似条件下，阴影和ringdown相关量可能作为探测PFDM效应的有用探针，为通过黑洞观测约束暗物质参数提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the optical, dynamical, and radiative properties of an Euler--Heisenberg black hole immersed in a perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) background. We analyze the photon sphere and shadow, the scalar quasinormal-mode spectrum in the eikonal regime, the grey-body factor through the eikonal QNM correspondence, the sparsity of Hawking radiation, and the corresponding energy emission rate. Our results show that both the black-hole charge and the PFDM parameter significantly affect the photon sphere, shadow size, quasinormal frequencies, Hawking temperature, and emission profile, whereas the Euler--Heisenberg correction is typically subleading in the parameter range explored, although it may become more visible in strong-charge regimes for selected observables. Overall, the dark-matter environment provides the dominant imprint on the phenomenology of the system, indicating that shadow and ringdown-related quantities may serve as useful probes of PFDM effects within the approximations considered.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过逆向应用诺特定理（Noether's theorem）到测地线拉格朗日量，推导出三种隐藏对称变换。这些变换与基林等距（Killing isometries）对易，并对赤道测地线的能量和角动量产生独立的平移和缩放作用。

Result: 成功识别出三种隐藏对称变换，它们分别对应LRL角、LRL基林矢量和LRL固有时这三个守恒量。这些变换与基林对称性共同构成了类时赤道测地线方程的完整诺特对称群。

Conclusion: 研究为史瓦西时空中类时测地线的隐藏守恒量提供了对称性基础，揭示了这些守恒量对应的三种隐藏对称变换，并与基林对称性共同形成了完整的诺特对称群结构。

Abstract: For the timelike geodesic equations in Schwarzschild spacetime, three hidden conserved quantities were found recently, which are analogues of dynamical quantities related to the well-known Laplace-Runge-Lenz (LRL) vector in Newtonian gravity. In particular, the geodesic equations possess an LRL angle, an LRL Killing-vector time and an LRL proper-time, each of which is a conserved quantity for all timelike geodesics. The present work provides a natural symmetry interpretation for these three quantities by applying Noether's theorem in reverse to the geodesic Lagrangian. This yields three hidden symmetry transformations. They are shown to commute with the Killing isometries and act on the equatorial geodesics by separate shifts and scaling of the geodesic energy and angular momentum. Together with the Killing symmetries, these transformations comprise the complete Noether symmetry group of the timelike equatorial geodesic equations.

### [118] [Memory of Robinson-Trautman waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16703)
*Glenn Barnich,Ali Seraj*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在明确计算Robinson-Trautman波的记忆效应，为此需要构建合适的坐标系框架，使Robinson-Trautman波在未来类光无穷远（future null infinity）处呈现局部渐近平坦（locally asymptotically flat）特性。

Method: 首先构建了结合框架旋转和坐标变换的坐标系，使Robinson-Trautman波在未来类光无穷远处呈现局部渐近平坦；其次构建了改进的广义质量方面（generalized mass aspect），作为流动的局部Lyapunov函数；详细研究了news-free解，并分析了其在BMS₄变换下的不变性。

Result: 证明了news-free解与欧几里得Liouville理论（Euclidean Liouville theory）的真空扇区完全一致，对应于一个经过boost和重新标度的Schwarzschild黑洞；同时证明了位移和非线性记忆效应在超平移（supertranslations）下不变，在BMS₄洛伦兹变换和常数重新标度下协变。

Conclusion: 本文成功推导了Robinson-Trautman波的记忆效应，建立了news-free解与Liouville理论的对应关系，并证明了记忆效应在BMS₄变换下的不变性，为理解低谐波修正流动提供了新的物理解释。

Abstract: The memory effect for Robinson-Trautman waves is explicitly worked out. In a first step, we construct the combined frame rotation and coordinate transformation in which Robinson-Trautman waves are manifestly locally asymptotically flat at future null infinity. This allows us to apply well-established results on how to derive the memory effect in this context. In a second step, we construct a suitably improved generalized mass aspect that provides a local Lyapunov function for the flow in the sense that it is manifestly positive. News-free solutions are studied in detail and shown to coincide with the vacuum sector of Euclidean Liouville theory. They correspond to a boosted and rescaled Schwarzschild black hole. As a by-product, we show that the displacement and non-linear memory effects in locally asymptotically flat spacetimes at future null infinity are invariant under supertranslations and covariant under $\mathrm{BMS}_4$ Lorentz transformations and constant rescalings. A novel interpretation of modified flows that control the low harmonics in terms of keeping the system in its instantaneous rest frame is provided.

</details>


### [119] [Reference-renormalized curvature-primitive Gauss-Bonnet formalism for finite-distance weak gravitational lensing in static spherical spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16807)
*Reggie C. Pantig,Ali Övgün*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于静态球对称时空中高斯-邦尼引力透镜有限距离计算的参考重整化（无光子球）归一化方案。该方法通过匹配外部区域物理几何与参考几何来固定规范，获得唯一的重整化差异原函数，从而在不依赖圆形零轨道的情况下推导有限距离偏转角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高斯-邦尼引力透镜计算通常依赖于光子球（photon sphere）的存在来进行轨道归一化（orbit normalization），但在某些物理光学区域不存在圆形零轨道（circular null orbit）的时空中，这种方法无法适用。需要发展一种不依赖光子球的统一计算方法。

Method: 提出参考重整化归一化方案，将用于简化高斯-邦尼曲率-面积积分的曲率原函数（curvature primitive）视为模加性常数（模加性规范自由度）的量。通过匹配物理几何在外部区域趋近的参考光学几何来固定规范，定义唯一的重整化差异原函数 $\mathcal{P}_e(r)$。

Result: 该方法成功推导出Ishihara-Li有限距离偏转角（finite-distance deflection angle），无需引用任何圆形零轨道。在渐近平坦（asymptotically flat）设置中，规范参考为闵可夫斯基几何；在Kottler型背景中，规范参考为静态补丁内的德西特几何。验证了方法在Schwarzschild、Reissner-Nordström和Kottler时空中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一条统一、几何透明的有限距离透镜计算路径，在适用情况下与轨道归一化方案保持兼容，并在轨道归一化真正不适用的情况下（如Janis-Newman-Winicour时空）提供了可行的计算框架。

Abstract: We develop a reference-renormalized (photon-sphere-free) normalization scheme for Gauss-Bonnet gravitational lensing at finite distance in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes. The method treats the curvature primitive used to reduce the Gauss-Bonnet curvature-area integral as a quantity defined only modulo an additive constant (an additive gauge freedom). We fix this gauge by matching to a physically chosen reference optical geometry in an outer regime where the physical geometry approaches that reference, thereby defining a unique renormalized discrepancy primitive $\mathcal{P}_e(r)$ by reference subtraction. The resulting master formula yields the Ishihara-Li finite-distance deflection angle without invoking any circular null orbit, while remaining fully compatible with orbit-normalized prescriptions whenever a suitable photon sphere exists (the two gauges differ only by a constant shift and give identical $α$). In asymptotically flat settings the canonical reference is Minkowski, while in Kottler-type backgrounds the canonical reference is de Sitter within the static patch, making the operational fiducial explicit. We validate the method by reproducing Ishihara's finite-distance weak-deflection formulas for Schwarzschild, Reissner-Nordström, and Kottler spacetimes, including the mixed $r_gΛ$ term in the Kottler case within the static-patch fiducial. We also present a demonstrative example in which orbit normalization is genuinely inapplicable because no circular null orbit exists in the physical optical region (the Janis-Newman-Winicour spacetime for $γ\le \tfrac12$). The result is a unified, geometrically transparent route to finite-distance lensing that preserves compatibility with orbit-normalized prescriptions whenever those apply.

### [120] [First-order thermodynamics of multi-scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16907)
*David S. Pereira*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Jordan框架张量-多标量引力理论中建立了热力学描述，将几何部分解释为有效非完美流体，推导了热流、惯性变量和标量诊断量，并构建了熵流和熵产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从爱因斯坦型场方程出发，对几何部分进行精确的协变1+3分解，将其解释为有效非完美流体；在FF-共动框架中定义惯性变量和标量诊断量，并推导输运方程。

Result: 热流可精确表示为q_a^{(g)}=-χ(a_a+W_a)，其中χ=-˙FF/(8πFF)；在FF-共动框架中得到惯性变量χ_FF≡K_FFT_FF和非零空间贡献W_a^{(FF)}；构建了标量诊断量𝔇_χ和𝔇_grad，并建立了精确的GR吸引子判据。

Conclusion: 多场热力学描述通常不能简化为单一KT型量；冻结有效耦合通常弱于完全弛豫到GR区域；均匀宇宙学抑制空间部分但保留非平凡类时多标量热力学动力学。

Abstract: We formulate a first-order thermodynamic description of Jordan-frame tensor--multi-scalar gravity. From the Einstein-like field equations we obtain the exact covariant $1+3$ decomposition of the geometric sector and interpret it as an effective imperfect fluid. In a generic frame, the heat flux can be written exactly as $q_a^{(g)}=-χ(a_a+W_a)$, with $χ=-\dot{\FF}/(8π\FF)$, where $\FF=\FF(φ^C)$ is the nonminimal coupling function, and with $W_a$ the residual temperature-gradient sector. In the $\FF$-comoving frame this yields the inertial variable $χ_{\FF}\equiv K_{\FF}T_{\FF}$ together with a generally nonvanishing spatial contribution $W_a^{(\FF)}$ sourced by scalar directions not aligned with the coupling, showing that the multi-field thermodynamic description is not generically reducible to a single $KT$-type quantity. We derive transport equations for $χ_{\FF}$, for the field-space thermal vector $χ^A$ and covector $χ_A$, and for the residual gradient sector. We further introduce the scalar diagnostics $\mathfrak D_χ=χ_Aχ^A$ and $\mathfrak D_{\rm grad}=\mathcal{B}_{AB}\D_a^{(\FF)}φ^A\D^a_{(\FF)}φ^B$, where $\mathcal{B}_{AB}$ is the field-space kinetic matrix of the multi-scalar theory and $\D_a^{(\FF)}$ is the covariant derivative projected orthogonally to the $\FF$-comoving 4-velocity. These diagnostics characterize the full time-like and spatial multi-scalar sectors and lead to a precise GR-attractor criterion: freezing the effective coupling is, in general, weaker than full relaxation to the GR sector. Finally, we construct the entropy current and entropy production in the coupling frame and show that homogeneous cosmology suppresses the spatial sector while retaining nontrivial time-like multi-scalar thermal dynamics.

### [121] [A note on complete gauge-fixing and the constraint algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16990)
*Ganga Singh Manchanda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了规范固定（gauge-fixing）的可容许性（admissibility）判据中，约束矩阵的行列式可分解为规范固定行列式的平方与第二类约束矩阵行列式的乘积，表明第二类约束（second-class constraints）与规范固定完全解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 规范固定的可容许性通常由矩阵Δ={σ^a,γ_b}的可逆性决定，其中σ^a是规范固定条件，γ_b是独立的第一类约束（first-class constraints）。研究旨在提供可容许性的替代判据，并探讨其在修正引力理论中的意义。

Method: 通过舒尔补（Schur complement）方法，证明由所有约束和规范固定条件构建的组合约束矩阵M={Φ_A, Φ_B}的行列式可分解为detM≈±(detΔ)^2 detC，其中C是第二类约束矩阵。在代数情形下，将Henneaux和Teitelboim的哈密顿可容许性判据与Motohashi、Suyama和Takahashi的拉格朗日完备性（completeness）判据等同起来。

Result: 行列式分解表明第二类约束与规范固定完全解耦，因为detC≠0。在球对称时空背景下，将度规ansatz识别为作用量层面的规范固定，并分析完备性。该分解确保完备性对修正引力理论中出现的第二类约束具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 规范固定的可容许性判据可通过约束矩阵的行列式分解来表征，其中第二类约束完全从规范固定中解耦。这一结果建立了哈密顿框架与拉格朗日框架下可容许性判据的等价性，并证明在修正引力理论中完备性不受第二类约束影响。

Abstract: The admissibility of a gauge-fixing is governed by the invertibility of $Δ=\{σ^a,γ_b\}$ where $σ^a$ are gauge-fixing conditions and $γ_b$ are independent first-class constraints. We prove, via the Schur complement, that the determinant of the combined constraint matrix $\mathcal{M}=\{Φ_A, Φ_B\}$ built from all constraints and gauge-fixing conditions factorises as $\det\mathcal{M}\approx\pm(\detΔ)^2\det C$, where $C$ is the second-class constraint matrix, providing an alternative criterion for admissibility. Since $\det C\neq0$ by definition, the second-class sector decouples entirely from the gauge-fixing sector. In the algebraic case, this factorisation identifies the Hamiltonian admissibility criterion of Henneaux and Teitelboim with the Lagrangian completeness criterion of Motohashi, Suyama, and Takahashi. We identify a metric ansatz as gauge-fixing at the action level and analyse completeness in the context of spherically symmetric spacetime. The factorisation ensures that completeness is robust to the second-class sector that arises in modified theories of gravity.

This establishes the bow-shaped Stokes topology as a direct signature of the naked singularity in the global analytic structure of the perturbation equation. ### [124] [Generalized relative locality and causal sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17272)
*Andrea Bevilacqua,Alice Boldrin*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该框架克服了传统相对局域性方法（以动量空间为底流形）的局限性，使其能够应用于一般背景的宇宙学。通过以时空为底流形的纤维丛构造，确保了因果性的显式表达，为PQG研究提供了更灵活且物理意义明确的形式体系。

Abstract: In this paper we introduce a new general framework for the study of phenomenological quantum gravity theories (PQG). The key idea is the introduction of two different types of spacetime, an observer-independent spacetime (modeled by a smooth orientable manifold) and an observer-dependent one (which has an inherently discrete causal set structure). The interaction between the two allows us to prove the main result of the paper: relative locality can be obtained in general PQG models, regardless of momentum-space curvature. {We also discuss the treatment of spacetime symmetries in our model, and introduce a direct link between spacetime symmetries and relative locality effects.} Our construction is presented in a coordinate-independent way and is based on fibre bundles where spacetime, rather than momentum-space, is the base manifold. This makes causality manifest even in general models with relative locality. Furthermore, it allows for the application of this formalism to cosmology on general backgrounds, something which is not clearly possible in the canonical approach to relative locality, where momentum-space serves as the base manifold.

### [125] [Geometric deformations of symmetric spacetimes with a string cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17279)
*Hiroshi Kozaki,Satsuki Matsuno,Tatsuhiko Koike,Yoshiyuki Morisawa,Hideki Ishihara*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一个针对高度对称爱因斯坦方程解的变形框架，通过三维η-爱因斯坦度规的单函数变形构造四维时空，统一处理包括FLRW、Kantowski-Sachs、LRS Bianchi宇宙模型和Reissner-Nordström-(A)dS黑洞在内的多种对称时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在建立统一的变形框架来处理高度对称的爱因斯坦方程解，将多种对称时空纳入统一的理论框架中，包括宇宙学模型和黑洞解。

Method: 通过从三维η-爱因斯坦度规出发，引入由单函数确定的变形，构造四维时空度规。该变形框架使得变形后的时空满足带有弦云源的爱因斯坦方程。

Result: 在宇宙学背景下，变形不改变尺度因子的演化方程，因此膨胀历史与未变形模型一致。对于变形的Reissner-Nordström-(A)dS黑洞，Killing视界结构对变形不敏感。

Conclusion: 该变形框架能够以统一方式处理广泛的对称时空，包括FLRW、Kantowski-Sachs、LRS Bianchi宇宙模型和Reissner-Nordström-(A)dS黑洞，为高度对称爱因斯坦方程解的研究提供了系统方法。

Abstract: We establish a deformation framework for highly symmetric solutions to the Einstein equations. In this framework, four-dimensional metrics are constructed from three-dimensional η-Einstein metrics admitting a deformation determined by a single function. Under this deformation, the resulting spacetime solves the Einstein equations with a string-cloud source. Within this framework , a wide range of symmetric spacetimes can be treated in a unified manner. These include FLRW, Kantowski-Sachs, and LRS Bianchi cosmological models (including Taub-NUT-(A)dS solutions), as well as Reissner-Nordström-(A)dS black holes admitting spherical, planar, or hyperbolic symmetry. In the cosmological setting, the deformation leaves the evolution equations for the scale factors unchanged, and hence the expansion history coincides with that of the corresponding undeformed models. For the deformed Reissner-Nordström-(A)dS black holes, the structure of Killing horizons is insensitive to the deformation.

</details>


### [126] [Weak Gravitational Lensing: A Brief Overview](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17355)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文对弯曲时空中的光线偏折进行了全面分析，从引力透镜的基本原理出发，系统研究了静态球对称几何和克尔时空中的光子运动，并扩展至轴对称时空的统一几何框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力透镜（gravitational lensing）是时空曲率最直接的观测表现之一，为研究致密天体提供了有力工具。论文旨在建立从基础到高级的完整理论框架，以深入理解弯曲时空中光线的偏折现象。

Method: 研究方法包括：从牛顿近似到相对论性透镜方程（lens equation）和透镜势（lensing potential）的逐步推导；利用弯曲时空中的有效折射率（effective refractive index）对费马原理（Fermat's principle）进行几何解释；分析静态球对称几何和克尔时空（Kerr spacetime）赤道面中的光子轨迹；应用林德勒-伊沙克方法（Rindler-Ishak method）和高斯-博内定理（Gauss-Bonnet theorem）计算偏折角；最后使用OIA和GW-OIA形式体系扩展至轴对称时空（axisymmetric spacetimes）。

Result: 推导出了控制光子轨道的最接近距离（closest approach distance）和临界参数（critical parameters）的解析表达式。建立了计算静态和旋转引力场中光线偏折的统一几何框架，为轴对称时空中的光偏折分析提供了系统方法。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了从基础到高级的完整引力透镜理论框架，涵盖了从牛顿近似到相对论性描述，从静态球对称到旋转克尔时空，再到一般轴对称时空的光线偏折分析。所发展的统一几何框架为计算各类引力场中的光偏折现象提供了系统工具。

Abstract: Gravitational lensing constitutes one of the most direct observational manifestations of spacetime curvature and provides a powerful probe of compact astrophysical objects. In this work, we present a comprehensive analysis of the bending of light in curved spacetime, beginning with the fundamental aspects of gravitational lensing and the Newtonian approximation to light deflection. The relativistic formulation of lensing is then developed through the lens equation, lensing potential, and a geometrical interpretation of Fermat's principle using an effective refractive index in curved spacetime. Photon trajectories and light deflection are subsequently investigated in static, spherically symmetric geometries, followed by a detailed study of photon motion in the equatorial plane of the Kerr spacetime. Analytical expressions for the closest approach distance and critical parameters governing photon orbits are derived. Furthermore, the bending angle is examined using the Rindler-Ishak method and the Gauss-Bonnet theorem within the optical geometry. Finally, the analysis is extended to axisymmetric spacetimes using the OIA and GW-OIA formalisms, providing a unified geometrical framework for computing light deflection in both static and rotating gravitational fields.

Abstract: These notes give a concise introduction to General Relativity at the advanced undergraduate level, starting from the weak field limit and gravitational waves, then introducing curved manifolds and Riemannian geometry. It is assumed that special relativity and electromagnetic waves have been previously studied. Some advanced topics such as Rindler and Hawking radiation are derived, and recent developments in gravitational wave detection are briefly covered. Problems are included, both those suitable for homework, and simpler ones that could be worked out by students during class sessions.

### [128] [Comment on Cosmological constraints on unimodular gravity models with diffusion (arXiv:2211.07424): thermodynamic inadmissibility of the H0 tension resolution mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17523)
*Mauricio Cataldo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在幺模引力（Unimodular Gravity）框架下，为缓解哈勃常数（H₀）张力而提出的扩散模型与热力学第二定律不相容。通过推导ΛCDM+扩散类的热力学可容性条件，作者建立了一个"不可能定理"：没有任何扩散函数Q(t)能同时满足第二定律和产生缓解H₀张力所需的增长有效宇宙学项（Λ_eff）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是检验幺模引力（Unimodular Gravity, UG）框架下扩散模型的热力学一致性。先前研究提出的ΛCDM+扩散模型旨在缓解哈勃常数（H₀）张力，但未充分考虑热力学第二定律的约束。

Method: 方法基于热力学分析：从无压物质流体的吉布斯方程（Gibbs equation）出发，推导出ΛCDM+扩散类的一般热力学可容性条件。通过分析扩散函数Q(t)与有效宇宙学项Λ_eff的关系，建立理论框架来检验模型的热力学一致性。

Result: 研究结果表明：热力学第二定律要求Q̇ < 0，这意味着能量必须从有效宇宙学项Λ_eff流向物质部门。作者建立了一个"不可能定理"（no-go theorem）：没有任何Q(t)能同时满足第二定律和产生Λ̇_eff > 0，而后者正是缓解H₀张力所必需的。这一结论在Perez等人和Landau等人的具体模型中得到验证。

Conclusion: 结论指出，幺模引力框架下ΛCDM+扩散模型与热力学第二定律的结构性不相容。这种不相容性适用于所有包含无压物质成分的ΛCDM+扩散模型，表明这些模型无法在满足热力学基本定律的同时缓解H₀张力。

Abstract: We show that the diffusion-based models proposed in Refs.~\cite{Perez2021,Landau2022} within the framework of Unimodular Gravity (UG) to alleviate the $H_0$ tension are incompatible with the second law of thermodynamics. Starting from the Gibbs equation for a pressureless matter fluid, we derive a general thermodynamic admissibility condition for the $Λ$CDM$+$diffusion class in UG, demonstrating that the second law requires $\dot{Q} < 0$, independently of the specific form of the diffusion function $Q(t)$. This condition implies that energy must flow from the effective cosmological term $Λ_{\rm eff}$ into the matter sector, rather than in the opposite direction. We then establish a no-go theorem: no choice of $Q(t)$ can simultaneously satisfy the second law and generate the growing effective cosmological term $\dotΛ_{\rm eff} > 0$ required to alleviate the $H_0$ tension. We confirm this result explicitly for the models of Perez, Sudarsky, and Wilson-Ewing~\cite{Perez2021} and Landau et al.~\cite{Landau2022}, noting that the former explicitly identify $\dotΛ_{\rm eff} > 0$ as a necessary feature of their proposal without addressing its thermodynamic implications. The incompatibility is therefore structural and applies to the entire class of $Λ$CDM$+$diffusion models in UG with a pressureless matter component.

Method: 采用标准膨胀标度变换 $(u,v,x)\mapsto (u,λ^2 v,λx)$，分析可容许的适应坐标变换如何退化为加权齐次主部。通过零滤过的分裂群定义残余加权规范群，并在未参数化零测地线流形上建立海森堡切模型。

Conclusion: 通过将结果模型拉回到时空点位于零测地线的关联空间，获得了与周围加权正规几何的标准同构连接。在接触标度的一阶jet丛上，彭罗斯极限被规范识别为相应连接时空邻域上的实际度量。

Abstract: We prove that the Penrose limit of a Lorentzian metric along an affinely parametrized null geodesic is intrinsic, but intrinsic on a weighted associated-graded model determined by the null filtration rather than on a canonically identified spacetime neighborhood. Under the standard dilation scaling $(u,v,x)\mapsto (u,λ^2 v,λx)$, admissible adapted coordinate changes collapse to their weighted homogeneous principal parts, so the large coordinate freedom of the classical construction degenerates to a small residual weighted gauge group, namely the group attached to the splittings of the null filtration. On the manifold of unparametrized null geodesics, the same weighted dilation is the grading derivation of a Heisenberg tangent model, and a $1$-jet of contact scale determines a realized degree-two direction without changing the underlying graded limit. These residual data assemble into an intrinsic unpolarized Penrose gauge bundle over the $1$-jet bundle of contact scales, with a polarized parabolic reduction after choosing a Lagrangian. Pulling the resulting model to the incidence space of spacetime points lying on null geodesics yields a canonical tautological soldering to the ambient weighted normal geometry, and fiberwise identifies the corresponding homogeneous plane-wave germ with the weighted associated graded of the ambient metric germ along the null geodesic. On the pullback of the incidence correspondence to the first jet bundle of contact scales, the tautological soldering canonically identifies the Penrose limit with an actual metric on the corresponding soldered spacetime neighborhood of the null geodesic.

We then construct a local inverse atlas for the Kerr $(\ell,m,n)=(2,2,0)$ map on an event-local detector-frame remnant box for GW250114 and propagate the resulting primary uncertainty into $(2,2,1)$ and $(4,4,0)$ consistency tests. The accepted windows form an intermediate post-peak band: earlier windows remain sensitive to start-time drift and structured nuisance fits, whereas later windows become variance dominated. Within that band, the recovered remnant remains consistent with the public inspiral--merger--ringdown estimates and supports a common-remnant Kerr interpretation that survives the full preprocessing and robustness checks. Method: 研究方法基于场论框架，从背景闵可夫斯基时空和庞加莱不变性出发，考察总能量-动量张量的守恒条件。其中场贡献由对称化的贝林范特张量（symmetrized Belinfante tensor）给出，研究对称二阶张量场（symmetric rank-2 tensor field）的场拉格朗日密度形式如何受总能量-动量守恒要求的约束。

Abstract: We present a novel approach to deriving the Einstein Lagrangian density based on energy-momentum conservation. In this framework, starting from a field-theoretic setting with background Minkowski spacetime and Poincaré invariance, we investigate whether conservation of the total energy-momentum tensor, in which the field contribution is given by the symmetrized Belinfante tensor, determines the form of the field Lagrangian density for a symmetric rank-2 tensor field. We find that the requirement of total energy-momentum conservation is satisfied only if the field Lagrangian density is proportional to the Einstein Lagrangian density.

### [132] [Parameter Estimation of the Gravitational-Wave Angular Power Spectrum in the Dirty-Map Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17610)
*Erik Floden,Alex Granados,Vuk Mandic*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种避免Fisher信息矩阵求逆的新方法，通过在"脏图（dirty map）"空间直接进行统计推断，用于各向异性随机引力波背景（SGWB）的角功率谱估计，成功恢复了模拟信号参数至ℓ_max=10。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 各向异性随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background, SGWB）搜索通常需要求逆包含小奇异值的Fisher信息矩阵，而正则化方法会引入偏差。本研究旨在避免这一矩阵求逆步骤，直接在"脏图"空间进行统计推断。

Method: 该方法将天图分解为球谐分量以获得角功率谱估计器，通过完全避免Fisher矩阵求逆，在所谓的"脏图（dirty map）"空间中引入统计模型推断方法。应用该方法于模拟信号，考虑SGWB自相关搜索及其与宇宙物质结构电磁示踪物的互相关搜索。

Result: 对于足够强的信号，该方法能够可靠地恢复模拟模型参数，最高可达球谐模式最大阶数ℓ_max=10。方法局限性主要源于复杂模型测试的计算成本、角功率谱高斯性假设，以及与基础信号强度成比例的类宇宙方差不确定性。

Conclusion: 提出的"脏图"空间统计推断方法有效避免了传统矩阵求逆带来的偏差问题，成功应用于Advanced LIGO第三观测期噪声环境下的各向异性SGWB角功率谱分析，为相关搜索提供了新的技术途径。

Abstract: We consider a search for the anisotropic stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB) that decomposes the sky map into its spherical harmonics components in order to obtain estimators of the angular power spectrum. Such a search often requires the inversion of a Fisher information matrix which contains small singular values. Rather than dealing with biases induced by regularization methods used to facilitate this matrix inversion, we opt to avoid this inversion step entirely by working in the so-called ``dirty map" space, and we introduce methodology for statistical model inference in this space. We apply our methodology to simulated model signals added to detector noise characterized by Advanced LIGO's third observing run and consider angular power spectra for both the SGWB auto-correlation search as well as a cross-correlation search between the SGWB and electromagnetic tracers of matter structure in the universe. In both cases we are able to reliably recover simulated model parameters for sufficiently strong signals up to maximum order spherical harmonic modes of $\ell_{max}=10$. We find the limitations of our methodology to arise from the computational cost of testing complex models, the assumption of Gaussianity of the angular power spectrum, and a cosmic variance-like source of uncertainty which scales with the strength of the underlying signal.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨分数熵（fractional entropy）应用于平坦弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（FLRW）宇宙视界的热力学和现象学意义，研究分数参数如何影响宇宙背景动力学。

Method: 采用热力学统一第一定律（unified first law of thermodynamics）和Kodama-Hayward温度，推导出由分数参数α∈(1,2]表征的广义弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equations）。使用截断分数模型与晚期观测数据联合样本进行约束，包括宇宙计时器、Pantheon+SH0ES超新星和最新DESI DR2重子声学振荡。

Result: 热力学分析表明比热C_V和C_p符号相同且仅依赖于减速参数，分数模型在晚期加速膨胀期间热力学稳定且无相变。观测数据拟合质量随α从广义相对论极限减小而单调下降，数据倾向于α接近2，此时H_0 = 69.50 ± 0.42 km/s/Mpc，Ω_{m0} = 0.292 ± 0.008。减小α会使H_0上移、Ω_{m0}下移。

Conclusion: 分数参数α以物理非平凡且观测可区分的方式调节背景膨胀，分数熵模型在热力学上稳定且与晚期加速膨胀兼容，但观测数据更支持接近广义相对论极限（α=2）的参数值。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic and phenomenological implications of a cosmological model governed by fractional entropy applied to the apparent horizon of a flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) universe. By utilizing the unified first law of thermodynamics alongside the Kodama-Hayward temperature, we derive a generalized set of Friedmann equations characterized by a fractional parameter $α\in (1,2]$. The thermodynamic analysis reveals that the specific heats $C_V$ and $C_p$ share the same sign and depend solely on the deceleration parameter, demonstrating that the fractional model is thermodynamically stable during the late-time accelerated expansion and does not exhibit phase transitions. To constrain the background dynamics, we confront the truncated fractional model with a joint sample of late-time observational data, including Cosmic Chronometers, Pantheon+SH0ES supernovae, and the latest DESI DR2 Baryon Acoustic Oscillations. Exploring the physically motivated range $ 1 < α\leq 2 $, we find that the fit quality degrades monotonically as $α$ decreases from the General Relativity limit, with the data favoring $α$ close to $2$ while yielding $H_0 = 69.50 \pm 0.42$ km/s/Mpc and $Ω_{m0} = 0.292 \pm 0.008 $ at $α= 2$. Decreasing $α$ coherently shifts $H_0$ upward and $Ω_{m0} $ downward, revealing that the fractional parameter modulates the background expansion in a physically nontrivial and observationally distinguishable way.

</details>


### [134] [Including higher-order modes in a quadrupolar eccentric numerical relativity surrogate using universal eccentric modulation functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17868)
*Tousif Islam,Adhrit Ravichandran,Peter James Nee,Scott E. Field,Vijay Varma,Harald P. Pfeiffer,Andrea Ceja,Noora Ghadiri,Lawrence E. Kidder,Prayush Kumar,Marlo Morales,Abhishek Ravishankar,Antoni Ramos-Buades,Katie Rink,Hannes R. Ruter,Mark A. Scheel,Md Arif Shaikh,Daniel Tellez*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在开发一个能够将多模态准圆形波形转化为偏心波形的框架，以扩展现有波形模型的能力。通过结合不同的波形模型，构建更全面的偏心波形模型，满足引力波数据分析中对偏心双星系统精确建模的需求。

Method: 研究采用gwNRHME框架，利用普适偏心调制函数（universal eccentric modulation functions）将多模态准圆形波形转化为偏心波形。具体方法包括：1）结合准圆形NR代理模型NRHybSur3dq8与四极矩非自旋偏心代理模型NRSurE_q4NoSpin_22；2）将框架与有效单体（effective-one-body, EOB）模型SEOBNRv5HM和TEOBResumS-Dali集成；3）开发偏心演化模型gwEccEvolve_q4NoSpin_Sur和gwEccEvNSv2。

Result: 构建的gwEccEvolve模型包含9个球谐模态：$(2,\{1,2\})$, $(3,\{1,2,3\})$, $(4,\{2,3,4\})$, 和$(5,5)$。与156个偏心SXS数值相对论波形对比，使用Advanced LIGO设计灵敏度计算的中值频域失配约为9×10⁻⁵，标准差约2×10⁻⁴。与EOB模型集成时，中值失配分别为2×10⁻⁴和10⁻³，标准差分别为2×10⁻³和2×10⁻²。

Conclusion: gwNRHME框架成功实现了多模态准圆形波形向偏心波形的转化，并展示了良好的模块化特性。该框架通过gwModels包公开可用，生成的波形模型将通过gwsurrogate包发布，为偏心双星系统的引力波数据分析提供了重要工具。

Abstract: \texttt{gwNRHME} is a framework that converts multi-modal (i.e., containing several spherical harmonic modes) quasi-circular waveforms into their eccentric counterparts, provided the quadrupolar eccentric mode is known, by exploiting universal eccentric modulation functions. Leveraging this framework, we combine the quasi-circular NR surrogate model \texttt{NRHybSur3dq8} with the quadrupolar, non-spinning, eccentric surrogate \texttt{NRSurE\_q4NoSpin\_22} to construct a multi-modal, non-spinning, eccentric model, denoted as \model{}, which includes nine modes: $(2,\{1,2\})$, $(3,\{1,2,3\})$, $(4,\{2,3,4\})$, and $(5,5)$. When compared against 156 eccentric SXS NR waveforms, \model{} achieves median frequency-domain mismatches (computed using the Advanced LIGO design sensitivity) of $\sim 9\times 10^{-5}$, with a standard deviation of $\sim 2 \times 10^{-4}$. To demonstrate the modularity of the framework, we further combine \texttt{NRSurE\_q4NoSpin\_22} with effective-one-body (EOB) models \texttt{SEOBNRv5HM} and \texttt{TEOBResumS-Dali} in their non-spinning limits, yielding eccentric waveforms with median mismatches of $\sim 2\times10^{-4}$ and $\sim 10^{-3}$, respectively, with standard deviation of $\sim 2 \times 10^{-3}$ and $\sim 2 \times 10^{-2}$ respectively. Finally, we provide both a surrogate model, \texttt{gwEccEvolve\_q4NoSpin\_Sur}, and an analytical model, \texttt{gwEccEvNSv2}, for the eccentricity evolution up to $2M$ before merger, based on eccentricity definitions derived from the universal modulation functions. The \texttt{gwNRHME} framework is publicly available through the \texttt{gwModels} package, and the resulting waveform models will be released via the \texttt{gwsurrogate} package.

*Yuji Takeuchi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在弯曲时空中，静态应力结构可产生类似浮力的效应，无需推进剂或循环内部运动，但效应极小且无法实际对抗引力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In curved spacetime, deformable bodies can undergo a displacement of their center of mass through cyclic internal motions without the use of propellant, as shown by Wisdom. In this paper, we demonstrate a different mechanism: in Schwarzschild spacetime, static structures with internal stress can generate a buoyancy-like force without non-gravitational external forces or cyclic internal motions. The resulting effect is extremely small for realistically sized structures and does not lead to an actual ascent against gravity. Nevertheless, it reveals a new aspect of extended-body dynamics in spacetimes with curvature gradients, in particular regarding the influence on motion of effects arising from the coupling between internal stress and spacetime curvature.

### [136] [Macroscopic Optical Nonreciprocity: A Black Hole as an Optical Diode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18101)
*Wentao Liu,Di Wu,Xiongjun Fang,Yu-Xiao Liu,Jieci Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值光线追踪模拟发现，在旋转黑洞中，自发洛伦兹对称性破缺会导致光学互易性被显著破坏，使黑洞阴影在光源与观测者互换时从类橄榄球形转变为泪滴形，从而将黑洞转化为宇宙尺度的光学二极管。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学互易性（optical reciprocity）是几何光学的基本原理，描述光在光源与探测器互换时沿相同路径传播的特性。本研究旨在探索在旋转黑洞中，当自发洛伦兹对称性破缺（spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking）引入具有优先方向的非最小耦合背景结构时，这种"对称保护"行为如何被定性颠覆。

Method: 采用数值光线追踪模拟（numerical ray-tracing simulations）方法，研究在自发洛伦兹对称性破缺引入非最小耦合背景结构的情况下，旋转黑洞中的光学路径反转效应。通过交换光源和观测者位置实现光学路径反转，分析黑洞阴影的形态变化。

Result: 模拟结果显示显著的宏观特征：当通过交换光源和观测者实现光学路径反转时，同一黑洞的阴影从准对称的橄榄球形状（rugby-ball shape）转变为独特的泪滴形轮廓（teardrop profile）。这种高对比度的非互易性（nonreciprocity）效应表明光学互易性在旋转黑洞中被显著破坏。

Conclusion: 研究证明旋转黑洞中的自发洛伦兹对称性破缺能够将黑洞转化为宇宙尺度的光学二极管（cosmic-scale optical diode）。这一发现为利用当前和下一代视界尺度成像技术探测基本对称性提供了新途径。

Abstract: Optical reciprocity--the principle that light retraces the same path when source and detector are interchanged--is a foundational concept in geometric optics. In this Letter, we demonstrate that this ``symmetry-protected'' behavior can be qualitatively overturned in a rotating black hole when spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking introduces a nonminimally coupled background structure with a preferred direction. Through numerical ray-tracing simulations, we reveal a striking macroscopic signature: upon optical-path reversal achieved by exchanging the source and the observer, the shadow of the same black hole morphs from a quasi-symmetric rugby-ball shape into a distinct teardrop profile. This high-contrast nonreciprocity effectively turns the black hole into a cosmic-scale optical diode, offering a novel pathway to probe fundamental symmetries using current and next-generation horizon-scale imaging.

</details>


### [137] [Holographic dark energy as a source for slowly rotating wormholes: Implications for null geodesics and shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18246)
*A. Errehymy,S. K. Maurya,M. Govender,K. N. Singh,J. Rayimbaev,B. Myrzakulova,S. Murodov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究首次探索了嵌入全息暗能量（holographic dark energy）中的缓慢旋转可穿越虫洞，分析了三种代表性全息暗能量模型（Rényi、混合、Moradpour）对虫洞几何结构、光子动力学和阴影形态的影响。

Method: 采用Teo型旋转虫洞度规（Teo-type rotating wormhole metric），直接从三种全息暗能量模型（Rényi、混合、Moradpour）的能量密度分布构造虫洞形状函数。考虑三种平滑双曲红移函数（Sinh、Cosh、Tanh）来捕捉不同红移行为的影响。

Result: 分析显示：尖峰状的Rényi分布产生更紧密的光子轨道和更强的非对称性，而平滑的混合和Moradpour分布允许更圆形的路径和更弱的参考系拖曳效应。Rényi支持的虫洞产生更小、非对称的阴影，而混合和Moradpour支持的虫洞产生更大、近乎圆形的轮廓。

Conclusion: 本研究为现实全息暗能量环境中缓慢旋转虫洞的光子动力学、阴影形态和相对论效应提供了详细的理论图景，为这些奇异天体的观测特征提供了潜在指导。

Abstract: In this work, we explore for the first time slowly rotating traversable wormholes embedded in holographic dark energy. We focus on three representative holographic dark energy models -- Rényi, mixed, and Moradpour -- and construct the wormhole shape functions directly from these energy density profiles using a Teo-type rotating wormhole metric. This allows us to examine the wormhole geometry in detail, including throat structure, the flaring-out condition for safe traversal, and violations of the null energy condition. To capture the effects of different redshift behaviors, we consider three smooth hyperbolic redshift functions -- Sinh, Cosh, and Tanh -- and study how they influence photon motion, null geodesics, effective potentials, photon-sphere locations, and Lense-Thirring precession caused by wormhole rotation. Our analysis shows that cuspy Rényi profiles produce tighter photon orbits and stronger asymmetry, while smoother mixed and Moradpour profiles allow more circular paths and weaker frame-dragging effects. Finally, we calculate the shadows cast by these wormholes, finding that Rényi-supported wormholes generate smaller, asymmetric shadows, whereas mixed and Moradpour-supported wormholes produce larger, nearly circular silhouettes. Altogether, this study provides a detailed theoretical picture of photon dynamics, shadow morphology, and relativistic effects in slowly rotating wormholes within realistic holographic dark energy environments, offering potential guidance for observational signatures of these exotic objects.

### [138] [New bounds for the area of MOTS and generalized ultra-massive spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18474)
*José M. M. Senovilla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了闭合边际陷俘面（MTS）的面积界限，这些界限不要求稳定性条件，由爱因斯坦张量分量和MTS稳定性常数决定。当加入稳定性条件时，面积界限会扩大。这些界限在具有特定几何结构的时空（包括动态视界和类时膜）中得以实现，对双星合并和致密天体吸积有潜在意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为一般闭合边际陷俘面（marginally trapped surfaces, MTS）建立面积界限，这些界限不依赖于稳定性假设。研究动机包括探索时空几何的极端性质，特别是当能量动量内容足够强时，即使在没有正宇宙常数的情况下也能产生类似"超质量时空"的行为。

Method: 方法基于爱因斯坦张量在边际陷俘面上的特定分量分析，结合决定MTS（不）稳定性的常数来推导面积界限。研究考虑了包含正宇宙常数的特殊情况，并扩展到非正宇宙常数的情形，通过能量动量内容的强度来补偿。

Result: 建立了不依赖稳定性的一般MTS面积界限，当加入稳定性条件时界限会扩大。发现这些界限在具有特定几何结构的时空中得以实现：包含一个具有恒定高斯曲率的显著球面$\bar S$，该球面将边际陷俘管分为动态视界（dynamical horizon）和类时膜（timelike membrane）两部分。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，即使在没有正宇宙常数的情况下，只要能量动量内容足够强，也能产生类似于"超质量时空"的极端行为，这些时空比黑洞更极端，因为没有事件视界且整个外部区域都在坍缩。这些发现可能对双星合并和致密天体吸积过程有重要影响。

Abstract: Bounds for the area of general closed marginally trapped surfaces (MTS) are presented. They do not require any kind of stability, and are determined by a constant that depends on a particular component of the Einstein tensor on the surface and another constant that rules the (in)stability of the MTS. When stability is added, the area bounds are enlarged. Such area bounds are realized in spacetimes that exhibit interesting generic properties. Concretely, they possess marginally trapped tubes foliated by marginally trapped topological spheres containing a distinguished round sphere $\bar S$ with constant Gaussian curvature that realizes the area bound. This prominent surface separates two distinct portions of the marginally trapped tubes: a dynamical horizon and a timelike membrane. The particular case where there is a positive cosmological constant leads to the well-known universal bound $4π/ Λ$ for spatially stable MTS, and to the recently introduced `ultra-massive spacetimes'. These spacetimes are more extreme than black holes, as there is no notion of event horizon and the entire external region is just collapsing with no possible escape. In this paper similar behaviours are found for non-positive $Λ$ if the energy-momentum content is powerful enough. The results may have implications on binary mergers and on accreting very compact objects.

</details>

### [139] [Revealing full molecular orientation distributions in organic thin films by nonlinear polarimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16692)
*Pierre-Luc Thériault,Emna Azek,Gabriel Juteau,Anagh Mukherjee,Heorhii V. Humeniuk,Zhechang He,Alexandre Malinge,Dmytro F. Perepichka,Lena Simine,Stéphane Kéna-Cohen*

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种结合多谐波非线性偏振测量与最大熵方法的新技术，无需先验假设即可重构分子取向概率分布，突破了传统表征技术仅能获取低阶矩的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机光电器件性能高度依赖于分子在薄膜中的取向，但传统表征技术仅能揭示取向分布的一阶和二阶矩。这种限制掩盖了真实的分子排列，因为不同的分布可能产生相同的低阶平均值却表现出截然不同的功能特性。

Method: 研究结合了多谐波非线性偏振测量（包括二次、三次和四次谐波）与最大熵方法，无需任何先验假设即可重构分子取向的概率分布。

Result: 该方法能够解析分布中的不对称性和双峰性等特征，这些特征对传统探测手段不可见。同时，该方法被用于基准测试分子动力学模拟，揭示这些模拟尽管能正确预测一阶和二阶矩，却常常无法捕捉复杂的分布特征。

Conclusion: 这项工作将分子取向从推断的平均值转变为精确的可观测物理量，为预测性材料设计建立了必要的验证标准。

Abstract: The performance of organic optoelectronic devices is critically dependent on how molecules orient within organic thin films. Yet, standard characterization techniques only reveal the first and second moments of the molecular orientation distribution. This limitation obscures the true molecular arrangement, as diverse distributions can yield identical low-order averages while exhibiting distinct functional properties. Here, we bridge this gap by combining multi-harmonic nonlinear polarimetry (second, third, and fourth harmonic) with the Maximum Entropy Method to reconstruct the probability distribution without any \textit{a priori} assumptions. This allows us to resolve features in the distribution such as asymmetry and bimodality, that remain invisible to conventional probes. Furthermore, we use this method to benchmark molecular dynamics simulations, revealing that these simulations often fail to capture the complex distribution despite correctly predicting the first and second moments. This work transforms molecular orientation from an inferred average into a precise observable, establishing essential validation standards for predictive material design.

### [140] [Universal compression of wave fields in weakly scattering media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17617)
*Pablo Jara,Alexey Yamilov*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出OSCAR（On-Shell Compression And Reconstruction）物理压缩方法，利用弱散射介质中波场的傅里叶表示被限制在薄色散壳上的特性，实现高达约380倍的压缩比，同时支持在压缩空间直接计算二阶物理量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模无序介质中的全波模拟产生海量场数据（随系统尺寸与波长比值的立方增长），造成严重的存储和后处理瓶颈。现有通用压缩方法无法在压缩数据上直接进行物理运算。

Method: 提出基于物理的OSCAR有损压缩方案，利用弱散射条件下波场傅里叶表示被限制在薄色散壳（dispersion shell）的普遍特性。该方法利用两种尺度分离：弱散射导致的壳上约束，以及亚波长离散化引入的额外傅里叶空间体积。

Result: 2D和3D电磁波数值模拟证实压缩比可达约380倍，场误差低于1%。关键优势在于二阶物理量（如强度、相关性和光学灵敏度）可通过卷积在压缩空间中直接计算，即使单个场重建存在显著误差也能保持准确。

Conclusion: OSCAR方法通过利用波传播的物理约束实现高效压缩，支持在压缩数据上直接进行物理运算，使生物医学光学、地震学和海洋声学等领域的常规系综研究成为可能。

Abstract: Advances in computational methods have made full-wave simulations in large disordered media increasingly feasible, but the resulting field data, scaling with the cube of the ratio of system size to wavelength, creates a severe storage and post-processing bottleneck. Generic compression methods are sample-specific and preclude operations on compressed data. We introduce OSCAR (On-Shell Compression And Reconstruction), a physics-based lossy compression scheme for weakly scattering media. OSCAR exploits the universal confinement of the Fourier representation of wave fields to a thin dispersion shell, a direct consequence of wave propagation when the scattering mean free path significantly exceeds the wavelength. The resulting compression ratio reflects two distinct scale separations: on-shell confinement due to weak scattering, and the excess Fourier-space volume introduced by sub-wavelength discretization of the scatterers. Crucially, second-order quantities such as intensity, correlations, and (optical) sensitivity can be computed via convolution entirely in compressed space and remain accurate even when individual field reconstruction incurs appreciable error, because coherent interference between independently compressed fields is preserved. Numerical simulations of electromagnetic waves in 2D and 3D confirm compression ratios up to ${\sim}380\times$ with sub-percent field error, enabling routine ensemble studies at scales relevant to biomedical optics, seismology, and underwater acoustics.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用可编程光子处理器结合了光计算的高速、大带宽和能效优势与软件定义硬件的灵活性，相比专用光子集成电路（ASPIC）具有更强的适应性和快速原型开发能力。

Method: 采用可循环砖块网格架构，通过可重构波导网格在单芯片上实现多种功能，包括开关、滤波和AI计算等，并支持通过反馈回路进行自校准和稳定化。

Result: 单个可编程光学系统可根据需求执行多种功能，同一网络经重编程后能实现从交叉网络到可变结构光学干涉电路的功能转换，并支持奇异值分解（Singular Value Decomposition）。

Abstract: General-purpose programmable photonic processors are considered a crucial technology because they combine the ultra high-speed, massive bandwidth, and energy efficiency of light-based computing with the flexibility of software-defined hardware. Unlike application-specific photonic integrated circuits (ASPIC) designed for one task, these processors use reconfigurable waveguide meshes to implement various functions, such as switching, filtering, or AI computation, on a single chip, allowing for rapid prototyping and versatile, on-demand hardware redefinition. Here we report a recirculating bricks mesh architecture that can be easily implemented in photonic neural networks. It will be shown that a single programmable optical system is capable of performing various functions depending on the requirements. In particular, we will show that the same network, after being reprogrammed, can perform many different functions, ranging from a crossbar network to optical interference circuits with variable structures, which can then be subjected to Singular Value Decomposition. Furthermore, the "bricks" mesh serves as an excellent foundation for implementing a monitoring system capable of monitoring the power in each location of the circuit and, subsequently, sel-fcalibrating and stabilizing the circuit using a feedback loop.
