### [142] [On The Mathematics of the Natural Physics of Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17645)
*I. M. Ross*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种将优化算法视为遵循某种非牛顿动力学（non-Newtonian dynamics）的隐藏原语（hidden primitives）的理论框架，通过最优控制（optimal control）与优化问题的等价性，构建了优化的自然物理（natural physics of optimization），并展示了如何生成和解释多种算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多优化算法受到牛顿运动物理学的启发，但本文探讨一个更深层的问题：算法本身是否遵循某种"运动自然定律"？研究动机在于建立优化算法的统一理论框架，揭示其背后的普适动力学原理。

Method: 通过将最优控制问题的终端横截性条件（terminal transversality conditions）与约束优化问题的广义KKT条件（Karush/John-Kuhn-Tucker conditions）等价起来，构建理论框架。利用庞特里亚金型最小值原理（Pontryagin-type minimum principle）产生局部作用，通过哈密顿-雅可比不等式（Hamilton-Jacobi inequality）实现全局化结果。

Result: 该理论表明，给定约束优化问题的数据函数会生成一个自然向量场（natural vector field），渗透整个隐藏空间并携带最优性条件信息。通过执行控制跳跃（control jumps）来耗散由搜索李雅普诺夫函数（search Lyapunov function）定义的量化"能量"，可以生成逆最优算法（inverse-optimal algorithm）。

Conclusion: 提出的优化自然物理理论能够生成和解释大量算法，为优化算法提供了统一的数学物理框架。该框架揭示了算法背后的普适动力学原理，将优化问题与最优控制理论建立了深刻联系。

Abstract: A number of optimization algorithms have been inspired by the physics of Newtonian motion. Here, we ask the question: do algorithms themselves obey some ``natural laws of motion,'' and can they be derived by an application of these laws? We explore this question by positing the theory that optimization algorithms may be considered as some manifestation of hidden algorithm primitives that obey certain universal non-Newtonian dynamics. This natural physics of optimization is developed by equating the terminal transversality conditions of an optimal control problem to the generalized Karush/John-Kuhn-Tucker conditions of an optimization problem. Through this equivalence formulation, the data functions of a given constrained optimization problem generate a natural vector field that permeates an entire hidden space with information on the optimality conditions. An ``action-at-a-distance'' operation via a Pontryagin-type minimum principle produces a local action to deliver a globalized result by way of a Hamilton-Jacobi inequality. An inverse-optimal algorithm is generated by performing control jumps that dissipate quantized ``energy'' defined by a search Lyapunov function. Illustrative applications of the proposed theory show that a large number of algorithms can be generated and explained in terms of the new mathematical physics of optimization.

</details>

### [143] [Adiabatic continuity in a partially reduced twisted Eguchi-Kawai model with one adjoint Dirac fermion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17848)
*Yudai Hamada,Tatsuhiro Misumi*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过数值研究大N SU(N)规范理论在空间紧致化下的中心对称禁闭相，使用部分约化的扭曲Eguchi-Kawai模型，发现轻费米子区域中Polyakov loop保持接近零值，支持禁闭相在大圆与小圆之间平滑连接的绝热连续性（adiabatic continuity）方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在数值验证大N SU(N)规范理论在空间紧致化（spatial compactification）下，中心对称（center-symmetric）禁闭相（confined phase）是否持续存在。具体探究理论在ℝ³ × S¹紧致化下的行为，检验禁闭相在大圆与小圆之间是否存在平滑连接。

Method: 采用部分约化的扭曲Eguchi-Kawai（TEK）模型，在1³ × L₄格点上引入伴随表示Wilson费米子（adjoint Wilson fermion）。测量沿S¹方向的Polyakov loop以及约化方向上的体积无关性（volume independence）序参数。参数设置为N=36，L₄=2，b=0.30-0.46，κ=0.03-0.16，并比较周期边界条件（periodic boundary conditions）与反周期边界条件（antiperiodic boundary conditions）下的行为。

Result: 在周期边界条件下，轻费米子区域（light-fermion regime）中Polyakov loop在圆尺寸减小时保持接近零值。对于修正扭曲（modified twist），体积无关性序参数在探索区域内也接近零，支持部分约化描述的有效性。这些结果为禁闭相在大圆与小圆之间平滑连接的绝热连续性方案提供了数值证据。相比之下，反周期边界条件下Polyakov loop显示出清晰的解禁闭转变（deconfinement transition）。

Conclusion: 在研究的约化模型设置和参数范围内，数值证据支持禁闭相在大圆与小圆之间平滑连接的绝热连续性（adiabatic-continuity）方案。该方案与底层四维理论的异常约束（anomaly constraints）兼容。对称扭曲（symmetric twist）作为有用比较被考察，但其体积无关性在当前N值下表现较弱。

Abstract: We numerically investigate whether the center-symmetric confined phase of large-$N$ $SU(N)$ gauge theory with one adjoint Dirac fermion persists under spatial compactification on $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$. To this end, we employ a partially reduced twisted Eguchi-Kawai (TEK) model on a $1^3 \times L_4$ lattice with an adjoint Wilson fermion, and measure both the Polyakov loop around $S^1$ and order parameters for volume independence in the reduced directions. For $N=36$, $L_4=2$, $b=0.30\text{-}0.46$, and $κ=0.03\text{-}0.16$, we find that, with periodic boundary conditions, the Polyakov loop remains near zero in the light-fermion regime as the circle size is reduced. For the modified twist, the volume-independence order parameters are also consistent with zero in the explored region, supporting the validity of the partially reduced description. These results provide numerical evidence, within the reduced-model setup and parameter range studied, for an adiabatic-continuity scenario in which the confined phase is smoothly connected between large and small circles. By contrast, with antiperiodic boundary conditions, the Polyakov loop exhibits a clear deconfinement transition. We also discuss how this scenario is compatible with the anomaly constraints of the underlying four-dimensional theory. The symmetric twist is examined as a useful comparison, although its volume-independence properties appear less robust at the present value of $N$.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将确定性量子虚时演化算法应用于二维纯$\mathbb{Z}_2$格点规范理论，以获取其基态。该方法旨在克服传统量子算法中因规范对称性约束带来的计算复杂性挑战。

Method: 方法包括：1）构造与高斯定律（Gauss's law）约束对易的泡利算符（Pauli operators）集合，确保确定性QITE保持规范不变性；2）使用张量网络（tensor networks）进行确定性QITE的经典数值模拟；3）与密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）结果比较以评估算法精度。

Result: 结果表明：确定性QITE在研究的耦合参数范围内，对多达十二个plaquette的系统能够实现小于0.1%的相对误差。研究还分析了误差对时间步数（time steps）的依赖性，并探讨了耦合强度和系统尺寸对算法性能的影响。

Conclusion: 确定性QITE算法在保持规范不变性的前提下，显著降低了测量和门成本，且不引入额外算法误差。该算法在中等规模格点规范理论系统中表现出高精度，为量子计算在规范场论研究中的应用提供了有效工具。

Abstract: In this paper, we apply the deterministic quantum imaginary time evolution (QITE) algorithm to obtain the ground state of a two-dimensional pure $\mathbb{Z}_2$ lattice gauge theory. We first construct the set of Pauli operators commuting with Gauss's law constraints, generalizing a previous result. This makes the deterministic QITE gauge-invariant and reduces both the measurement and gate costs significantly without adding extra algorithm errors in the QITE. Then, the classical numerical simulation of the deterministic QITE using tensor networks is performed, and the results are compared with the density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) to evaluate the accuracy of the algorithm. Specifically, we investigate the coupling and system size dependence, and find that the deterministic QITE can achieve a relative error of less than $0.1\%$ up to a twelve-plaquette system and coupling values in a regime that we study. Furthermore, the error dependence on the number of time steps is studied and discussed.

### [145] [Supersolid Rotation in an Annular Bose-Einstein Condensate coupled to a Ring Cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16573)
*Gunjan Yadav,Nilamoni Daloi,Pardeep Kumar,M. Bhattacharya,Tarak Nath Dey*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究理论分析了环形受限玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）与四镜环形腔耦合系统，在对称与非对称泵浦条件下实现了超固态相与持续超流循环共存，揭示了无物理搅拌的干涉驱动旋转机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用平均场理论（mean-field theory）分析环形受限BEC与支持行波光学模式的四镜环形腔耦合系统。研究对称驱动（对向传播的拉盖尔-高斯光束携带等值反向轨道角动量）和非对称泵浦（不同轨道角动量的拉盖尔-高斯光束）两种条件。

Result: 在对称驱动下，系统实现了与持续超流循环共存的超固态相（supersolid phases），包括具有特定绕数（winding number）L_p的BEC超固态态，以及两个不同L_p值相干叠加的超固态波包。非对称泵浦破坏手性对称性，导致不对称腔场振幅、定向密度调制和可调谐旋转动力学，产生旋转超固态密度结构和旋转波包。研究还探测到可通过腔输出谱非破坏性测量观察的Goldstone和Higgs模式。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了环形腔环形BEC系统作为生成手性量子物质、实现旋转传感设备和构建超固态原子电子电路的多功能平台。平均场理论揭示了无物理搅拌的干涉驱动旋转机制，区别于先前静态腔超固态研究。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate an annularly confined Bose-Einstein Condensate (BEC) coupled to a four-mirror ring cavity supporting traveling-wave optical modes. Under symmetric driving by counter-propagating Laguerre-Gaussian beams carrying equal and opposite orbital angular momenta, the system realizes supersolid phases coexisting with persistent superfluid circulation. Specifically, we obtain a supersolid state if we start with a BEC of winding number $L_p$ as well as supersolid packets with coherent superpositions of two different BEC $L_p$ values. Under asymmetric pumping, realized with Laguerre-Gaussian beams of different orbital angular momenta, chiral symmetry is broken in the system, resulting in asymmetric cavity field amplitudes, directional density modulations, and tunable rotational dynamics of the resulting supersolid lattice. This leads to rotating supersolid density structures for a single winding-number state, and rotating wave packets for an initial superposition of rotational eigenstates. Finally, we probe the presence of Goldstone and Higgs modes which can be observed using minimally destructive measurements of the cavity output spectrum. Our mean-field theory reveals interference-driven rotation without physical stirring, and distinguishes our work from prior static cavity supersolids. Our results establish the ring cavity annular BEC as a versatile platform for generating chiral quantum matter, implementing rotation-sensing devices and generating atomtronic circuits with supersolids.

### [146] [Dynamics of spinor Bose-Einstein condensates close to spin-spatial resonances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16732)
*W. Wills,D. Blume,Q. Guan*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个耦合通道框架来描述自旋玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（spinor BECs）的动力学，特别关注自旋动力学与空间激发之间共振附近的行为。该框架利用自旋相关和自旋无关散射长度的差异，通过Bogoliubov模式作为基函数，为不同长度尺度下的自旋BEC动力学提供了高效数值工具和清晰的物理解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自旋玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（spinor BECs）的动力学，特别关注自旋动力学与空间激发之间共振附近的行为。需要开发一个能够有效描述不同长度尺度下系统动力学的理论框架。

Method: 开发了一个耦合通道框架（coupled-channel framework），利用自旋相关和自旋无关散射长度的差异，将全系统哈密顿量中自旋无关部分的Bogoliubov模式作为描述系统动力学的有效基函数集。通过调节二次塞曼位移（quadratic Zeeman shift）来研究共振激发。

Result: 发现当二次塞曼位移远离任何共振时，系统在自旋动力学期间可以用单一空间波函数描述，即所谓的单模近似（single-mode approximation）成立。通过调节二次塞曼位移，发现了Bogoliubov模式的共振激发，这些激发可分为两类：具有粒子-空穴关联（particle-hole correlations）的和不具有粒子-空穴关联的。标准Bogoliubov理论中忽略的超二次项（beyond-quadratic-order terms）对于捕捉共振附近系统的长时间动力学变得越来越重要。

Conclusion: 该耦合通道框架不仅为描述由不同长度尺度支配的自旋BEC动力学提供了数值高效的工具，还为自旋BEC中的共振现象提供了清晰的物理解释。该方法可应用于其他系统，并可扩展到超越平均场（beyond-mean-field）领域。

Abstract: We develop a coupled-channel framework to describe the dynamics of spinor Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs), with particular emphasis on the behavior near resonances between spin dynamics and spatial excitations. Taking advantage of the disparity between the spin-dependent and spin-independent scattering lengths in typical spinor BECs, the Bogoliubov modes of the spin-independent part of the full system Hamiltonian provide an efficient set of basis functions for describing the system dynamics in a coupled-channel framework. For quadratic Zeeman shifts far from any resonance, the system can be described by a single spatial wavefunction during the spin dynamics, i.e., the so-called single-mode approximation holds. By tuning the quadratic Zeeman shift, we find resonant excitations of the Bogoliubov modes, which can be classified into two categories: those with particle-hole correlations and those without particle-hole correlations. We show that the beyond-quadratic-order terms that are neglected in standard Bogoliubov theories become increasingly important for capturing the long-time dynamics of the system near resonances. The coupled-channel framework is benchmarked against results from 1D Gross-Pitaevskii equation simulations. The framework developed in this work not only provides a numerically efficient tool for describing spinor BEC dynamics governed by different length scales, but also provides a clean physical interpretation of resonance phenomena in spinor BECs. Applications of this approach to other systems and extensions to the beyond-mean-field regime are also discussed.

</details>


### [147] [Scale invariance of the polaron energy at the Mott-superfluid critical point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17824)
*Matija Čufar,Ragheed Alhyder,C. J. Bradly,Victor E. Colussi,Georg M. Bruun,Joachim Brand,Alessio Recati*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子蒙特卡洛计算发现，弱相互作用移动杂质（mobile impurity）的能量可作为探测莫特绝缘体-超流体（Mott insulator-superfluid）量子相变临界行为的探针，其能量在临界点具有尺度不变性并揭示了一个理论尚未解释的标度指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续量子相变（continuous quantum phase transitions）通常通过序参数和相关函数来表征，但这些量在实验或数值模拟中往往难以直接获取。相比之下，杂质能量可通过极化子光谱（polaron spectroscopy）或蒙特卡洛方法进行探测。

Method: 采用基态量子蒙特卡洛（ground-state quantum Monte Carlo）计算，研究弱相互作用移动杂质与周围晶格玻色气体（lattice Bose gas）相互作用的能量。通过有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）分析能量在临界点的行为。

Result: 杂质能量在量子相变临界点呈现尺度不变性（scale invariant），并提取了一个理论尚未解释的标度指数（scaling exponent）。在小晶格系统中观察到杂质-玻色子密度-密度关联（impurity-boson density-density correlations）在临界点趋于平坦，暗示热力学极限下相应长度尺度的发散。

Conclusion: 杂质光谱（impurity spectroscopy）为探测量子相变临界性质提供了一种有效方法，这一发现具有普适意义，可推广到其他量子相变系统的研究中。

Abstract: Continuous quantum phase transitions are characterized by an order parameter and correlation functions that are often challenging to access experimentally or in direct numerical simulations. The energy of an added impurity can on the other hand be probed by established polaron spectroscopy, or numerically with Monte Carlo methods. We provide evidence from ground-state quantum Monte Carlo calculations that the energy of a mobile impurity interacting weakly with a surrounding lattice Bose gas provides access to the critical behavior of the Mott insulator-superfluid phase transition. Finite-size scaling of the energy reveals that its value is scale invariant at the critical point of the quantum phase transition, and we extract a scaling exponent that is currently unexplained by theory. For a small lattice we further observe a flattening of the impurity-boson density-density correlations at the critical point, which hints at a divergence of a corresponding length scale in the thermodynamic limit. Our results suggest that impurity spectroscopy represents a useful way to probe the critical properties of quantum phase transitions in general.

### [148] [Implosive Dynamics from Topological Quenches in Bose-Einstein Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17932)
*Marios Kokmotos,Dimitri M. Gangardt,Giovanni Barontini*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 通过拓扑淬火（topological quench）驱动排斥性玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（repulsive Bose-Einstein condensate）产生内爆动力学（implosive dynamics），实现从高电荷涡旋态到平凡扇区的突然转变，引发径向内流和中心密度积累。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用拓扑工程（topological engineering）作为研究量子流体（quantum fluids）中内爆动力学和对称性破缺不稳定性（symmetry-breaking instabilities）的新工具，特别是在排斥性相互作用下实现聚焦效应。

Method: 首先通过准绝热相位印刻（quasi-adiabatic phase imprinting）实现巨型涡旋（giant vortices），然后执行突然的反印刻（sudden anti-imprint）在单步中消除累积的缠绕数（winding），实现从高电荷涡旋态到平凡扇区（trivial sector）的直接拓扑淬火。

Result: 相位-密度失配引发快速径向内流（inward radial flow）和强烈的中心密度积累，存在初始缠绕数的清晰阈值；首次内爆后，动力学演化为圆形非线性波前，随后经历方位角对称性（axisymmetry）破缺，形成多边形结构，其形状由巨型涡旋构建方式决定。

Conclusion: 拓扑淬火能够驱动排斥性玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体产生内爆动力学，这些结果确立了拓扑工程作为研究量子流体中内爆动力学和对称性破缺不稳定性的新工具。

Abstract: We show numerically that a repulsive Bose-Einstein condensate can be driven into implosive dynamics by a direct topological quench. We first realize giant vortices by quasi-adiabatic phase imprinting, and then perform a sudden anti-imprint that cancels the accumulated winding in a single step, abruptly switching the condensate from a highly charged vortex state to the trivial sector. The resulting phase-density mismatch launches a rapid inward radial flow and produces a strong central density buildup, despite the repulsive interactions. We find a clear threshold in the initial winding for the onset of this focusing. After the first implosion, the dynamics evolves into circular nonlinear wave fronts that subsequently undergo breaking of azimuthal symmetry (axisymmetry) down to a polygonal one, whose shape is determined by the way the giant vortex is built. These results establish topological engineering as a new tool for studying implosive dynamics and symmetry-breaking instabilities in quantum fluids.

</details>


### [149] [Observation of low-lying impurity states in Bose-Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18033)
*A. M. Morgen,S. S. Balling,M. T. Strøe,T. G. Skov,M. R. Skou,K. K. Nielsen,A. Camacho-Guardian,G. M. Bruun,J. J. Arlt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过泵浦-探测弹出光谱技术（pump-probe ejection spectroscopy）研究嵌入39K原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中的杂质，发现除了预期的玻色极化子（Bose polaron）特征外，还存在显著低于极化子能量的低能信号，可能对应多玻色子激发的低能杂质态或由BEC介导的吸引相互作用形成的双极化子态（bipolaron）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）中杂质系统的光谱特性，特别是通过弹出光谱技术（ejection spectroscopy）揭示传统注入光谱（injection spectroscopy）未能观测到的低能态，以深入理解强相互作用下杂质与BEC的复杂耦合机制。

Method: 采用泵浦-探测弹出光谱序列（pump-probe ejection spectroscopy sequence）对嵌入39K原子BEC中的杂质进行光谱测量，系统研究了光谱信号随相互作用强度和泵浦-探测脉冲间演化时间的变化关系。

Result: 光谱信号显示出与先前注入光谱和理论一致的玻色极化子（Bose polaron）强特征，同时观测到显著低于极化子能量的光谱权重，该低能信号在注入光谱中不存在。低能信号的能量和光谱权重随相互作用强度和演化时间变化，与两种理论模型（多玻色子激发的低能杂质态和双极化子态）的预测进行比较。

Conclusion: 结果表明，在强相互作用条件下存在低于常规极化子的低能态，其中双极化子模型（bipolaron model）与观测到的光谱权重更为兼容。这些发现揭示了弱相互作用BEC的大压缩性（large compressibility）可能支持此类态的存在，需要进一步的实验研究来确认其性质。

Abstract: Impurities embedded in a Bose-Einstein Condensate (BEC) of 39K atoms are investigated with a pump-probe ejection spectroscopy sequence. The spectroscopic signal exhibits a strong feature corresponding to a Bose polaron in agreement with prior injection spectroscopy and theory. In addition, significant spectral weight at energies well below the energy of the polaron is observed, which is absent in injection spectroscopy. The energy and spectral weight of this signal are measured as a function of interaction strength and evolution time between the pump and probe pulses. We tentatively compare these results to two different theoretical models: a low-energy impurity state dressed by many bosonic excitations and a bipolaron state formed by two polarons due to attractive interactions mediated by the BEC. Such states can exist due to the large compressibility of the weakly interacting BEC. Both theories predict ejection spectra consistent with the low-energy signal, but only the bipolaron model is compatible with its spectral weight. These results indicate that lowenergy states below the usual polaron exist for strong interactions, calling for further experimental investigations

Method: 设计了包含紧凑模块化二维磁光阱（2D-MOT）源、科学室（science chamber）、精密真空内电极组件和高分辨率成像系统的真空系统。将双组分凝聚体（dual-species condensate）加载到垂直光学晶格（vertical optical lattice）的单层中制备二维气体混合物。

Conclusion: 该装置为研究量子杂质（quantum impurities）、量子液滴（quantum droplets）或低维极性分子（polar molecules）等多个有趣问题提供了多功能平台，拓展了低维量子系统的研究范围。

Abstract: Quantum gases confined in reduced dimensions have enabled the observation of many exotic quantum phenomena. While existing experiments primarily focus on homonuclear systems, we report here on the efficient preparation of a quasi-two-dimensional (2D) heteronuclear quantum degenerate mixture of ultracold $^{23}$Na and $^{87}$Rb. We describe the design of the vacuum system and detail the experimental procedures for preparing the 2D quantum mixture. The designed apparatus has several unique features, including compact and modular 2D-MOT sources, a science chamber that accommodates various lattice geometries, a precision in-vacuum electrode assembly, and high-resolution imaging for both atomic species. After loading the dual-species condensate into a single layer of a vertical optical lattice, we prepare a 2D gas mixture and observe quantum immiscibility in the in-situ equilibrium density profiles. The observed density profiles agree well with mean-field theories. The apparatus provides a versatile platform for investigating several interesting problems, including quantum impurities, quantum droplets, or polar molecules in low dimensions.

### [151] [Dynamics of one-dimensional Bose-Josephson Junction in a Box Trap: From Coherent Oscillations to Many-Body Dephasing and Dynamical Freezing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18165)
*Abhik Kumar Saha,L. F. Calazans de Brito,Rhombik Roy,Romain Dubessy,Barnali Chakrabarti,Arnaldo Gammal*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过多组态含时Hartree玻色子方法（MCTDHB）分析了一维盒势阱中玻色-约瑟夫森结的动力学，揭示了相互作用强度与初始布居数不平衡如何共同调控从相干振荡到关联主导行为的转变，包括退相干、平衡化和动力学冻结等不同机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解相干量子动力学如何在低维系统中演变为关联主导行为是量子多体物理的核心挑战。本研究旨在通过分析一维玻色-约瑟夫森结中相互作用与初始布居数不平衡的相互影响，揭示这一转变机制。

Method: 采用多组态含时Hartree玻色子方法（multiconfigurational time-dependent Hartree method for bosons, MCTDHB）研究一维盒势阱中玻色-约瑟夫森结的动力学行为，通过固定相互作用强度并改变初始布居数不平衡来探索不同动力学区域。

Result: 研究识别出多个由相干性与关联诱导碎裂（correlation-induced fragmentation）相互作用主导的动力学区域：弱相互作用下系统呈现相干约瑟夫森振荡，强初始不平衡导致阻尼；中等相互作用下，初始不平衡的变化引起动力学交叉，从近乎纯非碎裂振荡到多体退相干的塌缩-复苏行为，再到伴随强碎裂和可观测量饱和的平衡化；强相互作用下系统进入动力学冻结区域，密度呈现粒子分辨的分离峰且隧穿被强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一维约瑟夫森动力学中相干性、退相干、平衡化和动力学冻结如何出现并相互竞争的统一图像，阐明了量子多体系统中从相干动力学到关联主导行为的转变机制。

Abstract: Understanding how coherent quantum dynamics give way to correlation-dominated behavior in low-dimensional systems remains a central challenge in quantum many-body physics. Here, we address this problem by investigating the interplay of interactions and initial population imbalance in a one-dimensional Bose-Josephson junction confined in a box trap. Using the multiconfigurational time-dependent Hartree method for bosons (MCTDHB), we identify distinct dynamical regimes governed by the interplay between coherence and correlation-induced fragmentation. In the weakly interacting regime, the system exhibits coherent Josephson oscillations, while strong initial imbalance leads to damping. At intermediate interaction strength, fixing the interaction and varying only the initial imbalance, we uncover a crossover in the dynamics: very small imbalances yield nearly pure, non-fragmented oscillations; moderate imbalances induce many-body dephasing with collapse-and-revival behavior; and large imbalances drive equilibration accompanied by strong fragmentation and saturation of many-body observables, including orbital entropy and participation ratio. In the strongly interacting regime, the system enters a dynamical freezing regime characterized by pronounced fragmentation, where the density develops well-separated, particle-resolved peaks and tunneling is strongly suppressed. These results establish a unified picture of how coherence, dephasing, equilibration, and dynamical freezing emerge and compete in one-dimensional Josephson dynamics.

### [152] [Phonon number relaxation in a 3D superfluid with a concave acoustic branch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18298)
*Yvan Castin,Mariia Tsimokha*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究分析了三维超流体中声子气体通过多声子碰撞向热化学平衡演化的动力学过程，特别关注了五声子碰撞在实现完全平衡中的关键作用及其时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于理解超流体中声子气体向完全热化学平衡演化的动力学过程。由于三声子碰撞被能量-动量守恒禁止，而四声子碰撞仅能实现部分平衡，需要研究更慢的五声子碰撞机制来完成平衡过程。

Method: 研究方法包括使用声子模式占据数的动力学方程，并通过低温量子流体力学（quantum hydrodynamics）显式计算2φ→3φ碰撞振幅。通过总能量守恒分析声子气体的逸度演化。

Result: 研究发现逸度在短时间遵循非整数幂律∝t^{4/5}，长时间呈指数规律变化。熵变化速率始终为正，且渐近正比于逸度变化速率的平方，符合朗道（Landau）对任意缓慢绝热变换的预测。

Conclusion: 该研究完成了Khalatnikov于1950年开启的课题，相关结果可在BCS-BEC交叉（BEC-BCS crossover）的冷费米原子气体或高压超流液氦-4中进行实验验证。

Abstract: We consider the collisional evolution towards equilibrium of a spatially homogeneous and isotropic phonon gas of a three-dimensional superfluid with a concave acoustic excitation branch, at a non-zero but arbitrarily low temperature $T$. Three-phonon collisions $1φ\leftrightarrow 2φ$ are forbidden by conservation of energy-momentum. Four-phonon collisions $2φ\to 2φ$ of Landau and Khalatnikov lead, after a time $\propto T^{-7}$, only to a partial thermal equilibrium, a Bose law of non-zero chemical potential for the phonons, because they conserve the total number of phonons. Relaxation towards complete thermochemical equilibrium is therefore ensured by the much slower five-phonon collisions $2φ\leftrightarrow 3φ$ of Khalatnikov, in a time $\propto T^{-9}$. Using kinetic equations on the occupation numbers of the phonon modes and explicitly calculating the $2φ\to 3φ$ collisional amplitude with quantum hydrodynamics at low temperature, we determine the corresponding evolution of the fugacity $z_φ$ of the phonon gas from the non-degenerate regime $z_φ=0^+$ to complete equilibrium $z_φ=1^-$. Using the conservation of total energy, we find that the fugacity varies with a non-integer power law $\propto t^{4/5}$ at short times and an exponential law at long times; the speed of change of entropy, always positive, is asymptotically proportional to the square of the speed of change of fugacity, $(\mathrm{d}/\mathrm{d}t)S_φ\propto[(\mathrm{d}/\mathrm{d}t)z_φ]^2$, as Landau predicted for an arbitrarily slow adiabatic transformation. Our results bring to a close the study initiated by Khalatnikov in 1950 and could be experimentally verified in a gas of cold fermionic atoms on the BCS side of the BEC-BCS crossover, or in superfluid liquid helium-4 at sufficiently high pressure.

</details>


### [153] [Quantum quenches in a spin-1 chain with tunable symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18425)
*Luis Eduardo Ramos-Solís,Sayan Choudhury,Freddy Jackson Poveda-Cuevas,Eduardo Ibarra-García-Padilla*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，远离平衡态的相互作用量子系统动力学引起了广泛研究兴趣。随着量子模拟器的快速发展，各种非平衡现象已在实验中得到实现，需要理论框架来理解和预测这些现象。

Method: 采用时间演化块解耦（time-evolving block decimation, TEBD）方法研究各向异性自旋-1海森堡链的动力学。通过调节控制四极相互作用强度的参数J_q，系统可从非可积SU(2)海森堡模型连续变化到可积SU(3)海森堡模型。

Result: 研究了局域磁化、纠缠熵和自旋关联，并表征了它们对J_q的依赖性。在SU(3)对称点识别出新的守恒量，并建立了理论框架，用该守恒定律允许的可达态数量来解释数值观测结果。

Conclusion: 研究结果为在自旋-1晶格模型中实现丰富的非平衡行为提供了途径，这些模型可在多种实验平台（如光晶格中的超冷原子）中实现工程化设计。

Abstract: In recent years, the dynamics of interacting quantum systems far from equilibrium have attracted significant research interest. Driven by rapid progress in quantum simulators, various non-equilibrium phenomena have now been realized experimentally. In this work, we use the time-evolving block decimation (TEBD) method to investigate the dynamics of an anisotropic spin-1 Heisenberg chain for a wide range of experimentally accessible initial states. By adjusting the parameter $J_q$ that controls the quadrupolar interaction strength, we can tune the system from a non-integrable SU(2) Heisenberg model to an integrable SU(3) Heisenberg model. We examine the local magnetization, entanglement entropy, and spin correlations, and characterize their dependence on $J_q$. We identify a new conserved quantity at the SU(3) symmetric point and provide a theoretical framework to explain our numerical observations in terms of the number of accessible states permitted by this conservation law. Our results provide a route to realize a rich array of non-equilibrium behavior in spin-1 lattice models, which can be engineered in several experimental platforms such as ultracold atoms in optical lattices.

### [154] [Fermion Zero Modes and Fermion number $1/2$ of the Electroweak Monopole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16673)
*P. E. Mogaddam,S. S. Gousheh*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了电弱SU(2)单极子背景下费米子束缚态的性质，分析了不同耦合常数对零模波函数的影响，证明了费米子谱的镜像对称性并推断出电弱单极子具有1/2费米子数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究电弱SU(2)单极子背景下费米子束缚态的性质，特别是分析规范耦合常数$g$、希格斯自耦合常数$λ$和汤川耦合常数$y_q$对束缚态行为的影响。

Method: 通过数值求解参数空间中选定点处的耦合微分方程组，并对零模（zero mode）进行解析论证。分析单极子轮廓函数和零模波函数随耦合常数的变化规律。

Result: 数值解仅显示存在零模；单极子轮廓函数和零模波函数随$g$和$λ$增大而更加局域化；零模的右旋分量随$g$减小但随$y_q$增大。$g\to 0$极限下的零模与仅由希格斯场产生的零模不同，体现了系统的非线性和非微扰特性。

Conclusion: 证明了费米子的谱镜像对称性（spectral mirror symmetry），结合零模的存在性，推断出电弱单极子具有1/2费米子数（fermion number $1/2$）。

Abstract: Fermion bound states in the background of the electroweak SU(2) monopole are investigated for various values of gauge coupling constant $g$, the Higgs self-coupling constant $λ$, and the Yukawa coupling constant $y_q$. Numerical solutions to the set of coupled differential equations for various selected points in the parameter space reveal only a zero mode, for which we also present an analytic argument. We show that the monopole profile functions and the zero mode wave function become more localized with increasing $g$ and $λ$, while the right-handed component of the latter decreases with $g$. However, as expected, this component increases with $y_q$. We find that the zero mode in the limit $g\to 0$ differs from the zero mode held by the Higgs alone, highlighting the nonlinear and nonperturbative character of the system. Finally, we prove the spectral mirror symmetry of the fermion, whence, together with the existence of the zero mode, we infer the fermion number $1/2$ of the electroweak monopole.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Lin-Maldacena几何类的经典探针方法，使用质量点粒子探针，其固有动量等于矩阵模型中规范不变算子的尺寸。运用静电学方法和背景通量方法处理BMN平面波矩阵模型。

Abstract: We compute the rate of growth of operator size in matrix models by probing the Lin-Maldacena class of geometries with classical probes. We consider massive point particle probes whose proper momentum equals the size of the gauge invariant operator in the matrix model. We work out the example of the BMN Plane Wave Matrix Model using the electrostatic approach and the method of background fluxes. We also work out complexities in the D2 brane as well as NS5 brane limits of the BMN matrix model along with an example of the irrelevant deformation namely the non-Abelian T-dual of $AdS_5 \times S^5$. Finally, we carry out a possible calculation of the Krylov complexity on the matrix model counterpart by using a simple reduction ansatz known as the pulsating fuzzy sphere model. We outline an algorithm to define Krylov basis elements for the matrix model and compute a few Lanczos coefficients. Our analysis reveals that both the Krylov basis states as well as Lanczos coefficients are uniquely fixed in terms of the mass parameter of the matrix model.

### [156] [Bubble dynamics and vortex formation in holographic first-order superfluid phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17216)
*Zhen-han Jin,Yu-ping An,Li Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过全息超流体（holographic superfluid）模型探究一阶相变中的气泡动力学，发现临界行为由单一不稳定模主导，多气泡碰撞中的涡旋形成显著偏离测地线规则（geodesic rule），并识别出三气泡碰撞产生随后湮灭的涡旋-反涡旋对的新现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究具有自发U(1)对称性破缺的一阶相变中气泡动力学的非平衡行为，特别关注强耦合超流体中拓扑缺陷形成的机制，这些过程在传统平衡态理论框架下难以完全描述。

Method: 采用全息超流体模型研究一阶相变，分析气泡成核阈值附近的临界行为，考察多气泡碰撞过程中的涡旋形成机制，并与测地线规则进行对比。

Result: 研究发现：1) 成核阈值附近存在由单一不稳定模主导的普适临界行为，导致接近临界解的时间呈对数标度；2) 终端气泡壁速度随电荷密度增加但保持较小值；3) 多气泡碰撞中涡旋形成对初始相位敏感，显著偏离测地线规则；4) 三气泡碰撞可产生随后湮灭的涡旋-反涡旋对，其寿命与临界碰撞半径距离呈对数标度关系。

Conclusion: 研究结论强调非平衡动力学在强耦合超流体一阶相变中的关键作用，为拓扑缺陷形成机制提供了新见解，特别是揭示了测地线规则无法预测的涡旋-反涡旋对产生与湮灭现象。

Abstract: We investigate bubble dynamics in a holographic superfluid undergoing a first-order phase transition with spontaneous $U(1)$ symmetry breaking. Near the nucleation threshold, the system exhibits universal critical behavior governed by a single unstable mode, leading to logarithmic scaling of the time spent near the critical solution. The terminal bubble wall velocity increases with charge density but remains small due to strong dissipation. In multi-bubble collisions, vortex formation depends sensitively on the initial phases and deviates significantly from the geodesic rule. Notably, we identify a regime where three-bubble collisions produce a vortex-antivortex pair that subsequently annihilates, a phenomenon not predicted by the geodesic rule. The lifetime of this pair scales logarithmically with the distance to the critical collision radius. Our results underscore the crucial role of non-equilibrium dynamics in strongly coupled superfluids and provide new insights into topological defect formation during first-order phase transitions.

</details>


### [157] [Refined 3D index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17449)
*Dongmin Gang,Kibok Jeong,Taeyoon Kim,Soochang Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三维流形（3-manifold）的精细化3D指数（refined 3D index），该指数基于Dimofte-Gaiotto-Gukov和Gang-Yonekura构建的3D $\mathcal{N}=2$规范理论$T[M]$，通过引入额外分级来捕捉有效理论的增强味对称性（enhanced flavor symmetries）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于构建比现有3D指数更精细的不变量，以更好地区分三维流形及其相关规范理论的不同红外（IR）相。现有指数在区分能力上存在局限，需要引入额外结构来捕捉理论的更多对称性信息。

Method: 方法基于Dehn手术（Dehn surgery）表示，将三维流形$M$表示为理想三角剖分（ideally triangulated）的链环补（link complement）$N$。通过该表示推导出精细化指数的显式无穷和公式，并开发了计算工具\textsc{Refined Index Calculator}进行具体计算。

Result: 获得了精细化3D指数的显式公式，并在代表性示例中进行了非平凡验证。结果表明该指数在三角剖分变化、Dehn手术表示变化及其他辅助数据变化下保持不变，且作为严格更强的不变量，能够对三维流形及相关规范理论的不同红外相进行更精细的区分。

Conclusion: 本文成功构建了三维流形的精细化3D指数，该指数基于3D $\mathcal{N}=2$规范理论$T[M]$的超共形指数（superconformal index），通过引入额外分级增强了区分能力。开发的计算工具为具体计算提供了实用手段，该精细化指数在三维拓扑和规范理论研究中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: We introduce a refined version of the 3D index for 3-manifolds, building on the construction of the 3D $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theory $T[M]$ by Dimofte-Gaiotto-Gukov and Gang-Yonekura. The refined index is a superconformal index of $T[M]$ equipped with additional gradings that capture enhanced flavor symmetries of the effective theory. Our construction is based on a Dehn surgery presentation of $M$ in terms of an ideally triangulated link complement $N$. We derive an explicit infinite-sum formula for the refined index and provide nontrivial checks in representative examples, supporting its invariance under changes of triangulation, Dehn surgery presentation, and other auxiliary data. As a strictly stronger invariant, the refined index enables finer distinctions among 3-manifolds and among distinct IR phases of the associated gauge theories. We also introduce a computational tool, \textsc{Refined Index Calculator}, for its explicit evaluation.

Abstract: The coadjoint orbit action for a multifermion system, as an exact description of its dynamics, is considered. ### [159] [Electromagnetic Wightman functions and vacuum densities for a brane intersecting the AdS boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17583)
*A. A. Saharian,R. M. Avagyan,V. F. Manukyan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了AdS时空中膜（brane）与背景引力场对电磁真空局域特性的联合效应，分析了两种边界条件（PEC和PMC）下膜对真空期望值（VEVs）的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究AdS时空中膜与背景引力场对电磁真空局域特性的联合影响。特别关注膜的存在如何改变真空期望值（VEVs），包括电场和磁场的平方期望值以及能量-动量张量。

Method: 研究方法考虑了两种边界条件：完美电导体（PEC）和完美磁导体（PMC）边界条件的高维推广。通过提取膜对Wightman函数的贡献，并利用标量场类比来模拟真空期望值的行为，其中标量场的有效质量平方由AdS时空半径决定。

Result: 研究发现膜对真空期望值的贡献在PEC和PMC条件下符号相反。对于PMC条件，膜对电场平方的贡献为负，对磁场平方的贡献为正。能量-动量张量存在非零的非对角分量，且PMC条件下的真空能量密度为正。与Minkowski时空中的平面边界问题不同，在(3+1)维AdS时空中真空能量-动量张量不为零。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，AdS时空中膜的存在显著改变了电磁真空的局域特性，膜诱导的贡献在PEC和PMC条件下呈现相反的符号特征。与Minkowski时空相比，AdS时空中的真空能量-动量张量具有非平凡结构，这反映了背景引力场与膜边界的相互作用。

Abstract: We investigate the combined effects of a brane intersecting the AdS boundary and background gravitational field on the local characteristics of the electromagnetic vacuum. Two types of boundary conditions on the brane are considered, which are higher-dimensional generalizations of the perfect electric (PEC) and perfect magnetic (PMC) boundary conditions in Maxwell's electrodynamics. The brane-induced contributions to the Wightman functions of the vector potential and field tensor are explicitly extracted. Simple expressions in terms of elementary functions are provided. The behavior of the vacuum expectation values (VEVs) is mimicked by a scalar field with a negative effective mass squared determined by the radius of the AdS spacetime. The expectation values of the electric and magnetic fields squares and of the energy-momentum tensor are investigated as local characteristics of the vacuum state. The brane-induced contributions to these VEVs have opposite signs for the PEC and PMC conditions. For the PMC condition, this contribution is negative for the electric field squared and positive for the magnetic field squared. The VEV of the energy-momentum tensor has a nonzero off-diagonal component. The brane-induced vacuum energy density is positive for PMC condition, whereas the normal and parallel stresses change sign as functions of the distance from the brane. Unlike the problem involving a planar boundary in the Minkowski bulk, the vacuum energy-momentum tensor does not vanish in (3+1)-dimensional AdS spacetime.

### [160] [Holography and Optimal Transport: Emergent Wasserstein Spacetime in Harmonic Oscillator, SYK and Krylov Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17649)
*Koji Hashimoto,Norihiro Tanahashi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究从机器学习中的流形假设（manifold hypothesis）视角出发，探讨全息时空如何通过最优输运（optimal transport）从量子系统中作为Wasserstein空间涌现。以单量子谐振子为例，发现流形假设选择Husimi Q表示的1-Wasserstein距离，并产生涌现空间。Lindblad时间演化在Wasserstein空间中形成轨迹，产生具有黑洞时空性质的涌现Wasserstein时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用最优输运（optimal transport）和Wasserstein距离作为量化概率分布空间的主要工具。以单量子谐振子为简单示例，研究不同距离定义下流形假设如何选择Husimi Q表示的1-Wasserstein距离。通过Lindblad时间演化（形式为Fokker-Planck方程）分析谐振子与热库耦合，获得Wasserstein空间中的时间轨迹。该方法进一步应用于SYK模型的Lindbladian子系统。

Result: 研究发现流形假设选择Husimi Q表示的1-Wasserstein距离作为涌现空间的基础。Lindblad时间演化在Wasserstein空间中产生时间轨迹，形成具有黑洞时空和事件视界性质的涌现Wasserstein时空。在SYK模型应用中，Wasserstein空间与标准全息字典中的AdS₂黑洞几何一致。此外，1-Wasserstein距离被识别为广义Krylov复杂度（generalized Krylov complexity）。

Conclusion: 研究表明最优输运结合流形假设能够产生一般的涌现时空，将全息原理置于更广泛的基础上。该方法为理解量子系统如何涌现出具有黑洞性质的时空结构提供了新视角，建立了Wasserstein距离与量子复杂度之间的重要联系。

Abstract: Optimal transport and Wasserstein distance are prominent tools to quantify the space of probability distributions. From a novel viewpoint of manifold hypothesis in machine learning being a possible guide for the holographic principle, we study how holographic spacetime can emerge from quantum systems in general as a Wasserstein space through optimal transport. We employ the simplest example of a single quantum harmonic oscillator and demonstrate that, among various definitions of distance, the manifold hypothesis selects the 1-Wasserstein distance of optimal transport between Husimi Q-representations of states, and it gives rise to an emergent space. Furthermore, the Lindblad time evolution of the harmonic oscillator coupled to a bath, of the form of a Fokker-Planck equation, provides a time trajectory in the Wasserstein space, yielding an emergent Wasserstein spacetime that shares properties with black hole spacetimes and their event horizons. The methodology is applied to a Lindbladian subsystem of SYK model, revealing that the Wasserstein space is consistent with the AdS${}_2$ black hole geometry of the standard holographic dictionary. We remark that, in our examples, the 1-Wasserstein distance is identified as a generalized Krylov complexity, and argue that optimal transport with the manifold hypothesis can yield general emergent spacetimes, positioning the holographic principle on a broader basis.

### [161] [Holographic Schwinger Effect In a Step Dilaton Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17743)
*Sara Tahery,Qin Chang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究在具有阶梯状伸缩子（step dilaton）轮廓的禁闭背景下，分析了全息施温格效应（holographic Schwinger effect）。研究发现，与平滑软壁模型相比，阶梯状伸缩子背景对外部电磁场表现出更强的响应，为控制夸克-反夸克对产生提供了新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于从基本弦（fundamental string）的经典构型中提取夸克-反夸克势，直接分析真空不稳定性和对产生。通过狄拉克-玻恩-英费尔德（Dirac-Born-Infeld）作用量引入外部磁场，研究电磁场对势垒的变形效应。

Result: 无磁场时，阶梯状伸缩子导致势垒随电场增加而显著更急剧地被抑制，表明临界电场（critical electric field）的敏感性增强。加入外部磁场后，势垒出现非平凡且放大的变形，导致临界电场发生显著偏移，该偏移取决于磁场的大小和方向。

Conclusion: 阶梯状伸缩子背景对施温格效应对外部电磁场的响应比传统软壁模型强得多，为控制对产生提供了新机制，并突显了伸缩子结构在全息QCD非微扰动力学中的关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the holographic Schwinger effect in a confining background with a step dilaton profile, which induces a sharp transition between ultraviolet and infrared regimes and provides a qualitatively distinct realization of confinement. Within this framework, the quark--antiquark potential is extracted from the classical configuration of a fundamental string, allowing for a direct analysis of vacuum instability and pair production. In the absence of a magnetic field, the step dilaton leads to a significantly sharper suppression of the potential barrier as the electric field increases, implying an enhanced sensitivity of the critical electric field compared to smooth soft-wall models and demonstrating that the abrupt geometric transition qualitatively enhances the onset of vacuum decay. Incorporating an external magnetic field through the Dirac--Born--Infeld action, we find a nontrivial and amplified deformation of the potential barrier, resulting in a pronounced shift of the critical electric field that depends on both the magnitude and orientation of the magnetic field. Overall, the step dilaton background exhibits a substantially stronger response of the Schwinger effect to external electromagnetic fields than conventional soft-wall models, providing a novel mechanism for controlling pair production and highlighting the crucial role of dilaton structure in non-perturbative dynamics of holographic QCD.

Starting from the spindle solutions of five-dimensional STU gauged supergravity, we construct theories on a spindle which preserve supersymmetry via either the twist or anti-twist mechanism and admit two Killing spinors of opposite R-charge. Motivation: 主要动机源于单圈标量自能仅包含共形不变的费米子，而两圈图包含内部标量线会破坏共形不变性，预期将导致红外对数发散（infrared secular logarithms）的出现。

Method: 在暴胀德西特时空中对Yukawa理论进行两圈计算，执行了自能的重整化（renormalisation），并以初始Bunch-Davies真空为基准计算了圈修正的共位两点关联函数$\langle φ^2\rangle$。

Result: 标量自能中紫外（UV）自能的晚期贡献主导红外（IR）贡献；单圈和两圈下$\langle φ^2\rangle$的领头行为分别为$\ln^3 a$和$\ln^4 a$，这些是紫外与红外对数的混合；重求和表达式有界且随Yukawa耦合增大单调减小。

Conclusion: 研究证实了标量自能中红外对数发散的出现，并表明重求和的$\langle φ^2\rangle$有界且随耦合增大单调减小，相应地动态生成的标量质量随耦合增大而增加。

Abstract: We have considered the Yukawa theory at two loop in the inflationary de Sitter spacetime, for a massless minimally coupled scalar and a massless fermion. The one loop computation for the same has been investigated in detail in the earlier literatures. The chief motivation behind this study is the fact that at one loop, the scalar self energy contains only fermions, which are conformally invariant. At two loop, there are two diagrams, each containing one internal scalar line, thereby breaking the conformal invariance. This should result in the appearance of infrared secular logarithms in the scalar self energy. The renormalisation of this two loop self energy has been performed. We next compute the loop corrected coincident two point correlation function, $\langle φ^2\rangle$, due to the self energies. The expectation value has been taken with respect to the initial Bunch-Davies vacuum. We argue that the late time secular contribution from the local or UV self energy must dominate the non-local or IR ones in the present case, from the point of view of the powers of these large logarithms of the scale factor. This corresponds to the fact that fermion lines do not show any IR secular effect. The leading behaviour of $\langle φ^2\rangle$ at one and two loop are respectively found to be $\ln^3 a$ and $\ln^4 a$. These are hybrids of UV and IR logarithms, where the latter originate from the massless and minimal two external scalar lines. A resummed expression for $\langle φ^2\rangle$ has also been computed. The same is found to be bounded and decreasing monotonically with the increasing magnitude of the Yukawa coupling. Accordingly, the dynamically generated scalar mass increases with the increasing coupling.

</details>


### [165] [On the frame-like multispinor formalism for massive higher spins in d=4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18114)
*Yu. M. Zinoviev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文填补了高自旋（higher spin）文献中的空白，为d=4维度下的大质量（massive）高自旋场提供了显式的框架式（frame-like）、规范不变（gauge invariant）描述，并给出了任意整数和半整数自旋的显式解。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高自旋文献存在一些空白，需要为d=4维度下的大质量高自旋场提供显式的框架式、规范不变描述。这包括解决壳上约束（on-shell constraints）的问题，并为任意整数和半整数自旋提供系统解决方案。

Method: 从大质量自旋2和自旋5/2作为简单示例开始，然后推广到任意整数和半整数自旋。采用框架式、规范不变的描述方法，并显式求解壳上约束条件。

Result: 成功获得了d=4维度下大质量高自旋场的显式框架式、规范不变描述。该结果还能用于求解所谓的展开方程（unfolded equations），这些方程决定了壳上非零的所有物理场高阶导数。

Conclusion: 本文填补了高自旋理论文献的重要空白，为d=4维度下的大质量高自旋场提供了完整的框架式、规范不变描述，并展示了如何利用该结果求解展开方程，从而确定壳上所有非零的高阶导数。

Abstract: In this paper, we fill some gap in the existing literature on higher spins by presenting an explicit solution to the on-shell constraints for a frame-like, gauge invariant description of massive, higher spin fields in d=4. We begin with the massive spin 2 and massive spin 5/2 as simple illustrations, and then consider arbitrary integer and half-integer spin. We also show that our results allow us to find explicit solutions to the so-called unfolded equations that determine all higher-order derivatives of the physical field that are non-zero on-shell.

### [166] [Large-$N$ Dynamics of a QCD-Inspired Unitary Matrix Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18182)
*Anuj Malik*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究分析了受QCD启发的U(N)和SU(N)酉矩阵模型的大N极限，分别在实势（μ=0）和复势（有限μ）两种情况下，揭示了模型在无间隙相和有间隙相的不同行为及其相变特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究受量子色动力学（QCD）启发的酉矩阵模型，旨在理解其在实势和复势两种情况下的相结构，特别是复作用量如何驱动特征值进入复平面并导致对称性破缺。

Method: 采用大N极限分析U(N)和SU(N)酉矩阵模型，分别在μ=0（实势）和有限μ（复势）两种情况下进行研究。对于无间隙相（ungapped phase）获得解析解，对于有间隙相（gapped phase）则结合部分解析和数值方法求解。

Result: 在无间隙相获得了谱密度（spectral density）、威尔逊圈（Wilson loops）和自由能的解析表达式，重现了QCD的低温行为。发现复作用量导致特征值进入复平面，产生⟨U⟩≠⟨U⁻¹⟩的不对称性。μ=0时存在三阶相变，有限μ时则呈现至少二阶的连续相变。

Conclusion: 该酉矩阵模型成功捕捉了QCD的关键特征，特别是在复势情况下揭示了对称性破缺和相变行为，为理解QCD相结构提供了有价值的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the large-$N$ limit of $U(N)$ and $SU(N)$ unitary matrix models inspired by QCD. The model is analyzed in two cases: $μ= 0$, where the potential is real, and finite $μ$, where it becomes complex. The complex action drives the eigenvalues into the complex plane, leading to $\langle U \rangle \neq \langle U^{-1} \rangle$. In the ungapped phase, we obtain analytic expressions for the spectral density, Wilson loops, and free energy, which reproduce the low-temperature behaviour of QCD. In contrast, the gapped phase involves a nontrivial resolvent and is solved partially analytically and numerically. At $μ=0$, the model exhibits a $3^{rd}$ order phase transition, while at finite $μ$, it shows a continuous phase transition of at least second order.

### [168] [Large-c BCFT Entanglement Entropy with Deformed Boundaries from Emergent JT Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18405)
*Dominik Neuenfeld,Christopher Tellinger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了边界形变对二维边界共形场论（BCFT）中von Neumann熵的影响，并建立了形变边界熵与未形变BCFT中岛屿熵的对应关系，揭示了二维引力理论与高中心荷极限下BCFT的深层联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究边界形变如何影响二维边界共形场论（boundary conformal field theories, BCFTs）中子区域的von Neumann熵，特别是在零温和有限温度条件下。这种形变可视为边界位移算符（boundary displacement operator）引起的微扰效应。

Method: 研究方法采用无穷小全局共形变换（infinitesimal global conformal transformations）来移动边界，并考虑大中心荷（large central charge）极限。通过将BCFT与受Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）引力支配的AdS₂区域以透明边界条件（transparent boundary conditions）连接，分析形变边界熵与未形变BCFT中岛屿熵（island entropy）的对应关系。

Result: 研究结果表明，在形变边界存在的情况下，von Neumann熵可由未形变BCFT中相同区间的岛屿熵再现。这一对应关系要求BCFT谱和OPE系数满足温和条件，这些条件与指数大量轻算子（exponentially large number of light operators）的存在一致，比全息BCFTs的要求更弱。

Conclusion: 结论指出，BCFT结果并非由具有O(1)数量物质场的三维引力计算再现，而是由具有O(c)数量轻场的二维计算实现。这揭示了二维引力理论与高中心荷极限下BCFT的深层联系，其中膨胀子场（dilaton field）的边界条件由BCFT计算中的边界形变设定。

Abstract: We study the effect of boundary deformations on the von Neumann entropy of subregions in two-dimensional boundary conformal field theories (BCFTs) at zero and finite temperature. The deformations considered are infinitesimal global conformal transformations that move the boundary and can equivalently be viewed as the leading-order effect of certain BCFT perturbations with the boundary displacement operator. We demonstrate that at large central charge the von Neumann entropy in the presence of a deformed boundary is reproduced by the island entropy of the same interval in an undeformed BCFT acting as a bath and coupled to a gravitating spacetime. Here, the BCFT is joined to an AdS$_2$ region governed by Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity via transparent boundary conditions. The boundary condition for the dilaton field is set by the boundary deformation in the BCFT computation. Our analysis relies on mild assumptions about the spectrum and OPE coefficients of the BCFT. Notably, these conditions are consistent with an exponentially large number of light operators and are therefore weaker than those required for holographic BCFTs. This is possible since the BCFT result is not reproduced by a gravitational computation in three dimensions with an O(1) number of matter fields, but instead by a computation in two dimensions and with an O(c) number of light fields.

</details>


### [169] [Classical and quantum evolution of inflationary fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18416)
*Guillermo Ballesteros,Jesús Gambín Egea,Alejandro Pérez Rodríguez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究比较了暴胀扰动（inflationary perturbations）的量子与经典动力学计算的相关函数，发现即使两者在暴胀特定时刻被强制一致，只要相互作用相关，它们在暴胀结束时仍会存在差异，且差异随e-折叠数（e-folds）呈指数敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于比较暴胀扰动的量子与经典动力学计算的相关函数差异，特别关注即使两者在特定时间被强制一致，相互作用如何导致它们在暴胀结束时产生分歧。

Method: 研究方法包括比较量子与经典动力学的相关函数计算，分析两者差异对e-折叠数的指数敏感性，并以原初曲率扰动（primordial curvature fluctuation）的树级双谱（tree-level bispectrum）和张量模式（tensor modes）的单圈功率谱（one-loop power spectrum）为例进行说明。

Result: 研究结果表明，量子与经典相关函数在暴胀结束时存在差异，且该差异对从一致时刻起经过的e-折叠数呈指数敏感。同时证明，从有限时间开始的经典演化不会导致标量双谱（scalar bispectrum）中出现极点（poles）。

Conclusion: 结论指出，在暴胀扰动计算中，即使量子与经典动力学在特定时刻被强制一致，只要相互作用相关，它们在暴胀结束时仍会产生显著差异，且差异随e-折叠数指数增长，但经典演化不会在标量双谱中引入极点。

Abstract: We compare the correlation functions of inflationary perturbations computed either with quantum or classical dynamics. Even if they are enforced to agree at a specific time during inflation, classical and quantum correlations will differ at the end of inflation, provided that interactions are relevant. The difference between the results of the classical and quantum computations is exponentially sensitive to the number of e-folds elapsed from the time of agreement. We illustrate this finding with the tree-level bispectrum of the primordial curvature fluctuation and the one-loop power spectrum of tensor modes. We also show that classical evolution from a finite time does not imply the appearance of poles in the scalar bispectrum.

### [172] [Two New Molecular Nitrogen Phases near Megabar Pressures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16641)
*Alexander F. Goncharov,Elena Bykova,Iskander Batyrev,Maxim Bykov,Huawei Chen,William Palfey,Mahmood Mohammad,Stella Chariton,Vitali Prakapenka,Jesse S. Smith*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究在78-98 GPa高压下通过激光加热ζ-N₂合成了两种新的分子氮相：tζ-N₂（单斜C2/c结构的多型体，c轴三倍化，96原子/晶胞）和ξ-N₂（六方P6cc结构，112原子/晶胞）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在金刚石对顶砧（diamond anvil cell）中，通过激光加热ζ-N₂至1800-2500 K，压力为78-98 GPa。使用单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal X-ray diffraction）确定晶体结构，辅以拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）验证，并通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）支持。

Result: 成功合成了两种新相：tζ-N₂是单斜C2/c ζ-N₂的多型体，具有三倍化的c轴和96原子/晶胞；ξ-N₂是先前未报道的六方相（P6cc），包含112原子/晶胞。tζ-N₂很可能对应于先前报道的κ-N₂相。

Conclusion: 该研究发现了两种新的高压分子氮相，扩展了对氮在聚合转变附近结构多样性的认识，为理解氮的高压相图提供了新信息。

Abstract: Molecular nitrogen exhibits remarkable structural diversity near the polymeric transition, where multiple phases are metastable. Here, we report two new molecular phases. The first, $tζ$-N$_2$, is a polytype of monoclinic $C2/c$ $ζ$-N$_2$, characterized by a tripled $c$ axis and 96 atoms per unit cell. The second, $ξ$-N$_2$, is a previously unreported hexagonal phase ($P6cc$) containing 112 atoms per unit cell. Both phases were synthesized in a diamond anvil cell by laser heating $ζ$-N$_2$ to 1800--2500~K at pressures of 78--98~GPa. Their crystal structures were determined using single-crystal X-ray diffraction, corroborated by Raman spectroscopy, and supported by first-principles calculations. The $tζ$-N$_2$ phase likely corresponds to the previously reported $κ$-N$_2$ phase.

### [173] [On the Energy Dissipation in the Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16938)
*Kutay Kulbak,Mohamed Iyad Boualem,Charlie Masse,Mariana Delalibera de Toledo,Vasily V. Temnov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究在Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert框架下分析了铁磁纳米磁体中磁化强度在稳定平衡点附近的动力学行为，重点关注小角度进动时铁磁共振频率、阻尼常数和品质因子Q对自由能最小值附近局部曲率的依赖关系，特别研究了分岔点附近FMR衰减时间的行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究铁磁纳米磁体中磁化动力学的动机在于深入理解铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）频率、阻尼常数和品质因子Q对自由能最小值附近局部曲率的系统依赖性，特别是在分岔点（bifurcation points）附近，传统近似Q≈1/2α失效的情况。

Method: 研究方法基于Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert（LLG）理论框架，分析小角度进动（small angle precession）条件下铁磁纳米磁体的动力学行为，系统研究FMR参数对自由能最小值附近局部曲率的依赖关系。

Result: 研究结果表明，铁磁共振频率、阻尼常数和品质因子Q均与自由能最小值附近的局部曲率存在系统性依赖关系，特别揭示了在分岔点附近FMR衰减时间的行为特征，此时传统近似Q≈1/2α（其中α为Gilbert阻尼）不再适用。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了铁磁纳米磁体在LLG框架下的动力学行为，建立了FMR参数与自由能最小值局部曲率的定量关系，特别强调了在分岔点附近传统品质因子近似失效的情况，为理解铁磁共振的微观机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: The dynamics of magnetization near a stable equilibrium in ferromagnetic nanomagnets are examined within the Landau--Lifshitz--Gilbert (LLG) framework. For a small angle precession, the dependence of ferromagnetic resonance (FMR) frequency, the damping constant and the resulting quality factor $Q$ of the resonance on the local curvature around the free-energy minimum is systematically analyzed. Special attention is devoted to the behavior of the FMR decay time in the vicinity of bifurcation points, where the number of metastable energy minima changes and the commonly used approximation for the quality factor $Q\simeq 1/2α$ (where $α$ denotes the Gilbert damping) fails.

</details>


### [174] [Intrinsic grain-size gradients upon grain growth near a free surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16740)
*Jing Tang,Runlu Yan,Donglan Zhang,Ronald Schnitzer,Lorenz Romaner,Marlene Kapp,Marco Salvalaglio,Oliver Renk*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了自由表面对多晶镍晶粒生长动力学的显著影响，发现晶粒尺寸从表面到内部存在梯度分布，这一现象主要源于自由表面的弹性弛豫效应而非热沟槽作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析高纯度块体多晶镍的微观结构演化进行研究：一方面分析1毫米厚试样从表面到内部的横截面；另一方面对三种不同厚度（1毫米、40微米和10微米）试样进行面内（in-plane）研究，以识别晶粒尺寸梯度分布特征。

Result: 研究发现存在本征晶粒尺寸梯度（intrinsic grain-size gradient），表现为晶粒尺寸从表面向内部逐渐增大。这一梯度不仅限于最表层，而是延伸到5-10层晶粒深度，且热沟槽（thermal grooves）效应在此深度可忽略不计。该行为主要受自由表面弹性弛豫（elastic relaxation）的影响，改变了由剪切耦合晶界迁移（shear-coupled grain boundary migration）产生的内部应力场。

Conclusion: 自由表面对多晶材料的微观结构演化具有重要影响，弹性弛豫效应显著改变了晶粒生长动力学。这一发现强调了在理解多晶材料微观结构演化时必须考虑自由表面的作用，特别是其对剪切耦合晶界迁移产生的内部应力场的调制效应。

Abstract: Grain growth fundamentally shapes the microstructure of crystalline materials upon annealing, affecting their overall mechanical and functional properties. Recently, it has been rationalized that grain growth in polycrystals does not result solely from weighted curvature flow, but elastic effects (intrinsic stress) arised from shear coupling also need to be taken into account. We characterize and examine the effect of free surfaces on grain growth kinetics of high-purity, bulk polycrystalline nickel. By analyzing the microstructural evolution on cross sections of 1 mm thick specimens from the surface to the interior, as well as through in-plane investigations on specimens with varying thickness (1 mm, 40 $μ$m, and 10 $μ$m), an intrinsic grain-size gradient was identified, characterized by a gradual increase in grain size towards the interior. Interestingly, this grading was not restricted to the very surface but continued to depths of five to ten layers of grains, where effects from thermal grooves are considered negligible. We demonstrate that this behavior is significantly affected by elastic relaxation at the free surface, which alters the internal stress fields generated by shear-coupled grain boundary migration. These findings emphasize the relevance of free surfaces to the microstructural evolution of polycrystal.

### [175] [On the complementary roles of anisotropic crack density and anisotropic crack driving force in phase-field modeling of mixed-mode fracture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16828)
*Guk Heon Kim,Minseo Kim,Kwangsan Chun,Jaemin Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究阐明了各向异性相场断裂模型中两个互补机制的不同作用：裂纹密度各向异性控制裂纹路径和韧性，而各向异性应变能控制断裂驱动力，在应力集中几何中额外控制弹性应变能分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Pranavi等人提出了各向异性相场断裂的统一框架，但裂纹密度各向异性（控制方向相关断裂阻力）和各向异性应变能（控制断裂驱动力）这两个机制的具体作用及其相互作用尚未得到研究。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 首先通过软弹性体混合模式断裂实验验证公式，然后对单边缺口（SEN）和开孔拉伸（OHT）试样进行系统参数研究，以分离每个机制的作用。

Result: SEN研究表明，裂纹密度各向异性控制裂纹路径和韧性而不改变弹性响应，而各向异性应变能会偏转裂纹但快速饱和。OHT研究揭示了几何依赖的作用扩展：各向异性应变能控制纤维取向相关的刚度、峰值力和断裂位移。当两个机制共同作用时，组合响应表现出超过个体贡献线性和的非线性协同相互作用。

Conclusion: 研究确立了裂纹密度各向异性控制裂纹路径（断裂阻力），而各向异性应变能控制驱动力，并在应力集中几何中额外控制应力集中器周围的弹性应变能分布。

Abstract: Phase-field models for anisotropic fracture employ two complementary mechanisms: (i) the anisotropic crack density function, controlling direction-dependent fracture resistance, and (ii) the anisotropic strain energy, governing the fracture driving force. Although the unified framework was presented in Pranavi et al.[Comput. Mech., 73 (2024)], the distinct roles of these mechanisms and their interaction remain uninvestigated. This work addresses this gap by first validating the formulation against mixed-mode fracture experiments on a soft elastomer (Lu et al. [Extreme Mech. Lett., 48 (2021)]), and then conducting systematic parametric studies on single-edge-notched (SEN) and open-hole tension (OHT) specimens to isolate each mechanism. The SEN studies show that the crack density anisotropy controls the crack path and toughness while leaving the elastic response unchanged, whereas the anisotropic strain energy deflects the crack but saturates rapidly. The OHT studies reveal a geometry-dependent role expansion: the anisotropic strain energy governs fiber-orientation-dependent stiffness, peak force, and fracture displacement. When both mechanisms act together, the combined response exhibits nonlinear synergistic interaction exceeding the linear sum of the individual contributions. These results establish that the crack density anisotropy governs the crack path (fracture resistance), while the anisotropic strain energy governs the driving force and, in stress-concentration geometries, additionally controls the elastic strain energy distribution around the stress concentrator.

### [176] [Quantum Computing of Phonon Spectra and Thermal Properties of Crystalline Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16863)
*Naman Khandelwal,Bikash K. Behera,Ashok Kumar,Prasanta K. Panigrahi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用变分量子本征求解器（variational quantum eigensolver）和变分量子收缩法（variational quantum deflation）处理声子哈密顿量（phonon Hamiltonians）。将质量加权动力学矩阵映射到量子比特编码的厄米算符，使用缩减的量子比特寄存器计算硅和石墨烯的声子谱，并与经典对角化方法进行直接基准测试。

Conclusion: 尽管经典声子方法在计算上仍具优势，但该研究确立了基于声子的热力学作为评估近量子设备上变分量子算法的严格且物理透明的基准。这为量子计算在材料科学中的应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Variational quantum algorithms offer a promising framework for solving eigenvalue problems on near-term quantum hardware, yet their applicability beyond electronic structure calculations remains relatively unexplored. In this work, we investigate the quantum computing of lattice vibrational and thermodynamical properties by applying the variational quantum eigensolver and variational quantum deflation to phonon Hamiltonians derived from first-principles force constants obtained using density functional theory. The mass-weighted dynamical matrix is mapped onto a qubit-encoded Hermitian operator, enabling computation of the full set of acoustic and optical phonon branches of crystalline silicon and graphene using a reduced qubit register and direct benchmarking against classical diagonalization. The quantum-computed phonon spectrum is further used to evaluate vibrational entropy, constant-volume specific heat, and thermal expansion coefficient, reproducing expected low-temperature quantum behavior and the high-temperature Dulong-Petit limit. We further demonstrate that combined error mitigation strategies help recover phonon dispersions and thermodynamic behavior consistent with expected trends on near-term quantum hardware. Although classical phonon methods remain computationally superior, our results establish phonon-based thermodynamics as a stringent and physically transparent benchmark for assessing variational quantum algorithms on near-term quantum devices.

Here, we show that linearly polarized photoluminescence from WS2/WSe2 moiré excitons is largely insensitive to the excitation polarization and therefore is not primarily governed by valley-contrast selection rules. Automated polarization-resolved photoluminescence and Raman mapping at cryogenic temperatures reveal that the degree of linear polarization correlates strongly with local Raman shifts and moiré-exciton observables, identifying strain as the dominant experimental correlate. Exhaustive linear-regression analysis further shows that strain-related descriptors provide the best prediction of the observed polarization. Here, we use hyperspectral photoluminescence mapping and peak-decomposition-free spectral analyses to determine how this spectral complexity is organized in space. A 20 x 20 map acquired with a 400 nm pitch reveals three dominant spectral families that form contiguous real-space domains. Feature-wise spatial correlation analysis and whole-spectrum similarity yield a characteristic micron-scale length of 1.27-2.05 um, all exceeding the 0.85 um optical spot size. At the same time, individual pixels retain a dense, multi-peak structure, implying an unresolved local spectral manifold below optical resolution. Correlations among centroid, dominant energy, asymmetry, width, entropy, sharp fraction, and roughness indicate that the micron-scale energy landscape and local manifold complexity can be statistically separated, while remaining correlated across the map, consistent with a hierarchical organization of the emission spectrum. Abstract: Altermagnets provide a promising platform for unconventional transport and optical responses beyond conventional ferromagnets and antiferromagnets. In this work, we develop a medium-throughput first-principles workflow to evaluate transport and optical properties in approximately 150 known altermagnetic compounds collected from the MAGNDATA database. By combining density functional theory, Wannier interpolation, and symmetry analysis, we investigate representative linear and nonlinear responses, including the anomalous Hall effect, magneto-optical Kerr effect, and bulk photovoltaic effect. We find that these responses are strongly constrained by magnetic symmetry and further shaped by spin-orbit coupling, band structure, and inversion symmetry breaking. Abstract: Advancement in quantum information and quantum technologies has ushered in a new era of technological revolution in large scale atomistic simulation and efficient system on a chip device fabrication. This has led to innovative ways of harnessing rigorous search algorithms for functional quantum materials and steered scientists to dig deeper into the world of quantum phenomenon and applications. In this work, we delineate the advanced electronic structure and vibrational properties utilizing the popular meta-GGA functionals, spectral signatures of the Raman active phonon modes, explored their average mean free paths, and whether they conserve helicity, by leveraging first principles density functional theory and density functional perturbation theory. Abstract: We have investigated NdCo2-xNix cubic Laves compounds with 0 <= x <= 1 using neutron diffraction and bulk magnetization measurements to study the influence of partial Ni substitutions of Co on the phase transitions and the magnetocaloric effect. Upon cooling, NdCo2 undergoes a cubic to tetragonal transition at 100 K, and a tetragonal to orthorhombic transition at 42 K. Additionally, there was a reduction in the magnetic moment upon increasing the Ni substitution of Co. ### [184] [Modern Solid Electrolytes for All-Solid-State Batteries: Materials Chemistry, Structure, and Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17380)
*Denys Butenko,Mustafa Khan,Liusuo Wu,Jinlong Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了从晶体对称性到非晶态局域多面体排列的无机固态电解质结构-性能关系，重点分析了氧化物、硫化物和卤化物三大化学体系，强调离子传导取决于框架拓扑、缺陷化学和局域柔性的耦合效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在通过结构-性能关系（structure property relationships）的视角，系统审视无机固态电解质，特别是氧化物、硫化物和卤化物三大化学框架，以理解其离子传导机制并指导材料设计。

Method: 采用综述分析方法，从晶体对称性（crystallographic symmetry）到非晶态局域多面体排列（amorphous local polyhedra arrangement）的角度，比较氧化物、硫化物和卤化物固态电解质的结构特征与传导性能关系。

Result: 研究发现快速离子传导不仅取决于成分或晶体扩散路径，而是框架拓扑（framework topology）、缺陷化学（defect chemistry）和局域阴离子柔性（local anion flexibility）的耦合效应。氧化物在化学稳定但几何受限的框架中传导，硫化物通过软晶格拓宽低能迁移路径，卤化物则通过紧密堆积的阴离子亚晶格和混合阴离子配位实现有效传导。

Conclusion: 长程离子传导应理解为统计连接的局域低势垒迁移事件的宏观结果，而非沿单一理想路径的运动。未来需要建立多尺度结构-性能关系，并设计同时优化电导率、稳定性和加工性的传导活性框架（transport active frameworks）。

Abstract: In this review, from crystallographic symmetry to amorphous local polyhedra arrangement and combinations, we examine inorganic solid state electrolytes through the lens of structure property relationships, with oxides, sulfides, and halides representing three major framework chemistries. Halide solid electrolytes and their derivatives, including mixed anion halides and antiperovskite related materials, have expanded this landscape further by introducing new ways to regulate local coordination chemistry, defect populations, and transport active frameworks. Across these families, fast ion conduction depends not simply on composition or crystallographic diffusion pathways, but on the coupled effects of framework topology, site energy distribution, defect chemistry, bottleneck response, and local anion flexibility. Oxides illustrate transport within chemically robust but geometrically constrained frameworks. Sulfides demonstrate that a soft, easily polarizable lattice can broaden the array of low energy migration pathways. Halides occupy an intermediate state, in which the closely packed anion sublattices, an approximately degenerate lithium environment, and mixed anion coordination enable effective transport while simultaneously enhancing oxidation stability and compatibility with cathodes. Building on these comparisons, we argue that long range ion transport is increasingly understood not as motion along a single idealized pathway, but as the macroscopic outcome of statistically connected low barrier local migration events distributed across the structure. We further discuss the experimental and computational approaches required to establish such multiscale structure property relationships and outline future strategies for designing transport active frameworks in which conductivity, stability, and processability are optimized together.

### [185] [Designer metal-free altermagnetism in honeycomb two-dimensional frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17386)
*Hongde Yu,Thomas Brumme,Thomas Heine*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在蜂窝状二维晶体中实现无金属反铁磁（altermagnetism）的分子设计策略，通过降低三角烯衍生自由基的单体点群对称性，选择性破坏反演对称性，实现了17 meV的d波自旋劈裂，为室温有机反铁磁材料开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁（altermagnetism）结合了相反自旋通道的动量依赖自旋劈裂和零净磁化强度，实现了对外部磁场鲁棒的自旋输运电场控制。尽管在无机系统中广泛探索，但具有π自旋劈裂的无金属反铁磁材料，特别是在二维有机框架中，仍然难以实现。

Method: 通过将三角烯衍生自由基的单体点群对称性从D3h降低到C2v，选择性破坏反演对称性同时保持二分晶格。采用自旋极化密度泛函理论计算，并构建最小紧束缚模型分析各向异性最近邻跃迁的微观起源。

Result: 计算显示强反铁磁耦合（-130 meV）、M点处17 meV的d波自旋劈裂（d-wave spin splitting）和1.26 eV的Mott-Hubbard能隙，均与Lieb定理完全一致。双轴压缩应变可将自旋劈裂增强至27 meV，各向异性最近邻跃迁是自旋劈裂和反铁磁的微观起源。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种实现室温有机反铁磁材料的通用方法，通过工程化的反演对称性破缺为碳基反铁磁开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Altermagnetism combines momentum-dependent spin splitting of opposite-spin channels with zero net magnetization, enabling electric-field control of spin transport that is robust against external magnetic fields. Although widely explored in inorganic systems, metal-free altermagnets with pi-spin splitting, particularly in two-dimensional organic frameworks, have remained elusive. Here, we introduce a molecular design strategy that achieves designer metal-free altermagnetism in honeycomb 2D crystals. By reducing the monomer point-group symmetry from D3h to C2v in triangulene-derived radicals, inversion symmetry is selectively broken while the bipartite lattice is preserved. Spin-polarized density-functional-theory calculations reveal strong antiferromagnetic couplings of -130 meV, d-wave spin splitting of 17 meV at the M point, and Mott-Hubbard gaps of 1.26 eV, all fully consistent with Lieb's theorem. A minimal tight-binding model shows that anisotropic nearest-neighbor hopping arising from direction-dependent pi-orbital overlap is the microscopic origin of spin splitting and altermagnetism. Biaxial compressive strain further enhances the spin splitting to 27 meV. These results establish a general approach to room-temperature organic altermagnets and open a pathway toward carbon-based altermagnetism via engineered inversion-symmetry breaking.

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) van der Waals (vdW) heterostructures (HSs) provide a versatile platform for tailoring electronic, optical, and magnetic properties via proximity effects at their interfaces. The HSs exhibit multiple sharp excitonic peaks that do not appear in the individual constituent materials, indicating the emergence of localized intralayer WSe2 excitons confined by interface-induced potentials. Notably, these excitons exhibit spontaneous circular polarization even in the absence of an external magnetic field, suggesting a magnetic proximity effect induced by uncompensated spins at the NiPS3 interface. Magneto-PL measurements further reveal nonlinear Zeeman splitting, consistent with the presence of an interfacial exchange field that alters the valley exciton dynamics. Abstract: Metal-site density strongly influences oxygen reduction activity and selectivity in M-N-C electrocatalysts, but the descriptors that predict these trends remain under debate. Using constrained-magnetization calculations combined with Landau analysis, we find that the ground-state magnetic moments vary only weakly across a broad range of metal-site densities, suggesting that magnetic descriptors alone cannot account for the pronounced performance changes. Incorporating these PZC shifts into a pH-field-coupled microkinetic model captures the density-dependent activity trends and reproduces the experimentally observed increase in two-electron selectivity at lower site densities under acidic conditions. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子分辨率电子显微技术已常规用于研究高性能锰基氧化物阴极的微观结构，这些材料常包含类尖晶石有序。本研究旨在评估STEM-HAADF成像和傅里叶滤波作为表征δ-DRX尖晶石域及其反相边界工具的有效性，这些边界对材料电化学性能起关键作用。

Here, we evaluate STEM-HAADF imaging and subsequent Fourier filtering as tools for characterizing δ-DRX spinel domains and their antiphase boundaries, which play a central role in the material's electrochemical performance. Using electron microscopy simulations and recent theoretical insight into the structural makeup of δ-DRX, we attempt to characterize the crystallographic spinel variants which occur in its multi-domain structure. We show that each domain interface, arising from pairings among eight distinct variants, can be categorized into one of four Fourier filtered profiles, one of which leaves the boundary undetectable in atomically resolved electron microscopy when viewed along the preferred [110] zone axis. Our results also suggest that the appearance of seemingly disordered or layered-like regions might actually arise from low energy domain boundaries which are slanted relative to the [110] viewing direction. Our findings highlight the need for careful interpretation of atomic-resolution micrographs of phase transitions, where local reordering drives transformations from higher to lower symmetry structures while maintaining lattice coherence.

Abstract: While the recursive property of entropy is well known in information theory, it is rarely utilized in thermodynamics, despite entropy originating in this field. Abstract: Integrating two-dimensional semiconductors such as MoS$_2$ with dielectric materials remains a central challenge for their use in future logic technologies.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用时间分辨磁光法拉第效应（time-resolved magneto-optical Faraday effect），使用两种独立的泵浦-探测配置：1030/515 nm和800/400 nm波长组合，对外延NiCo2O4薄膜进行测量。

Abstract: Rare-earth-ferrimagnetic oxides are emerging as attractive platforms for investigating ultrafast spin dynamics. Here, we study the photoinduced magnetization dynamics of epitaxial NiCo2O4 (NCO) thin films by time-resolved magneto-optical Faraday effect using two independent pump-probe configurations: 1030/515 nm and 800/400 nm. In both measurements, photoexcitation induces an immediate reduction of the magneto-optical signal within the experimental time resolution, followed by a reproducible slower demagnetization component with a characteristic timescale of approximately 5-6 ps and a subsequent recovery on the ~100 ps timescale. Importantly, this picosecond demagnetization component is observed consistently across the two experimental configurations and excitation wavelengths, demonstrating that it is an intrinsic feature of the ultrafast magnetic response of NCO thin films. Because the earliest-time dip may contain a transient optical contribution, we describe the overall response as type-II-like, rather than assigning a definitive textbook type-II classification solely on the basis of the sub-resolution signal. These results establish a robust two-step ultrafast demagnetization behavior in NCO and highlight rare-earth-free oxide ferrimagnets as promising systems for exploring Mult sublattice spin dynamics on ultrafast timescales.

### [193] [SWORD: Symmetry and Wyckoff-sequence of Ordered and Disordered crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17994)
*Yuyao Huang,Wei Nong,Shuya Yamazaki,Martin Hoffmann Petersen,Jianghai Wang,Ruiming Zhu,Kedar Hippalgaonkar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出SWORD方法，一种基于Wyckoff位置、具有对称性感知的晶体结构字符串表示法，适用于有序和无序晶体，能够标准化对称等价结构描述、显式表示部分占据位点的共占物种，并通过混合度描述符量化复杂无序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料发现中的新颖性要求候选材料具有独特性、非冗余性和热力学合理性。随着晶体学数据库规模和复杂性的增加，特别是在涉及晶体学无序时，部分占据位点极大地扩大了结构-组成空间，使得有效可靠的新颖性评估变得困难。

Method: 引入SWORD方法，这是一种对称性感知、基于Wyckoff位置的字符串表示法，兼容有序和无序晶体。该方法提供：(1) 将对称等价结构描述标准化为一致标签；(2) 显式表示部分占据位点上的共占物种；(3) 通过混合度描述符量化复杂无序，捕捉位点化学计量的连续变化。

Result: 与现有指纹和结构匹配方法相比，SWORD在保持恒等变换不变性的同时，对结构扰动保持可解释的敏感性。在关联未弛豫和中间构型与其最终弛豫状态方面表现出竞争力，可直接从部分弛豫甚至未弛豫的生成结构进行更可靠的新颖性评估。成功应用于无机晶体结构数据库的无序感知去重和整理。

Conclusion: SWORD方法能够实现高效的结构分组、重复识别和无序结构的精细细化。整理后的ICSD数据库将为人工智能时代下的材料信息学和数据驱动材料设计提供基础。

Abstract: Novelty in materials discovery requires candidates to be distinct, non-redundant, and thermodynamically plausible. While crystallographic databases continue to expand in both size and complexity, making efficient and reliable novelty assessment has become increasingly difficult. This becomes particularly acute when crystallographic disorder is involved, as partial occupancies greatly enlarge the structure-composition space and obscure the identification of genuinely distinct structures. Here, we introduce SWORD, a symmetry-aware, Wyckoff-based string representation compatible with both ordered and disordered crystals. SWORD provides (i) standardization of symmetry-equivalent structural descriptions into a consistent label, (ii) explicitly represents co-occupying species on partially occupied sites, and (iii) quantifies complex disorder through a degree of mixing descriptor that captures continuous variation in site stoichiometry. These features enable efficient structure grouping, duplicate identification, and finer refinement of disordered structures. Benchmarking against existing fingerprint and structure-matching methods shows that SWORD remains invariant under identity-preserving transformations while retaining interpretable sensitivity to structural perturbations. In addition, SWORD shows competitive performance in associating unrelaxed and intermediate configurations with their final relaxed states along relaxation trajectories. This feature could enable more reliable novelty assessment directly from partially relaxed or even unrelaxed generated structures. Finally, SWORD was used to showcase its capability of disorder-aware database-scale deduplication and curation for the Inorganic Crystal Structure Database (ICSD). The curated ICSD would serve as the basis for the materials informatics and data-driven materials design in the era of artificial intelligence.

### [194] [A unified framework for grain boundary distributions in textured materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17997)
*Ralf Hielscher,Rüdiger Kilian,Erik Wünsche,Katharina Tinka Marquardt*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶界平面分布被广泛用于推断多晶材料中晶界形成的机制，但本文指出这种解释存在固有歧义性，需要更严谨的理论框架来区分不同的形成过程。

Method: 采用统一的八参数边界分布框架，推导了晶界特征分布（GBCD）和晶界法向分布（GBND），并识别了边界网络形成的两种极限情况：宏观驱动网络和晶体学驱动网络。

Result: 在宏观驱动网络中，晶体框架下的GBND由试样GBND与取向分布函数（ODF）卷积给出；而在晶体学驱动网络中，试样GBND由晶体GBND与ODF卷积获得。这种对偶性表明GBND的各向异性可能源于宏观排列效应而非内在晶体学选择。

Conclusion: 晶界法向分布（GBND）或晶界特征分布（GBCD）单独不足以识别晶界形成机制，但两者与织构的关系可用于识别微观结构中主导的形成过程。多种模拟微观结构的评估证实了理论预测的关系。

Abstract: Grain boundary plane distributions are widely used to infer the mechanisms governing grain boundary formation in polycrystalline materials. We show that such interpretations are inherently ambiguous. Using a unified eight-parameter boundary distribution framework, we derive both the grain boundary character distribution (GBCD) and the grain boundary normal distribution (GBND) and identify two limiting cases of boundary network formation.
  We show that in macroscopically driven networks, the crystal-frame GBND is given by a convolution of the specimen GBND with the orientation distribution function (ODF), whereas in crystallographically driven networks the specimen GBND is obtained by convolution of the crystal GBND with the ODF. This duality implies that anisotropy in the GBND may arise from macroscopic alignment effects rather than intrinsic crystallographic selection. Conversely, this relationship may be used to identify the dominant formation process in the measured mcirostructures.
  Evaluation of a wide variety of simulated microstructures confirm the theoretically predicted relationships between texture, GBND and GBCD. In particular, our examples confirm that the GBND or GBCD alone are not sufficient for identifying grain boundary formation mechanisms.

### [197] [Evaluating dispersion models for ab initio simulation of G-I and G-II molten fluoride salts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18139)
*Shubhojit Banerjee,Rajni Chahal Crockett,Julian Barra,Stephen T Lam*
