TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了Grimme的DFT-D和非局域范德华（vdW-DF）修正对熔融氟化物（LiF、NaF、KF、BeF₂、MgF₂、CaF₂）性质预测的影响，发现色散修正对密度预测有显著影响但对扩散系数影响较小，为熔盐模拟中的色散模型选择提供了系统框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的第一性原理分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）是模拟熔盐的有力方法，但标准交换关联泛函常忽略色散相互作用，导致性质预测存在潜在误差。虽然常用色散修正来匹配实验盐密度，但其对熔盐结构、热物理和输运性质预测的系统性影响尚未得到检验。

Method: 本研究评估了Grimme的DFT-D和非局域范德华（van der Waals, vdW-DF）修正对第I族（LiF、NaF、KF）和第II族（BeF₂、MgF₂、CaF₂）熔融氟化物的影响，这些氟化物与反应堆应用相关。通过跨成分和温度的系统性基准测试，比较了不同色散模型的预测准确性。

Result: 结果显示色散修正对结合能影响较小但对密度预测有显著影响。系统性基准测试表明，半经验色散模型（semi-empirical dispersion models）通常比vdW-DF产生更准确的密度预测。扩散系数在固定密度下对色散修正基本不变，而配位数分布则根据所选色散模型表现出显著差异。特别是BeF₂与其他氟化物不同，在缺乏色散修正时显示出明显的结构和动力学差异。

Conclusion: 这些发现强调了色散效应对促进中长程有序的高电荷密度阳离子的必要性，为熔盐模拟中选择色散模型提供了系统性框架，从而改进了密度和结构预测的准确性。

Abstract: Ab initio molecular dynamics (AIMD) based on density functional theory (DFT) is a powerful approach for modeling molten salts. However, standard exchange-correlation functionals often neglect dispersion interactions, introducing potential errors in property predictions. Dispersion corrections are commonly applied ad hoc to match experimental salt densities, but their systematic impact on predicting structure, thermophysical, and transport properties of salt remains unexamined. This study evaluates the impact of Grimme's DFT-D and nonlocal van der Waals (vdW-DF) corrections on molten fluorides of Group-I (LiF, NaF, KF) and Group-II (BeF$_2$, MgF$_2$, CaF$_2$), which are relevant to reactor applications. Results indicate that dispersion corrections have a minor effect on binding energies but significantly influence density predictions. Systematic benchmarking across compositions and temperatures reveals that semi-empirical dispersion models often produce more accurate densities compared to vdW-DF. Diffusion coefficients remain largely invariant to dispersion corrections at fixed densities, while coordination number distributions exhibit notable differences based on chosen dispersion. BeF$_2$, in particular, deviates from other fluorides, showing pronounced structural and dynamical differences in the absence of dispersion corrections. This highlights the necessity of dispersion effects for high-charge-density cations that promote intermediate- to long-range ordering. These findings provide a systematic framework for selecting dispersion models in molten salt simulations, improving density and structural predictions.

</details>


### [198] [Uncertainty-aware phase fraction prediction and active-learning-guided out-of-domain discovery of refractory multi-principal element alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18322)
*A. K. Shargh,C. D. Stiles,J. A. El-Awady*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 难熔多主元合金（RMPEAs）具有广阔的成分设计空间和极端条件下的优异机械性能潜力，但现有机器学习方法依赖从成分特征到相标签的确定性映射，忽略了预测中固有的不确定性。

Method: 采用基于混合密度网络（Mixture Density Networks, MDNs）的深度学习框架，使用CALPHAD衍生数据训练最多六个组成相的独立模型；通过基于扰动的特征重要性分析确定最小充分输入集；提出基于不确定性的主动学习策略来发现含新元素的目标相合金。

Result: 该方法实现了高预测精度，同时捕捉了相形成的概率性质；确定了在保持预测性能和不确定性校准的同时的最小充分输入特征集；能够探索模型引导发现中的探索-利用权衡。

Conclusion: 这种不确定性感知框架有潜力加速和提高发现新型高性能合金的可靠性，并具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: Refractory multi-principal element alloys (RMPEAs) represent a novel class of alloys characterized by an extensive compositional design space and the potential for exceptional mechanical performance under extreme conditions. While accurate phase stability prediction is essential for their robust design, existing machine learning approaches rely on deterministic mappings from composition-derived features to phase labels, neglecting the uncertainty inherent in such predictions. In this study, we present a deep learning framework based on Mixture Density Networks (MDNs) to predict phase fractions in RMPEAs and quantify the associated aleatoric uncertainty across a wide temperature range. By training separate models for up to six constituent phases of RMPEAs using CALPHAD derived data, our approach achieves high predictive accuracy while capturing the probabilistic nature of phase formation. To address epistemic uncertainty arising from incomplete knowledge of the most informative features, we perform a perturbation-based feature importance analysis and identify a minimally sufficient input set that maintains both predictive performance and uncertainty calibration. Finally, we propose an uncertainty-based active learning strategy to discover novel RMPEAs with the target phase incorporating previously unseen elements, while investigating the exploration-exploitation trade-off in model-guided discovery. Our uncertainty-aware framework has the potential to accelerate and improve the reliability of discovering novel high-performance alloys and is broadly applicable.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Altermagnets结合了铁磁和反铁磁材料的特性，具有自旋分离能带但净磁化强度为零。其对称性导致四极压磁性和双曲波色散，这引发了一个问题：哪些特性本质与磁性相关，哪些仅由对称性决定？

Method: 通过引入基于电极化的"alterelectrics"概念来区分这些概念，在一个简化模型中进行概念性演示，并提供了第一性原理材料实现。

Result: Alterelectrics展示出四极压电性和双曲色散特性。与自旋分离能带对应的是表面模式，这些模式允许表面依赖的各向异性电子输运，类似于altermagnets中提出的自旋电子学应用。

Abstract: Altermagnets are an emergent class of materials combining features of ferro- and antiferro-magnetic materials. They have spin-separated bands normally associated with ferromagnets, but a vanishing net magnetization. Moreover the symmetries giving rise to $d$-wave altermagnetism can provide them with a particular anisotropic, quadrupolar (i.e. with equal and opposite values when strained in perpendicular directions) piezomagnetism. Observing that the same symmetries provide a natural place to look for hyberbolic wave dispersion, this raises the question which properties are intrinsically linked to magnetism and which are determined by the symmetry. Here, we disentangle these concepts by introducing an alternative to altermagnets, based on electric polarization. These alterelectrics display quadrupolar piezoelectricity and a hyperbolic dispersion, which we demonstrate conceptually within a simplified model as well as a first-principles material realization. We furthermore establish that a counterpart of the spin-separated bands is formed by surface modes which allow for surface dependent anisotropic electronic transport analogous to the spintronic applications proposed for altermagnets.

### [200] [Direct observation of quadruple spin-texture locking in a 2D d-wave altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18337)
*Dan Mu,Bei Jiang,Qingchen Duan,Zulin Xu,Xingkai Cheng,Yusen Xiao,Xinru Han,Xinyu Liang,Zhaokun Luo,Ryan L. Kong,Qiheng Wang,Junwei Liu,Jianxin Zhong,Ruidan Zhong,Qiangqiang Gu,Baiqing Lv,Hong Ding*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究首次在原子尺度上直接观测到RbV2Se2O中的d波型自旋纹理，证实了自旋-晶格锁定（spin-lattice locking）现象，并发现了一种新的自旋-条纹锁定（spin-stripe locking）机制，为反铁磁体（altermagnets）提供了统一的四重自旋纹理锁定图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体（altermagnets）结合了零净磁化与非相对论性、动量依赖的自旋劈裂，为自旋电子学提供了新范式。然而，尽管经过广泛努力，自旋-晶格锁定（spin-lattice locking）这一反铁磁态的关键机制在原子尺度上的直接可视化证据仍然缺乏。

Method: 研究采用原位场可切换的自旋极化Cr针尖，在相同能量下实现准粒子干涉（quasiparticle interference）的自旋对比映射，克服了反铁磁体中长期存在的实验障碍。

Result: 在RbV2Se2O中观测到亚晶格水平的d波型自旋纹理，提供了自旋-晶格锁定的首个原子尺度证据。干涉图案显示显著的自旋依赖调制，建立了自旋散射锁定（spin scattering locking）和自旋动量锁定（spin momentum locking）作为实空间和倒空间的体现。意外发现了由长周期条纹调制组织的自旋选择性散射响应，形成了新的自旋-条纹锁定（spin-stripe locking）现象。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了d波反铁磁体中四重自旋纹理锁定现象的统一图像，并将反铁磁体定位为探索自旋、晶格、动量、莫尔势（moiré potential）和谷（valley）等相互交织自由度间多体相互作用的通用平台。

Abstract: Altermagnets combine vanishing net magnetization with nonrelativistic, momentum-dependent spin splitting, offering a new paradigm for spintronics. Spin-crystal symmetry coupling, namely spin-lattice locking, is the defining mechanism of altermagnetism, enforcing opposite spin sublattices in real space and spin-momentum-locked electronic structure in reciprocal space. Direct atomic-scale visualization of spin-lattice locking therefore constitutes a decisive benchmark of the altermagnetic state, yet such evidence has remained elusive despite extensive efforts. Here we show that the electronic states in RbV2Se2O exhibit a d-wave-like spin texture at the sublattice level, providing the first atomic-scale evidence of spin-lattice locking with a predominantly c-axis spin orientation. By employing an in-situ, field-switchable spin-polarized Cr tip, we realize spin-contrast mapping of quasiparticle interference at identical energies, overcoming a long-standing experimental barrier in altermagnets. The resulting interference patterns exhibit pronounced spin-dependent modulations, establishing spin scattering locking and spin momentum locking as the real and reciprocal space manifestations. Unexpectedly, we uncover that the spin-selective scattering response is organized by a long-period stripe modulation, giving rise to a previously unidentified form of spin-texture locking, spin-stripe locking. We attribute this behavior to the emergence of a spin-density-wave moiré pattern. Together, these results establish a unified picture of quadruple spin-texture locking phenomena in a d-wave altermagnet, and position altermagnets as a versatile platform for exploring many-body interactions among intertwined degrees of freedom, including spin, lattice, momentum, moiré potential and valley.

Here we demonstrate a plasmonic photocatalyst that enables CH4 and N2O conversion under ambient conditions to form C2 and C3 hydrocarbons. By systematically tuning AuPd alloys on TiO2, we identify an optimal composition (AuPd0.05) where Au enhances light harvesting and Pd enables selective C-H activation and C-C coupling. Under visible-light illumination, this catalyst produces C2H4, C2H6, C3H6, and C3H8 with ~80% selectivity while suppressing CO2 formation. In-situ spectroscopy and hot-carrier calculations show that plasmon-generated carriers redistribute interfacial hydroxyl intermediates, shifting the hydrophilic center to suppress overoxidation. Our work illustrates how engineering interfacial electronic and adsorbate dynamics enables selective multicarbon formation.

### [202] [Moire Control of Alterelectric Quadrupolar Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18428)
*Alejandro Lopez-Bezanilla*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究展示了莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）能够将交替电性（alterelectricity）这种补偿性铁电态转变为可控相，通过莫尔场调控四极矩取向，实现可编程的各向异性电子功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交替电性是一种补偿性铁电态（compensated ferroic state），其中四极矩电子序（quadrupolar electronic order）重塑低能电子结构但不产生净极化。研究旨在探索莫尔超晶格如何将这种序转变为可控相。

Method: 采用布洛赫周期双轨道理论（Bloch-periodic two-orbital theory），将缓慢变化的层间配准（interlayer registry）粗粒化为作用于自洽双分量交替电四极矩（two-component alterelectric quadrupole）的有效莫尔场（effective moiré field）。通过配准相位扫描（registry-phase sweep）探索四极矩空间内的连续路径。

Result: 该相在强填充依赖的不稳定性阈值之上发展，从弱选择区域过渡到稳健的轴向主导基态（axial-dominated ground state），而对角主导分支仅作为弱竞争者存在。莫尔超晶格不仅稳定交替电性，还能调控其内部取向，这种取向选择直接编码在莫尔布里渊区（moiré Brillouin zone）低能谱权重的重新分布中。

Conclusion: 莫尔超晶格是实现可控交替电序和可编程各向异性电子功能的通用途径，通过莫尔场对四极矩取向的调控，为设计功能性电子材料提供了新策略。

Abstract: Alterelectricity is a compensated ferroic state in which quadrupolar electronic order reshapes low-energy electronic structure without producing a net polarization. Here we show that a moiré superlattice can turn such order into a controllable phase. Within a Bloch-periodic two-orbital theory, the slowly varying interlayer registry is coarse-grained into an effective moiré field acting on a self-consistent two-component alterelectric quadrupole. The resulting phase develops above a strongly filling-dependent instability threshold and crosses over from a weakly selected regime into a robust axial-dominated ground state, while the diagonal-dominated branch remains only a weak competitor. A registry-phase sweep supplies an explicit continuous path through internal quadrupole space, demonstrating that the moiré superlattice does more than stabilize alterelectricity: it steers its internal orientation. This orientational selection is encoded directly in the redistribution of low-energy spectral weight across the moiré Brillouin zone. These results identify moiré superlattices as a generic route to controllable alterelectric order and to programmable anisotropic electronic functionality.

</details>

### [203] [Metric-Deformed Heisenberg Algebras and the $q$-Dirac Operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16508)
*Julio César Jaramillo Quiceno*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文引入了一族度量形变海森堡代数（metric-deformed Heisenberg algebras）$M_1$和$M_2$，其交换关系直接由对角洛伦兹度规（diagonal Lorentzian metric）分量表达。这些代数统一了多个已知的$q$-形变海森堡代数，并建立了度量符号（metric signature）与形变参数之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立时空几何（spacetime geometry）与$q$-形变量子代数（$q$-deformed quantum algebras）之间的统一框架。通过引入度量形变海森堡代数，旨在将多种已知的$q$-形变代数纳入一个共同的理论体系。

Method: 方法包括：1）引入度量形变海森堡代数$M_1$和$M_2$，其交换关系直接由对角洛伦兹度规分量表达；2）利用西尔维斯特惯性定理（Sylvester's theorem of inertia）建立度量符号与形变参数之间的关联；3）从形变达朗贝尔算子（deformed D'Alembertian）构造$q$-狄拉克算子（$q$-Dirac operator）$D_q$。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）$M_1$和$M_2$代数统一了多个已知的$q$-形变海森堡代数，包括$q$-$\hbar$代数、新$q$-海森堡代数（new $q$-Heisenberg algebra）和$q$-广义海森堡代数（$q$-generalized Heisenberg algebra）；2）证明了$D_q^2$恢复了形变克莱因-戈登算子（deformed Klein-Gordon operator）；3）将此构造与作者先前引入的二次$q$-狄拉克算子相关联。

Conclusion: 结论是成功构建了一个统一框架，将时空几何与$q$-形变量子代数联系起来。该框架通过度量形变海森堡代数及其与$q$-狄拉克算子的关联，为理解几何结构与代数形变之间的深层联系提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We introduce a family of metric-deformed Heisenberg algebras $M_1$ and $M_2$, where the commutation relations are expressed directly in terms of the components of a diagonal Lorentzian metric. We show that these algebras unify several known $q$-deformed Heisenberg algebras, including the $q$-$\hbar$ algebra, the new $q$-Heisenberg algebra, and the $q$-generalized Heisenberg algebra, which embed as special cases. Using Sylvester's theorem of inertia, we establish a connection between the metric signature and the deformation parameters. We construct a $q$-Dirac operator $D_q$ from the deformed D'Alembertian and prove that $D_q^2$ recovers the deformed Klein-Gordon operator. Furthermore, we relate this construction to the quadratic $q$-Dirac operator previously introduced by the author, providing a unified framework that bridges spacetime geometry and $q$-deformed quantum algebras.

</details>

Conclusion: 概念上，基于关联几何（correlation geometry）的物理系统基本描述更接近热力学（thermodynamics）而非量子理论（quantum theory）。这表明关联几何为物理系统提供了与热力学相似的基本描述框架。

A key focus here is on the manner in which the framework deals with gauge transformations, including diffeomorphisms via the principle of unitary equivalence. We will argue that, conceptually, the fundamental description of a physical system in terms of its correlation geometry is much closer to thermodynamics than quantum theory.

### [205] [Continuum honeycomb Schrödinger operators with incommensurate line defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16712)
*Pierre Amenoagbadji,Michael I. Weinstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究构建了二维蜂窝结构中沿非公度（"无理"）线缺陷或边缘的波传播理论框架，通过三维哈密顿量限制和多尺度分析，证明了在扰动体谱隙中存在无限多个边缘态本征对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解二维蜂窝结构中沿非公度（non-commutative）或"无理"（irrational）线缺陷的边缘态波传播。由于沿边缘缺乏平移不变性，这类边缘态的严格定义具有挑战性，需要发展新的数学框架来处理非公度几何结构。

Method: 方法核心是将二维哈密顿量表达为三维（退化椭圆）哈密顿量的限制，该三维介质包含二维界面且具有周期性。通过多尺度分析（multiscale analysis）在三维设置中构造近似边缘态，再通过限制获得沿无理边缘准周期（quasiperiodic）的二维边缘态。这些边缘态由有效狄拉克算子（Dirac operator）的本征函数"播种"，该算子因非公度几何而具有无限块对角结构。

Result: 主要结果是获得了三维哈密顿量的解析解展开（resolvent expansion），其主导项为块对角狄拉克算子的解析解。该展开的有效性要求未扰动蜂窝哈密顿量的色散函数满足全向非共振（无折叠）条件（omnidirectional non-resonance/no-fold condition），该条件在强束缚区（strong binding regime）下成立。与早期公度边缘研究不同，此全向条件独立于边缘特性。

Conclusion: 研究证明在非公度边缘情况下，无限多个边缘态本征对会出现，其能量在扰动体谱隙中稠密分布。该结果为后续在丢番图条件（Diophantine condition）下严格构造这些填隙边缘态提供了关键工具，揭示了非公度几何对边缘态谱结构的深刻影响。

Abstract: We study wave propagation in 2D honeycomb structures with a non-commensurate or ``irrational'' line defect or edge. Our model is a Schrödinger operator which interpolates, across the edge, between two distinct bulk (asymptotic) Hamiltonians with a common spectral gap about the ``Dirac point'' of an unperturbed honeycomb operator. We seek edge states, eigenstates that are bounded and oscillatory parallel to the edge, and decaying in the transverse direction. For non-commensurate edges, the rigorous definition of these states is nontrivial due to the lack of translation invariance along the edge. To address this, we exploit quasiperiodicity along the edge by expressing the Hamiltonian as the restriction of a 3D (degenerate elliptic) Hamiltonian describing a 3D medium with a 2D interface within which there is periodicity. Via multiscale analysis, we construct approximate edge states in this 3D setting and obtain by restriction 2D edge states which are quasiperiodic along the irrational edge. These edge states are seeded by eigenfunctions of an effective Dirac operator, which has an infinite block-diagonal structure due to the non-commensurate geometry. A consequence is that infinitely many edge state eigenpairs arise, whose energies are dense in the perturbed bulk spectral gap. In a forthcoming paper, we rigorously construct these gap-filling edge states under a Diophantine condition. The main result here is a key tool in this construction: a resolvent expansion for the 3D Hamiltonian, whose leading term is the resolvent of the block-diagonal Dirac operator. The validity of this expansion requires an omnidirectional non-resonance (no-fold) condition on the dispersion functions of the unperturbed honeycomb Hamiltonian. This condition is satisfied in the strong binding regime. In contrast with earlier works on commensurate edges, the omnidirectional condition is independent of the edge.

</details>

*Peng Tian,Roman Riser,Eugene Kanzieper*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视French等人于1978年首次提出的数方差与第L个有序特征值方差之间的"神秘"关系，该关系在随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）中具有重要意义但缺乏严格证明。

Method: 基于能级间距自协方差（level spacing auto-covariances）的未知求和规则进行证明，该推导依赖于作者先前关于随机矩阵理论中特征值涨落的功率谱（power spectrum）描述工作。对β=2对称类进行解析证明，并推测性地扩展到β=1和β=4对称类。

Result: 证明了对于β=2 Dyson对称类，数方差与第L个有序特征值方差之间的关系是渐近精确的。通过全面的数值分析验证了理论结果，并提出了对β=1和β=4对称类的推测性扩展。

Conclusion: 该研究严格证明了French等人提出的"神秘"关系对于β=2对称类的渐近精确性，建立了能级间距自协方差的求和规则，并将结果扩展到其他Dyson对称类，深化了对随机矩阵理论中特征值统计性质的理解。

Abstract: A "mysterious" relation between the number variance and the variance of the $L$-th ordered eigenvalue, first suggested by French et al. [Ann. Phys. 113, 277 (1978)], is revisited and proven to be asymptotically exact for the $β=2$ Dyson symmetry class. Central to the proof is a previously unknown sum rule for the level spacing auto-covariances. Its derivation hinges on our previous work on the power spectrum description of eigenvalue fluctuations in random matrix theory. Analytical results for $β=2$ are complemented by conjectural extensions to the $β=1$ and $β=4$ symmetry classes. Our findings are corroborated by a comprehensive numerical analysis.

Method: 方法采用渐近展开形式构建类孤子和类峰子解，将解表示为所有解共有的正则背景项与捕捉其独特特征的奇异分量之和，其中主要奇异项的精确定义起核心作用。

  The solution is expressed as the sum of a regular background common to all soliton- and peakon-like solutions and a singular component that captures their distinctive features, with the precise definition of the main singular term playing a central role. In the one-phase case, this term is determined, and the solvability of higher-order singular corrections is established in suitable functional spaces, enabling the construction of asymptotic solutions to arbitrary accuracy in a small parameter. The study also addresses the construction of two-phase soliton- and peakon-like solutions.
  Theorems on the asymptotic accuracy of the constructed asymptotic solutions have been proved. Each of the considered cases is illustrated by nontrivial examples for which, in accordance with the obtained general results, approximate solutions are derived in explicit form and their graphs are presented.

Abstract: We study resonances for the semiclassical magnetic Laplacian in the full plane with a compactly supported magnetic field in the framework of semiclassical complex scaling and black box scattering theory. Assuming that the magnetic field is locally constant, we prove the existence of semiclassical resonances near the Landau levels with exponentially small imaginary parts. We also prove that resonances emerge from a magnetic step discontinuity along a curved interface or a non-degenerate magnetic well, and in the vicinity of anharmonic Landau levels if the field has an isolated zero.

Abstract: We present a physics based numerical model that estimates the seismic radiation generated by water sediment flows in gravel-bed rivers. The model reproduces the trajectories of individual particles, evaluates impact and rolling forces from grain scale dynamics, and accounts for broadband turbulence and vortex shedding in the water column. Synthetic seismic signals are propagated to the receivers using the Rayleigh wave Green s function approach and synthetic ground-velocity signals are estimated. Application to a controlled test case shows how intermittent, size selective sediment transport mechanisms produce distinct spectral signatures. Comparison with seismic data from a flood event in a mountain torrent in the Tuscan Apennines displays general agreement with the observed frequency bands and clarifies the relative width of particle collisions and turbulent flow. These results show that resolved grain scale dynamics provides a framework for discriminating sediment transport and flow induced contributions to river seismic noise.

### [210] [Spherical singularities in compactified Ruijsenaars--Schneider systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18023)
*L. Feher,H. R. Dullin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究通过准哈密顿对偶约化构造的刘维尔可积系统，这些系统可视为紧致化三角Ruijsenaars-Schneider系统。重点分析类型(ii)情况下作用映射奇异纤维的几何结构，证明其为光滑连通各向同性子流形，并在特定参数范围内确定奇异顶点对应的纤维微分同胚于三维球面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用几何方法研究刘维尔可积系统的奇异纤维结构。通过分析作用映射（即$\mathbb{T}^{n-1}$动量映射）在类型(ii)情况下稠密定义环面作用补集中的纤维，证明这些奇异纤维为光滑连通各向同性子流形，并建立纤维模型作为$\mathrm{SU}(n)$子群相对于另一子群作用的商空间。

Result: 研究证明所有奇异纤维均为光滑连通各向同性子流形。在$n\geq 4$且$π/(n-1) <y < π/(n-2)$的最简类型(ii)情况下，确定了作用变量填充多面体的顶点，并证明奇异顶点对应的纤维微分同胚于$S^3 \simeq \mathrm{SU}(2)$，即三维球面。

Conclusion: 本文系统分析了紧致化三角Ruijsenaars-Schneider系统的奇异纤维结构，丰富了具有球面奇点的刘维尔可积系统示例。研究结果为理解这类可积系统的几何性质提供了新的视角和具体实例。

Abstract: We investigate certain Liouville integrable systems constructed earlier via reduction of the quasi-Hamiltonian double of $\mathrm{SU}(n)$. These systems live on compact connected symplectic manifolds of dimension $2(n-1)$ and can be interpreted as compactified trigonometric Ruijsenaars--Schneider systems. Depending on the value of a parameter $0<y< π$, they arise in two drastically different forms: in type (i) these are toric systems, while in the type (ii) cases they possess globally continuous action variables that generate a Hamiltonian torus action (only) on a dense open subset of the phase space. The principal goal of the paper is to study those fibers of the action map (alias the $\mathbb{T}^{n-1}$ momentum map) which are contained in the complement of the domain of the densely defined torus action occurring in the type (ii) cases. We demonstrate that all such `singular fibers' are smooth connected isotropic submanifolds. We also work out a model of the fibers as quotient spaces of certain subgroups of $\mathrm{SU}(n)$ with respect to an action of another subgroup. The general results are exemplified by determining the vertices of the polytope filled by the action variables in the simplest type (ii) cases that appear for any $n\geq 4$ with $π/(n-1) <y < π/(n-2)$, and proving that the fibers over the `singular vertices' are diffeomorphic to $S^3 \simeq \mathrm{SU}(2)$ in these cases. In this way, our findings enrich the set of examples of Liouville integrable systems with spherical singularities.

Abstract: Motivated by the analogy between spectral moments of random matrices and associated zeta functions, we study inverse power trace moments of the Laguerre ensemble of dimension $N$ and inverse temperature parameter $β>0$. We consider a large $N$ regime determined by the low-lying eigenvalues of the ensemble known as the hard edge. In the classical cases $β\in \{1,2,4\}$, we obtain explicit results for the inverse moments and extend these to formulae for the corresponding Mellin transforms. In the case of general $β>0$, by a result of Fyodorov and Le Doussal, we obtain a different formula for the moments given as a sum over partitions. We use this to consider a low temperature limit where $β\to \infty$ as $N \to \infty$. In this limit, we show that the moments are given in terms of the Bessel zeta function.

Method: 利用非交换L^p范数（non-commutative L^p norms）的凸性性质，构建忠实态与任意激发态之间相对熵的数学界定框架。该方法适用于广义冯·诺依曼代数，包括量子场论中的III型局部代数。

Result: 成功建立了不依赖相对模算子（relative modular operator）的相对熵界定方法。作为应用，证明了光线上手征流（chiral current）的真空态与稠密单粒子态集合之间的相对熵具有一致有界性。

Conclusion: 该方法为量子场论中III型代数相对熵的计算提供了新工具，特别适用于相对模算子未知的情况，并通过手征流的具体实例验证了其有效性。

Abstract: We show how one can use the convexity of non-commutative $L^p$ norms to bound the relative entropy between a faithful state on a von Neumann algebra and an arbitrary excitation thereof. Our results hold for general von Neumann algebras, including the local algebras of type III that are ubiquitous in quantum field theory, and do not require knowledge of the relative modular operator. As an application of our results, we prove that for the chiral current on a light ray, the relative entropy between the vacuum and a dense set of single-particle states is uniformly bounded.

</details>


### [214] [Eigenvalue asymptotics of Müller minimizers for atoms and molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18386)
*Rupert L. Frank,Long Meng,Phan Thành Nam,Heinz Siedentop*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了原子和分子Müller泛函极小化子的谱性质，证明了在特定条件下第k个特征值以A_* k^{-8/3}的渐近行为趋于无穷，其中常数A_*由极小化子的密度显式确定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有N个电子和总核电荷Z的原子和分子的Müller泛函极小化子的谱性质。特别关注特征值在k→∞时的渐近行为，这对于理解量子系统的电子结构具有重要意义。

Method: 采用Müller理论框架，证明过程受到Sobolev关于薛定谔基态单粒子密度矩阵渐近行为研究的启发。分析需要处理极小化子积分核在对角线附近的奇异行为以及无穷远处的衰减性质等新要素。

Result: 在Z和N满足适当假设条件下，Müller极小化子γ_*的第k个特征值具有A_* k^{-8/3}的渐近行为，其中常数A_*>0由γ_*的密度显式确定。在原子情况下，当Z足够大且N≤Z-C_0 Z^{1/3}时假设成立。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了Müller泛函极小化子特征值的渐近标度律（scaling law），揭示了其与薛定谔基态不同的数学特性，为量子化学中的密度泛函理论提供了重要的理论支持。

Abstract: We study the spectral properties of minimizers of the Müller functional for atoms and molecules with $N$ electrons and total nuclear charge $Z$. We prove that under some suitable assumptions on $Z$ and $N$, the $k$-th eigenvalue of a Müller minimizer $γ_*$ behaves as $A_* k^{-8/3}$ when $k\to \infty$, with a constant $A_*>0$ determined explicitly by the density of $γ_*$. In particular, in the atomic case $V=Z|x|^{-1}$ our assumption holds if $Z$ is sufficiently large and $N\le Z- C_0 Z^{1/3}$. While our proof is inspired by Sobolev's work on the asymptotic behavior of the one-particle density matrix of Schrödinger ground states, the analysis in Müller theory requires several new ingredients concerning both the singular behavior of the integral kernel of the minimizers near the diagonal and the decay properties at infinity.

*Nicholas R. Allgood*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了有限维希尔伯特空间张量积中同步子空间的保持与稳定性，建立了ε-相容动力学的漂移界限，并在群对称性下刻画了同步保持动力学的代数结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析量子系统中同步子空间的动力学行为，特别是当局部子系统存在自伴算子时，如何量化同步状态的保持程度及其在对称性下的结构特性。

Method: 方法包括：定义同步子空间为差分算子$K = T_A \otimes I - I \otimes T_B$的核；分析ε-相容动力学条件$||[H,K]|| \leq ε$；在有限群对称性下利用张量积分解和等变分量理论。

Result: 主要结果包括：1) 对于ε-相容动力学，初始同步状态偏离核的速率至多为时间的线性函数，斜率为ε，且该估计在主导阶是最优的；2) 在有限群对称性下，同步子空间与张量积分解中的对角等变分量重合，同步保持动力学的代数结构被刻画为群作用和同步算子交换子的交集。

Conclusion: 结论表明同步子空间在近似相容动力学下具有线性漂移特性，且在群对称性框架下具有清晰的代数结构，为量子同步现象的分析提供了严格的理论基础。

Abstract: We study the preservation and stability of synchronization subspaces in tensor products of finite-dimensional Hilbert spaces. Given self-adjoint operators $T_A$ and $T_B$ on local subsystems, the synchronization subspace is defined as the kernel of the difference operator $K = T_A \otimes I - I \otimes T_B$. We establish two main results: First for $ε$-compatible dynamics satisfying $||[H,K]|| \leq ε$, we prove a sharp drift bound where any initially synchronized state deviates from the kernel at a rate at most linear in time with slope $ε$. We show by explicit construction that this estimate is optimal to leading order. Second in the presence of finite group symmetry, we show that the synchronization subspace coincides with the diagonal isotypic component in the tensor product decomposition and we characterize the algebra of synchronization-preserving dynamics as the intersection of the commutants of the group action and synchronization operator.

</details>

Result: 与完整求和参考方法相比，采样伙伴近似在显著降低计算成本的同时保持了良好的一致性，使大规模低噪声模拟成为可能，并揭示了离散动量空间网格引起的系统性数值振荡。

Abstract: We investigate Pauli-consistent ensemble Monte Carlo simulations of graphene with explicit intraband electron-electron scattering. Comparison with the full-sum reference shows close agreement together with a substantial reduction in computational cost, enabling large-ensemble low-noise simulations. In this regime, systematic oscillatory components become clearly resolved in ensemble-averaged time traces. We show that these oscillations are numerical and originate from deterministic drift on the discretized momentum-space grid. We also discuss a procedure for reducing their impact in recorded observables without modifying the underlying Monte Carlo dynamics.

### [217] [Emergent Information Formation in Prebiotic Protocell Clusters: A Computational Mechanics Framework of $ε$-Machines and Attractor Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16553)

Method: 采用物理引导的粗粒化方法，将Casimir-Lifshitz力作用下形成的介观尺度簇系统表示为ε-机器（ε-machine）。这种确定性自动机的因果状态对应簇吸引子，状态转移编码有序重构路径。

Result: Casimir-Lifshitz力在生命起源前真实条件下驱动原始细胞形成四面体、八面体和13细胞二十面体等高度对称介观簇。这些簇作为持久宏观态，其确定性重构路径可被ε-机器精确描述，形成信息、因果和计算闭合的自主原软件层。

Conclusion: 生命前信息并非源于聚合物，而是来自物理簇过程中的吸引子记忆和结构化转移动力学。这种基于Casimir-Lifshitz力的机制为生命起源提供了一种新的物理-信息框架。

This interaction stabilizes mesoscale clusters such as tetrahedra, octahedra, and 13-cell icosahedra. These highly symmetric assemblies act as persistent macrostates whose transitions remain reproducible despite microscopic noise. A physics-guided coarse-graining yields a well-defined mesodynamics that can be represented as an $ε$-machine: a small deterministic automaton whose causal states correspond to cluster attractors and whose transitions encode ordered reconfiguration pathways. The theory of Rosas et al. (Software in the natural world) shows that such systems can become informationally, causally, and computationally closed, thereby forming an autonomous proto-software layer. In this framework, prebiotic information does not arise from polymers but from attractor-based memory and structured transition dynamics in a purely physical cluster process.

### [218] [Conformal Elastodynamics in 2D Dilational Metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16637)
*Neel Singh,Audrey A. Watkins,Giovanni Bordiga,Vincent Tournat,Katia Bertoldi,Zeb Rocklin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了柔性机械超材料（flexible mechanical metamaterial）在有限频率驱动下的非线性波响应，发现其均匀膨胀机制（uniform dilational mechanism）产生了共形对称性（conformal symmetry），导致低频响应由边界集中的空间变化旋转和膨胀主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 柔性机械结构在小载荷下可发生大变形，能够在有限频率驱动下产生复杂非线性波响应。研究旨在探索由刚性正方形通过柔性铰链（flexible hinges）连接构成的典型柔性机械超材料的动力学特性。

Method: 研究采用由刚性正方形通过柔性铰链连接构成的典型柔性机械超材料模型。在理想关节（ideal joints）极限下，该材料具有-1的泊松比（Poisson ratio），并支持均匀膨胀变形模式。

Result: 研究发现该系统的均匀膨胀变形模式产生了共形对称性，动力学在广泛的物理变换——共形映射（conformal maps）下近似不变。低频响应由边界集中的空间变化旋转和膨胀主导，即使在高频下，每个共形映射也意味着守恒的空间复动量（spatially complex momentum）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个新框架，为探索膨胀超材料中的共形波现象开辟了基本途径，并为控制非线性波和振动提供了潜在策略。实验参数如材料刚度、几何形状和晶胞数量等允许实验共形动量接近守恒状态。

Abstract: Flexible mechanical structures can undergo large deformations under small loads, enabling large, complex, and nonlinear wave responses under finite-frequency driving. Here, we study a dynamically driven canonical flexible mechanical metamaterial composed of rigid squares connected at their corners by flexible hinges. This metamaterial supports a uniform dilational mechanism and, in the limit of ideal joints, exhibits a Poisson ratio of -1. The presence of this dilational mode of deformation gives rise to a conformal symmetry, in which the dynamics are approximately invariant under a wide class of physical transformations -- conformal maps. We find that the low-frequency response of the system is dominated by conformal deformations consisting of spatially varying rotations and dilations concentrated at the boundary. Even at high frequencies, each conformal map implies a conserved spatially complex momentum. We explore how experimental parameters such as material stiffnesses and the geometry and number of unit cells allow experimental conformal momenta to approach this conservation, varying slowly compared to the non-conformal momenta of same order. These results constitute a new framework opening fundamental avenues for the study of conformal wave phenomena in dilational metamaterials as well as potential strategies for controlling nonlinear waves and vibrations.

### [220] [Impact dynamics of flexible hydrogels on solid substrates of different wettabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16811)
*Akash Chowdhury,Surjyasish Mitra,Sushanta K. Mitra*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验探究了聚丙烯酰胺水凝胶球在不同弹性数（El）下的撞击行为，揭示了从低El的混合多孔弹性响应到高El的neo-Hookean能量平衡描述的转变机制，并发现冲击力标度关系和回弹抑制现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解水凝胶球撞击固体表面时的复杂动力学行为，特别是在广泛的剪切模量和冲击速度范围内，探究弹性数（elastic number, El）对瞬态铺展形态和冲击力的影响。

Method: 采用球形聚丙烯酰胺水凝胶球进行实验，覆盖五个数量级的弹性数变化范围，在亲水和疏水基底上进行撞击。通过同步高速成像和压电力传感技术，同时解析瞬态铺展形态和冲击力。

Result: 在低弹性数（El < 1）时，水凝胶表现出混合多孔弹性响应：液体富集的接触足从聚合物网络中排出并独立铺展，而主体液滴经历粘弹性接触线钉扎形成薄饼状几何。在高弹性数（El > 1）时，接触足铺展被抑制，变形可由neo-Hookean能量平衡准确描述。归一化峰值冲击力在El < 1时符合Wagner极限，在El > 1时遵循幂律标度F* ∼ El^{0.38}。

Conclusion: 水凝胶撞击行为由弹性数主导，存在从多孔弹性到纯弹性响应的转变。撞击后回缩在几乎所有参数空间都被抑制，仅当弹性恢复力超过粘附功时才发生回弹，这归因于吸附的聚合物链将凝胶网络锚定在基底上。

Abstract: In this work, we perform experiments with spherical polyacrylamide (PAAm) hydrogel drops/spheres, spanning a broad range of shear moduli and impact velocities on hydrophilic (plasma-treated glass) and hydrophobic (silane-coated) substrates, yielding an elastic number El variation of five orders of magnitude. Transient spreading morphology and impact force were simultaneously resolved using synchronized high-speed imaging and piezoelectric force sensing. At low elastic numbers ($El < 1$), impacting hydrogels exhibit a hybrid poroelastic response: a liquid-rich contact foot is expelled from the polymer network and spreads independently, while the bulk drop undergoes viscoelastic contact-line pinning into a pancake geometry at maximum deformation. At high elastic numbers ($El > 1$), contact foot spreading is suppressed, and deformation is accurately described by a neo-Hookean energy balance, yielding a maximum spreading factor independent of substrate wettability. Further, we show that the normalized peak impact force $F^*$ collapses to a constant value consistent with the Wagner limit for $El < 1$ and follows a power-law scaling $F^* \sim El^{0.38}$ for $El > 1$, in close agreement with both Hertzian and neo-Hookean predictions, and independent of substrate wettability. Furthermore, we highlight that post-impact retraction is suppressed across nearly the entire parameter space due to adsorbed polymer chains anchoring the receding gel network to the substrate, producing circumferential ridge instabilities; rebound occurs only when elastic restoring forces overcome the work of adhesion.

### [221] [Motility and interfacial instability of confined chemically active droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16994)
*Pawan Kumar,Sobiya Ashraf,Naveen Tiwari,Dipin Pillai,Rahul Mangal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了液晶微液滴在受限通道中从稳态形状向动态界面波动转变的现象，发现表面活性剂浓度变化可触发界面波动，并识别出Yih-Marangoni不稳定性作为振荡机制，为受限活性物质的自适应运动提供了新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微生物在狭窄空间中运动面临显著的水动力学挑战，需要自适应策略维持高效运动。虽然人工微液滴能够穿越比其直径更窄的通道，但现有研究主要局限于稳态形状机制，缺乏对动态界面波动行为的理解。

Method: 研究使用5CB（4'-戊基-4-氰基联苯）液滴置于溴化三甲基铵（TTAB）水溶液中，通过改变溶质浓度或表面活性剂浓度来触发界面波动。采用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）识别振荡的物理机制。

Result: 在稀溶液中液滴保持稳态形状，而添加溶质或提高表面活性剂浓度会引发显著的界面波动。两种状态下的液滴速度对受限比（confinement ratio）有相似依赖性：先减速后饱和，由润滑膜（lubrication film）内的水动力阻力与泳动流（phoretic flow）竞争决定。表面活性剂浓度增加会提高毛细数（capillary number），形成更厚的润滑层，促进对称破缺转变（symmetry-breaking transition）。

Conclusion: 线性稳定性分析确定Yih-Marangoni不稳定性是界面振荡的潜在机制，揭示了受限活性物质（confined active matter）中一种先前未被认识的自适应运动模式。界面波动从双侧波动转变为单侧局域模式，形成与液滴前部流场波动强耦合的行波模式（traveling-wave pattern）。

Abstract: Microorganisms navigating through narrow spaces encounter significant hydrodynamic challenges. To overcome these constraints and sustain efficient motion, they employ adaptive strategies, including adaptive oscillatory body deformations. While artificial microdroplets can traverse channels narrower than their diameter, studies of their locomotion have thus far been largely restricted to steady-shape regimes. In this work, we demonstrate a transition from steady shape to dynamic interfacial undulations in 5CB (4'-pentyl-4-cyanobiphenyl) droplets within aqueous trimethylammonium bromide (TTAB) solutions. We show that while droplets in dilute, additive-free solutions maintain a steady shape, the introduction of solutes or higher surfactant concentrations triggers pronounced interfacial undulations. Notably, both steady and undulating droplets exhibit a comparable velocity dependence on the confinement ratio, characterized by an initial deceleration followed by saturation, governed by the competition between hydrodynamic resistance and phoretic flow within the lubrication film. Furthermore, we find that increased surfactant concentration increases the capillary number, resulting in a thicker lubrication layer that facilitates a symmetry-breaking transition. Upon varying confinement, the droplet interface shifts from bilateral undulations to a mode localized on one side, forming a traveling-wave pattern strongly coupled to flow field fluctuations at the droplet's anterior. Linear stability analysis identifies the Yih-Marangoni instability as the underlying mechanism for these oscillations, revealing a previously unrecognized mode of adaptive locomotion in confined active matter.

</details>


### [222] [From Flow to Form: Emergence of the Cytokinetic Ring via Active Cortical Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17349)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细胞分裂过程中，皮层（cortex）内发生主动流动，这些流动和应力导致细胞形状变化，特别是细胞中部的尖锐内陷。研究旨在理解皮层流动模式如何形成并驱动细胞分裂过程中的形态变化。

Method: 采用三维相场模拟（3D phase field simulation）活性可变形壳层（active deformable shell），捕捉皮层速度与向列序（nematic order）的耦合动力学。同时分析更简单的活性梯度驱动压缩流模型（activity gradient driven compressive flow model）。

Result: 模拟显示类向列型肌动球蛋白环（nematic like actomyosin ring）在赤道处自发形成并驱动尖锐内陷（sharp invagination）。不同皮层流动模式（包括分裂沟附近的逆向旋转流）源于初始向列排列偏差（bias in the initial nematic alignment），而非肌动蛋白丝固有手性（intrinsic chirality）。

Conclusion: 皮层流动模式的形成机制揭示了系统的记忆效应（memory effect），通过分析简化模型阐明了导致内陷和逆向流动的表面不稳定性（surface instability）主要成分。

Abstract: During cell division active flows occur in the cortex, a thin layer of gel like network of acto myosin filaments, beneath the cell surface. The cortical flow and the associated stresses bring about change in the cell shape, in particular a sharp invagination at the mid cell. Using 3D phase field simulation of an active deformable shell, which captures coupled dynamics of cortical velocity and nematic order, we show how a nematic like actomyosin ring spontaneously emerge at the equator and drive sharp invagination. We further demonstrate how different cortical flow patterns, including counter rotating flows emerge near the division furrow. We show that these flow patterns, often attributed to intrinsic chirality of actomyosin filaments can instead arise from bias in the initial nematic alignment, revealing a memory effect in the system. By analyzing a simpler model of activity gradient driven compressive flow on a flat interface we decipher the main ingredients for surface instability leading to invagination and counter moving flows.

</details>


### [223] [Observation of Compressional Acoustic Wave Responses in Cell Culture Media Using a Quartz Crystal Microbalance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17403)
*Hansa Kannan,Ram Prakash Babu,Trisha Ghosh,Arpita Mohapatra,Mainak Dutta,Adarsh Ganesan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了石英晶体微天平（QCM）在细胞培养基（DMEM和RPMI-1640）中由压缩波（compressional wave）效应引起的周期性振荡现象，揭示了液滴体积对振荡频率和幅度的显著影响，强调了在细胞存在条件下解释QCM数据时需明确考虑此类压缩波伪影。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典QCM理论主要考虑剪切波（shear-wave）在半无限牛顿流体中的耦合，但有限液体厚度和声学反射会产生显著的压缩波（longitudinal wave）效应，强烈调制共振频率和运动电阻。在液相传感（如细胞悬浮液）中，必须正确考虑此类压缩波响应。

Method: 使用5 MHz AT-cut QCM，在不同液滴体积下系统研究DMEM和RPMI-1640细胞培养基中的压缩波响应。时间分辨测量通过四个参数进行分析：压缩声波的时间周期（Tca）、共振频率与电阻振荡之间的相位偏移时间（Tp）、频率峰峰值偏移（Δfpp）和电阻峰峰值偏移（ΔRpp）。

Result: DMEM和RPMI-1640均表现出强烈的体积依赖性周期性振荡。在较低体积时，呈现约40分钟的低频振荡；随着体积增加，逐渐演变为约5分钟的高频振荡（Tca）。Δfpp约为100-150 Hz，ΔRpp约为40-60 Ω，共振频率与电阻振荡之间存在约10分钟的相位偏移（Tp）。

Conclusion: 即使在简单的细胞培养基中也会出现压缩波伪影（compressional-wave artifacts），因此在细胞存在条件下解释QCM数据时，必须明确考虑这些效应。该发现对生物和软物质界面研究中的QCM应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Quartz Crystal Microbalance (QCM) sensors are widely used to study biological and soft-matter interfaces due to their exceptional sensitivity to mass loading and interfacial mechanical properties. While classical QCM theory assumes predominantly shear-wave coupling into a semi-infinite Newtonian liquid, finite liquid thickness and acoustic reflections give rise to pronounced compressional (longitudinal) wave effects that strongly modulate both resonance frequency and motional resistance. Such compressional acoustic-wave responses should be properly accounted for when sensing in the liquid phase, for instance when working with cell suspensions. In this work, we systematically investigate compressional-wave responses in cell culture media including DMEM and RPMI-1640 across varying droplet volumes using a 5 MHz AT-cut QCM. Time-resolved measurements are analyzed using four parameters: the time period of compressional acoustic waves (Tca), the time associated with a phase shift between resonance frequency and resistance oscillations (Tp), the peak-to-peak shifts in frequency (Δfpp) and resistance (ΔRpp). DMEM and RPMI-1640 both exhibit strong volume-dependent periodic oscillations. At lower volumes, they exhibit low-frequency oscillations with a time period of approximately 40 minutes. However, as volume increases, the oscillations gradually evolve into high-frequency oscillations with a time period Tca of approximately 5 minutes. The peak-to-peak shifts (Δfpp) and (ΔRpp) are approximately 100-150 Hz and 40-60 Ω, respectively. The resonance frequency and resistance oscillations also exhibit a phase shift Tp of approximately 10 minutes. These results highlight that compressional-wave artifacts occur even in simple cell culture media, necessitating their explicit consideration when interpreting QCM data in the presence of cells.

### [224] [Hydrodynamic theory of chemically active emulsions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17539)
*Efe Ilker,Kathrin Laxhuber,Jean-Francois Joanny,Frank Jülicher*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了化学活性乳液（chemically active emulsions）在流体力学极限下的系统理论，构建了热力学一致框架，通过燃料分子的化学稳态（chemo-stating）打破平衡。该理论扩展了活性模型B+（Active Model B+），预测了微相分离、气泡相分离和动态活性丝状相等新相行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立化学活性乳液在流体力学极限下的系统理论框架。通过构建热力学一致（thermodynamically consistent）的框架，在平衡被燃料分子的化学稳态打破的情况下，研究三元溶液（ternary solutions）中活性化学反应的有效动力学。

Method: 方法包括构建热力学一致框架，考虑时间反演对称性破缺（broken time reversal symmetry），推导长时空尺度下守恒场动力学的有效动力学。理论扩展了活性模型B+（Active Model B+），包含梯度展开中的高阶项。数值研究采用具有活性化学反应的Flory-Huggins模型。

Result: 理论预测当有效界面能系数变为负值时形成微相（microphases）。包含噪声时存在气泡相分离（bubbly phase separation）。识别出新相行为——动态活性丝状相（dynamic active filament phase）。稳态熵产率（entropy production rate）随驱动化学势增加，在向动态活性丝状相转变时呈现类扭结奇异性（kink-like singularity）。

Conclusion: 研究表明活性相分离（active phase separation）的通用行为可在化学活性乳液中涌现。该工作扩展了活性模型B+理论，为化学活性乳液系统提供了热力学一致的理论框架，揭示了多种新相行为及其与熵产率的关系。

Abstract: We present a systematic theory of chemically active emulsions in the hydrodynamic limit by constructing a thermodynamically consistent framework in which the equilibrium is broken by chemo-stating of fuel molecules. For ternary solutions with active chemical reactions, we obtain an effective dynamics of the conserved field dynamics at long length and time scales. The effective dynamics takes into account the broken time reversal symmetry that manifests itself by the emergence of gradient terms akin to those of Active Model B+, which is a generic theory of active phase separation. In addition to the active coefficients modifying the interfacial energy coefficient, the theory contains higher order terms in the gradient expansion that are necessary to correctly describe the dynamics of chemically active emulsions, extending thus Active Model B+. We study numerically a Flory-Huggins model with active chemical reactions. Our theory predicts the formation of microphases when the effective interfacial energy coefficient becomes negative. Moreover, including noise, we show the existence of bubbly phase separation. We also identify a new type of phase behavior, a dynamic active filament phase. Finally, we discuss the steady state entropy production rate in the system resulting from the active chemical reactions. We observe that the total entropy production rate increases with the driving chemical potential and exhibits a kink-like singularity at the transition to the dynamic active filament phase. Our work shows that the generic behaviors of active phase separation can emerge in chemically active emulsions.

*Hao Wu,Zhong-Can Ou-Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电胶体晶体中静电屏蔽与弹性形变存在微妙的相互作用。在各项异性弹性介质中，膨胀与局部离子环境的耦合具有方向依赖性，导致特定晶轴方向的纵向声学响应优先软化。

Method: 从由标量耦合常数λ_g重整化的有效静态弹性张量出发，推导了立方晶体在一般静电-弹性耦合下的长波长静态稳定性条件。通过球形维格纳-赛茨元胞中的泊松-玻尔兹曼理论对λ_g进行了微观推导。

Result: 获得了均匀不稳定性发生的显式条件：最先失去刚度的方向由该方向上的逆克里斯托费尔矩阵确定。给出了[100]、[110]和[111]高对称方向的临界耦合λ_g^c的闭合形式表达式。

Conclusion: 该框架可作为诊断工具，用于解释静态压缩性或低频声学软化中的方向异常，无需完整晶格动力学计算即可识别最脆弱方向，并通过软胶体组装的实验测量弹性模量验证了判据的预测能力。

Abstract: Charged colloidal crystals exhibit a subtle interplay between electrostatic screening and elastic deformation. In an anisotropic elastic medium the coupling between dilation and the local ionic environment becomes direction dependent, leading to a preferential softening of the longitudinal acoustic response along specific crystallographic axes. This article provides a self-contained derivation of the long-wavelength static stability condition for cubic crystals subject to a generic electrostatic-elastic coupling. Starting from an effective static elastic tensor renormalized by a scalar coupling constant $λ_g$, we obtain an explicit condition for the onset of a homogeneous instability: the direction $\hat{\mathbf{k}}$ that first loses rigidity is determined by the inverse Christoffel matrix evaluated along that direction. Closed-form expressions for the critical coupling $λ_g^c$ are given for the $[100]$, $[110]$, and $[111]$ high-symmetry directions. We further provide a microscopic derivation of $λ_g$ from the Poisson-Boltzmann theory in a spherical Wigner-Seitz cell, linking the phenomenological constant to experimentally accessible parameters such as salt concentration, particle charge, and volume fraction. The analysis reveals that the most fragile direction can be identified without full lattice-dynamical calculations, and the associated unstable strain patterns are discussed. Numerical illustrations using experimentally measured elastic moduli of soft colloidal assemblies demonstrate the predictive power of the criterion. The present framework serves as a diagnostic tool for interpreting directional anomalies in static compressibility or low-frequency acoustic softening.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁活性弹性体（magneto-active elastomers, MAEs）在外部磁场下表现出强磁-力耦合效应，具有可调刚度、可逆形状变化和非线性磁响应等特性。理解MAEs中磁滞（magnetic hysteresis）的起源对于材料设计和实际应用优化至关重要。

Method: 研究提出了一个多尺度理论框架（multiscale theoretical framework），将系统总能量表述为磁性能和微观力学贡献之和。首先通过纯偶极子-偶极子相互作用（dipole-dipole interactions）模拟粒子相互作用，然后扩展到包括近距离粒子分离时的高阶近场效应（higher-order near-field effects）。

Result: 结果表明，具有软磁颗粒的MAEs中的磁滞主要源于被困的微观结构重排（trapped microstructural rearrangements），导致在增加和减少磁场下形成不同的粒子构型。参数研究表明，粒子体积分数、样品纵横比和基体刚度强烈影响微观结构演化和磁滞回线宽度。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架为建模磁滞现象提供了坚实基础，这对于MAEs在实际应用中的设计和优化至关重要。该研究揭示了微观结构演化在磁滞形成中的关键作用。

Abstract: Magneto-active elastomers (MAEs) are polymer composites consisting of magnetic microparticles embedded in an elastomeric matrix. These materials exhibit strong magneto-mechanical coupling under external magnetic fields, resulting in tunable stiffness, reversible shape changes, and nonlinear magnetic responses. This study presents a multiscale theoretical framework to investigate the origin of magnetic hysteresis in MAEs, with emphasis on the evolution of the internal microstructure during magnetization and demagnetization. The total energy of the system is formulated as the sum of magnetic and micromechanical contributions, while macroscopic deformation of a cylindrical MAE sample is fully constrained. Particle interactions are modeled first via pure dipole-dipole interactions and then extended to include higher-order near-field effects at close particle separations. The results show that hysteresis in MAEs with magnetically soft particles primarily arises from trapped microstructural rearrangements, leading to distinct particle configurations under increasing and decreasing magnetic fields. Parametric studies demonstrate that particle volume fraction, sample aspect ratio, and matrix stiffness strongly influence the microstructure evolution and the width of resulting hysteresis loops. The proposed framework provides a solid foundation for modeling magnetic hysteresis, which is essential for the design and optimization of MAEs in practical applications.

### [227] [Thermodiffusion in Aqueous Alkali Halide Solutions from Ambient to Supercooled Conditions: Ion-Specific, Structural, and Mass Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18084)
*Guansen Zhao,Fernando Bresme*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过非平衡分子动力学模拟，揭示了水电解质溶液中热扩散的微观机制，发现温度、浓度和离子种类对热导率和Soret系数的影响规律，以及热输运中结构和动力学贡献的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水电解质溶液中的热扩散（thermodiffusion）对温度、浓度和盐组成表现出复杂的依赖性，但其微观起源尚未完全理解。研究旨在通过扩展分析到含K⁺和I⁻离子的系统，评估离子特异性效应。

Method: 采用非平衡分子动力学（non-equilibrium molecular dynamics, NEMD）模拟，研究碱金属卤化物水溶液在240-300 K温度范围和1 m、4 m浓度下的热输运和热扩散现象。在先前NaCl和LiCl研究基础上，扩展到含K⁺和I⁻离子的系统。

Result: 所有系统中，热导率随冷却而降低，且在高盐浓度下普遍降低。Soret系数通常随温度升高而增加，溶液从低温下的亲热性（thermophilic）行为转向高温下的疏热性（thermophobic）行为。观察到明显的离子依赖性趋势，Na⁺和K⁺盐通常比Li⁺盐表现出更强的疏热响应，尤其在碘化物溶液中。

Conclusion: 较低温度和较低浓度有利于形成更四面体有序、类低密度液体（LDL-like）的水环境，这与增强的亲热性相关。反转温度（inversion temperatures）和质量效应分析表明，热输运（heat of transport）包含结构和动力学贡献。这些发现为水电解质中水合结构、离子质量和热扩散输运之间的相互作用提供了分子水平见解。

Abstract: Thermodiffusion in aqueous electrolyte solutions exhibits complex dependencies on temperature, concentration, and salt composition, yet its microscopic origins remain incompletely understood. Here, we employ non-equilibrium molecular dynamics (NEMD) simulations to investigate thermal transport and thermodiffusion in aqueous alkali halide solutions over the temperature range 240-300 K at concentrations of 1 m and 4 m. Building on previous studies of NaCl and LiCl, we extend the analysis to systems containing K$^+$ and I$^-$ ions to assess ion-specific effects. Across all systems studied, the thermal conductivity decreases upon cooling and is generally reduced at higher salt concentration. The Soret coefficient generally increases with temperature, shifting the solutions from thermophilic behavior at low temperature toward more thermophobic behavior at high temperature. Clear ion-dependent trends are observed, with Na$^+$ and K$^+$ salts generally showing stronger thermophobic responses than Li$^+$ salts, especially in iodide solutions. We estimate that the shift in the inversion temperatures of the iodide salts relative to experiment corresponds to a small local offset of the effective heat of transport, 4-5 kJ/mol, showing that small changes in hydration thermodynamics or heat-mass coupling can strongly affect the sign change of the Soret coefficient. Structural analyses indicate that lower temperatures and lower concentrations favor more tetrahedrally ordered, LDL-like water environments, which are associated with enhanced thermophilicity. Analysis of inversion temperatures and mass effects further suggests that the heat of transport contains both structural and kinetic contributions. These findings provide molecular-level insight into the interplay between hydration structure, ionic mass, and thermodiffusive transport in aqueous electrolytes.

### [228] [Impact of Initial Charge Distributions on the Kinetics of Charged Particle Coagulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18415)
*Gustavo Castillo,Nicolás Mujica*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了Smoluchowski凝聚方程，纳入带电簇间的静电相互作用，通过随机蒙特卡洛模拟揭示了电荷分布对粒子聚集动力学的影响，发现电荷异质性在不同时间尺度上可加速或延迟聚集过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解带电颗粒系统中静电相互作用对聚集动力学的影响，扩展经典的Smoluchowski凝聚方程以更准确地描述实际物理系统中的聚集过程，如气溶胶、天体物理凝聚、火山灰聚集等。

Method: 采用随机蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）方法实现扩展的Smoluchowski凝聚方程，将静电相互作用直接纳入经典的布朗碰撞核（Brownian collision kernel），研究不同电荷分布和系统净电荷对簇生长动力学的影响。

Result: 模拟揭示了不同的生长机制：在中间时间尺度，电荷异质性根据初始电荷分布可加速或延迟聚集；在长时间尺度，系统趋向于准稳态，其性质取决于净电荷。高斯分布与柯西-洛伦兹（Cauchy-Lorentz）初始电荷统计的比较表明，重尾分布促进更快的簇生长。

Abstract: We investigate the kinetics of particle aggregation within the framework of the Smoluchowski coagulation equation, extending it to account for electrostatic interactions among charged clusters. Using a stochastic Monte Carlo implementation, we examine how different charge distributions and net system charge affect cluster growth dynamics. Electrostatic interactions are incorporated directly into the classical Brownian collision kernel, yielding charge-dependent modifications of the collision rates that may either enhance or suppress aggregation depending on the signs and magnitudes of the interacting charges. Our simulations reveal distinct regimes of growth: at intermediate times, charge heterogeneity accelerates or delays aggregation depending on the initial underlying charge distribution, while at long times the system tends toward quasi--stationary states whose properties depend on the net charge. Comparisons between Gaussian and Cauchy--Lorentz initial charge statistics highlight the role of heavy-tailed distributions in promoting faster cluster growth. These findings contribute to a unified understanding of coagulation kinetics in charged particulate systems, with potential implications for aerosol and astrophysical coagulation processes, volcanic ash aggregation, and clustering in industrial fluidized granular beds.

### [229] [Diffusion compaction coupling controls pore pressure dynamics in granular fluid flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18462)
*Eric C. P. Breard,Claudia Elijas Parra,Mattia de' Michieli Vitturi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文揭示了颗粒-流体混合物中过剩孔隙压力（excess pore pressure）的表观扩散率（apparent diffusivity）并非固有属性，而是源于孔隙压力扩散与颗粒压实（compaction）的耦合作用。研究通过引入无量纲源-扩散比Ψ₀，统一解释了床层高度变化近两个数量级时的有效扩散率标度关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒-流体混合物中的过剩孔隙压力能够暂时抑制摩擦接触并显著增强流动迁移性，但其演化通常使用恒定有效扩散率进行建模。现有模型未能充分解释孔隙压力扩散与颗粒骨架变形之间的耦合机制。

Method: 从可变形、气体饱和颗粒集合体的两相质量守恒出发，推导出包含颗粒骨架变形的过剩孔隙压力演化方程。在薄流、小过剩压力极限下，该方程简化为具有时间依赖源项的一维扩散-压实方程。通过模态分析得到简化的基底方程，分离扩散排水与压实驱动作用。

Result: 研究引入的无量纲源-扩散比Ψ₀控制了扩散与压实过程的竞争关系，能够将高分辨率双流体模拟中获得的有效扩散率在床层高度变化近两个数量级范围内统一标度。将这一物理机制纳入深度平均模型后，能够重现实验中观察到的孔隙压力衰减和流动距离的厚度依赖性。

Conclusion: 研究结果为颗粒-流体流动中的孔隙压力演化提供了物理基础描述，阐明了扩散-压实耦合如何控制流动迁移性。表观扩散率及流动迁移性并非固有属性，而是通过扩散与压实竞争依赖于流动厚度。

Abstract: Excess pore pressure in granular--fluid mixtures can transiently suppress frictional contacts and dramatically enhance flow mobility, yet its evolution is commonly modeled using constant effective diffusivities. Here we show that the apparent diffusivity is not intrinsic but emerges from the coupling between pore-pressure diffusion and granular compaction.
  Starting from two-phase mass conservation for a deformable, gas-saturated granular assembly, we derive an evolution equation for excess pore pressure that captures deformation of the granular skeleton. In the thin-flow, small-excess-pressure limit, this reduces to a one-dimensional diffusion--compaction equation with a time-dependent source term controlled by porosity changes.
  A modal analysis yields a reduced basal equation that separates diffusive drainage from compaction-driven forcing and identifies the corresponding timescales. This framework introduces a dimensionless source-to-diffusion ratio, $Ψ_0$, which governs the competition between these processes and collapses effective diffusivities obtained from high-resolution two-fluid simulations over nearly two orders of magnitude in bed height. This scaling implies that the apparent diffusivity, and thus flow mobility, is not intrinsic but depends on flow thickness through the competition between diffusion and compaction.
  Incorporating this physics into a depth-averaged model demonstrates that the resulting closure reproduces the thickness dependence of pore-pressure decay and runout observed in experiments. These results provide a physically grounded description of pore-pressure evolution in granular--fluid flows and clarify how diffusion--compaction coupling controls their mobility.

</details>

### [230] [Effect of gap width on turbulent transition in Taylor-Couette flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16495)
*Chang-Quan Zhou,Hua-Shu Dou,Lin Niu,Wen-Qian Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该研究通过泰勒-库埃特（Taylor-Couette）构型的数值模拟，揭示了间隙宽度对湍流转捩（turbulent transition）的影响规律：间隙宽度越大，流动越稳定，转捩发生越晚。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究泰勒-库埃特流动中，间隙宽度对湍流转捩过程的影响机制，以深化对这类经典旋转流动稳定性的理解。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，在泰勒-库埃特构型下进行过渡流动模拟，保持内柱半径和转速不变，系统改变间隙宽度参数。

Result: 研究发现：1）间隙宽度增大时，流动稳定性增强，转捩延迟；2）间隙内平均速度分布趋近自由涡流（free vortex flow）；3）能量梯度函数（energy gradient function）最大值随间隙宽度增加而减小；4）仅基于间隙宽度的雷诺数（Reynolds number）不足以表征流动行为，需考虑半径比（radius ratio）的影响。

Conclusion: 间隙宽度是影响泰勒-库埃特流动稳定性的关键参数，较大间隙通过改变速度分布和降低能量梯度来延迟湍流转捩，且流动行为的完整描述需要同时考虑间隙宽度和半径比。

Abstract: Simulations of the transitional flow in Taylor-Couette configuration are carried out to study the effect of the gap width on turbulent transition. The research results show that, under the same radius and the rotating speed of the inner cylinder, as the gap width increases, the flow becomes more stable. It is discovered that the average velocity distribution in the gap approaches the free vortex flow as the width increase and the stability of the flow is enhanced. It is found that, as the gap width increases, the maximum of the energy gradient function (from the energy gradient theory) in the gap decreases, which delays the turbulent transition. As such, the larger the gap width, the later the transition occurs. As the gap width increases, the Reynolds number based on the gap width alone is not able to characterize the flow behavior in Taylor-Couette flows, and the effect of the radius ratio should be taken into account.

</details>


### [231] [Directed droplet motion -- Its versatile nature and anticipated applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16974)
*Panagiotis E. Theodorakis,Andrey Milchev*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该论文综述了定向液滴运动（directed droplet motion）领域的关键进展，重点关注利用表面刚度梯度（stiffness gradient）等特性变化实现液滴传输的机制，并展望了在数字微流控（digital microfluidics）和生物诊断（bio-diagnostics）等领域的应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字微流控和生物诊断等应用依赖于液滴运动，其中刚度梯度引发的趋硬性（durotaxis）是实现液体、细胞或纳米物体传输的重要现象。利用表面特性在特定方向上的变化，可作为实现流体传输的通用概念，无论是否有外部能量供给。

Method: 论文采用综述方法，系统回顾了多年来定向液滴运动领域的关键成果与进展。通过分析表面特性变化（如基底图案、拉普拉斯压力变化、润湿性梯度等）对液滴运动的影响机制，探讨了这些现象在技术应用中的潜力。

Result: 论文总结了利用表面特性梯度实现定向液滴运动的关键发现，包括趋硬性现象及其在流体传输中的应用。这些特性变化可引发多种有趣现象，为各种技术中的创新应用提供了基础。

Conclusion: 定向液滴运动研究为流体传输提供了重要机制，特别是在数字微流控和生物诊断领域具有广阔应用前景。论文不仅总结了该领域的关键进展，还提供了对未来应用前景的展望和启示。

Abstract: Applications such as digital microfluidics and bio-diagnostics rely on droplet locomotion. A prominent example of such motion is durotaxis, a phenomenon that requires a stiffness gradient along a surface for the transport of liquids, cells, or other nano-objects. Using surfaces with varying properties in specific directions can be exploited as a universal concept for fluid transport with or without external energy supply. Changes in properties may refer to substrate patterns, Laplace pressure changes, wettability gradients, etc., leading to exciting phenomena, which can be employed in novel applications in various technologies. Here, we report on key results and progress in the area of directed droplet motion over the years, and we provide perspectives and implications for anticipated applications.

</details>


### [232] [Tangential and normal partial slip at the liquid-fluid interfaces: application to a small liquid droplet, gas bubble, and aerosol](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17793)
*Peter Lebedev-Stepanov*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文获得了小液滴在无限大储层中缓慢运动的解析解，推广了传统的Navier和Maxwellian部分滑移边界条件，并推导出描述气泡上升和气溶胶沉降终端速度的新方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在推广传统的部分滑移边界条件，将法向滑移和切向部分滑移纳入分析框架。法向滑移伴随流体密度梯度，仅适用于界面接触相中有一相为气体的情况。

Method: 采用滑移长度（slip length）的广义形式化方法，而非传统的摩擦系数形式化方法。证明被界面分隔的两种流体各自具有独立的滑移长度，并基于此获得解析解。

Result: 获得了描述气泡上升和气溶胶沉降终端速度的新方程，证明上升气泡内部和沉降液滴周围的空气密度不均匀。密度增量相对大小随气泡或气溶胶尺寸增大而增加，结果与实验进行了比较。

Conclusion: 广义Hadamard-Rybczynski方程（HRE）最适用于疏水液体和亲水液体的界面（如水和碳氢化合物、水和高级醇等）。这些乳液在石油工业和医学领域具有重要应用价值，同时考虑了确定滑移长度的实验方法。

Abstract: An analytical solution is obtained for the problem of the slow movement of a small drop of a fluid in another immiscible fluid in an infinitely large reservoir with the boundary condition of the normal slip and/or tangential partial slip at the interface. That generalizes the conventional Navier and Maxwellian boundary conditions of partial slip. Normal slip is accompanied by the density gradient in the fluid and is applicable only if one of the phases in contact at the interface is a gas. Although tangential partial slip and the associated generalization of the Hadamard-Rybczynski equation (HRE) have been considered previously, they were done using the friction coefficient formalism. Here, this issue is discussed within the more general formalism of slip lengths. It is proven that each of the two fluids separated by an interface has its own slip length. New equations describing the terminal velocity of gas bubble rise and aerosol falling have been obtained. The result is compared with experiment. It has been shown that the gas density within a rising bubble and around a falling droplet in the air is not uniform. The relative magnitude of the density increment increases with the size of the bubble or aerosol. Presumably, the best applicability of the generalized HRE should be expected for the interface of hydrophobic liquid and hydrophilic one (water and hydrocarbons, water and higher alcohols, in general: aqueous emulsions, water, lipophilic organic liquids and oils, etc.). These are quite important emulsions in practical terms, for example, for the oil industry and medicine. Experimental methods for determining the slip length are considered.

</details>

### [233] [CaTherine wheels from trees and Liouville quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17170)
*Danny Calegari,Ewain Gwynne*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究凯瑟琳轮（CaTherine wheel）——一种空间填充曲线，并建立了其与二维球面上拓扑树之间的对应关系。特别地，该研究证明了对于γ-Liouville量子引力（LQG）度量的测地树，存在唯一的对应凯瑟琳轮，从而构造了LQG测地树的轮廓探索空间填充曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凯瑟琳轮是一种特殊的空间填充曲线，它能产生二维球面上的一对不相交的稠密拓扑树。研究动机在于建立这类拓扑树与凯瑟琳轮之间的对应关系，并将此理论应用于量子引力领域。

Method: 论文首先给出了凯瑟琳轮的严格数学定义，然后建立了拓扑树成为凯瑟琳轮对应树的充分必要条件。最后将此理论应用于γ-Liouville量子引力（LQG）度量的测地树（geodesic tree）研究。

Result: 研究获得了二维球面上拓扑树成为凯瑟琳轮对应树的充要条件。应用此结果证明了对于γ∈(0,2)的γ-Liouville量子引力（LQG）度量，存在唯一的凯瑟琳轮对应于以无穷远点为根的测地树（geodesic tree）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构造了LQG测地树的轮廓探索（contour exploration）空间填充曲线，建立了凯瑟琳轮理论与量子引力几何结构之间的重要联系，为理解LQG度量下的几何结构提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: A CaTherine wheel is a space-filling curve $f : S^1\to S^2$ such that for every closed interval $J\subset S^1$, $f(J)$ is homeomorphic to a closed disk and $f(\partial J)$ is contained in $\partial f(J)$. A CaTherine wheel gives rise to a pair of disjoint, dense topological trees in $S^2$ which roughly speaking lie to the left and right of $f$. We give necessary and sufficient conditions for a topological tree in $S^2$ to arise as one of these trees for some CaTherine wheel $f$. We apply this result to show that there is a unique CaTherine wheel corresponding to the geodesic tree rooted at $\infty$ for the $γ$-Liouville quantum gravity (LQG) metric, for $γ\in (0,2)$. In other words, we construct the space-filling curve which is the contour exploration of the LQG geodesic tree.

</details>


### [234] [Uniform analyticity of local observables in FK-percolation and analyticity of the Ising spontaneous magnetisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18558)
*Lucas D'Alimonte,Loïc Gassmann*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了在FK渗流（FK-percolation）模型中，局部事件的概率在渗流参数p下具有一致解析性（uniform analyticity），并满足一致指数增长界。该结果进一步用于证明Potts模型的磁化强度（magnetisation）在特定参数范围内的解析性，以及q色Potts模型在亚临界区间（subcritical interval）的磁化率（susceptibility）解析性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究FK渗流模型中局部事件概率的解析性质，旨在建立这些概率在渗流参数p下的一致解析性和指数增长界。这一基础结果对于分析相关统计物理模型的解析性质至关重要，特别是Potts模型在超临界（supercritical）和亚临界（subcritical）区域的各种物理量。

Method: 采用概率论方法，在测度满足适当混合条件（mixing assumptions）的前提下，证明FK渗流模型中局部事件概率的一致解析性。基于这一核心结果，进一步推导Potts模型磁化强度和磁化率的解析性质，涵盖多维Ising模型（Ising case）和任意q≥2的Potts模型。

Result: 主要结果包括：1) FK渗流模型中局部事件概率在渗流参数p下具有一致解析性，并满足一致指数增长界；2) Potts模型的磁化强度在适当参数范围内解析，包括所有维度d≥3的Ising模型在整个超临界区域；3) 任意q≥2的q色Potts模型磁化率在整个亚临界区间解析；4) FK渗流测度中多种量的解析性，包括多点（multi-point）和截断多点连通概率（truncated multi-point connectivity probabilities）。

Conclusion: 研究建立了FK渗流模型局部事件概率的一致解析性质，并成功应用于证明Potts模型在超临界和亚临界区域关键物理量的解析性。这些结果为统计力学模型中相变（phase transition）区域的解析行为提供了严格数学基础，特别是对Ising模型和一般Potts模型的解析性质研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: We prove that, in the FK-percolation model, the probabilities of local events are uniformly analytic in the percolation parameter $p$ under suitable mixing assumptions on the measure, and satisfy a uniform exponential growth bound. This result allows us to prove that the magnetisation of the Potts model is analytic in a suitable range of parameters, including the Ising case in all dimensions $d \geq 3$ in the whole supercritical regime. We also provide a proof of the analyticity of the susceptibility of the Potts model with $q$ colours, for any $q \geq 2$ in the whole subcritical interval. Finally, we prove the analyticity of various quantities in the FK-percolation measure, including the multi-point and truncated multi-point connectivity probabilities.

</details>


### [235] [Expected perimeter of the convex hull of planar Brownian motion stopped upon exiting the unit disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18427)
*Hugo Panzo,Stjepan Šebek*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该研究计算了平面布朗运动（planar Brownian motion）在单位圆盘（unit disk）内运行直至退出时的凸包（convex hull）的期望周长（expected perimeter），并获得了精确表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是计算平面布朗运动在单位圆盘内运行直至退出时的凸包期望周长，以补充近期关于受限几何中反射布朗运动（reflecting Brownian motion）凸包的研究结果。

Method: 方法是将问题简化为计算布朗运动在退出时刻的最大水平位移（maximum horizontal displacement）的期望值，然后将此最大值重新表述为在"截断圆盘（truncated disk）"域中的调和测度（harmonic measure）问题。

Result: 获得了凸包期望周长的精确表达式，同时得到了凸包期望面积（expected area）的非平凡边界（nontrivial bounds）。

Conclusion: 计算精确的期望面积是一个更为困难的问题，但研究成功获得了期望周长的精确解，为受限布朗运动凸包研究提供了重要补充。

Abstract: We study the convex hull of planar Brownian motion run until the exit time from the unit disk. Our primary objective is to compute the expected perimeter of this convex hull, thereby complementing recent results on the convex hull of reflecting Brownian motion in confined geometries. We reduce the problem to computing the expected value of the Brownian motion's maximum horizontal displacement at the exit time, and then recast this maximum in terms of harmonic measure in a domain we call the truncated disk. In particular, we obtain an exact expression for the expected perimeter. We also obtain nontrivial bounds on the expected area of this convex hull and comment on why computing the exact expected area is a much harder problem.

</details>

### [236] [Continuous-wave nuclear laser absorption spectroscopy of Thorium-229](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16640)
*I. Morawetz,T. Riebner,L. Toscani De Col,F. Schneider,N. Sempelmann,F. Schaden,M. Bartokos,G. A. Kazakov,S. Lahs,K. Beeks,B. Gerstenecker,A. Grüneis,M. Pimon,T. Schumm,V. Lal,G. Zitzer,J. Tiedau,M. V. Okhapkin,V. Petrov,E. Peik*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次使用连续波激光（功率<1 nW）成功激发钍-229同位素的低能核跃迁，并通过吸收光谱而非荧光检测共振信号，为开发高稳定固态光学核钟提供了关键技术突破。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钍-229同位素的低能核跃迁为实现高稳定固态光学核钟提供了前景，但此前需要脉冲激光系统且只有少量光子与窄核跃迁共振。本研究旨在开发更高效的连续波激光激发和检测方法。

Method: 采用基于三次连续倍频的连续波激光系统，从1187 nm二极管激光器开始，通过吸收光谱（absorption spectroscopy）而非荧光检测来定量表征氟化钙中两种不同的钍中心（Th-centers）。

Result: 成功使用功率小于1 nW的连续波激光激发核共振，并通过吸收检测获得共振信号。测量了两种钍中心的异构体位移（isomeric shift），其中一个中心显示出极小的静态电场晶体场梯度（<0.1 V/Å²），表明其具有高对称性离子环境。

Conclusion: 连续波激光激发结合吸收检测方法消除了缓慢的核荧光衰变过程，为快速信号采集的时钟操作提供了显著优势。高对称性钍中心的发现预示着对晶格间距不敏感的核共振谱线，推动了固态光学核钟的发展。

Abstract: A low-energy nuclear transition in the isotope thorium-229 has been excited in thorium-doped crystals with laser light. This opens the perspective towards a highly stable and robust solid-state optical nuclear clock. The required laser radiation at 148 nm wavelength has so far been produced using pulsed laser systems where only a small fraction of the incident photons has been resonant with the narrow nuclear transition. Here we show that the nuclear resonance can be excited with a continuous-wave laser source with a power of less than 1 nW, and that the resonance signal can be detected in absorption rather than in fluorescence. This eliminates the slow nuclear fluorescence decay from the detection process and offers a considerable advantage for clock operation through fast signal acquisition. The laser is based on three sequential frequency doublings, starting from a diode laser at 1187 nm that is well suited for linewidth narrowing and for frequency comparisons with optical atomic clocks. We use absorption spectroscopy for the quantitative characterization of two different Th-centers in calcium fluoride and measure the isomeric shift between them. One of the centers shows a very small static electric crystal field gradient < 0.1V/$Å^2$, to be compared to gradients in the range of 100 V/$Å^2$ observed earlier. This indicates a center with high symmetry of the ions surrounding the Th nucleus, promising nuclear resonance lines that are less sensitive to the lattice spacing.

</details>

### [237] [AURORA: A High Performance DAQ Framework for Next-Generation Rare-Event Search Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17218)
*Yihan Guo,Xiaofeng Shang,Chang Cai,Weihao Wu,Xun Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了AURORA分布式数据采集框架，采用模块化架构，利用现代I/O和网络技术，包括多级缓冲、延迟和异步处理等优化手段。

Result: 在基准测试中，AURORA在聚合节点上实现了超过3 GB/s的预计吞吐量，能够满足PandaX-xT实验的数据处理需求。

Conclusion: AURORA框架虽然为PandaX-xT开发，但具有实验无关性，可轻松适配其他大规模粒子和核物理实验的数据采集需求。

Abstract: The upcoming PandaX-xT experiment will deploy over 3,000 readout channels operating at a 500 MSa/s sampling rate, generating a sustained data bandwidth up to 1.6 GB/s. To meet this demanding requirement, we present AURORA, a high-performance, distributed data acquisition (DAQ) framework designed for scalability, low latency, and efficient resource utilization. Built on a modular architecture and leveraging modern I/O and networking technologies, including multi-level buffering, deferred and asynchronous processing, AURORA achieves a projected throughput of over 3 GB/s on the aggregation node in benchmark tests. While developed to support PandaX-xT, the framework is experiment-agnostic and readily adaptable to other large-scale particle and nuclear physics experiments.

</details>


### [238] [Nuclear Heterodyne Interferometry for Gravitational Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17157)
*Ralf Röhlsberger*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于同步辐射时间分辨核共振散射的相位敏感外差干涉测量新方法，用于核引力光谱学测试，将引力红移检测从能量域转换到时域干涉测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代光学时钟已能以极高精度探测电子跃迁的引力响应，但核领域的引力测试自Pound和Rebka的穆斯堡尔引力红移测量以来进展甚微。需要开发新方法来测试引力与核结构的耦合。

Method: 引入基于同步辐射时间分辨核共振散射的相位敏感外差干涉测量（phase-sensitive heterodyne interferometry）新方法。在该方案中，引力红移表现为延迟外差拍频信号的缓慢累积相位漂移，将核引力光谱学从能量域检测转换为时域干涉测量。

Result: 基于费舍尔信息分析（Fisher-information analysis）和蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）的研究表明，$^{57}$Fe的核引力红移可在几米垂直基线上数小时内检测到，对广义相对论偏差的百分级精度测试可在天尺度时间范围内实现。

Conclusion: 该方法建立了一个实验上现实且可扩展的平台，用于精确测试引力与核结构的耦合，为核引力光谱学提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: Gravitational spectroscopy tests the coupling of gravity to matter by measuring gravitationally induced frequency shifts of quantum transitions. While modern optical clocks probe the gravitational response of electronic transitions with extraordinary precision, tests in the nuclear sector have not progressed since the Mössbauer measurements of the gravitational redshift by Pound and Rebka. Here we introduce a new approach to nuclear gravitational spectroscopy based on phase-sensitive heterodyne interferometry of time-resolved nuclear resonant scattering of synchrotron radiation. In this scheme the gravitational redshift appears as a slowly accumulating phase drift of a delayed heterodyne beat signal, converting nuclear gravitational spectroscopy from energy-domain detection to time-domain interferometry. A Fisher-information analysis supported by Monte Carlo simulations and experimentally confirmed photon count rates shows that the nuclear gravitational redshift of $^{57}$Fe can be detected within hours on a few-meter-scale vertical baseline, with percent-level precision on deviations from general relativity becoming accessible on day-scale timescales. The method thus establishes an experimentally realistic and scalable platform for precision tests of gravitational coupling to nuclear structure.

</details>

### [239] [Contagion or Macroeconomic Fluctuations? Identifiability in Aggregated Default Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18118)
*Shintaro Mori*

Main category: q-fin.RM

TL;DR: 本文研究能否从聚合违约数据推断传染效应，通过比较三种依赖结构发现：在独立同分布设定下，Vasicek模型（共同因子依赖）提供最佳拟合；在允许违约概率跨年变化的分层设定下，年度违约计数的大部分变异由违约条件跨年变动而非年内传染解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨能否从聚合违约数据中推断出传染效应，将其视为可识别性问题，研究传染是否会在违约计数分布中产生与宏观经济波动诱导的组分不同的可区分组分。

Method: 研究比较了三种依赖结构：Lo-Davis模型中的累积传染、Torri模型中的阈值型传染，以及Vasicek模型中的共同因子依赖。首先在独立同分布（i.i.d.）设定下分析，随后通过分层设定允许违约概率跨年变化。

Result: 在独立同分布设定下，Vasicek模型提供最佳整体拟合，尤其在尾部，表明平滑混合结构比阈值型传染更能有效捕捉聚合层面的年度违约聚类。在分层设定下，年度违约计数的大部分变异由违约条件跨年变动而非年内传染解释。阈值型传染在聚合后无法分离出稳定组分，而累积传染则保留了一个小而持久的组分。

Conclusion: 研究结果阐明了在何种情况下仍能从粗粒度数据推断传染效应，以及在何种情况下传染效应被有效吸收到宏观经济变异中。阈值型传染在聚合后难以识别，而累积传染则保留了可识别的持久组分。

Abstract: Can contagion be inferred from aggregated default data? We study this as a problem of identifiability, asking whether contagion generates components in default count distributions that remain distinct from those induced by macroeconomic fluctuations. We compare three dependence structures: cumulative contagion in the Lo-Davis model, threshold-type contagion in the Torri model, and common-factor dependence in the Vasicek model. Under an i.i.d. specification, the Vasicek model provides the best overall fit, especially in the tail, indicating that a smooth mixture structure captures annual default clustering more effectively than threshold-type contagion at the aggregate level. We then allow the default probability to vary across years through a hierarchical specification. Under this extension, most of the variation in annual default counts is explained by cross-year movements in default conditions rather than by within-year contagion. What remains, however, depends on the interaction mechanism. In the Torri model, threshold-type contagion does not leave a stable component that can be separated from macroeconomic heterogeneity after aggregation. In the Lo-Davis model, by contrast, a small but persistent component remains visible in both the variance decomposition and the tail behavior. These results clarify when contagion can still be inferred from coarse-grained data and when it is effectively absorbed into macroeconomic variation.

### [240] [Enabling Lie-Algebraic Classical Simulation beyond Free Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16701)
*Adelina Bärligea,Matthew L. Sims-Goh,Jakob S. Kottmann*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文扩展了李代数模拟（$\mathfrak{g}$-sim）的应用范围，使其超越自由费米子体系，通过识别新的多项式维数DLA家族和引入对称性适配的基表示，实现了对具有大Pauli展开的结构化量子电路的经典模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有李代数模拟主要局限于自由费米子（matchgate）体系，无法有效处理生成元具有大Pauli展开的其他结构化电路。需要扩展该模拟范式以覆盖更广泛的量子动力学系统。

Method: 方法包括识别新的多项式维数动力学李代数（DLA）家族，并引入对称性适配的基表示：针对置换等变动力学开发了显式的Pauli轨道基，针对有界汉明权重（U(1)-等变）动力学开发了子空间适配的修正广义Gell-Mann基，同时优化了自由费米子Pauli代数的计算流程。

Result: 数值基准测试证实了有利的预处理缩放特性，并验证了大规模概念验证模拟的有效性。这些构造显著扩展了$\mathfrak{g}$-sim作为结构化量子动力学统一模拟工具的实际应用范围。

Conclusion: 通过识别新的多项式维数DLA家族和开发对称性适配的基表示，成功将李代数经典模拟扩展到自由费米子体系之外，为结构化量子动力学提供了更广泛的统一模拟框架。

Abstract: Efficient classical simulation has matured to a critical component of the quantum computing stack, driving hardware validation, algorithm design, and the study of structured quantum dynamics. Lie-algebraic simulation ($\mathfrak{g}$-sim) is a compelling approach: it replaces exponentially large Hilbert-space evolution by dynamics in a reduced adjoint space whose dimension is set by the dynamical Lie algebra (DLA) of the circuit, enabling efficient simulation whenever the DLA grows only polynomially with system size. In practice, however, existing applications of $\mathfrak{g}$-sim have been confined to free-fermionic (matchgate) regimes, and it has been unclear how to extend the paradigm to other structured circuits whose generators may have large Pauli expansions. Here we enable Lie-algebraic classical simulation beyond free fermions by identifying additional non-trivial families of polynomial-dimensional DLAs and introducing symmetry-adapted basis representations that make the adjoint space mapping tractable. In particular, we develop an explicit Pauli orbit basis for permutation-equivariant dynamics, supporting cubic-dimensional algebras despite exponential Pauli support, and a subspace-adapted (modified) generalized Gell-Mann basis for bounded Hamming-weight ($U(1)$-equivariant) dynamics, yielding polynomial costs on fixed excitation sectors. Together with streamlined routines for free-fermionic Pauli algebras and translation-invariant variants thereof, these constructions significantly broaden the practical scope of $\mathfrak{g}$-sim as a unifying simulation tool for structured quantum dynamics. Numerical benchmarks confirm favorable preprocessing scaling and validate large-scale proof-of-concept simulations.

### [241] [Causality from Projection and Hardy-Space Analyticity of Non-Markovian Memory Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17058)
*Kejun Liu*
