<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kramers-Kronig色散关系在线性响应理论中已标准化，但其在开放量子系统中非马尔可夫记忆核的适用性尚未严格建立。记忆核是描述约化动力学的核心对象，其因果性分析需要数学上的严格证明。

Method: 通过证明Nakajima-Zwanzig记忆核属于向量值Hardy空间H+p(B)，建立了严格的KK重构公式。发展了三个新理论结果：CP-Hardy阻碍定理、被动性-解析性定理和基于矩的Carleman判据。

Result: 在因子化初始态和连续谱密度条件下，记忆核属于Hardy空间，确保了KK关系的有效性。研究还发现关联初始态会破坏Hardy性质，这类似于Gavassino机制中因果微观动力学产生非因果宏观方程的现象。

Conclusion: 该研究为开放量子系统中非马尔可夫记忆核的Kramers-Kronig色散关系提供了严格的数学基础，建立了因果性、稳定性和解析性之间的深层联系，并揭示了初始关联对Hardy性质的破坏机制。

Abstract: The Kramers-Kronig (KK) dispersion relations connect the real and imaginary parts of a causal response function through a Hilbert transform. While standard for linear-response theory, their validity for non-Markovian memory kernels -- the central object governing reduced dynamics in open quantum systems -- has not been rigorously established. We prove that the Nakajima-Zwanzig memory kernel belongs to the vector-valued Hardy space H+p(B) for every p>1, provided the initial system-bath state is factorized and the bath has a continuous spectral density. This membership yields rigorous KK reconstruction formulas. We establish three new results, including (i) a CP-Hardy obstruction theorem showing that upper-half-plane poles in approximate kernels imply non-physical (non-CPTP) dynamics; (ii) a passivity-analyticity theorem connecting dissipative kernels to the Herglotz-Nevanlinna class, realizing Gavassino's stability-causality chain for open quantum systems; and (iii) a moment-based Carleman criterion guaranteeing that Pade-reconstructed kernels from Memory Kernel Coupling Theory automatically satisfy KK. We validate the framework on solvable models and construct a counterexample demonstrating that correlated initial states break the Hardy property -- the quantum analogue of Gavassino's mechanism for how acausal macroscopic equations emerge from causal microscopic dynamics.

### [242] [Map-Dependent Quantum Characteristic Functions and CP-Divisibility in Non-Markovian Quantum Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17185)
*Koichi Nakagawa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于量子动力学映射的归一化Choi算符构建的映射依赖量子特征函数（map-dependent quantum characteristic functions）。通过证明Bochner-Choi正定性定理，建立了关联Gram矩阵的正型条件与底层量子通道完全正定性之间的等价关系。将该构造应用于中间动力学映射，获得了CP可分性（CP-divisibility）与双时特征函数正定性之间的表征关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于从量子动力学映射的归一化Choi算符（normalized Choi operator）构造映射依赖量子特征函数。通过证明Bochner-Choi正定性定理（Bochner-Choi positivity theorem），建立关联Gram矩阵的正型条件与量子通道完全正定性之间的等价关系。将该构造应用于中间动力学映射（intermediate dynamical maps），分析CP可分性。

Result: 研究证明了Gram矩阵的正型条件等价于底层量子通道的完全正定性。对于振幅阻尼（amplitude damping）和纯退相位（pure dephasing）模型的数值示例表明，Gram矩阵的负性（negativity）与CP可分性的破坏以及信息回流（information backflow）的出现相吻合。该框架为量子统计学特征函数方法与量子动力学映射结构性质之间建立了新的联系。

Conclusion: 提出的框架在量子统计学中的特征函数方法与量子动力学映射的结构性质之间建立了新的桥梁。通过映射依赖量子特征函数和Bochner-Choi正定性定理，为分析量子通道的完全正定性和CP可分性提供了有效的理论工具，并通过数值示例验证了该框架的实际应用价值。

Abstract: We introduce map-dependent quantum characteristic functions constructed from the normalized Choi operator of quantum dynamical maps. We prove a Bochner--Choi positivity theorem establishing that the positive-type condition of the associated Gram matrix is equivalent to complete positivity of the underlying quantum channel. Applying the construction to intermediate dynamical maps, we obtain a characterization of CP-divisibility in terms of positivity of two-time characteristic functions. Numerical examples for amplitude damping and pure dephasing models demonstrate that negativity of the Gram matrix coincides with the breakdown of CP-divisibility and the emergence of information backflow. The proposed framework provides a new bridge between characteristic-function methods in quantum statistics and structural properties of quantum dynamical maps.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用系统解耦方法，结合分形辐射的严格热迹（thermal trace）与板状自相似几何的零温度积分真空迹（integrated vacuum trace）。分析由尺度依赖的卡西米尔系数 $C(d_s, \ln(d/\ell_*))$ 支配的系统，并严格区分有效宏观反作用与分形边界上的第一性原理局域迹反常。

Result: 对于由尺度依赖卡西米尔系数支配的系统，各向异性应力-能量张量产生与对数跑动 $\partial_{\ln d}C$ 成正比的积分真空迹。建立了有限层级（n）预分形实现的解析先决条件，使该有效形式主义能够转化为可实验验证的定量电磁理论。

Conclusion: 本文系统区分了分形几何中量子场相互作用的不同物理机制，建立了统一的有效框架，并为将该形式主义转化为可实验验证的定量理论提供了必要的解析基础。

Abstract: The interaction of quantum fields with fractal and self-similar geometries encompasses multiple distinct physical regimes, including spectral geometry on intrinsic fractals, macroscopic self-similar Casimir configurations, and bounded Euclidean cavities with fractal boundaries. While the thermal equations of state and spectral asymptotics for these systems are well established, a cohesive treatment of the vacuum trace frequently conflates rigorous mathematical bounds with phenomenological models. In this manuscript, we systematically decouple these regimes and advance a unified effective framework combining the rigorous thermal trace of fractal radiation with a zero-temperature integrated vacuum trace for plate-like self-similar geometries. We demonstrate that for systems governed by a scale-dependent Casimir coefficient $C(d_s, \ln(d/\ell_*))$, the anisotropic stress-energy tensor produces an integrated vacuum trace proportional to its logarithmic running, $\partial_{\ln d}C$. We strictly differentiate this effective macroscopic backreaction from first-principles local trace anomalies on genuine fractal boundaries. Finally, we analyze finite-level ($n$) prefractal realizations, establishing the analytical prerequisites necessary to transition this effective formalism into a quantitatively predictive electromagnetic theory amenable to experimental verification.

### [244] [Optomechanical Detection of Individual Gas Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18371)

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [245] [Quantum channel tomography: optimal bounds and a Heisenberg-to-classical phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17369)
*Kean Chen,Filippo Girardi,Aadil Oufkir,Nengkun Yu,Zhicheng Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子信道层析（quantum channel tomography）的最优查询复杂度，发现其依赖于膨胀率τ = r d₂/d₁，并在τ=1时呈现海森堡标度（1/ε），在τ≥1+Ω(1)时呈现经典标度（1/ε²），揭示了海森堡到经典的相变现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信道层析（quantum channel tomography）是量子硬件表征与验证的基础任务，但现有研究对其最优查询复杂度（optimal query complexity）的理解尚不充分。论文旨在确定学习未知量子信道完整经典描述所需的最小查询次数。

Method: 研究针对输入维度d₁、输出维度d₂、Kraus秩（Kraus rank）至多为r的未知量子信道，以误差ε进行层析。引入膨胀率（dilation rate）τ = r d₂/d₁作为关键参数，分析其在三个不同τ区间的最优查询复杂度。

Result: 在边界区间（τ=1），Choi迹范数（Choi trace norm）误差下的查询复杂度为Θ(r d₁ d₂/ε)，钻石范数（diamond norm）误差下界为Ω(r d₁ d₂/ε)，上界为O(min{r d₁¹·⁵ d₂/ε, r d₁ d₂/ε²})。在远离边界区间（τ≥1+Ω(1)），两种误差度量的查询复杂度均为Θ(r d₁ d₂/ε²)。

Conclusion: 量子信道层析的查询复杂度存在从海森堡标度（Heisenberg scaling）到经典标度（classical scaling）的尖锐相变（phase transition）。在τ=1时呈现1/ε的海森堡标度，在τ≥1+Ω(1)时呈现1/ε²的经典标度，而在近边界区间（1<τ<1+o(1)）则呈现混合标度行为。

Abstract: How many black-box queries to a quantum channel are needed to learn its full classical description? This question lies at the heart of quantum channel tomography (also known as quantum process tomography), a fundamental task in the characterization and validation of quantum hardware. Despite extensive prior work, the optimal query complexity for quantum channel tomography is far from fully understood.
  In this paper, we study tomography of an unknown quantum channel with input dimension $d_1$, output dimension $d_2$, and Kraus rank at most $r$, to within error $\varepsilon$. We identify the dilation rate $τ= r d_2 / d_1$ (which always satisfies $τ\geq 1$ due to the trace preservation of quantum channels) as a key parameter, and establish that the optimal query complexity of channel tomography exhibits distinct scaling laws across three regimes of $τ$.
  - In the boundary regime ($τ= 1$): we show that the query complexity is $Θ(r d_1 d_2/\varepsilon)$ for Choi trace norm error $\varepsilon$, and is upper bounded by $O(\min\{r d_1^{1.5} d_2/\varepsilon, r d_1 d_2/\varepsilon^2\})$ and lower bounded by $Ω(r d_1 d_2/\varepsilon)$ for diamond norm error $\varepsilon$.
  - In the away-from-boundary regime ($τ\geq 1+Ω(1)$): we show that the query complexity is $Θ(r d_1 d_2/\varepsilon^2)$ for both Choi trace norm and diamond norm errors $\varepsilon$.
  Our results uncover a sharp Heisenberg-to-classical phase transition in the query complexity of quantum channel tomography: at $τ=1$, the optimal query complexity exhibits Heisenberg scaling $1/\varepsilon$, whereas for $τ\geq 1+Ω(1)$, it exhibits classical scaling $1/\varepsilon^2$. In addition, we show that in the near-boundary regime ($1< τ< 1+o(1)$), the query complexity exhibits a mixture of Heisenberg and classical scaling behaviors.

</details>


### [246] [Complex Quaternionic Formulations of Dirac, Electrodynamic, and Electroweak Fields and Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16766)
*James Henry Atwater,David Lambert,Yuri Rostovtsev*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一个简单的代数转换，将标准$\mathfrak{sl}_2\mathbb{C}$表示与复四元数（$\mathbb{H}\otimes_\mathbb{R}\mathbb{C}$）联系起来，并利用这一转换构建了狄拉克理论、电动力学乃至标准模型电弱部分的新超复数描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在通过建立$\mathfrak{sl}_2\mathbb{C}$标准表示与复四元数（complex-quaternions）之间的代数转换，为狄拉克理论、电动力学和电弱理论构建一个新颖的超复数描述框架。

Method: 建立$\mathfrak{sl}_2\mathbb{C}$标准表示与复四元数（$\mathbb{H}\otimes_\mathbb{R}\mathbb{C}$）之间的简单转换，并利用这一代数结构构建狄拉克旋量（Dirac spinors）的超复数描述。通过将构造的狄拉克旋量与电磁场耦合，并扩展至电弱理论，探索自发对称性破缺条件。

Result: 研究发现，将构造的狄拉克旋量与电磁场耦合能够给出带电自旋-1/2粒子的正确磁矩。电弱理论的扩展需要引入轻子场与希格斯场（Higgs fields）之间的代数区分，这是标准模型中所没有的。使用弱同位旋（weak isospin）和超荷（hypercharge）的替代表示探索自发对称性破缺条件，该表示与标准模型在弱中性流（weak neutral currents）的整体符号上存在分歧。

Conclusion: 论文成功建立了$\mathfrak{sl}_2\mathbb{C}$与复四元数之间的代数转换，并基于此构建了狄拉克理论和电弱理论的新超复数描述。该框架能够正确描述带电自旋-1/2粒子的磁矩，但在电弱理论部分与标准模型在弱中性流的符号上存在差异，为理论物理提供了新的数学描述视角。

Abstract: A simple translation between a standard representation of $\mathfrak{sl}_2\mathbb{C}$ and the complex-quaternions ($\mathbb{H}\otimes_\mathbb{R}\mathbb{C}$) is established and exploited to construct a novel hyper-complex description of the Dirac theory, electrodynamics, and ultimately the electroweak sector of the standard model. We find that coupling the constructed Dirac spinors to electromagnetism yields the correct magnetic moment for charged spin-1/2 particles. Extending electrodynamics to electroweak theory necessitates an algebraic distinction between the structures of the leptonic and Higgs fields not present in the standard model. The conditions of spontaneous symmetry breaking are explored using an alternative representation of weak isospin and hypercharge equivalent to an irreducible representation of $\mathfrak{su}(2)\oplus\mathfrak{u}(1)$ on $\mathbb{C}^4$. This alternative representation disagrees with the standard model on the overall signs of weak neutral currents.

### [249] [Time evolution of quantum gates and the necessity of complex numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17086)
*M. P. Vaughan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了量子门（quantum gates）的动力学能否用实数量子力学（real QM）建模。研究表明，许多量子门无法用相同维度的实向量空间中的特殊正交群（special orthogonal group）表示，而常用的复向量空间到实向量空间的映射本质上仍表示复数矩阵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索量子门（quantum gates）的动力学是否可以用实数量子力学（real QM）来建模。特别关注量子计算中常见单量子门（unary gates）在布洛赫球（Bloch sphere）上的轨迹以及复数相位在产生两量子比特纠缠（entanglement）中的作用。

Method: 论文采用了一种简单方案，将量子门效应描述为有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）在特征时间内的作用。通过分析特殊正交群（special orthogonal group）在实向量空间中的表示能力，研究了从复向量空间到实向量空间的映射关系，特别是从$\mathbb{C}^{2^{n-1}}$到$\mathbb{R}^{2^{n}}$的映射。

Result: 研究发现，许多具有行列式-1的量子门无法用相同维度的实向量空间中的特殊正交算子（special orthogonal operators）建模。常用的复向量空间到实向量空间的映射实际上只是复数标量表示到其$2\times2$矩阵等价的同构映射，因此得到的矩阵本质上仍是复数矩阵的表示。

Conclusion: 结论表明，实数量子力学无法完全模拟量子门的动力学演化。从$\mathbb{C}^{2^{n-1}}$到$\mathbb{R}^{2^{n}}$的映射仅将$\mathrm{End}(\mathbb{C}^{2^{n-1}})$的元素映射到$\mathrm{End}(\mathbb{R}^{2^{n}})$的一个受限子空间，该子空间仅能复现复数矩阵的"实数"表示。

Abstract: As physical systems, qubits must evolve from input to output state. We describe a simple scheme in which the effect of a quantum gate is described by the action of an effective Hamiltonian acting for some characteristic time. This model shows that the action of common unary gates is to induce Bloch sphere trajectories along lines of latitude relative to an eigenvector of the gate. Such trajectories would immediately move a `rebit', initially confined to a line of latitude, off this line and acquire a complex phase. The role of the complex phase in bringing about the entanglement of two qubits is also highlighted. It is then asked whether such dynamics could be modelled using real QM. It is shown that the continuous evolution required for such dynamics can only be provided by members of the special orthogonal group of the vector space. Since the matrices representing many quantum gates of interest have determinant -1, no real special orthogonal operators can model their evolution if the dimension of the real vector space is the same as that of the complex space. Next we look at the mapping from a complex vector space of dimension $N$ to a real space of dimension $2N$ that is often used to construct `real' QM. It is shown that this is just an isomorphic mapping from the scalar representation of complex numbers to their $2\times2$ matrix equivalents, so that the resulting matrices are actually represent complex matrices. Finally, we investigate the endomorphism of real vector spaces of dimension $N = 2^{n}$, where $n \in \mathbb{Z}^{+}$, suitable for the modelling of $n-1$ qubits. We confirm that the mapping from $\mathbb{C}^{2^{n-1}} \to \mathbb{R}^{2^{n}}$ only maps elements of $\mathrm{End}(\mathbb{C}^{2^{n-1}})$ to a restricted subspace of $\mathrm{End}(\mathbb{R}^{2^{n}})$ that reproduces the `real' representation of complex matrices.

</details>

In this context, low-dimensional platforms, including quantum dots, superconducting nanowires and layered materials have emerged as crucial frontiers of research. This review explores the state-of-the-art of different low-dimensional SPD platforms, focusing on the engineering physics across their device architectures, performance parameters and application potential. ### [251] [Repeated weak measurements: watching quantum correlations evolve](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17719)
*Emine Altuntas,Ian B. Spielman*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于弱量子测量的非侵入式协议，通过关联两次时间分离的测量直接获取动力学关联函数，无需外部扰动，并在玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中实验验证了该方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多体量子系统测量常受测量反作用（measurement backaction）限制，且动力学性质通常需要通过扰动系统并测量其响应来获取。本研究旨在开发一种非侵入式测量方法，将测量反作用转化为优势。

Method: 采用基于一对弱量子测量（weak quantum measurements）的最小侵入协议，通过关联时间分离的测量：首次测量检测任何类型的涨落，第二次测量追踪其时间演化。该方法使用相位对比成像（phase-contrast imaging）在原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）中实现，并通过Aharonov的后选择量子弱值（post-selection-based quantum weak values）分离量子反作用的影响。

Result: 该方法直接测量了动力学关联函数，获得了双时密度-密度关联函数（two-time density-density correlation function），即Van Hove函数，并通过其傅里叶变换得到了动力学结构因子（dynamical structure factor）。这些量是中子散射、X射线散射和原子布拉格光谱学的基础。

Conclusion: 该弱测量方法具有广泛适用性，能够获取任何一对可弱测量可观测量之间的关联函数，超越了传统强测量的能力。通过利用测量反作用而非避免它，为量子系统动力学研究提供了新范式。

Abstract: Experimental access to many-body quantum systems is often limited by measurement backaction, and key dynamical properties are typically obtained by perturbing a system and measuring its response. Here we replace this active paradigm with a minimally invasive protocol based on a pair of weak quantum measurements that leverages measurement backaction as a strength. By correlating time-separated measurements with the first detecting fluctuations -- of any sort -- and the second tracking their time evolution, our method directly measures dynamical correlation functions without external perturbation. We demonstrate this technique in an atomic Bose-Einstein condensate using phase-contrast imaging to obtain the two-time density-density correlation function known as the Van Hove function and, through its Fourier transform, the dynamical structure factor. Due to the role of spatial correlations in scattering, these quantities underpin neutron and X-ray scattering and atomic Bragg spectroscopy. This approach is broadly applicable, providing access to correlation functions between any pair of observables amenable to weak measurement, thereby going beyond the capabilities of conventional strong measurements. We further isolate the role of quantum backaction through Aharonov's post-selection-based quantum weak values.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Dark and subradiant states have emerged as a promising resource for stabilizing open quantum batteries against dissipation, but existing studies are largely limited to qubit ensembles and symmetry-based constructions. Focusing on a minimal model of two interacting qutrits coupled to a common bath, we analytically construct dark, bright, and funnel states-excited states that decay exclusively into protected manifolds. We also derive quantitative robustness conditions governed by the ratio of interaction strength to anharmonicity. We show that multilevel ladder structure and exchange interactions enable energetic storage states beyond the qubit case. Numerical simulations confirm that these states exhibit long-lived energy storage under realistic dissipation. Finally, we show that high-energy funnel states provide a natural design target for multilevel quantum batteries, as their decay pathways are highly structured and directed toward protected manifolds. Knowledge of these pathways offers a principled basis for developing future protection and control strategies in superconducting multilevel platforms.

### [253] [Quantum many-body scars in random unitary circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18244)
*Luca Capizzi,Benoît Ferté*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含单个量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scar）的可解析随机幺正电路，从第一性原理推导了其微扰的热化机制，并发现尽管疤痕对局域可观测量热力学无关，却在纠缠动力学中留下明显印记，驱动了局域测量无法探测的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了一个包含单个量子多体疤痕的可解析随机幺正电路（random unitary circuit），并从第一性原理推导了控制其微扰的热化机制，该机制由涨落界面（fluctuating interfaces）的图像描述。

Result: 研究发现，尽管量子多体疤痕对局域可观测量（local observables）在热力学上无关，却在纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics）中留下尖锐的指纹印记。疤痕驱动了一个随微扰强度变化的相变，该相变无法被任何局域测量探测。

Conclusion: 量子多体疤痕在纠缠动力学中具有显著影响，能够驱动局域测量无法探测的相变，揭示了疤痕态在非局域性质中的持久性特征。

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars are rare exceptions to thermalization: they sustain non-thermal stationary states without the protection of any local conservation law, and are generally expected to be fragile. Here we construct an analytically tractable random unitary circuit hosting a single scar, and derive from first principles the thermalization mechanism governing perturbations thereof - described by a picture of fluctuating interfaces. Surprisingly, despite being thermodynamically irrelevant for local observables, the scar leaves a sharp fingerprint in the entanglement dynamics, driving a transition as a function of perturbation strength that is not probed by any local measurement.

### [254] [Random-State Generation and Preparation Complexity in Rydberg Atom Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18457)
*Edison S. Carrera,Grégoire Misguich*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过随机全局脉冲序列在周期性里德堡原子链中生成量子态，分析其统计特性与Haar随机态的差异。研究发现强相互作用下希尔伯特空间探索受限，弱相互作用下系统在长时间尺度上接近Haar统计特性，并探索了在该区域利用量子最优控制高效制备对称量子态的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究里德堡原子阵列（Rydberg atom arrays）作为量子多体系统平台的特性，特别关注在硬件约束和固定演化时间下，通过随机全局脉冲序列生成的量子态统计性质。旨在理解不同相互作用强度下量子态的演化特性及其与Haar随机态的差异。

Method: 采用周期性链上的里德堡-伊辛哈密顿量（Rydberg-Ising Hamiltonian），通过数值模拟研究受硬件约束和固定演化时间的随机全局脉冲序列生成的态系综。比较这些态与相关晶格对称性区域中Haar随机态的统计特性，并分析不同相互作用强度下的演化行为。

Result: 强相互作用（短原子间距）下，有效阻塞效应限制希尔伯特空间探索和纠缠增长，约化密度矩阵的能级间距统计接近随机矩阵预测，但测量概率分布偏离Porter-Thomas行为。弱相互作用（大原子间距）下，系统在长时间尺度上接近Haar统计特性，表现为纠缠熵、纠缠谱统计和测量概率分布的变化。中间相互作用强度下，在实验相关时间尺度上观察到类似行为。

Conclusion: 在中间相互作用区域，可以利用量子最优控制（quantum optimal control）高效制备具有广泛熵分布的对称量子态，保真度较高（9个自旋的保真度误差在10^-5到3×10^-2之间）。然而保真度随目标态纠缠熵增加而降低，表明高纠缠态在实际约束下本质上更难制备。

Abstract: Rydberg atom arrays are powerful platforms for studying quantum many-body systems. We consider the Rydberg-Ising Hamiltonian on periodic chains and numerically study ensembles of states generated by random global pulse sequences subject to hardware constraints and fixed evolution times. We compare the statistical properties of such states with those of Haar-random states within the relevant lattice symmetry sector. In the strong-interaction regime (short interatomic distance), the dynamics is governed by an effective blockade that restricts Hilbert-space exploration and limits entanglement growth. In this regime, level-spacing statistics of reduced density matrices are close to random-matrix predictions, while the distribution of measurement probabilities deviates from Porter-Thomas behavior. For weaker interactions (larger interatomic distance), the system approaches Haar-like statistics at long times, as reflected in entanglement entropy, entanglement spectrum statistics, and the distribution of measurement probabilities. At intermediate interactions, this behavior is observed on experimentally relevant timescales. Motivated by this observation, we investigate whether generic symmetric quantum states can be efficiently prepared using quantum optimal control in this regime. Employing target states drawn from an ensemble with a broad entropy distribution, we observe high fidelities (infidelities between $10^{-5}$ and $3\times 10^{-2}$ for 9 spins). The fidelity, however, decreases with the entanglement entropy of the target state, demonstrating that highly entangled states are intrinsically harder to prepare under realistic constraints.

</details>


### [255] [Dissipative Preparation of Correlated Quantum States in Dipolar Rydberg Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18542)
*Mingsheng Tian,Zhen Bi,Thomas Iadecola,Bryce Gadway*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于可控耗散辅助原子的非互易、能量选择性跃迁协议，用于引导偶极量子系统向目标多体态演化，无需哈密顿量先验知识即可稳定多体谱中的任意态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 制备关联量子态对新兴技术至关重要，但在多体系统中仍具挑战性。现有方法通常局限于基态制备且需要哈密顿量先验知识。

Method: 通过引入两种可控耗散辅助原子（controllable dissipative auxiliary atoms），分别作为非互易激发和退激发通道，实现希尔伯特空间中的定向行走（directional walk）。该方法专为偶极里德堡阵列（dipolar Rydberg arrays）设计，但适用于具有类似能力的系统。

Result: 该协议能够稳定多体谱（many-body spectrum）中的任意态，不限于基态，且无需哈密顿量先验知识。提供了一种灵活且可扩展的态制备框架。

Conclusion: 该耗散协议为可编程平台中的态制备提供了灵活且可扩展的框架，通过非互易、能量选择性跃迁引导系统向目标多体态演化，突破了传统方法的限制。

Abstract: Preparing correlated quantum states is essential for emerging technologies, but remains challenging in many-body systems. Here we propose a dissipative protocol that engineers nonreciprocal, energy-selective transitions to steer dipolar quantum systems toward desired many-body states. This is realized by introducing two types of controllable dissipative auxiliary atoms that act as nonreciprocal excitation and de-excitation channels, respectively, enabling a directional walk in Hilbert space. This approach enables stabilization of states across the many-body spectrum, not limited to the ground state and requiring no \textit{a priori} knowledge of the Hamiltonian. Our approach is designed for neutral atoms in dipolar Rydberg arrays, but applies broadly to setups with similar capabilities, providing a flexible and scalable framework for state preparation in programmable platforms.

</details>

### [256] [A fully parallel densely connected probabilistic Ising machine with inertia for real-time applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17109)
*Ruomin Zhu,Abhishek Kumar Singh,Jérémie Laydevant,Fan O. Wu,Ari Kapelyan,Davide Venturelli,Kyle Jamieson,Peter L. McMahon*

Main category: cs.ET

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种改进的伊辛自旋动力学方法，通过添加惯性项实现了伊辛机（Ising machine）的完全并行同步更新，显著提升了求解密集连接问题的速度和成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于概率比特（p-bits）的伊辛机在并行更新时会导致求解能力下降，这限制了其在密集连接问题中作为快速求解器的应用。现有方法认为伊辛自旋（Ising spins）无法在不破坏求解能力的情况下进行并行更新。

Method: 研究引入了改进的伊辛自旋动力学，通过添加惯性项（inertia term）实现完全并行同步更新。该方法通过算法仿真、FPGA硬件仿真和FPGA实验进行了验证。

Result: 在多种抽象和实际应用基准测试中，完全并行更新带来了超线性增长的速度优势。对于200个自旋的问题，平均加速比达到约35倍，最佳单实例加速比达到150倍。该方法能够满足5G无线网络中实时MIMO检测的严格要求。

Conclusion: 该研究成功克服了伊辛机并行更新的限制，通过算法-硬件协同设计实现了在保持求解质量的同时满足实时应用需求，为伊辛机在密集连接优化问题中的实际应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Ising machines -- special-purpose hardware for heuristically solving Ising optimization problems -- based on probabilistic bits (p-bits) have been established as a promising alternative to heuristic optimization algorithms run on conventional computers. However, it has -- until now -- been thought that Ising spins that are connected in probabilistic Ising machines cannot be updated in parallel without ruining the machine's solving ability. This has been a major challenge for using probabilistic Ising machines as fast solvers for densely connected problems. Here, we circumvent this by introducing a modified Ising spin dynamics with an added inertia term, and verify in algorithm simulations, FPGA hardware emulation, and FPGA experiments that it enables fully parallel, synchronous updates while improving rather than degrading success probability.
  We evaluated on various types of abstract (Max-Cut and Sherrington-Kirkpatrick-model) and application-derived (MIMO, wireless detection) dense Ising benchmark instances. Performing fully parallel updates results in a speed advantage that grows faster than linearly with the number of spins, giving rise to large time-to-solution increases for practical problem sizes. For both Max-Cut and the SK-1 model at a problem size of 200, our approach achieved an average speedup of $\approx 35\times$, with the best single-instance speedup reaching $150\times$.
  As an example of the practical utility of our approach in an application where speed is critical, we further show by co-designing the algorithm dynamics with the hardware implementation -- co-optimizing for solver ability and silicon resource usage -- that probabilistic Ising machines based on our approach satisfy the stringent solution quality and latency/throughput requirements for real-time MIMO detection in modern 5G cellular wireless networks while using a practically reasonable silicon area.

</details>

### [257] [Hodge Atoms at Conifold Degenerations: F-Bundles, Limiting Mixed Hodge Modules, and the Rigid-Flexible Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17754)
*Abdul Rahman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文扩展了Katzarkov-Kontsevich-Pantev-Yu的Hodge原子框架，应用于Calabi-Yau三维流形的一参数锥形退化。对于具有r个普通双奇点的退化，构造了光滑纤维Hodge原子的规范刚性-柔性分解，其非分裂结构由相交矩阵控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将Hodge原子（Hodge atoms）框架扩展到Calabi-Yau三维流形的一参数锥形退化（conifold degenerations）。主要动机是理解这类退化过程中Hodge结构的精确行为，特别是处理具有普通双奇点（ordinary double points）的退化情形。

Method: 方法的核心是构造一个规范的刚性-柔性分解（rigid-flexible decomposition），将光滑纤维的Hodge原子分解为刚性原子和柔性原子。技术核心是Stokes-扩展识别（Stokes--Extension Identification），将Dubrovin连接在锥形轨迹处的Stokes矩阵与混合Hodge模实现下的变分态射矩阵等同起来。

Result: 对于具有r个普通双奇点的退化，构造了修正退化对象所附光滑纤维Hodge原子的规范刚性-柔性分解。刚性原子在退化过程中保持不变，而柔性原子是秩为一的贡献，每个消失循环对应一个。总退化原子构成一个精确序列，其非分裂结构由相交矩阵控制。

Conclusion: 本文成功扩展了Hodge原子框架到Calabi-Yau三维流形的锥形退化，建立了Hodge原子的刚性-柔性分解理论。该分解揭示了退化过程中Hodge结构的精确行为，并通过Stokes-扩展识别建立了几何与表示论之间的联系。

Abstract: We extend the Hodge atoms framework of Katzarkov--Kontsevich--Pantev--Yu to one-parameter conifold degenerations of Calabi--Yau threefolds. For a degeneration $π\colon X \to Δ$ whose central fiber $X_0$ has $r$ ordinary double points, we construct a canonical rigid-flexible decomposition of the Hodge atoms of the nearby smooth fiber attached to the corrected degeneration object. The rigid atom $A(\IC^H_{X_0})$ is preserved across the degeneration, while the flexible atoms $A(i_{k*}\QQ^H_{\{p_k\}}(-1))$ are rank-one contributions, one for each vanishing cycle. The total degeneration atom $A(P^H)$ is the atom of the corrected mixed Hodge module $P^H\in\MHM(X_0)$ and fits into an exact sequence of atoms whose non-split structure is controlled by the intersection matrix $(\langleδ_i,δ_j\rangle)$. The technical core is the Stokes--Extension Identification, which identifies the Stokes matrix of the Dubrovin connection at the conifold locus with the matrix of the variation morphism $\varF\colon\varphi_π(F) \to ψ_π(F)$ under mixed Hodge module realization.

</details>

### [258] [Effective theory of quantum phases in the dipolar planar rotor chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16999)
*Estêvão V. B. de Oliveira,Muhammad Shaeer Moeed,Pierre-Nicholas Roy*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过时间无关微扰理论（time-independent perturbation theory）和小角度二次近似（small angle quadratic approximation）建立了相互作用的偶极平面转子（dipolar planar rotors）集体行为的理论描述，分析了系统的有序和无序量子相（quantum phases）的基态性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是发展一个理论框架来描述相互作用的偶极平面转子的集体行为，特别是针对系统的有序和无序量子相的基态性质。

Method: 采用时间无关微扰理论处理无序相（disordered phase），对于有序相（ordered phase）则基于偶极有序的稳定平衡构型构建二次近似，并证明包含势能展开的四次项对于修正量子化模糊性（quantization ambiguities）引起的能谱偏移至关重要。

Result: 研究直接计算并分析了系统有序和无序量子相的基态性质，证明了时间无关微扰理论适用于无序相，同时使用精确对角化（Exact Diagonalization）和密度矩阵重整化群（Density Matrix Renormalization Group）等数值技术对两种近似的质量进行了基准测试。

Conclusion: 该工作为相互作用的偶极平面转子系统提供了完整的理论描述框架，通过结合微扰理论和二次近似方法，成功处理了不同量子相的基态性质，并通过数值方法验证了理论近似的可靠性。

Abstract: In this work, we develop a theoretical description of the collective behavior of interacting dipolar planar rotors by using time independent perturbation theory and a small angle quadratic approximation. The ground state properties for both the ordered and disordered quantum phases of the system are directly calculated and analyzed. Time-independent perturbation theory is shown to be appropriate for the disordered phase. For the ordered phase, we construct a quadratic approximation based on the stable equilibrium configurations of the dipolar ordering; we show that the inclusion of the quartic terms from the expansion of the potential energy are essential to correct the shift in the energy spectrum due to quantization ambiguities. Numerical techniques such as Exact Diagonalization and Density Matrix Renormalization Group are used for the benchmark the quality of both approximations.

</details>
